# Enriched Recipe Catalog

*Total Recipes: 430*

# Category: Asian Cuisine

## Sushi
- **Original Servings:** 4-6 rolls (32-48 pieces)
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups uncooked short-grain Japanese rice (sushi rice)
- 1/4 cup rice vinegar
- 1 tbsp sugar
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 pack of dried seaweed sheets (Nori)
- 1/2 lb sushi-grade raw salmon or tuna, sliced into strips
- 1 cucumber, sliced into matchsticks
- 1 avocado, sliced
- Soy sauce, for serving
- Wasabi paste, for serving
- Pickled ginger (Gari), for serving

### Instructions
1. Rinse the rice until the water runs clear. Cook according to package instructions (usually 1:1.2 rice-to-water ratio).
1. While the rice is hot, gently fold in the mixture of rice vinegar, sugar, and salt. Let the rice cool to room temperature.
1. Slice fish and vegetables into long, thin strips (about 4 inches long).
1. Place a bamboo rolling mat on a flat surface. Lay a sheet of nori (shiny side down) on the mat.
1. Wet hands with water and spread a thin, even layer of rice over the nori, leaving a 1-inch border at the top edge.
1. Place fillings in a horizontal line across the center of the rice.
1. Using the mat, lift the edge closest to you and roll it tightly over the fillings.
1. Dampen the 1-inch border of nori with water to seal the roll.
1. Use a sharp knife to cut the roll into 6–8 equal pieces, wiping the knife with a damp cloth between cuts.
1. Serve immediately with soy sauce, wasabi, and ginger.

---

## Sashimi
- **Original Servings:** 2-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/2 lb to 1 lb sushi-grade fish (Tuna, Salmon, or Yellowtail)
- Japanese soy sauce (Shoyu)
- Wasabi (paste or freshly grated)
- Pickled ginger (Gari)
- Shredded Daikon radish (Tsuma), for garnish
- Fresh Shiso leaves, for garnish
- Lemon wedges, for garnish

### Instructions
1. Keep the fish in the refrigerator until ready to slice to ensure firmness.
1. Peel and julienne Daikon radish into thin strips. Soak in ice water for 5 minutes, then drain and pat dry.
1. Place the fish block on a clean cutting board.
1. Using a very sharp knife, cut across the grain of the fish into slices approximately 1/4 to 1/3 inch (6-8 mm) thick using one fluid pulling motion.
1. Arrange the fish slices in a fanned-out, overlapping row against the Daikon and Shiso leaf garnish.
1. Serve immediately with individual dishes of soy sauce and a dollop of wasabi and ginger on the side.

---

## Tempura Shrimp
- **Original Servings:** 2-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 12-15 Large or Jumbo Shrimp (peeled and deveined, tails on)
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour or cornstarch (for dredging)
- 1 large egg, cold
- 1 cup ice-cold water (or sparkling water)
- 1 cup all-purpose flour, sifted
- Neutral oil (vegetable or canola), for frying
- Pinch of salt (optional)

### Instructions
1. Prepare shrimp by making 3-4 shallow horizontal slits across the belly. Press down on the back to straighten them until they 'pop'. Pat dry.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C) in a pot (2-3 inches deep).
1. Make the batter by lightly beating the cold egg and adding ice-cold water.
1. Add sifted flour all at once and mix with chopsticks for only 10-20 seconds. The batter should remain lumpy; do not overmix.
1. Dredge each shrimp in dry flour/cornstarch, shaking off excess.
1. Dip shrimp into the cold batter holding the tail, and gently lower into the hot oil.
1. Fry for 2-3 minutes until pale golden and crispy. Drain on a wire rack or paper towels.
1. Serve hot with Tentsuyu dipping sauce or sea salt.

---

## Takoyaki
- **Original Servings:** 30-32 pieces
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup (150g) all-purpose flour
- 2 cups (500ml) cold dashi stock
- 2 large eggs
- 1 tsp soy sauce
- 1/4 tsp salt
- 4-5 oz boiled octopus, cut into 1/2-inch cubes
- 2-3 green onions, finely chopped
- 2 tbsp pickled ginger (Beni Shoga), finely chopped
- 1/4 cup Tenkasu (tempura bits)
- Takoyaki sauce, for topping
- Japanese mayonnaise (Kewpie), for topping
- Aonori (dried seaweed flakes), for topping
- Katsuobushi (dried bonito flakes), for topping

### Instructions
1. Whisk eggs, soy sauce, and salt in a bowl. Gradually add dashi stock and flour, whisking until a thin, smooth batter forms.
1. Heat a takoyaki pan over medium-high heat and grease each cavity and the flat surface generously with oil.
1. Pour batter into the holes until they overflow slightly onto the flat surface.
1. Drop one piece of octopus into each hole. Sprinkle green onions, pickled ginger, and tenkasu over the entire pan.
1. After 2-3 minutes, use a pick to 'cut' the excess batter and flip each ball 90 degrees, tucking excess batter inside.
1. Continue rotating the balls frequently until they form a spherical shape and become golden brown and crispy (about 4-5 minutes).
1. Transfer to a plate and drizzle with takoyaki sauce and mayonnaise.
1. Top with aonori and bonito flakes. Serve immediately.

---

## Teriyaki Salmon
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 salmon fillets (approx. 6 oz each)
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- 1/4 cup water
- 2 tbsp mirin
- 2 tbsp brown sugar or honey
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp olive or vegetable oil
- Green onions and toasted sesame seeds, for garnish
- 1 tsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tsp water (optional slurry)

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, water, mirin, brown sugar, sesame oil, ginger, and garlic to make the sauce.
1. Optionally marinate salmon in half the sauce for 15-20 minutes. Reserve remaining sauce.
1. Heat oil in a non-stick skillet over medium-high heat. Season salmon with salt and pepper.
1. Sear salmon skin-side up for 4-5 minutes until golden. Flip and cook for another 3-4 minutes until done. Remove salmon.
1. Pour reserved sauce into the skillet. Bring to a simmer. If using, add cornstarch slurry to thicken.
1. Return salmon to the pan and coat with the glaze.
1. Serve immediately garnished with green onions and sesame seeds.

---

## Pad Thai with Shrimp
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 5 oz dried flat rice noodles (medium width)
- 12 large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 3 tbsp fish sauce
- 3 tbsp tamarind paste (concentrate)
- 2-3 tbsp palm sugar or brown sugar
- 1 tsp chili flakes
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1/4 cup extra-firm tofu, cut into small batons
- 1 shallot, finely sliced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 cup fresh bean sprouts
- 3 scallions, cut into 1-inch pieces
- 3 tbsp vegetable oil
- 1/4 cup roasted peanuts, crushed
- 1 lime, cut into wedges

### Instructions
1. Soak rice noodles in lukewarm water for 30–40 minutes until al dente. Drain and set aside.
1. Whisk together fish sauce, tamarind paste, sugar, and chili flakes to make the sauce.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a wok over high heat. Sear shrimp until pink (1-2 mins per side). Remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil, shallots, garlic, and tofu. Stir-fry for 1-2 minutes until lightly browned.
1. Add noodles and sauce. Stir-fry vigorously, adding 1-2 tbsp water if needed until noodles are tender.
1. Push noodles to the side, pour in eggs, and scramble until mostly set. Toss into the noodles.
1. Add shrimp, bean sprouts, and scallions. Toss for 30-60 seconds.
1. Serve topped with crushed peanuts and lime wedges on the side.

---

## Thai Fish Curry
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs firm white fish (snapper, cod, or halibut), cut into 2-inch pieces
- 2-3 tbsp Thai red or yellow curry paste
- 1 can (14 oz) full-fat coconut milk
- 1/2 cup water or broth
- 1 onion, diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp fish sauce
- 1 tbsp lime juice
- 1 tbsp brown sugar
- 2-3 cups mixed vegetables (carrots, snap peas, bell peppers)
- 1-2 tbsp coconut oil
- Fresh cilantro and lime wedges, for garnish

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium heat. Sauté onion until soft (3-5 mins). Add garlic and ginger and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in curry paste and cook for 1-2 minutes until fragrant.
1. Add coconut milk, water, fish sauce, and sugar. Bring to a gentle simmer.
1. Add vegetables and simmer for 3-5 minutes until they start to soften.
1. Nestle fish pieces into the sauce. Cover and simmer for 4-6 minutes until fish is opaque and flakes easily.
1. Stir in lime juice. Adjust seasoning with more fish sauce if needed.
1. Serve hot over jasmine rice, garnished with cilantro.

---

## Tom Yum Seafood Soup
- **Original Servings:** 2-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 cups water or seafood stock
- 2 stalks lemongrass, bruised and cut into 2-inch pieces
- 1-inch piece galangal, sliced
- 5-6 makrut lime leaves, torn
- 3-6 Thai bird’s eye chilies, lightly smashed
- 1 lb mixed seafood (prawns, squid, mussels, fish)
- 1 cup oyster or straw mushrooms
- 1 medium tomato, wedged
- 2-3 small shallots, peeled and smashed
- 2-3 tbsp fish sauce
- 3-4 tbsp fresh lime juice
- 1-2 tbsp Thai roasted chili paste (Nam Prik Pao)
- 1 tsp sugar
- Fresh cilantro, for garnish

### Instructions
1. Bring stock to a boil in a large pot. Add lemongrass, galangal, lime leaves, and shallots. Simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Add mushrooms, tomatoes, and chili paste. Stir until dissolved.
1. Add seafood and cook for 2-3 minutes until prawns are pink and mussels open.
1. Season with fish sauce and sugar. Taste and adjust flavors.
1. Turn off heat and stir in lime juice and smashed chilies.
1. Garnish with cilantro and serve hot.

---

## Sweet and Sour Fish
- **Original Servings:** 3-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb white fish fillets, cut into bite-sized pieces
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup cornstarch
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1/2 cup pineapple juice
- 1/4 cup rice vinegar
- 1/4 cup tomato ketchup
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 1 tbsp cornstarch dissolved in 2 tbsp water (slurry)
- 1 onion, 1 red bell pepper, 1 green bell pepper (cut into chunks)
- 1/2 cup pineapple chunks
- 1 tsp minced ginger, 2 cloves minced garlic
- Oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Marinate fish with soy sauce, salt, and pepper for 10 minutes.
1. Dip fish in egg, then coat with flour and cornstarch mixture.
1. Deep fry fish in hot oil until golden brown and crispy (3-4 mins per side). Drain and set aside.
1. In a clean pan, sauté ginger and garlic. Add onion, bell peppers, and pineapple. Stir-fry for 2 minutes.
1. Add pineapple juice, vinegar, ketchup, sugar, and soy sauce. Simmer.
1. Stir in cornstarch slurry to thicken.
1. Toss the fried fish into the sauce quickly to coat and serve immediately with rice.

---

## Steamed Fish with Ginger
- **Original Servings:** 2-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs whole fish (sea bass or snapper) or 2 large fillets
- 2-inch piece ginger, julienned
- 4-5 stalks green onions, shredded
- 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine
- Pinch of salt
- 2 tbsp light soy sauce
- 1 tsp sugar
- 1 tbsp water
- 3 tbsp neutral oil
- Fresh cilantro and sesame oil, for garnish

### Instructions
1. Rinse fish, pat dry, and make diagonal slashes if using whole fish. Rub with salt and cooking wine.
1. Place half the ginger and onions on a plate, lay fish on top, and scatter remaining ginger over fish.
1. Steam on high heat for 8-10 minutes (fillets) or 10-12 minutes (whole fish).
1. Drain excess liquid from the plate. Top fish with fresh shredded onions and cilantro.
1. Heat oil in a small pan until smoking.
1. Pour hot oil over the onions and ginger to sear them.
1. Whisk soy sauce, sugar, and water, then drizzle around the base of the fish.
1. Garnish with sesame oil and serve hot.

---

## Shrimp Fried Rice
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 cups cooked white rice, preferably day-old and cold
- 1 lb medium shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 3 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1 cup frozen peas and carrots, thawed
- 3 green onions, thinly sliced (separate whites and greens)
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, minced
- 3 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame oil
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a wok. Season shrimp with salt and pepper, cook for 1-2 mins per side until pink. Set aside.
1. Lower heat, add a splash of oil, and scramble eggs until just set. Set aside.
1. Add remaining oil, white parts of green onions, garlic, and ginger. Sauté for 30 seconds. Add peas and carrots, cook for 2 mins.
1. Add cold rice, breaking up clumps. Stir-fry for 3-5 minutes until heated through.
1. Pour soy sauce and sesame oil over rice. Add shrimp and eggs back into the pan.
1. Toss together for 1-2 minutes.
1. Stir in green parts of green onions and serve immediately.

---

## Chili Crab
- **Original Servings:** 2-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1-2 large Mud crabs (1-1.5kg), cleaned and cut into pieces (claws cracked)
- 5-6 shallots, minced
- 4-5 cloves garlic, minced
- 1-inch knob ginger, grated
- 3-5 fresh red chilies, minced
- 1/2 cup tomato ketchup
- 1/4 cup chili sauce
- 1.5 cups chicken broth or water
- 1-2 tbsp sugar
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar or lime juice
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1 tbsp cornstarch dissolved in 2 tbsp water (slurry)
- 3-4 tbsp vegetable oil
- Fresh cilantro and green onions, for garnish

### Instructions
1. Clean and quarter the crab; crack the claws.
1. Sauté shallots, garlic, ginger, and chilies in oil for 1-2 minutes until fragrant.
1. Add crab pieces and stir-fry for 2-3 minutes until shells turn red.
1. Add broth, ketchup, chili sauce, sugar, and salt. Cover and simmer for 5-8 minutes.
1. Stir in cornstarch slurry and simmer until thickened and glossy.
1. Lower heat, drizzle in the beaten egg, and gently swirl into the sauce after 10 seconds.
1. Stir in vinegar or lime juice. Garnish and serve immediately with mantou or rice.

---

## Fish Head Curry
- **Original Servings:** 4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large fish head (600g-800g, Red Snapper or Grouper), cleaned and halved
- 6-8 okra (Lady’s Fingers)
- 2 tomatoes, quartered
- 1 small eggplant, sliced
- 1 cup coconut milk
- 1 onion, sliced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 inch ginger, minced
- 4-5 tbsp fish curry powder (mixed into a paste with water)
- 3 tbsp tamarind paste diluted in 2 cups water
- 1 tsp salt, 1 tsp sugar
- 4 tbsp cooking oil
- 1 tsp mustard seeds, 1/2 tsp fenugreek seeds, 2 sprigs curry leaves

### Instructions
1. Sauté mustard seeds, fenugreek, onions, garlic, ginger, and curry leaves in oil until fragrant.
1. Add curry powder paste and stir-fry until oil separates.
1. Pour in tamarind water and coconut milk. Bring to a boil.
1. Add eggplant and okra; simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Gently add fish head and tomatoes. Cover and simmer for 10-12 minutes until fish is cooked.
1. Season with salt and sugar. Serve hot with rice.

---

## Laksa
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb rice noodles
- 1/2 lb shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/2 lb chicken breast, sliced
- 8-10 tofu puffs, halved
- 1 can (14 oz) coconut milk
- 4 cups chicken or shrimp stock
- Laksa Paste: 4-6 dried chilies, 3 shallots, 4 garlic cloves, 1-inch ginger/galangal, 2 stalks lemongrass, 1 tsp turmeric, 1 tsp coriander, 1 tbsp shrimp paste
- 1/2 cup bean sprouts
- 2 hard-boiled eggs, halved
- Fresh cilantro/laksa leaves, fried shallots, lime wedges
- 1 tbsp palm sugar, fish sauce to taste

### Instructions
1. Blend laksa paste ingredients until smooth.
1. Fry the paste in oil for 5-8 minutes until oil separates.
1. Add stock, coconut milk, sugar, fish sauce, and tofu puffs. Simmer for 10-15 minutes.
1. Add chicken and shrimp to the broth; cook for 3-5 minutes.
1. Prepare noodles and place in bowls.
1. Ladle hot broth and proteins over noodles.
1. Top with bean sprouts, egg, herbs, and shallots. Serve with lime.

---

## Sambal Prawns
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g large prawns, peeled and deveined (tails on)
- 10-15 dried red chilies, 3-5 fresh red chilies
- 6 shallots, 3 cloves garlic, 1 inch ginger
- 1 tsp toasted shrimp paste (Belacan)
- 1 tbsp tamarind paste mixed with 3 tbsp water
- 1 tsp sugar, 1/2 tsp salt
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil

### Instructions
1. Blend chilies, shallots, garlic, ginger, and shrimp paste into a smooth sambal.
1. Fry the sambal in oil for 5-8 minutes until oil separates.
1. Stir in tamarind water, sugar, and salt; simmer to thicken.
1. Add prawns and toss to coat. Cook for 3-4 minutes until pink and opaque.
1. Serve hot with steamed rice.

---

## Grilled Fish with Sambal
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large whole fish (1.5-2 lbs, Snapper or Sea Bass)
- Sambal: 10 shallots, 4 garlic cloves, 2 lemongrass stalks, 1 inch ginger, 1 inch galangal, 4-6 red chilies, 1 tsp turmeric, 1 tbsp shrimp paste, 2 tbsp tamarind paste, 2 tbsp sweet soy sauce, 1 tbsp palm sugar, 1 tsp salt
- Banana leaves for wrapping (optional)
- Lime wedges, sliced cucumber for serving
- 1/4 cup cooking oil

### Instructions
1. Blend sambal ingredients and fry in oil until oil separates. Let cool.
1. Clean fish and make diagonal slashes. Rub cooled sambal all over fish.
1. Marinate for at least 1-2 hours.
1. Wrap fish in banana leaves or foil.
1. Grill over medium-high heat for 10-12 minutes per side until cooked through.
1. Serve hot with lime and rice.

---

## Sinigang na Isda
- **Original Servings:** 4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g - 1kg fish (Bangus, Salmon, or Snapper)
- 1 pack sinigang tamarind mix
- 6-8 cups water
- 2 tomatoes, quartered
- 1 onion, sliced
- 2 tbsp fish sauce
- 1 radish, sliced
- 1 bundle kangkong (water spinach)
- 5-8 okra, 1 eggplant (sliced)
- 2-3 long green peppers

### Instructions
1. Boil water with onions and tomatoes; simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Stir in sinigang mix.
1. Add fish and green peppers; simmer for 5-8 minutes.
1. Add radish, okra, and eggplant; simmer until tender (3-5 mins).
1. Season with fish sauce.
1. Add kangkong leaves, turn off heat, and cover to let residual heat cook them.
1. Serve hot with rice.

---

## Inihaw na Bangus
- **Original Servings:** 2-4 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large whole milkfish (Bangus), cleaned
- 2 tomatoes, diced
- 1 red onion, chopped
- 1 thumb-sized ginger, minced
- 1 tbsp calamansi or lemon juice
- 1 tbsp soy sauce (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Banana leaves or foil for wrapping

### Instructions
1. Clean fish, leave scales on, and rub with salt and pepper.
1. Mix tomatoes, onion, ginger, calamansi juice, and soy sauce to make stuffing.
1. Stuff the mixture into the fish cavity.
1. Wrap fish in banana leaves or foil.
1. Grill over medium heat for 10-15 minutes per side.
1. Serve hot with toyomansi dipping sauce.

---

## Adobong Pusit
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs squid, cleaned (keep ink sacs)
- 1 onion, diced
- 2 tomatoes, diced
- 5-6 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup soy sauce
- 1/3 cup cane vinegar
- 1 tsp peppercorns, 2 bay leaves, 1 tsp sugar
- 2 tbsp cooking oil

### Instructions
1. Clean squid, separating ink sacs into a small bowl. Slice bodies into rings.
1. Sauté garlic, onion, and tomatoes until soft.
1. Add soy sauce, vinegar, squid ink, bay leaves, and peppercorns. Boil without stirring for 2 minutes.
1. Add squid; simmer for 3-5 minutes only to prevent toughness.
1. Add sugar and season with salt if needed.
1. Serve hot with rice.

---

## Kinilaw
- **Original Servings:** 4-6 people
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb fresh firm-fleshed fish (Tuna or Tanigue), cubed
- 1/2 cup vinegar (for rinsing)
- 1/2 cup coconut or cane vinegar (for marinade)
- 3-4 tbsp calamansi juice
- 1 red onion, sliced
- 2 tbsp ginger, minced
- 2-3 bird's eye chilies, chopped
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Optional: 1 small cucumber, diced

### Instructions
1. Rinse fish cubes in 1/2 cup vinegar for 1-2 minutes; drain and discard vinegar.
1. Add ginger, onion, and chilies to the fish. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Pour in fresh vinegar and calamansi juice. Add cucumber if using.
1. Toss well and chill for 10-15 minutes until fish turns opaque.
1. Serve chilled immediately.

---

## Korean Grilled Mackerel
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 fresh mackerel, filleted into 2 or 4 pieces (or butterflied whole)
- Sea salt (or kosher salt), to taste
- 1 tbsp lemon juice (optional)
- 1 tsp ginger juice (optional)
- Cooking oil, to lightly oil grill/pan (as needed)

### Instructions
1. Cut a few slashes on the skin side. Pat fish dry.
1. Drizzle with optional lemon and ginger juice. Season both sides liberally with salt and let sit 20 to 30 minutes.
1. Shake off excess salt.
1. Grill over medium-high heat, skin-side down, 2 to 3 minutes until edges brown and flesh turns opaque; flip and cook about 2 minutes more (or pan-fry/broil using the same timing cues).
1. Serve hot with rice and simple sides.

---

## Haemul Pajeon
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 tbsp potato starch
- 1/2 tsp kosher salt, plus a pinch
- Pinch of ground black pepper
- 3/4 cup stock (anchovy-kelp, chicken, vegetable) or water
- 12 green onions, trimmed to fit skillet (about 8 to 9 inches long)
- 4 to 5 oz mixed seafood (shrimp, squid, clams), chopped
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1 fresh red pepper, sliced
- 4 tbsp vegetable oil (for frying)
- Dipping sauce: 2 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tbsp vinegar, 1/2 tsp gochugaru, 1 chopped green onion, 1 tsp toasted sesame seeds

### Instructions
1. Make dipping sauce by combining soy sauce, vinegar, gochugaru, chopped green onion, and sesame seeds; set aside.
1. Season chopped seafood with a pinch of salt and pepper.
1. Whisk flour, potato starch, 1/2 tsp salt, pepper, and stock/water into a smooth batter.
1. Heat 2 tbsp oil in a large nonstick skillet over medium-high. Coat green onions in batter and lay side by side in the pan to form a rectangle.
1. Mix seafood into remaining batter and spread over the scallions. Top with red pepper and pour beaten egg over the pancake.
1. Reduce heat to medium and cook about 6 minutes until bottom is light brown and crisp. Add remaining oil as needed and flip; cook until the other side is crisp and golden.
1. Cut into pieces and serve with dipping sauce.

---

## Fish Curry
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil
- 1 large onion, chopped
- 1 garlic clove, chopped
- 1 to 2 tbsp Madras curry paste
- 400 g can chopped tomatoes
- 200 ml vegetable stock
- Sustainable white fish fillets, skinned and cut into big chunks
- Cooked rice or naan, to serve

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a deep pan and gently fry onion and garlic about 5 minutes until soft.
1. Add curry paste and stir-fry 1 to 2 minutes.
1. Add chopped tomatoes and stock; bring to a simmer.
1. Add fish and gently cook 4 to 5 minutes until it flakes easily.
1. Serve immediately with rice or naan.

---

## Prawn Masala
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large onion, roughly chopped
- 1 thumb-sized piece ginger, peeled and grated
- 2 large garlic cloves
- 1 tbsp rapeseed oil
- 2 to 3 tbsp tikka curry paste
- 400 g can chopped tomatoes
- 2 tbsp tomato puree
- 1/2 tbsp light brown soft sugar
- 3 cardamom pods, bashed
- 3 tbsp ground almonds
- 300 g raw king prawns
- 1 tbsp double cream
- 1/2 bunch coriander, roughly chopped
- Cooked rice and naan (optional), to serve

### Instructions
1. Blitz onion, ginger and garlic to a smooth paste.
1. Heat oil in a pan over medium heat. Fry the onion paste about 8 minutes until lightly golden.
1. Stir in curry paste and fry 1 minute. Add tomatoes, tomato puree, sugar and cardamom; simmer covered about 10 minutes.
1. Remove cardamom, then blend sauce smooth and return to pan.
1. Stir in ground almonds and prawns; cook about 5 minutes until prawns are pink and cooked through.
1. Season to taste, then stir in cream and coriander. Serve with rice and naan if desired.

---

## Goan Fish Curry
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 pieces sea fish of choice (firm fish)
- 1 tsp Kashmiri red chilli powder
- 1 tsp turmeric powder
- 2 tsp kokum concentrate (or 2 tsp lemon juice)
- Salt, to taste
- 1/2 cup fresh coconut (grated or chopped)
- 2 small onions, peeled
- 1 tomato
- 2 tsp whole coriander seeds
- 1 tsp cumin seeds
- 5 Bedgi red chilies (or dried red chilies)
- 5 whole black peppercorns
- 2 whole cloves
- 4 garlic cloves
- 1 tbsp cooking oil
- 1 tsp mustard seeds
- 6 curry leaves

### Instructions
1. Marinate fish with salt, Kashmiri chilli powder, turmeric and kokum (or lemon). Set aside.
1. Blend coconut, onions, tomato, dried red chilies, peppercorns, cloves and garlic into a very smooth paste (add a little water if needed).
1. Heat oil in a pot. Add mustard seeds; when they crackle, add curry leaves.
1. Add blended coconut paste and cook covered about 10 minutes until the raw smell cooks off.
1. Add marinated fish and simmer gently about 5 minutes (or until fish is just cooked).
1. Serve hot with steamed rice.

---

# Category: European Cuisine

## Fish and Chips
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- About 1 litre sunflower oil (for frying)
- 2 thick skinless white fish fillets (whiting, ling, pollock, haddock or cod), about 150 g each
- 2 large Maris Piper potatoes
- 1 tsp malt vinegar (plus extra to serve)
- Batter: 75 g self-raising flour (plus extra for dusting), 25 g cornflour, pinch ground turmeric, 125 g cold lager (or fizzy water), salt
- Tartare sauce (optional): cornichons, capers, shallot, parsley, mayonnaise
- Salt, to serve

### Instructions
1. Cut potatoes into chips. Soak 5 minutes, rinse until water runs clear, then simmer in salted water with 1 tsp malt vinegar 10-12 minutes until just cooked. Drain and chill on a tray in a single layer.
1. Make batter by quickly mixing flours and turmeric with cold beer/fizzy water and a pinch of salt; do not overmix. Keep chilled.
1. Heat oil to about 180 C and fry chips 8-10 minutes until golden and crisp; drain on paper.
1. Increase oil to about 185 C. Dust fish in flour, dip in batter, and fry about 4 minutes, turning once, until deep golden and cooked through.
1. Serve fish with chips, salt and vinegar (and tartare sauce if using).

---

## Smoked Salmon
- **Original Servings:** 8-10 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 8 oz cream cheese, softened
- 2 oz capers, roughly chopped
- 1/4 cup finely chopped red onion
- 1 lemon, zested and juiced
- Kosher salt and freshly ground black pepper, to taste
- Rye toast points (or crackers), for serving
- 6 oz smoked salmon

### Instructions
1. Mix cream cheese, capers, red onion, lemon zest and juice; season with salt and pepper.
1. Spread mixture on rye toast points or crackers.
1. Top with smoked salmon and serve.

---

## Gravlax
- **Original Servings:** 8-10 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lb center-cut, skin-on salmon fillet
- 2/3 cup kosher salt
- 1/3 cup sugar
- 2 tbsp white peppercorns
- 1 tbsp fennel seeds
- 1 tbsp caraway seeds
- 1 cup dill sprigs (plus 1/3 cup chopped dill for coating)
- Optional: 1/4 cup aquavit

### Instructions
1. Coarsely grind peppercorns, fennel and caraway; mix with salt and sugar.
1. Lay salmon on plastic wrap on a plate. Cover with salt-sugar mixture, dill sprigs, and aquavit if using. Wrap tightly.
1. Refrigerate 48-72 hours, turning every 12 hours and redistributing the brine.
1. Unwrap, discard brine and dill, rinse salmon briefly and pat dry.
1. Press the flesh side into chopped dill to coat. Slice thinly on the diagonal and serve.

---

## Bouillabaisse
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 onions, chopped
- 1 leek, white finely sliced (green top reserved if using for stock)
- 1 fennel bulb, chopped (fronds reserved for garnish)
- 4 garlic cloves, minced
- 4 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tbsp tomato puree
- 4 large ripe tomatoes, chopped (or canned tomatoes)
- Large pinch saffron strands
- 3 bay leaves
- Small bunch thyme
- Parsley (stalks for stock, leaves chopped for serving)
- 2 strips orange peel (optional)
- 1 mild red chilli (optional)
- 2 tbsp Pernod (optional)
- Fish stock (enough for a generous soup base)
- Mixed seafood: firm white fish pieces plus shellfish (e.g., mussels, shrimp/prawns)
- Salt and black pepper, to taste
- To serve (optional but classic): rouille and toasted bread

### Instructions
1. Make the soup base: saute onion, leek and fennel in olive oil until softened. Add garlic and tomato puree and cook briefly.
1. Add tomatoes, saffron, bay, thyme, parsley stalks, orange peel and chilli; cook down a few minutes, then add fish stock and simmer to develop flavor.
1. Add firm fish pieces first and simmer gently until nearly cooked, then add quicker-cooking seafood (shrimp/mussels) and cook just until done and mussels open (discard any that stay shut).
1. Taste and season, then serve hot with chopped herbs (and rouille + toast if using).

---

## Sole Meunière
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 fillets sole or plaice, skin-on (about 140 g each)
- 6 tbsp plain flour
- Salt and black pepper, to taste
- 3 tbsp light olive oil (or sunflower oil)
- 85 g butter (ideally unsalted)
- Juice of 1 lemon
- 2 tbsp small capers (optional)

### Instructions
1. Season flour with salt and pepper. Coat fish in flour and shake off excess.
1. Heat oil in a large frying pan. Cook fish skin-side down about 2 minutes, then flip and cook 1 to 2 minutes until golden and just cooked.
1. Remove fish to a warm plate and season. Wipe out the pan, then melt butter until it turns light brown.
1. Stir in lemon juice and capers (optional). Return fish briefly and spoon sauce over.
1. Serve immediately.

---

## Moules Marinières
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 litres fresh mussels
- 1 onion, finely chopped
- 1 bunch parsley, chopped
- 30 g butter
- 200 ml dry white wine
- 1 bay leaf
- 1 sprig thyme
- Salt and black pepper, to taste
- Optional: 3 tbsp creme fraiche (to enrich the sauce)

### Instructions
1. Clean mussels: scrub shells, remove beards, and rinse quickly with cold water (do not soak).
1. Melt butter in a large pot. Add onion and cook about 1 minute.
1. Add mussels and white wine. Season and add parsley, bay and thyme.
1. Cook over high heat about 6 minutes, shaking/stirring regularly, until mussels open (discard any that stay shut).
1. Remove bay and thyme. Pour cooking juices over mussels and serve hot.

---

## Paella
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 400 g can chopped tomatoes
- 600 ml chicken stock
- 1 heaped tsp smoked paprika
- 2 pinches saffron
- 1 onion, chopped
- 3 garlic cloves, crushed
- 4 tbsp olive oil
- 300 g paella rice
- 4 skinless boneless chicken thighs, halved
- 200 g chorizo, sliced
- 85 g frozen peas
- 150 g raw king prawns
- 250 g mussels, cleaned
- 1 lemon, quartered (optional)

### Instructions
1. Heat oven to 220 C/200 C fan. Heat tomatoes, stock, paprika and saffron until steaming hot.
1. Roast onion and garlic with olive oil in a large ovenproof pan 20 minutes until starting to brown.
1. Stir in rice, chicken, chorizo and hot stock mixture; season and bake uncovered 20 minutes.
1. Stir in peas, add prawns, and press mussels into rice. Bake 5 to 10 minutes more until rice is cooked, prawns are pink and mussels opened (discard any that stay shut).
1. Serve with lemon wedges if using.

---

## Gambas al Ajillo
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 12 large raw prawns, peeled and deveined
- 3 garlic cloves, thinly sliced
- 100 ml olive oil
- 3 dried cayenne chillies (or other dried chilli)
- 1 tbsp chopped flat-leaf parsley
- Sea salt and black pepper, to taste

### Instructions
1. Season prawns lightly with salt.
1. Put garlic, olive oil and dried chillies in a small flameproof dish or frying pan over high heat.
1. When garlic starts to turn golden, add prawns and cook 1 to 2 minutes per side until just pink.
1. Sprinkle with parsley and a little black pepper and serve immediately with bread.

---

## Bacalao
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 8 pieces desalted cod (or salt cod soaked/desalted for about 48 hours, changing water several times)
- 400 ml olive oil
- 8 garlic cloves, sliced
- 1 dried chilli (or chilli flakes), to taste
- Salt, if needed (often not needed if cod is salted)

### Instructions
1. Warm olive oil in a pan over medium heat. Add garlic and chilli and cook until the garlic starts to brown; remove and reserve.
1. Take the pan off the heat and let oil cool slightly.
1. Add cod pieces to the oil (skin-side up) and gently cook about 5 minutes, keeping the heat low so oil doesn't bubble vigorously.
1. Move cod to a second pan. Add a few spoonfuls of oil, let rest briefly, then return to low heat and swirl the pan in circles to emulsify the sauce, gradually adding more oil until thickened (pil-pil).
1. Serve cod with the emulsified sauce and top with the reserved garlic and chilli.

---

## Calamari Fritti
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings (starter)
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 300 g baby squid, cleaned
- 200 g plain flour
- 2 tbsp capers, drained and finely chopped
- Vegetable or sunflower oil, for frying
- 1 garlic clove, crushed
- 5 tbsp mayonnaise
- Lemon wedges, to serve
- Salt and black pepper, to taste

### Instructions
1. Slice squid into rings about 1/2 cm thick.
1. Season flour well and mix in chopped capers. Coat squid in the flour mixture and shake off excess.
1. Mix garlic into mayonnaise for a quick dipping sauce.
1. Heat frying oil in a deep pan (no more than one-third full). Fry squid in batches about 3 minutes until crisp and lightly golden.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve immediately with garlic mayo and lemon wedges.

---

## Seafood Risotto
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 onion, finely chopped
- 1 fennel bulb, finely sliced
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 300 g risotto rice
- 500 ml fish stock (or vegetable stock)
- 300 g frozen seafood mix, defrosted
- 100 g frozen peas
- 3 tbsp grated parmesan
- 1 lemon, zest and juice
- Handful parsley leaves, roughly chopped
- Salt and black pepper, to taste

### Instructions
1. Microwave onion and fennel with olive oil 5 minutes until softened.
1. Stir in rice and stock, cover and microwave on High 10 to 15 minutes until rice is almost cooked.
1. Stir in seafood and peas, cover and microwave 2 to 3 minutes until rice is cooked and seafood is hot.
1. Stir in parmesan and lemon juice; rest briefly.
1. Mix parsley with lemon zest and scatter over to serve.

---

## Spaghetti alle Vongole
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 140 g spaghetti
- 500 g fresh clams in shells
- 2 ripe tomatoes
- Olive oil
- 1 fat garlic clove, chopped
- 1 small fresh red chilli, finely chopped
- Splash of white wine
- Chopped parsley
- Salt and black pepper, to taste

### Instructions
1. Rinse clams well in several changes of cold water; discard any open or damaged.
1. Peel and deseed tomatoes, then chop the flesh.
1. Cook spaghetti according to package directions.
1. Heat olive oil in a large pan; briefly fry garlic and chilli. Add tomatoes, then clams and a splash of wine; bring to the boil.
1. Cover and cook 3 to 4 minutes until clams open (discard any that stay shut).
1. Drain pasta, add to the clam pan with parsley, toss and serve.

---

## Baccalà alla Vicentina
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg soaked baccalà (salt cod), boned and cut into pieces
- Flour, for dredging
- Extra-virgin olive oil
- 1 small onion (about 100 g), chopped
- 1 garlic clove, minced
- 3 anchovy fillets, minced
- 1 tbsp chopped parsley
- 3 tbsp breadcrumbs
- 2 tbsp grated Parmigiano Reggiano
- Water, as needed
- Salt, to taste (check at end)
- Polenta, to serve

### Instructions
1. Lightly dredge baccalà pieces in flour and brown briefly in a pan with olive oil; remove and keep warm.
1. Gently saute chopped onion in olive oil. Add baccalà pieces, keeping them intact.
1. Mix garlic, anchovies and parsley; combine with breadcrumbs and Parmigiano and sprinkle over the fish.
1. Add about 1 cup water, then cook uncovered on very low heat 45 to 60 minutes, adding a little water if it dries out.
1. Check and adjust salt near the end. Serve with polenta.

---

## Fish Soup (Halászlé)
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 500 g carp tail (or other freshwater fish on the bone)
- 500 g catfish fillet (or another firm fish), cut into portions
- 1 onion, finely chopped
- 3 to 4 tbsp vegetable oil (or lard)
- 2 to 3 tbsp sweet Hungarian paprika
- 6 cups water
- Salt, to taste

### Instructions
1. Stir paprika into oil/lard in a soup pot (off the heat briefly if needed so paprika doesn't burn).
1. Add water, chopped onion, salt, and the carp pieces. Simmer until the fish is tender and the meat falls from the bone.
1. Remove fish pieces and press the cooked fish meat and broth through a strainer back into the pot to enrich the soup base.
1. Add catfish fillets and simmer a couple of minutes until just cooked.
1. Serve hot with white bread.

---

## Pickled Herring
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg fresh herring fillets, cut into bite-size pieces
- 200 ml distilled white vinegar (about 12%)
- 1 tbsp salt
- 100 g sugar
- 2 small red onions, finely sliced
- 2 carrots, thinly sliced
- 3 bay leaves
- 15 white peppercorns
- 10 juniper berries
- To serve: chopped dill and chives (optional)

### Instructions
1. Pre-salt the herring: combine 500 ml water, 100 ml vinegar and salt and soak herring in the fridge 4 to 5 hours; drain well.
1. Make pickling brine: combine remaining vinegar with sugar, onions, carrots, bay leaves, peppercorns and juniper berries plus 500 ml water; bring to a boil and stir to dissolve sugar, then cool completely.
1. Pour cooled brine over herring in a non-reactive container and refrigerate overnight (ideally 24 hours).
1. Serve chilled with chopped dill/chives if desired.

---

## Shrimp Cocktail
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 to 1.5 lbs large shrimp, peeled and deveined, tails left on
- 1 lemon, halved
- 1 tbsp Old Bay seasoning or pickling spice
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 cup ketchup
- 2 tbsp prepared horseradish
- 1 tsp fresh lemon juice
- 1/2 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- Dash of hot sauce (optional)

### Instructions
1. Fill a large pot with water. Squeeze in lemon juice and drop in the halves. Add seasoning and salt. Bring to a boil.
1. Add shrimp to boiling water. Turn off heat, cover, and let sit for 3–4 minutes until pink and opaque.
1. Immediately transfer shrimp to a bowl of ice water to stop the cooking. Once cold, drain and pat dry.
1. Whisk cocktail sauce ingredients (ketchup, horseradish, lemon juice, Worcestershire, and hot sauce) in a small bowl.
1. Arrange shrimp on a platter or in glasses with the sauce in the center. Garnish with extra lemon wedges.

---

## Fish Pie
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 600g mixed fish fillets (cod, salmon, and smoked haddock), cut into bite-sized chunks
- 30g butter
- 30g plain flour
- 600ml whole milk
- 2 tsp Dijon mustard
- Handful of fresh parsley, finely chopped
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 150g frozen peas
- 1kg floury potatoes, peeled and chopped
- 25g butter (for mash)
- Splash of milk or cream
- 100g mature cheddar cheese, grated

### Instructions
1. Boil chopped potatoes in salted water for 15–20 minutes until soft. Drain and mash with butter and milk until smooth.
1. Melt 30g butter in a saucepan, whisk in flour to form a roux and cook for 1 minute. Gradually whisk in milk until the sauce thickens. Stir in mustard, parsley, salt, and pepper.
1. Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F). Place fish chunks and peas in a large ovenproof baking dish. Pour the white sauce over and stir gently.
1. Spoon mashed potatoes over the fish mixture, spread evenly, and create peaks with a fork. Sprinkle with grated cheddar cheese.
1. Bake for 20–25 minutes until the sauce is bubbling and the top is golden brown and crispy.

---

## Lobster Thermidor
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 whole cooked lobsters (approx. 1.5–2 lbs each)
- 3 tbsp unsalted butter
- 1 medium shallot, finely diced
- 1–2 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup dry white wine or 2 tbsp Cognac
- 1 cup heavy cream
- 1/2 cup seafood or fish stock (optional)
- 1 tbsp Dijon mustard
- 1 tbsp fresh tarragon, chopped
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- 1 tsp lemon juice
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 1/2 cup Gruyère or Parmesan cheese, grated

### Instructions
1. Cut lobsters in half lengthwise. Remove meat from tails and claws, chop into bite-sized chunks, and set aside. Place empty shells on a baking sheet.
1. Melt butter in a skillet over medium heat. Sauté shallots and garlic until soft. Stir in flour and cook for 1–2 minutes.
1. Pour in white wine (or Cognac) and reduce by half. Slowly whisk in heavy cream and stock, simmering until thickened.
1. Stir in Dijon mustard, tarragon, parsley, lemon juice, salt, and pepper. Remove from heat and gently fold in the lobster meat.
1. Divide the mixture among the lobster shell halves and sprinkle with grated cheese.
1. Place under a preheated broiler for 3–5 minutes until the cheese is melted and golden brown.

---

## Crab Bisque
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/4 cup unsalted butter
- 1 small yellow onion or 3 large shallots, finely minced
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- 4 cups fish stock
- 2 cups heavy cream
- 1/2 cup dry sherry
- 1 lb fresh lump crabmeat
- 1 tsp Old Bay seasoning
- 1/2 tsp kosher salt
- 1/4 tsp white pepper
- Pinch of nutmeg
- Fresh chives or parsley, finely chopped

### Instructions
1. Melt butter in a large pot. Sauté onion or shallots until soft (about 3–5 minutes).
1. Whisk in flour and cook for 1–2 minutes to create a blond roux.
1. Slowly whisk in fish stock and bring the mixture to a gentle simmer.
1. Stir in heavy cream, Old Bay, salt, pepper, and nutmeg. Simmer on low heat for 10 minutes.
1. Gently fold in crabmeat and stir in the dry sherry. Heat through for 3–5 minutes.
1. Ladle into bowls and garnish with fresh herbs.

---

## Seafood Pasta
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Linguine or Spaghetti
- 1/2 lb large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/2 lb sea scallops
- 1/2 lb mussels, scrubbed and debearded
- 1/2 lb clams, scrubbed
- 4 tbsp unsalted butter
- 2 tbsp extra virgin olive oil
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 shallot, finely diced
- 3/4 cup dry white wine
- 1/4 cup fresh Italian parsley, chopped
- 1 lemon, zest and juice
- 1/2 tsp red pepper flakes
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Cook pasta in salted water until al dente. Reserve 1 cup of pasta water before draining.
1. Sear seasoned shrimp and scallops in 1 tbsp butter and 1 tbsp olive oil for 2 minutes per side until golden. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté shallot in remaining butter and oil, then add garlic and red pepper flakes for 30 seconds.
1. Pour in white wine, add clams and mussels, cover and steam for 5–7 minutes until shells open. Discard any closed shells.
1. Return shrimp and scallops to the pan. Add cooked pasta, lemon zest, juice, and parsley.
1. Toss together over low heat, adding reserved pasta water as needed to coat the noodles.
1. Serve immediately in warm bowls.

---

## Grilled Sea Bass
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 Chilean Sea Bass fillets
- 3 tbsp olive oil (divided)
- 1 tsp coarse kosher salt
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1 tsp onion powder
- 1/2 tsp lemon pepper
- 5 tbsp unsalted butter
- 5 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/4 cup white wine
- 1 tsp fresh cracked black pepper
- 1/2 tsp red pepper flakes
- 1 tsp fresh lemon juice
- 2 tbsp capers
- Zest from 1/2 lemon
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, finely chopped

### Instructions
1. Preheat grill to medium-high heat (375°F–400°F).
1. Blot fillets dry and make shallow diagonal cuts in the skin. Coat with 1 tbsp olive oil and season with salt, garlic powder, paprika, onion powder, and lemon pepper.
1. Place fillets on the grill flesh-side down and cook for 7 minutes.
1. In a saucepan, melt butter with 2 tbsp olive oil. Whisk in minced garlic, white wine, cracked pepper, red pepper flakes, lemon juice, capers, and zest. Keep warm.
1. Flip fillets and grill for another 7 minutes. Whisk parsley into the butter sauce during the final 2 minutes.
1. Remove fish when the internal temperature reaches 145°F and spoon sauce over the fillets to serve.

---

## Octopus Salad
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 lbs cooked octopus tentacles, cut into bite-sized pieces
- 2 celery ribs, diced
- 1/4 cup vinegar peppers, diced
- 1/2 cup canned black olives, sliced
- 3 cloves garlic, finely chopped
- 1/3 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- 1/8 tsp dried oregano
- 1/3 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1/3 cup fresh lemon juice
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/8 tsp black pepper

### Instructions
1. Combine octopus, garlic, celery, parsley, vinegar peppers, and olives in a large mixing bowl.
1. Pour in olive oil and lemon juice. Add salt, pepper, and oregano, then toss thoroughly.
1. Cover and refrigerate for at least 4 hours (or overnight) to let flavors marry.
1. Remove from the refrigerator 20 minutes before serving. Toss again and serve with crusty bread.

---

## Stuffed Squid
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 800g whole squid, cleaned (tubes and tentacles separated)
- 3 tbsp breadcrumbs
- 80g black olives, minced
- 1 tbsp capers, minced
- 2 cloves garlic (1 minced, 1 whole)
- Small bunch of fresh parsley, minced
- Pinch of fresh oregano
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 350g peeled tomatoes, diced
- 3 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 100ml dry white wine (optional)

### Instructions
1. Finely chop the squid tentacles and sauté with minced garlic in 1 tbsp olive oil for 2–3 minutes. Stir in breadcrumbs, olives, capers, parsley, oregano, salt, and pepper.
1. Spoon the mixture into each squid tube (fill 3/4 full) and seal with a toothpick.
1. In a large sauté pan, heat remaining olive oil with the whole garlic clove. Once fragrant, add tomatoes (and wine if using).
1. Remove the whole garlic clove and place the stuffed squid in the pan. Cover and simmer gently for 20–25 minutes.
1. Remove toothpicks and serve the squid with the tomato sauce.

---

## Fried Anchovies
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb fresh or thawed anchovies, cleaned (heads and innards removed)
- 1 cup all-purpose or semolina flour
- 1–2 cups high-smoke point oil for frying
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- Lemon wedges and chopped parsley for garnish

### Instructions
1. Rinse cleaned anchovies and pat completely dry with paper towels.
1. Combine flour, salt, and pepper in a shallow bowl. Dredge the anchovies in the mixture and shake off any excess.
1. Heat oil in a skillet to 350°F (175°C).
1. Fry anchovies in batches for 2–3 minutes, flipping once, until golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and sprinkle with extra salt while hot.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve immediately with lemon wedges.

---

## Sardines on Toast
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 slices of crusty bread
- 1 can (4 oz) sardines in olive oil
- 1 small clove garlic, peeled
- 1/2 lemon, juice and zest
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper
- Optional: red chili flakes and fresh parsley

### Instructions
1. Toast the bread until golden brown.
1. While still hot, lightly rub the raw garlic clove over the surface of the toast.
1. Place sardines directly onto the toast (or mash with lemon juice and pepper first).
1. Drizzle a teaspoon of oil from the sardine can over the fish.
1. Top with a squeeze of lemon juice, zest, salt, pepper, and optional chili flakes or parsley.
1. Serve immediately.

---

# Category: American Cuisine

## Cajun Shrimp Boil
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs large shrimp (shell-on recommended)
- 1 lb smoked sausage (Andouille or Kielbasa), cut into 1-inch rounds
- 1.5 lbs baby red potatoes (whole)
- 4 ears of sweet corn, husked and snapped in half
- 1/2 cup Cajun seasoning (e.g., Old Bay or Zatarain’s)
- 2 large lemons, halved
- 1 whole head of garlic, halved crosswise
- 1 large yellow onion, quartered
- 3–4 bay leaves
- 6–8 quarts water
- 1/2 cup melted butter (for serving)
- Fresh parsley, chopped (for garnish)
- Lemon wedges (for serving)

### Instructions
1. Fill a large stockpot with water. Add Cajun seasoning, lemons (squeeze juice in first), garlic, onion, and bay leaves. Bring to a boil and simmer for 10 minutes.
1. Add the potatoes and boil for 10–15 minutes until just starting to become tender.
1. Add the sausage and corn. Continue to boil for another 8–10 minutes.
1. Add the shrimp and boil for 2–3 minutes until pink and opaque. Do not overcook.
1. Drain immediately or let soak for 5 minutes for extra spice.
1. Serve on a platter or paper-lined table. Drizzle with seasoned melted butter and garnish with parsley and lemon wedges.

---

## Shrimp and Grits
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1 cup stone-ground or quick-cooking grits
- 2 cups water
- 2 cups milk
- 1/2 cup shredded sharp Cheddar cheese
- 1/4 cup shredded Parmesan cheese
- 2 tbsp butter
- 4 slices bacon, diced
- 5 oz white mushrooms, sliced
- 1/3 cup red bell pepper, diced
- 2–3 cloves garlic, minced
- 4 green onions, sliced (whites and greens separated)
- 1/2 cup chicken broth
- 1/2 cup heavy cream
- 1/2 tbsp lemon juice
- 1 tsp fresh thyme (or 1/2 tsp dried)
- Hot sauce (to taste)
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Bring water, milk, and salt to a gentle boil in a saucepan. Whisk in grits. Reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer (5-7 mins for quick grits, 40-45 mins for stone-ground) until creamy. Stir in butter and cheeses.
1. In a large skillet, fry diced bacon until crispy. Remove bacon and leave 1-2 tbsp of fat in the pan.
1. Sauté mushrooms and red bell pepper in the bacon fat for 3 minutes.
1. Add shrimp, garlic, thyme, and the white parts of green onions. Cook for 2-3 minutes until shrimp turn pink.
1. Pour in chicken broth, heavy cream, lemon juice, and hot sauce. Simmer for 2-3 minutes to thicken sauce. Stir in crispy bacon and green onion tops.
1. Spoon cheesy grits into bowls and top with the shrimp and gravy mixture.

---

## Clam Chowder
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 (6.5 oz) cans chopped clams (juice reserved)
- 1.5 lbs Russet or Yukon Gold potatoes, peeled and diced
- 1 medium yellow onion, diced
- 3 ribs celery, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 4 tbsp butter
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 cup low-sodium chicken broth
- 1 cup whole milk
- 1 cup half-and-half (or heavy cream)
- 3 bay leaves
- 1 tbsp red wine vinegar (optional)
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste
- Garnish: Crispy bacon bits, fresh parsley, or oyster crackers

### Instructions
1. Drain canned clams, reserving the juice. Add the juice, chicken broth, diced potatoes, and bay leaves to a stockpot. Simmer until potatoes are tender (15–20 minutes).
1. In a separate skillet, heat butter and olive oil. Sauté onion, celery, and garlic until soft (4–5 minutes).
1. Sprinkle flour over the vegetables and stir for 1 minute. Slowly whisk in milk and half-and-half until smooth and thickened.
1. Combine the creamy vegetable mixture into the stockpot with the potatoes and broth.
1. Add the reserved clams, salt, pepper, and red wine vinegar. Simmer for 5 minutes (do not boil vigorously).
1. Remove bay leaves and serve hot with garnishes.

---

## Lobster Roll
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb cooked lobster meat, chopped into large bite-sized chunks
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise
- 1/4 cup celery, finely diced
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 tbsp fresh chives or parsley, finely chopped
- 4 New England-style (top-split) hot dog buns
- 2–3 tbsp unsalted butter, softened
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste
- Optional: Pinch of Old Bay seasoning or lettuce leaves

### Instructions
1. In a bowl, whisk together mayonnaise, lemon juice, celery, and herbs. Gently fold in the lobster meat. Season with salt and pepper. Refrigerate for 30 minutes.
1. Spread softened butter on the outer sides of the split-top buns.
1. Heat a skillet over medium heat and toast the buns on their sides until golden brown (1–2 minutes per side).
1. Fill the warm buns with the chilled lobster salad, piling it high. Use a lettuce leaf as a barrier if desired.
1. Serve immediately with potato chips and a lemon wedge.

---

## Crab Cakes
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lump crab meat, picked over for shells
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise
- 1 tbsp Dijon mustard
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tsp Old Bay seasoning
- 1/2 cup Panko breadcrumbs (or crushed saltines)
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, finely chopped
- 1 tsp lemon zest (optional)
- 2 tbsp butter or neutral oil (for frying)
- Serving: Lemon wedges and tartar sauce

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, whisk egg, mayonnaise, mustard, Worcestershire sauce, and Old Bay.
1. Gently fold in the crab meat, breadcrumbs, and parsley. Avoid breaking up large crab lumps.
1. Form the mixture into 6–8 patties (about 1 inch thick).
1. Refrigerate the patties for 30–60 minutes to help them stay together.
1. Heat butter/oil in a skillet over medium heat. Fry crab cakes for 4–5 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Alternatively, bake at 425°F (220°C) for 12–15 minutes.
1. Serve immediately with lemon and tartar sauce.

---

## Jambalaya
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb boneless skinless chicken (thighs or breast), bite-sized
- 1 lb Andouille sausage, sliced into rounds
- 1 lb medium shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1.5 cups long-grain white rice (uncooked)
- 3 cups chicken broth
- 1 can (14.5 oz) crushed or diced tomatoes
- 1 large yellow onion, diced
- 1 green bell pepper, diced
- 2 stalks celery, diced
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp Creole or Cajun seasoning
- 1 tsp dried oregano
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 2 bay leaves
- 3 tbsp olive oil or butter
- Garnish: Green onions and fresh parsley

### Instructions
1. Brown chicken and sausage in a large Dutch oven with oil. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onion, bell pepper, and celery in the same pot for 5 minutes. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in rice and Creole seasoning, toasting the rice for 1–2 minutes.
1. Return chicken and sausage to the pot. Add chicken broth, tomatoes, Worcestershire, and bay leaves. Bring to a boil.
1. Reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for 20–25 minutes until rice is tender.
1. Gently fold in the raw shrimp, cover, and cook for another 5 minutes until pink.
1. Remove bay leaves and garnish with green onions and parsley.

---

## Shrimp Étouffée
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs medium shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/2 cup butter
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 cup onion, finely chopped
- 1/2 cup green bell pepper, chopped
- 1/2 cup celery, chopped
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 cups seafood stock (or chicken broth)
- 1 tbsp Cajun or Creole seasoning
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1–2 tsp hot sauce
- 1 bay leaf
- 4 cups cooked white rice (for serving)
- Garnish: Green onions and fresh parsley

### Instructions
1. Melt butter in a heavy skillet. Gradually whisk in flour and stir constantly for 10–15 minutes to make a peanut butter-colored roux.
1. Add the 'holy trinity' (onion, bell pepper, celery) to the roux and sauté for 5–8 minutes. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Slowly whisk in stock. Add Cajun seasoning, Worcestershire, hot sauce, and bay leaf. Simmer for 15–20 minutes until thickened.
1. Add shrimp and cook for 3–5 minutes until pink and opaque.
1. Remove bay leaf. Adjust seasoning and stir in some green onions and parsley.
1. Serve over warm white rice and garnish with remaining herbs.

---

## Fried Catfish
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs catfish fillets, patted dry
- 1 cup yellow cornmeal
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 tbsp Old Bay or Cajun seasoning
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp onion powder
- 1/2 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)
- 2 large eggs
- 1/2 cup buttermilk (or water)
- 1 tbsp hot sauce
- 1 quart neutral oil for frying
- Serving: Lemon wedges and tartar sauce

### Instructions
1. In one bowl, whisk eggs, buttermilk, and hot sauce. In another bowl, combine cornmeal, flour, and dry seasonings.
1. Dip each catfish fillet into the egg mixture, then dredge thoroughly in the cornmeal mixture, pressing gently to adhere.
1. Heat 2–3 inches of oil in a heavy pot or cast-iron skillet to 350°F (175°C).
1. Fry fillets 2–3 at a time for 3–5 minutes per side until golden brown and flaky.
1. Drain on a wire rack or paper towel-lined plate.
1. Serve hot with lemon wedges, tartar sauce, and traditional sides like hush puppies.

---

## Fish Tacos
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb white flaky fish (Cod, Halibut, or Tilapia), cut into strips
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 tsp baking powder
- 1 cup cold light beer
- 2 cups shredded cabbage
- 1/4 cup red onion, sliced
- 1/4 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
- 1/2 cup sour cream
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise
- 1–2 chipotle peppers in adobo, minced
- 8–10 small corn or flour tortillas
- Lime wedges (for serving)
- Vegetable oil (for frying)

### Instructions
1. Mix sour cream, mayo, chipotle, and lime juice for the crema. Toss cabbage, onion, cilantro, and lime juice for the slaw.
1. Whisk flour, baking powder, and salt. Add cold beer and whisk into a smooth batter.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C). Pat fish dry, dip in batter, and fry for 2–3 minutes per side until golden and crispy.
1. Warm tortillas. Place fried fish on each, top with slaw and crema drizzle.
1. Serve immediately with extra lime wedges.

---

## Ceviche
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs fresh firm white fish (Sea Bass, Halibut, or Mahi-Mahi)
- 1 cup fresh lime juice (approx. 15–20 limes)
- 1 large red onion, very thinly sliced
- 1–2 chili peppers (Aji Limo or Habanero), halved or diced
- 2–3 sprigs fresh cilantro, plus chopped for garnish
- Salt to taste
- Traditional sides: Boiled sweet potato, large-kernel corn (choclo), toasted corn (cancha)

### Instructions
1. Cut chilled fish into 1-inch cubes. Place in a glass or ceramic bowl.
1. Soak sliced onions in ice water for 5–10 minutes, then drain.
1. Season fish with a generous amount of salt and let sit for 1–2 minutes.
1. Add lime juice, chili peppers, and cilantro sprigs. The juice should almost cover the fish.
1. Cover and refrigerate to marinate for 5–15 minutes for Peruvian style (longer if you prefer fish more 'cooked' by acid).
1. Remove chili halves and cilantro sprigs. Fold in half of the onions.
1. Serve on chilled plates with lettuce, sweet potato, corn, and remaining onions.

---

## Aguachile
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Raw Shrimp (large or medium, peeled and deveined)
- 3/4 cup Fresh Lime Juice
- 1/2 tsp Kosher Salt
- 2-3 Serrano Peppers
- 1/2 cup Fresh Cilantro
- 1 Cucumber (peeled, seeded, and sliced)
- 1/2 Red Onion (thinly sliced)
- 1 Avocado (sliced or cubed)
- Tostadas or Saltine Crackers (for serving)

### Instructions
1. Butterfly the shrimp by slicing along the back almost all the way through.
1. Place shrimp in a shallow glass dish, pour half the lime juice over them, sprinkle with salt, and marinate in the fridge for 10-15 minutes.
1. Blend the remaining lime juice, serrano peppers, and cilantro until smooth.
1. Pour the green sauce over the shrimp. Add red onions and cucumbers.
1. Chill in the fridge for another 5-10 minutes.
1. Top with avocado slices and serve immediately with tostadas or crackers.

---

## Seafood Gumbo
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup All-purpose Flour
- 1 cup Vegetable or Canola Oil
- 2 cups Yellow Onions (chopped)
- 1 cup Green Bell Pepper (chopped)
- 1 cup Celery (chopped)
- 2 tbsp Fresh Garlic (minced)
- 5 cups Seafood Stock
- 5 cups Chicken Broth
- 1 tbsp Creole or Cajun Seasoning
- 1 tsp Dried Thyme
- 4 Bay Leaves
- 2 tbsp Worcestershire Sauce
- 2 lbs Large Shrimp (peeled and deveined)
- 1 lb Lump Crab Meat
- 2 cups Okra (sliced)
- Cooked White Rice (for serving)

### Instructions
1. Make a dark roux by cooking oil and flour over medium-low heat for 20-30 minutes, stirring constantly until chocolate brown.
1. Add onions, bell peppers, and celery to the roux and sauté for 5-8 minutes. Add garlic and cook for 2 more minutes.
1. Slowly whisk in seafood stock and chicken broth. Add Cajun seasoning, thyme, bay leaves, and Worcestershire sauce.
1. Simmer for 1 to 1.5 hours.
1. Add okra and simmer for 15 minutes.
1. Add shrimp and crab meat; cook for 5-10 minutes until shrimp are opaque.
1. Serve over warm white rice.

---

## Blackened Fish
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 (6-oz) Fillets of firm white fish (Redfish, Mahi-mahi, or Snapper)
- 1 stick Unsalted Butter (melted)
- 1 tbsp Smoked Paprika
- 1 tsp Kosher Salt
- 1 tsp Garlic Powder
- 1 tsp Onion Powder
- 1 tsp Dried Thyme
- 1 tsp Dried Oregano
- 1 tsp Black Pepper
- 1/2 tsp Cayenne Pepper

### Instructions
1. Whisk together paprika, salt, garlic powder, onion powder, thyme, oregano, black pepper, and cayenne in a small bowl.
1. Pat fish fillets completely dry with paper towels.
1. Dip each fillet into melted butter, then coat generously with the spice mix on both sides.
1. Heat a large cast-iron skillet over high heat until extremely hot.
1. Sear fillets for 2-3 minutes per side until the crust is dark brown and fish is opaque.
1. Serve immediately with lemon wedges.

---

## Grilled Salmon
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2-4 Salmon Fillets (4-6 oz each, skin-on preferred)
- 1-2 tbsp Olive Oil or Avocado Oil
- 1/2 tsp Kosher Salt
- 1/2 tsp Black Pepper
- 1 tbsp Fresh Lemon Juice
- 2 tbsp Melted Unsalted Butter

### Instructions
1. Pat salmon fillets completely dry with paper towels.
1. Drizzle with oil and season with salt and pepper.
1. Preheat grill to medium-high (375°F-450°F) and oil the grates.
1. Place salmon flesh-side down and grill for 3-4 minutes undisturbed.
1. Flip and grill skin-side down for another 3-5 minutes until internal temperature reaches 125°F-130°F.
1. Remove from grill, drizzle with melted butter and lemon juice, and rest for 2-3 minutes before serving.

---

## Seafood Paella (Latin style)
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Large Shrimp (peeled and deveined)
- 1 lb Mussels or Clams
- 1/2 lb Squid rings
- 1/2 lb Firm White Fish (chunks)
- 2 cups Long-grain White Rice
- 4 cups Seafood Stock (hot)
- 1/2 cup Dry White Wine
- 3 tbsp Olive Oil
- 1 large Yellow Onion (diced)
- 1 Red Bell Pepper (diced)
- 4-5 cloves Garlic (minced)
- 2 Roma Tomatoes (chopped)
- 1 tsp Achiote Powder
- 1/2 tsp Ground Cumin
- 1/2 cup Frozen Peas
- Fresh Cilantro and Lemon wedges (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Sauté onion and bell pepper in oil until soft. Add garlic and tomatoes, cooking until jam-like.
1. Stir in achiote powder, cumin, and rice. Toast rice for 2 minutes.
1. Add white wine and hot seafood stock. Distribute rice evenly and do not stir again.
1. Simmer covered for 15 minutes.
1. Arrange seafood and peas on top of the rice. Cover tightly.
1. Cook for another 8-10 minutes until seafood is cooked and shells open.
1. Rest for 5 minutes, then garnish and serve.

---

## Coconut Shrimp
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Jumbo Raw Shrimp (peeled and deveined, tails on)
- 1/3 cup All-purpose Flour
- 1/2 tsp Salt
- 1/4 tsp Black Pepper
- 2 Large Eggs (beaten)
- 3/4 cup Panko Breadcrumbs
- 1 cup Sweetened Shredded Coconut
- 2 cups Canola or Vegetable Oil (for frying)

### Instructions
1. Set up three bowls: 1) flour with salt/pepper, 2) beaten eggs, 3) Panko mixed with shredded coconut.
1. Dredge shrimp in flour, dip in egg, and press firmly into coconut-panko mixture.
1. Heat oil in a skillet to 350°F.
1. Fry shrimp in batches for about 2 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with sweet chili sauce.

---

## Escovitch Fish
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs Whole Red Snapper (cleaned and scaled)
- 1 Lime or Lemon
- 1 tsp Salt
- 1 tsp Black Pepper
- Vegetable Oil for frying
- 1 Onion (sliced into rings)
- 1 Carrot (julienned)
- 1/2 Red Bell Pepper (sliced)
- 1/2 Green Bell Pepper (sliced)
- 1-2 Scotch Bonnet Peppers (sliced)
- 1/2 cup White Vinegar
- 1 tbsp Sugar
- 6-8 Pimento Berries (Allspice)
- 2-3 sprigs Fresh Thyme

### Instructions
1. Rinse fish with lime juice, pat dry, and score sides. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Fry fish in hot oil for 5-7 minutes per side until very crispy. Place on a platter.
1. In 2 tbsp of oil, sauté onions, carrots, bell peppers, and Scotch bonnet for 2-3 minutes.
1. Add pimento berries, thyme, vinegar, and sugar. Simmer for 2-3 minutes.
1. Pour hot pickled vegetables and liquid over the fried fish.
1. Let sit for 15-30 minutes before serving.

---

## Conch Fritters
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Conch Meat (tenderized and minced)
- 1 1/2 cups All-purpose Flour
- 1 tsp Baking Powder
- 2 Large Eggs (beaten)
- 1/2 cup Milk or Beer
- 1/2 cup Onion (minced)
- 1/2 cup Green Bell Pepper (minced)
- 1/4 cup Red Bell Pepper (minced)
- 2 cloves Garlic (minced)
- 1 Scotch Bonnet Pepper (minced)
- 1 tsp Salt
- 1/2 tsp Black Pepper
- 1/2 tsp Cayenne Pepper
- Oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Whisk flour, baking powder, and dry seasonings in a large bowl.
1. Mix eggs and milk/beer in a separate bowl, then combine with dry ingredients to form a batter.
1. Fold in minced conch, onion, bell peppers, garlic, and Scotch bonnet.
1. Heat oil to 350°F-365°F.
1. Drop rounded spoonfuls of batter into oil and fry for 5-7 minutes until deep golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with Calypso sauce.

---

## Moqueca
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5-2 lbs Firm White Fish (chunks)
- 2 tbsp Fresh Lime Juice
- 1 tsp Kosher Salt
- 2 tbsp Olive Oil or Dendê Oil
- 1 large Yellow Onion (sliced)
- 3-4 cloves Garlic (minced)
- 2-3 Bell Peppers (sliced into rings)
- 2 cups Tomatoes (diced)
- 1 tbsp Tomato Paste
- 1 tsp Paprika
- 1/2 tsp Cumin
- 1 can (14 oz) Coconut Milk
- Fresh Cilantro and Scallions (chopped)

### Instructions
1. Marinate fish in lime juice and salt for 15-20 minutes.
1. Sauté onion, garlic, and bell peppers in oil until soft.
1. Add tomato paste, paprika, cumin, and diced tomatoes. Cook until tomatoes break down.
1. Pour in coconut milk and bring to a gentle simmer.
1. Nestle fish chunks into the broth. Cover and simmer for 8-12 minutes until fish is opaque.
1. Stir in cilantro and scallions and serve over white rice.

---

## Peruvian Seafood Stew
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Firm White Fish (chunks)
- 12-16 Mussels
- 12-16 Large Shrimp
- 8-10 Scallops
- 1/2 lb Squid rings
- 8 cups Seafood Stock
- 1 Red Onion (diced)
- 4 cloves Garlic (minced)
- 2 large Tomatoes (diced)
- 2 tbsp Ají Panca Paste
- 1 tbsp Ají Amarillo Paste
- 1/2 cup Dry White Wine
- Fresh Cilantro, Parsley, and Lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Sauté red onion until translucent. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in ají panca and ají amarillo pastes, then add tomatoes and cook until thick.
1. Add white wine and simmer for 2 minutes, then add seafood stock and simmer for 10 minutes.
1. Add mussels first and cook for 3-4 minutes.
1. Add fish, shrimp, scallops, and squid. Simmer for 3-5 minutes until cooked.
1. Stir in cilantro and parsley. Serve in deep bowls with lime wedges.
