# Category: Middle Eastern & African Cuisine

## Sayadieh
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 to 2 lbs (approx. 800g) of firm white fish fillets (Cod, Sea Bass, Snapper, or Halibut)
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour (for dusting)
- 1 tsp cumin, 1/2 tsp salt, 1/2 tsp black pepper (for fish)
- Vegetable or sunflower oil for frying
- 2 cups Basmati or Jasmine rice (rinsed and drained)
- 4 large onions, thinly sliced
- 3 to 3.5 cups water or fish stock
- 1.5 tsp ground cumin (for rice)
- 1 tsp Lebanese 7-spice (or cinnamon)
- 1/2 tsp turmeric (optional)
- 1/4 cup pine nuts and/or slivered almonds
- Fresh parsley, chopped
- Lemon wedges

### Instructions
1. Fry the pine nuts and almonds in a little oil until golden brown. Set aside.
1. Lightly coat the fish fillets in a mixture of flour, cumin, salt, and pepper. Fry until golden and crispy. Set aside.
1. In the same pot, cook sliced onions over medium-high heat until they reach a deep dark brown color (the secret to the rice's color).
1. Add the rinsed rice to the onions and stir for a minute. Add cumin, 7-spice, turmeric, and salt.
1. Pour in the water or stock. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low, cover, and simmer for 15-20 minutes until the liquid is absorbed.
1. Fluff the rice with a fork. Place the fish on top of the rice and garnish with toasted nuts and fresh parsley. Serve with lemon wedges.

---

## Grilled Hammour
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg Hammour (4 large fillets or 1 medium whole fish, cleaned and scaled)
- 3 tbsp Olive oil
- 2 tbsp Fresh lemon juice
- 4 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 tsp Ground cumin
- 1 tsp Ground coriander
- 1/2 tsp Turmeric powder
- 1/2 tsp Paprika (smoked or sweet)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Fresh parsley, chopped
- Lemon wedges
- Optional: Garlic butter sauce (melted butter, minced garlic, lemon juice)

### Instructions
1. Prepare the fish: make diagonal slits if whole, or pat dry if fillets.
1. Whisk together olive oil, lemon juice, garlic, and all spices to create a marinade.
1. Rub the marinade over the fish and refrigerate for at least 30 minutes.
1. Preheat grill to medium-high and oil the grates.
1. Grill fillets for 4-5 minutes per side, or whole fish for 8-10 minutes per side until opaque and flaky.
1. Let rest for 3-5 minutes, drizzle with lemon or garlic butter, garnish with parsley and serve.

---

## Fish Tagine
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 to 2 lbs firm white fish (cod, halibut, sea bass, or tilapia), cut into large chunks
- 1 bunch cilantro, finely chopped
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp ground cumin, 2 tsp paprika, 1 tsp salt
- 1/4 cup + 3 tbsp olive oil
- 2 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 large onion, sliced into rings
- 2 large potatoes, sliced into 1/4 inch rounds
- 2 carrots, sliced into rounds
- 2 tomatoes, sliced
- 2 bell peppers, sliced into strips
- 1/2 cup olives (green or red)
- 1 lemon (sliced) or 1 preserved lemon (quartered)
- 1/2 tsp turmeric, 1/2 tsp ground ginger
- 1/4 to 1/2 cup water

### Instructions
1. Create chermoula marinade by mixing cilantro, garlic, cumin, paprika, salt, 3 tbsp olive oil, and lemon juice. Marinate fish for 30 minutes.
1. In a tagine or heavy skillet, pour 1/4 cup olive oil and arrange onion rings as a base.
1. Layer carrots then potatoes over the onions. Season with turmeric, ginger, salt, and pepper.
1. Place tomato slices over potatoes, then arrange the marinated fish on top. Pour remaining marinade over.
1. Garnish with bell pepper strips, olives, and lemon slices.
1. Carefully pour water down the side, cover, and simmer over medium-low heat for 45-60 minutes until vegetables are tender.
1. Rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Chermoula Fish
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 cups fresh cilantro and 1.5 cups fresh flat-leaf parsley
- 3-4 cloves garlic, minced
- Zest and juice of 1 large lemon
- 1 tbsp paprika, 1 tsp ground cumin, 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper
- 6 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 1/2 tsp sea salt and 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 4 (5-6 oz) firm white fish fillets (halibut, cod, sea bass, or tilapia)

### Instructions
1. In a food processor, pulse garlic, cilantro, parsley, and lemon zest until finely chopped.
1. Add lemon juice, olive oil, paprika, cumin, cayenne, salt, and pepper; process until it forms a thick paste.
1. Pat fish dry and spread half the chermoula over both sides. Marinate for 15-30 minutes.
1. Broil on high for 5-7 minutes or pan-sear for 4-5 minutes per side until fish flakes easily.
1. Serve topped with the remaining fresh chermoula and lemon wedges.

---

## Shrimp Tagine
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 4 large ripe tomatoes (grated) or 14 oz crushed tomatoes
- 6 garlic cloves, minced
- 2-3 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 2 tbsp each of fresh flat-leaf parsley and cilantro, chopped
- 1 tsp sweet paprika, 1/4 tsp ground cumin, 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper
- 1 bay leaf
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste
- 3-4 lemon slices and extra cilantro for garnish

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a tagine or skillet. Sauté grated tomatoes and garlic for 10-12 minutes until thickened.
1. Reduce heat and stir in parsley, cilantro, paprika, cumin, cayenne, and bay leaf. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Arrange shrimp in a single layer in the sauce. Cook for 1 minute, then flip.
1. Place lemon slices around the edges and add 2 tbsp water for steam. Cover and cook for 8-10 minutes until shrimp are pink.
1. Serve hot directly from the pot with crusty bread.

---

## Egyptian Fish Sayadeya
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 whole Tilapia or Sea Bass, cleaned and scaled (or fillets)
- 4 cloves garlic (crushed), 1 tsp ground cumin, 1 tsp salt, 1/2 tsp black pepper, juice of 1 lemon (for fish)
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- Vegetable oil for frying
- 2 cups Egyptian short-grain rice (or Basmati)
- 2 large onions, finely chopped
- 3 to 3.5 cups hot water or fish stock
- 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp salt, 1/2 tsp sugar (for rice)
- 3 tbsp vegetable oil (for rice)

### Instructions
1. Marinate fish with garlic, cumin, salt, pepper, and lemon juice for 30 minutes.
1. For the rice: Heat 3 tbsp oil and caramelize chopped onions until they are a very dark brown (chocolate color), but not burnt.
1. Pour hot water over onions, add salt, cumin, and sugar. Boil for 2-3 minutes.
1. Add rice, bring to a boil, then cover and simmer on low for 15-20 minutes.
1. While rice cooks, coat marinated fish in flour and fry in hot oil until golden brown and crispy (5-7 minutes per side).
1. Plate the brown rice with the fried fish on top, garnished with parsley and lemon.

---

## Spicy Fish Stew
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb cod, halibut, or tilapia fillets, cut into 1-inch pieces
- 1/2 cup red onion, finely chopped
- 12 oz jar roasted red bell peppers, drained and chopped
- 14.5 oz can diced tomatoes with juice
- 1 tsp minced fresh garlic, 1/4 tsp red pepper flakes
- 1/4 cup chopped fresh cilantro
- 1/2 tsp fresh lemon zest, 2 tsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 tbsp olive oil, salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Sauté red onion in olive oil for 3-4 minutes until soft.
1. Stir in roasted peppers, diced tomatoes, garlic, and red pepper flakes. Simmer for 10 minutes.
1. Add lemon zest, juice, and cilantro to the tomato mixture.
1. Gently fold in fish pieces and simmer for 5-7 minutes until opaque and flaky.
1. Season with salt and pepper and serve with crusty bread or over rice.

---

## Prawn Peri-Peri
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2 lbs) Large prawns, deveined
- 6-8 Bird's eye chilies
- 4 Cloves of garlic
- 1 Red bell pepper, charred and peeled
- 1/2 cup Extra virgin olive oil
- 3 tbsp Red wine vinegar or lemon juice
- 1 tbsp Smoked paprika, 1 tsp dried oregano
- 1 tsp Salt, 1/2 tsp black pepper

### Instructions
1. Blend charred pepper, chilies, garlic, olive oil, vinegar, paprika, oregano, salt, and pepper to create Peri-Peri sauce.
1. Marinate prawns in half the sauce for 1-4 hours in the refrigerator.
1. Grill for 2-3 minutes per side or pan-sear for 2 minutes per side until opaque and charred.
1. Baste with remaining sauce during the last minute of cooking. Serve with savory rice or baguette.

---

## Grilled Tilapia
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 Tilapia fillets (4-6 oz each)
- 2 tbsp Olive oil
- 1 large Lemon (half juiced, half in wedges)
- 2 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 tsp salt, 1/2 tsp black pepper, 1/2 tsp paprika
- 1 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped

### Instructions
1. Preheat grill to medium-high (400°F-450°F) and oil the grates.
1. Whisk olive oil, lemon juice, garlic, salt, pepper, and paprika together.
1. Pat fillets dry and brush both sides with the mixture.
1. Grill for 3-4 minutes per side until opaque and flakes easily with a fork.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve with lemon wedges.

---

## Fish Couscous
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (675g) firm white fish, cut into 2-inch cubes
- 1/3 cup olive oil
- 1 medium onion, 1 red bell pepper, 1 medium zucchini (all diced)
- 2 garlic cloves, finely chopped
- 2 tbsp tomato paste, 2 tbsp lemon juice, 1 tsp harissa sauce
- 2 cups chicken or vegetable broth
- 19 oz can chickpeas, rinsed and drained
- 2 cups dry couscous
- 3/4 cup fresh flat-leaf parsley, finely chopped
- 1 tsp ground cumin, 1/2 tsp paprika, 1/2 tsp ground turmeric

### Instructions
1. Sear fish cubes in half the olive oil for 2 minutes per side; remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onion, bell pepper, and dry spices in remaining oil until soft (5 minutes).
1. Stir in zucchini, garlic, tomato paste, lemon juice, and harissa; cook for 2 minutes.
1. Add broth and chickpeas; bring to a boil and simmer for 2 minutes.
1. Stir in dry couscous and seared fish. Cover tightly and remove from heat.
1. Let sit for 5-7 minutes until liquid is absorbed and fish is cooked through.
1. Fluff with a fork, stir in parsley, and serve with lemon wedges.

---

## Sardine Balls
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) fresh sardines (cleaned, deboned, minced) or 2-3 cans of sardines in olive oil (drained)
- 1/2 cup cooked white rice or 1/4 cup breadcrumbs
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- 1/4 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp paprika
- 1/2 tsp turmeric
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp harissa paste or pinch of cayenne pepper (optional)
- 1 tbsp lemon juice
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- Tomato Sauce: 2 tbsp olive oil, 1 small onion (chopped), 3 cloves garlic (minced), 1 can (15 oz) crushed tomatoes, 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp paprika, 1/2 tsp salt, pinch of sugar, 1/2 cup water, 1 bay leaf, 1/2 cup green olives (optional)

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Sardine Mixture: Pulse fresh sardines in a food processor or mash canned sardines. Combine with rice/breadcrumbs, garlic, herbs, spices, lemon juice, and olive oil.
1. Form the Balls: Roll the mixture into walnut-sized balls (approx. 1.5 inches).
1. Make the Sauce: Sauté onion and garlic in olive oil. Stir in tomatoes, spices, sugar, water, and bay leaf. Simmer for 10 minutes.
1. Cook the Sardine Balls: Gently add balls to the sauce in a single layer. Cover and simmer on low for 15-20 minutes. Add olives in the last 5 minutes if using.
1. Garnish with lemon juice and extra herbs before serving.

---

## Seafood Harira
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/2 lb (250g) shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/2 lb (250g) firm white fish (cod, monkfish, or sea bass), cut into chunks
- 1/4 lb mussels or calamari (optional)
- 6-8 cups fish stock
- 1/2 cup dried green or brown lentils, rinsed
- 1 can (15 oz) cooked chickpeas, drained and rinsed
- 1 can (14 oz) crushed tomatoes or 4 large fresh tomatoes (grated)
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1 large onion, finely chopped
- 2 stalks celery with leaves, finely chopped
- 1/2 cup chopped cilantro
- 1/2 cup chopped parsley
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tsp ground ginger
- 1 tsp ground turmeric
- 1/2 tsp ground cinnamon
- Pinch of saffron threads (optional)
- Salt and pepper to taste
- 1 lemon, juiced
- Thickener: 3 tbsp flour mixed with 1/2 cup water
- 1/4 cup fine vermicelli or orzo (optional)

### Instructions
1. Sauté onion and celery in olive oil for 5 minutes.
1. Add ginger, turmeric, cinnamon, salt, pepper, and half of the herbs. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
1. Add tomatoes, tomato paste, lentils, and fish stock. Simmer for 30 minutes until lentils are tender.
1. Stir in chickpeas and vermicelli (if using). Cook for 5-10 minutes.
1. Add white fish, shrimp, and other seafood. Simmer for 3-5 minutes until cooked.
1. Slowly pour in the flour-water slurry while stirring. Simmer for 2-3 minutes to thicken.
1. Stir in remaining herbs and lemon juice. Serve with lemon wedges and dates.

---

## Fried Red Snapper
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs Red Snapper (whole cleaned or large fillets)
- Vegetable oil for frying
- Marinade: 1/4 cup fresh lemon juice, 4 cloves garlic (minced), 1 tsp ground cumin, 1 tsp ground coriander, 1/2 tsp turmeric, 1/2 tsp paprika or red pepper flakes, salt and black pepper
- Coating: 1 cup all-purpose flour, 1/4 cup cornmeal (optional), 1/2 tsp cumin, 1/2 tsp salt

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Fish: Pat dry. If whole, make 2-3 diagonal slits on each side.
1. Marinate: Mix marinade ingredients and rub over fish. Refrigerate for 30-60 minutes.
1. Dredge: Coat fish thoroughly in the seasoned flour mixture, shaking off excess.
1. Fry: Heat oil to 350°F (175°C). Fry for 5-7 minutes per side (whole) or 3-4 minutes per side (fillets) until golden and crispy.
1. Drain on a wire rack or paper towels. Serve with tahini sauce and lemon wedges.

---

## Fish Pepper Soup
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1 kg) fresh fish (catfish, tilapia, croaker, or snapper), cut into steaks
- 1-2 tbsp Pepper Soup Spice Mix (Ehuru, Uda, Uziza blend)
- 1-2 tbsp ground crayfish
- 1 tsp smoked paprika (optional)
- 1/2 tsp cayenne pepper
- 1-2 Scotch Bonnet or Habanero peppers, chopped
- 1/2 medium onion, finely diced
- 1-inch piece ginger, grated
- 2-3 cloves garlic, minced
- 6 cups water
- 2 seasoning cubes (Maggi or Knorr)
- Salt to taste
- 1 lime or lemon (for washing fish)
- Handful of Scent Leaves or Utazi Leaves (or basil/parsley)

### Instructions
1. Prepare Fish: Wash fish with lime/lemon. For catfish, pour hot water over it for 30 seconds to remove slime, then rinse.
1. Start Broth: Place fish, water, onions, ginger, garlic, and peppers in a large pot.
1. Season: Add pepper soup spice, crayfish, seasoning cubes, and salt.
1. Simmer: Bring to a boil, then reduce heat. Simmer covered for 15-20 minutes. Jiggle the pot instead of stirring to avoid breaking the fish.
1. Final Touch: Adjust seasoning, add scent leaves, and simmer for 2-3 minutes. Serve hot.

---

## Coconut Fish Curry
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) firm white fish fillets, cut into large chunks
- 1 tsp turmeric powder
- 1 tbsp lemon or lime juice
- 1/2 tsp salt and black pepper
- 2 tbsp coconut oil or ghee
- 1 large red onion, finely diced
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1-inch piece fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp Baharat (Middle Eastern 7-spice mix)
- 1 dried black lime (Loomi), pierced, or 1 tbsp tamarind paste
- 1 green chili, slit lengthwise (optional)
- 1 can (14 oz) full-fat coconut milk
- 2 medium tomatoes, finely chopped
- 1 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/2 cup fish or vegetable stock
- Garnish: Fresh cilantro, parsley, lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Marinate the Fish: Toss fish with turmeric, lemon juice, salt, and pepper. Sit for 15 minutes.
1. Sauté Aromatics: Heat oil/ghee. Sauté onions until soft. Add garlic, ginger, and chili; cook for 2 minutes.
1. Toast Spices: Add Baharat and dried lime (or tamarind). Stir for 1 minute. Add tomato paste and tomatoes; cook until softened.
1. Simmer Base: Add coconut milk and stock. Simmer and thicken for 10 minutes.
1. Poach Fish: Nestle fish into sauce. Cover and cook for 5-7 minutes until opaque. Do not overstir.
1. Finish: Remove dried lime. Stir in fresh herbs and serve with rice or chapati.

---

# Category: International / Fusion

## Seafood Pizza
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 ball (250g) pizza dough
- Thai Green Curry Pesto: 2 tbsp green curry paste, 1/2 cup cilantro, 1/4 cup Thai basil, 1 clove garlic, 1 tbsp lime juice, 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1/2 lb (225g) medium shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/4 lb (115g) bay scallops or calamari rings
- 1 tbsp butter and 1 clove garlic for sautéing
- 1.5 cups shredded Mozzarella
- 2 tbsp crumbled Feta
- Toppings: 1/4 red onion (sliced), 1/2 red bell pepper (julienned), 1/4 cup matchstick carrots
- Garnish: 2 tbsp crushed roasted peanuts, fresh cilantro, lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 450°F (230°C).
1. Make Pesto: Blend green curry paste, cilantro, basil, garlic, lime juice, and olive oil.
1. Flash-Sear Seafood: Sauté shrimp and scallops in butter and garlic for 60-90 seconds. Drain.
1. Assemble: Roll out dough. Spread pesto, then mozzarella. Add seafood and vegetables. Top with feta.
1. Bake: Cook for 10-12 minutes until crust is golden and cheese bubbles.
1. Garnish: Sprinkle with peanuts and cilantro. Serve with lime wedges.

---

## Seafood Pasta Alfredo
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb fettuccine noodles
- 1 lb large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/2 lb to 1 lb sea scallops, patted dry
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- Salt and white pepper to taste
- 4 tbsp unsalted butter
- 3-4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 small shallot, finely chopped
- 1/2 cup dry white wine (optional)
- 2 cups heavy whipping cream
- 1 1/2 cups freshly grated Parmesan cheese
- 1/4 tsp ground nutmeg (optional)
- Fresh parsley, chopped

### Instructions
1. Cook Pasta: Boil fettuccine until al dente. Reserve 1/2 cup pasta water, then drain.
1. Sear Seafood: Sauté seasoned shrimp (2-3 mins) and scallops (90 secs per side) in olive oil. Set aside.
1. Sauté Aromatics: Melt butter, sauté shallots and garlic for 1-2 minutes.
1. Deglaze: Add white wine (if using) and reduce by half.
1. Make Sauce: Simmer heavy cream, then whisk in Parmesan and nutmeg until thickened (3-5 mins).
1. Combine: Toss pasta and seafood into the sauce. Use reserved pasta water to adjust thickness if needed.
1. Garnish with parsley and extra Parmesan before serving.

---

## Garlic Butter Shrimp
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb large raw shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 4 tbsp unsalted butter
- 4-6 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 tsp paprika (optional)
- 1/4 tsp red pepper flakes (optional)
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped

### Instructions
1. Prep: Pat shrimp dry and season with salt, pepper, and paprika.
1. Melt Butter: Heat butter in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Sauté Garlic: Cook garlic for 30-60 seconds until fragrant.
1. Cook Shrimp: Add shrimp in a single layer. Cook 2-3 minutes per side until pink and opaque.
1. Finish: Stir in lemon juice and red pepper flakes. Toss to coat.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve immediately.

---

## Honey Garlic Salmon
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 salmon fillets (6 oz each)
- 3 tbsp honey
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tbsp butter (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Garnish: Green onions, lemon wedges

### Instructions
1. Prep: Pat salmon dry and season with salt and pepper.
1. Sauce: Whisk honey, garlic, soy sauce, and lemon juice in a bowl.
1. Sear: Heat olive oil. Cook salmon flesh-side down for 3-4 minutes until golden. Flip fillets.
1. Glaze: Reduce heat. Add butter and honey garlic sauce. Baste salmon with bubbling sauce for 2-3 minutes until cooked through.
1. Serve immediately with extra glaze and garnishes.

---

## Chili Garlic Crab
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 large crabs (Blue or Mud), cleaned and halved/quartered
- 1 head garlic, minced
- 3 tbsp ginger, minced
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 2-3 Thai bird's eye chilies, chopped (optional)
- 3 tbsp cooking oil
- 1 cup water
- 1/2 cup tomato ketchup
- 1/2 cup sweet chili sauce
- 2-3 tbsp fish sauce or soy sauce
- 1 tbsp sugar
- 1 large egg, beaten
- Slurry: 1 tbsp cornstarch in 2 tbsp water
- Garnish: Green onions or cilantro

### Instructions
1. Sauté Aromatics: Fry garlic, ginger, and onion in oil until golden and soft.
1. Cook Crab: Add crab and water. Cover and steam for 5-7 minutes until shells turn red.
1. Add Sauce: Stir in ketchup, sweet chili sauce, fish sauce, and sugar. Toss to coat and simmer for 2-3 minutes.
1. Thicken: Stir in cornstarch slurry until the sauce glazes.
1. Add Egg: Slowly pour in beaten egg, stirring gently for 30 seconds to create ribbons.
1. Garnish and serve hot with white rice or mantou buns.

---

## Seafood Stir-Fry
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb mixed seafood (shrimp, scallops, and squid or crab meat)
- 1-inch piece ginger, julienned or minced
- 3 cloves garlic, finely sliced
- 3-4 green onions, sliced (whites and greens separated)
- 1 red or green bell pepper, sliced into strips
- 1 cup snap peas or green beans, trimmed
- 1 cup sliced mushrooms (shiitake or button)
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp oyster sauce
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1 tsp sugar
- 1/2 cup chicken stock or water
- 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp water (slurry)
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil

### Instructions
1. In a small bowl, whisk together soy sauce, oyster sauce, sesame oil, sugar, and chicken stock.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a wok over high heat. Stir-fry seafood for 2-3 minutes until opaque; remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil to the pan. Sauté ginger, garlic, and white parts of green onions for 30 seconds.
1. Add bell peppers, snap peas, and mushrooms. Stir-fry for 3-4 minutes until tender-crisp.
1. Return seafood to the pan and pour in the sauce mixture.
1. Stir in the cornstarch slurry and cook for 1 minute until the sauce thickens and becomes glossy.
1. Toss in green parts of onions and serve immediately over rice.

---

## Seafood Fried Rice
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 oz raw shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 6 oz scallops or firm white fish chunks
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 3 cups cooked jasmine rice (preferably day-old and cold)
- 2-3 tbsp vegetable oil
- 2 tsp minced garlic
- 1 cup mixed vegetables (peas, carrots, and corn)
- 3 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp oyster sauce (optional)
- 2 tsp sesame oil
- Salt and white pepper to taste
- 2 green onions, chopped

### Instructions
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a wok over medium-high heat. Stir-fry shrimp and scallops for 2-3 minutes until cooked; remove and set aside.
1. Scramble the eggs in the same pan until just set; remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil and sauté garlic and mixed vegetables for 2 minutes.
1. Turn heat to high, add cold rice, and stir-fry for 3 minutes, breaking up any clumps.
1. Add seafood and eggs back to the pan. Pour in soy sauce, oyster sauce, and sesame oil.
1. Toss everything together for 1-2 minutes until steaming hot.
1. Season with salt and white pepper. Garnish with green onions.

---

## Mixed Seafood Grill
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb firm white fish (halibut, swordfish, or cod), cut into 1.5-inch pieces
- 1 lb extra-large shrimp, peeled and deveined (tails on)
- 2 tbsp butter, melted
- 1 tsp lemon-pepper seasoning
- 1/2 tsp crushed fennel seed
- 1/4 tsp salt
- Lemon wedges and fresh parsley for garnish

### Instructions
1. Preheat a gas or charcoal grill to medium-high heat. If using a grill basket, preheat it on the grill.
1. In a large bowl, combine melted butter, lemon-pepper seasoning, fennel seeds, and salt.
1. Add fish and shrimp to the bowl and toss gently to coat evenly.
1. Place seafood in the preheated grill basket (or on skewers).
1. Grill for 5-10 minutes, shaking the basket occasionally, until the fish flakes easily and shrimp are opaque.
1. Serve immediately with lemon wedges and fresh parsley.

---

## Seafood Chowder
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 oz salt pork or thick-cut bacon, finely diced
- 1 large onion, diced
- 2-3 medium potatoes, peeled and cubed
- 1 cup seafood stock or water
- 1/2 lb raw shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1/2 lb sea scallops
- 1/2 lb firm white fish chunks (cod or haddock)
- 1/2 lb lobster or crab meat (optional)
- 2 cups whole milk
- 1 cup heavy cream
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- A pinch of Old Bay seasoning
- Fresh parsley or chives for garnish

### Instructions
1. Fry salt pork or bacon in a large pot until crisp; remove bits and set aside for garnish.
1. Sauté onions in the rendered fat until soft (about 5 minutes).
1. Add potatoes and stock. Simmer, covered, for 10-12 minutes until potatoes are tender.
1. Add fish, shrimp, and scallops. Simmer for 5-7 minutes until cooked through.
1. Stir in milk and heavy cream. Heat slowly until steaming, but do not let it boil.
1. Season with salt, pepper, and Old Bay.
1. Ladle into bowls and garnish with reserved bacon bits and fresh herbs.

---

## Seafood Platter
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 12-18 fresh oysters, shucked
- 1 lb jumbo shrimp, cooked and chilled
- 2-3 cooked lobsters, split or tails only
- 1 lb crab legs or cracked crab
- 12 raw clams on the half shell (optional)
- Mignonette sauce (vinegar, shallots, pepper)
- Cocktail sauce (ketchup, horseradish, lemon)
- Mustard sauce or aioli
- Melted butter
- Lemon wedges and fresh dill for garnish
- Crushed ice

### Instructions
1. Fill a large platter or tiered stand with a thick layer of crushed ice.
1. Arrange the largest items like lobster and crab clusters on the ice first.
1. Nestle shucked oysters and clams into the ice so they remain level.
1. Arrange chilled shrimp in the remaining gaps.
1. Tuck lemon wedges and fresh dill sprigs around the seafood.
1. Place small bowls of sauces on the platter or serve alongside.
1. Keep refrigerated until the moment of serving.

---

## Baked Salmon with Herbs
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 (6-ounce) salmon fillets
- 2 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped
- 1 tbsp fresh dill, chopped
- 1 tbsp fresh chives or basil, chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 lemon (zested and sliced into rounds)
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C) and line a baking sheet with parchment paper.
1. In a small bowl, whisk together olive oil, garlic, lemon zest, and chopped herbs.
1. Pat salmon dry and place on the baking sheet. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Spoon the herb mixture over the fillets and spread evenly.
1. Place lemon slices on top of each fillet.
1. Bake for 12-15 minutes until salmon is opaque and flakes easily.
1. Let rest for 2-3 minutes before serving.

---

## Lemon Butter Fish
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 white fish fillets (approx. 6 oz each, e.g., cod or halibut)
- 4-6 tbsp unsalted butter
- 1 large lemon (zested and juiced)
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1/2 tsp onion powder
- 1/4 tsp paprika
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour (optional)
- Fresh parsley for garnish

### Instructions
1. Pat fillets dry and season with salt, pepper, garlic powder, onion powder, and paprika. Lightly dust with flour if desired.
1. Heat a skillet over medium-high heat and melt 2-3 tbsp of butter.
1. Sear fish for 2-3 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Add remaining butter, lemon zest, and half the lemon juice to the pan.
1. Spoon the melting lemon butter over the fish for the final 2 minutes of cooking.
1. Remove from heat, add remaining lemon juice, and garnish with parsley.

---

## Seafood Kebabs
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb firm white fish (halibut or swordfish), cut into 1-inch chunks
- 12-16 large raw shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 12-16 sea scallops
- 1 red bell pepper, 1 zucchini, and 1 red onion (all cut for skewering)
- 12 cherry tomatoes
- 1 lemon, sliced into thin rounds
- 1/4 cup olive oil
- 3 tbsp lemon juice
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp dried oregano, salt, and pepper

### Instructions
1. Soak wooden skewers in water for 30 minutes.
1. Whisk olive oil, lemon juice, garlic, and seasonings to make a marinade.
1. Toss seafood and vegetables with half the marinade; let sit for 15-20 minutes.
1. Thread seafood, vegetables, and folded lemon slices onto skewers.
1. Grill over medium-high heat for 8-10 minutes, turning once.
1. Baste with the remaining marinade during the last 2 minutes of grilling.
1. Serve hot over rice or salad.

---

## Seafood Salad
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb imitation crab, chopped into bite-sized pieces
- 1/2 lb cooked small shrimp
- 1/2 cup finely diced celery
- 1/4 cup finely diced red or green onion
- 1 cup mayonnaise
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 tsp Old Bay seasoning
- 1 tbsp fresh dill, chopped
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, combine the chopped imitation crab, shrimp, celery, and onions.
1. In a small bowl, whisk together mayonnaise, lemon juice, Old Bay, and dill.
1. Pour the dressing over the seafood mixture and fold gently until evenly coated.
1. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
1. Cover and refrigerate for at least 30-60 minutes before serving to allow flavors to meld.
1. Serve chilled on lettuce or in rolls.

---

## Seafood Spring Rolls
- **Source:** 100_Seafood_Dishes_Categorized.docx

### Ingredients
- 150g shrimp, finely chopped
- 100g scallops, finely chopped
- 100g crab meat, shredded
- 1/2 cup shredded carrots and 1/2 cup shredded cabbage
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1 tsp grated ginger
- 1 tsp soy sauce, 1/2 tsp sesame oil, salt, and white pepper
- 1 pack large spring roll wrappers
- 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp water (slurry)
- Vegetable oil for deep-frying

### Instructions
1. Combine chopped seafood, vegetables, aromatics, and seasonings in a large bowl.
1. Place a wrapper in a diamond shape and put 2 tbsp of filling on the lower third.
1. Fold the bottom corner over, fold in the sides, and roll up tightly.
1. Seal the final corner with a dab of cornstarch slurry.
1. Heat 2 inches of oil to 350°F (175°C).
1. Fry rolls in batches for 3-5 minutes until golden brown and crisp.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve hot with sweet chili sauce.

---

# Category: Dessert

## Chocolate Mug Cake
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake / Microwave
- **Original Servings:** 1 serving
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 3 tbsp milk
- 3 tbsp sugar
- 3 tbsp vegetable oil
- 2 tbsp cocoa powder
- 1 pinch of salt
- 1 egg

### Instructions
1. In a large microwave-safe mug (at least 12 oz), whisk together the flour, sugar, and cocoa powder until no clumps remain.
1. Add the egg and whisk thoroughly into the dry mixture.
1. Stir in the milk and vegetable oil until the batter is smooth and well-combined.
1. Microwave on high for 1 minute 30 seconds to 2 minutes. The cake is done when it has risen and the top looks set.
1. Let the cake rest for 1-2 minutes before serving.

---

## Banana Ice Cream
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 ripe bananas (frozen)
- 1 tbsp honey (optional)
- 1 tbsp peanut butter (optional)

### Instructions
1. Slice frozen bananas into small pieces.
1. Place frozen banana slices in a high-powered blender or food processor and pulse until they look like small crumbs.
1. Add honey and peanut butter if using.
1. Process on high until the mixture becomes smooth and reaches a soft-serve consistency, scraping down the sides as needed.
1. Serve immediately for soft-serve or freeze for 1-2 hours for a firmer, scoopable texture.

---

## Chocolate Mousse
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 200g dark chocolate
- 1 cup heavy cream
- 3 eggs (separated)
- 2 tbsp sugar

### Instructions
1. Melt the dark chocolate in a heatproof bowl over simmering water or in the microwave in 30-second bursts. Let it cool slightly.
1. Whisk the egg yolks into the melted chocolate one at a time until smooth.
1. In a separate bowl, whip the heavy cream until stiff peaks form. Set aside.
1. In another clean bowl, beat the egg whites while gradually adding the sugar until stiff, glossy peaks form.
1. Gently fold the whipped cream into the chocolate mixture.
1. Carefully fold in the beaten egg whites in batches until no white streaks remain, being careful not to deflate the mixture.
1. Spoon into serving dishes and refrigerate for at least 2-4 hours before serving.

---

## Peanut Butter Cookies
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 24 cookies
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup peanut butter
- 1 egg
- 1 cup sugar
- 1 tsp vanilla extract

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Line a baking sheet with parchment paper.
1. In a medium bowl, stir together the peanut butter, sugar, egg, and vanilla extract until smooth.
1. Roll the dough into 1-inch balls and place them 2 inches apart on the baking sheet.
1. Flatten each ball with a fork, making a criss-cross pattern.
1. Bake for 8-10 minutes until the edges are lightly browned.
1. Let the cookies cool on the baking sheet for 5 minutes before transferring to a wire rack.

---

## Brownies
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 16 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/2 cup butter
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 cup sugar
- 1/3 cup cocoa powder
- 2 eggs
- 1 pinch of salt

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease an 8x8 inch square baking pan.
1. Melt the butter and stir in the sugar and eggs until well combined.
1. Whisk in the cocoa powder, flour, and salt until the batter is smooth.
1. Spread the batter evenly into the prepared pan.
1. Bake for 25-30 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out with a few moist crumbs.
1. Allow the brownies to cool completely in the pan before cutting into squares.

---

## Rice Krispie Treats
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 16 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 tbsp butter
- 6 cups rice cereal
- 4 cups marshmallows

### Instructions
1. In a large saucepan, melt the butter over low heat.
1. Add the marshmallows and stir until completely melted and smooth. Remove from heat.
1. Add the rice cereal and stir gently until all cereal is evenly coated with the marshmallow mixture.
1. Press the mixture evenly into a greased 13x9 inch pan using a buttered spatula or wax paper.
1. Let the treats cool completely at room temperature before cutting into squares.

---

## Strawberry Shortcake
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 8 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups all-purpose flour
- 3/4 cup milk
- 2 tbsp sugar
- 1 cup sliced strawberries
- 1 tbsp baking powder
- 1 cup whipped cream
- 1/2 cup butter (cold, cubed)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 425°F (220°C) and grease a baking sheet.
1. In a large bowl, whisk together the flour, baking powder, and sugar.
1. Cut the cold, cubed butter into the flour mixture using a pastry cutter or fork until it resembles coarse crumbs.
1. Stir in the milk until the dough just comes together.
1. Drop large spoonfuls of dough onto the baking sheet and bake for 12-15 minutes until golden brown.
1. Allow shortcakes to cool slightly, then split them in half.
1. Assemble by layering the bottom half with sliced strawberries and whipped cream, then replacing the top half.

---

## Creme Brulee
- **Sub-Category:** Custard
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups heavy cream
- 1 tsp vanilla extract
- 5 egg yolks
- 6 tbsp extra sugar (for topping)
- 1/2 cup sugar

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 325°F (163°C). Place 6 ramekins in a large baking dish.
1. Heat the heavy cream in a saucepan over medium heat until it begins to simmer. Stir in the vanilla extract and remove from heat.
1. In a bowl, whisk the egg yolks and 1/2 cup sugar until pale and well blended.
1. Slowly whisk a small amount of the hot cream into the egg mixture to temper them, then gradually add the remaining cream while whisking constantly.
1. Divide the custard among the ramekins. Pour hot water into the baking dish until it reaches halfway up the sides of the ramekins.
1. Bake for 30-35 minutes until the edges are set but the center still jiggles slightly.
1. Cool to room temperature, then refrigerate for at least 4 hours.
1. Before serving, sprinkle the extra sugar over the chilled custards and caramelize with a kitchen torch or under the broiler until golden brown.

---

## Tiramisu
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 250g mascarpone cheese
- 20 ladyfinger biscuits
- 3 eggs (separated)
- 1 cup strong espresso (cooled)
- 3 tbsp sugar
- 2 tbsp cocoa powder for dusting

### Instructions
1. In a medium bowl, whisk the egg yolks and sugar until thick and pale. Fold in the mascarpone cheese until smooth.
1. In a separate clean bowl, whisk the egg whites until stiff peaks form. Gently fold them into the mascarpone mixture.
1. Quickly dip 10 ladyfingers one by one into the cooled espresso and layer them in the bottom of a small rectangular dish.
1. Spread half of the mascarpone cream over the ladyfingers.
1. Repeat with a second layer of dipped ladyfingers and the remaining cream.
1. Cover and refrigerate for at least 4-6 hours (overnight is best).
1. Just before serving, dust the top generously with cocoa powder.

---

## Lemon Bars
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 12 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 cup sugar
- 1/4 cup powdered sugar
- 1 cup fresh lemon juice
- 1/2 cup butter (softened)
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour (for filling)
- 2 eggs

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease or line an 8x8 inch square baking pan.
1. Mix the softened butter, 1 cup flour, and 1/4 cup powdered sugar until crumbly. Press into the bottom of the pan.
1. Bake the crust for 15-20 minutes until lightly golden.
1. Whisk together the eggs, 1 cup sugar, lemon juice, and 2 tbsp flour until smooth.
1. Pour the lemon mixture over the hot crust and return to the oven.
1. Bake for 18-22 minutes until the filling is set.
1. Cool completely at room temperature, then refrigerate for at least 2 hours before slicing into bars.

---

## Classic Cheesecake
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 8 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 200g graham crackers (crushed)
- 3/4 cup sugar
- 1/2 cup butter (melted)
- 2 eggs
- 500g cream cheese (softened)
- 1 tsp vanilla extract

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 325°F (160°C) and grease a 7-inch springform pan.
1. Mix crushed graham crackers with melted butter and press firmly into the bottom of the pan.
1. In a large bowl, beat softened cream cheese and sugar until smooth and creamy.
1. Add eggs one at a time, mixing on low speed just until combined. Stir in vanilla extract.
1. Pour the cream cheese mixture over the prepared crust.
1. Bake for 45-55 minutes until the edges are set but the center still jiggles slightly.
1. Turn off the oven, crack the door open, and let the cheesecake cool inside for 1 hour to prevent cracking.
1. Refrigerate for at least 6 hours or overnight before serving.

---

## Apple Crumble
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 apples (peeled and sliced)
- 1 cup rolled oats
- 1/2 cup sugar
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 tsp cinnamon
- 1/2 cup butter (cold)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).
1. In a large bowl, toss the sliced apples with a portion of the sugar and cinnamon. Spread them evenly into a baking dish.
1. In another bowl, combine the rolled oats, flour, and remaining sugar.
1. Cut the cold butter into small pieces and work it into the oat mixture using your fingers or a pastry cutter until it resembles coarse crumbs.
1. Sprinkle the crumble mixture evenly over the apples.
1. Bake for 40-45 minutes until the topping is golden brown and the apples are tender.
1. Serve warm, ideally with a scoop of vanilla ice cream.

---

## Panna Cotta
- **Sub-Category:** Custard
- **Original Servings:** 4-6 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups heavy cream
- 2 tsp gelatin powder
- 1/4 cup sugar
- 2 tbsp cold water
- 1 tsp vanilla extract

### Instructions
1. In a small bowl, sprinkle the gelatin over 2 tablespoons of cold water. Let it sit for 5-10 minutes to bloom.
1. In a saucepan, combine the heavy cream and sugar. Heat over medium-low, stirring constantly, until the sugar is dissolved (do not let it boil).
1. Remove the saucepan from the heat and stir in the bloomed gelatin and vanilla extract until completely dissolved.
1. Pour the mixture into ramekins or small serving bowls.
1. Refrigerate for at least 4-6 hours, or until the panna cotta is firm and set.
1. Serve chilled, optionally topped with fresh berries or fruit sauce.

---

## Chocolate Truffles
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 20 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 200g dark chocolate
- 2 tbsp butter
- 1/2 cup heavy cream
- 1/2 cup cocoa powder for rolling

### Instructions
1. Finely chop the dark chocolate and place it in a heat-proof bowl with the butter.
1. In a small saucepan, heat the heavy cream over medium heat until it just begins to simmer.
1. Pour the hot cream over the chocolate and butter. Let it sit for 5 minutes undisturbed.
1. Gently stir the mixture until it is completely smooth and glossy.
1. Cover the bowl and refrigerate for 2-3 hours until the mixture is firm enough to handle.
1. Use a spoon or small scoop to portion the ganache and roll quickly between your palms to form 1-inch balls.
1. Roll each truffle in cocoa powder until evenly coated. Store in the refrigerator.

---

## Vanilla Pudding
- **Sub-Category:** Custard
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups milk
- 1 tsp vanilla extract
- 1/4 cup sugar
- 2 tbsp butter
- 3 tbsp cornstarch

### Instructions
1. In a medium saucepan, whisk together the sugar and cornstarch.
1. Gradually whisk in the milk, ensuring there are no lumps.
1. Place the saucepan over medium heat and cook, stirring constantly, until the mixture thickens and begins to bubble.
1. Once thickened, remove from the heat and stir in the butter and vanilla extract until smooth.
1. Pour the pudding into individual serving bowls.
1. To prevent a skin from forming, press plastic wrap directly onto the surface of the pudding.
1. Refrigerate for at least 2 hours before serving.

---

## Banana Bread
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 8-10 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 ripe bananas (mashed)
- 1 tsp vanilla extract
- 1/3 cup melted butter
- 1 tsp baking soda
- 3/4 cup sugar
- 1 1/2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 egg

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C) and grease an 8x4-inch loaf pan.
1. In a large bowl, mash the ripe bananas with a fork until smooth.
1. Stir the melted butter into the mashed bananas. Add the sugar, beaten egg, vanilla, and baking soda. Mix well.
1. Gently stir in the flour until just combined. Do not overmix.
1. Pour the batter into the prepared loaf pan.
1. Bake for 50-60 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
1. Let the bread cool in the pan for 10 minutes, then transfer to a wire rack to cool completely.

---

## Fruit Parfait
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup granola
- 1 cup mixed fresh fruits
- 2 cups plain yogurt
- 2 tbsp honey

### Instructions
1. Wash and slice the fresh fruits into bite-sized pieces.
1. In two tall glasses or jars, start by spooning a layer of yogurt (about 1/2 cup) into the bottom of each.
1. Add a layer of mixed fruits, followed by a layer of granola.
1. Repeat the layers with the remaining yogurt, fruits, and granola.
1. Drizzle 1 tablespoon of honey over the top of each parfait just before serving for extra sweetness.

---

## Coconut Macaroons
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 24 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 cups shredded coconut
- 2 egg whites
- 2/3 cup sweetened condensed milk
- 1 pinch of salt
- 1 tsp vanilla extract

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 325°F (165°C) and line a baking sheet with parchment paper.
1. In a large bowl, stir together the shredded coconut, sweetened condensed milk, and vanilla extract until well combined.
1. In a separate clean bowl, beat the egg whites with a pinch of salt until stiff peaks form.
1. Gently fold the whipped egg whites into the coconut mixture until just combined.
1. Using a tablespoon or small cookie scoop, drop rounded mounds of the mixture onto the prepared baking sheet.
1. Bake for 20-25 minutes until the edges are golden brown.
1. Allow the macaroons to cool completely on the baking sheet before moving them.

---

## Chia Pudding
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/4 cup chia seeds
- 2 tbsp honey
- 1 cup coconut milk
- 1/2 tsp vanilla extract

### Instructions
1. In a mason jar or bowl, combine the chia seeds, coconut milk, honey, and vanilla extract.
1. Whisk or stir the mixture thoroughly to ensure the chia seeds are evenly distributed.
1. Let the mixture sit for 10 minutes, then stir again to break up any clumps of seeds.
1. Cover and refrigerate for at least 2 hours, or preferably overnight, until it reaches a thick pudding consistency.
1. Serve chilled, optionally topped with fresh fruit or nuts.

---

## Affogato
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 1 serving
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 scoop vanilla ice cream
- 1 shot hot espresso

### Instructions
1. Place one large scoop of vanilla ice cream or gelato into a small chilled glass or bowl.
1. Brew a fresh, hot shot of espresso (about 1 ounce).
1. Slowly pour the hot espresso directly over the ice cream.
1. Serve immediately with a small spoon before the ice cream melts completely.

---

## Churros
- **Sub-Category:** Fried
- **Original Servings:** 4-6 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup water
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 2 cups oil for frying
- 2 tbsp sugar
- 1/2 cup cinnamon sugar for coating

### Instructions
1. Prepare the coating by whisking together 1/2 cup sugar and cinnamon in a shallow bowl. Set aside.
1. In a small saucepan over medium heat, combine water, 2 tbsp sugar, salt, and 2 tbsp of oil. Bring to a boil.
1. Remove from heat and immediately stir in the flour until the mixture forms a smooth, thick ball of dough. Let it cool for 5 minutes.
1. Heat oil in a deep pot to 375°F (190°C).
1. Transfer the dough into a piping bag fitted with a large star tip.
1. Pipe 4- to 6-inch strips of dough directly into the hot oil, using scissors to snip the end.
1. Fry 3–4 churros at a time for 2–3 minutes per side until golden brown and crisp.
1. Drain on paper towels for a few seconds, then roll in the cinnamon-sugar mixture while still hot.

---

## Glazed Donuts
- **Sub-Category:** Fried
- **Original Servings:** 12 donuts
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 1/4 tsp active dry yeast
- 1/3 cup butter (softened)
- 3/4 cup warm milk
- 2 1/2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/3 cup sugar
- 2 cups oil for frying
- 1 egg
- 1 cup powdered sugar (for glaze)

### Instructions
1. In a small bowl, whisk together warm milk, yeast, and 1 tsp of sugar. Let sit for 5-10 minutes until foamy.
1. In a large bowl, whisk together the softened butter, egg, and the remaining sugar. Stir in the yeast mixture.
1. Gradually stir the flour and salt into the wet ingredients until a shaggy dough forms.
1. Knead the dough on a floured surface for about 5 minutes until smooth and elastic.
1. Place in an oiled bowl, cover, and let rise in a warm spot until doubled (about 1-1.5 hours).
1. Punch down the dough and roll it out to 1/2-inch thickness. Cut into donut shapes.
1. Place on parchment paper, cover, and let rise again for 30-60 minutes until puffy.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C) and fry donuts for about 1 minute per side until golden.
1. Whisk powdered sugar with a little milk and vanilla to make a glaze. Dip warm donuts into the glaze.

---

## Mochi
- **Sub-Category:** Steamed
- **Original Servings:** 12 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup glutinous rice flour
- 1/2 cup filling of choice (red bean paste, ice cream)
- 1/4 cup sugar
- 1/4 cup cornstarch for dusting
- 3/4 cup water

### Instructions
1. In a microwave-safe bowl, whisk together the glutinous rice flour and sugar.
1. Gradually add the water and whisk until the batter is smooth and lump-free.
1. Cover the bowl loosely with plastic wrap and microwave on high for 2 minutes.
1. Stir the mixture with a wet spatula; it will be sticky and partially translucent.
1. Cover again and microwave for another 1 to 2 minutes until fully translucent and very sticky.
1. Generously dust a work surface with cornstarch.
1. Transfer the hot mochi onto the starch and dust the top. Flatten and cut into 12 pieces.
1. While still warm, place a small amount of filling in the center of each piece and pinch the edges to seal.

---

## S'mores Bars
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 16 pieces
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups graham cracker crumbs
- 2 cups chocolate chips
- 1/2 cup butter (melted)
- 2 cups mini marshmallows

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C) and grease an 8x8-inch baking pan.
1. In a bowl, combine graham cracker crumbs and melted butter. Press half of the mixture firmly into the bottom of the pan.
1. Evenly spread the chocolate chips over the graham cracker base.
1. Spread the mini marshmallows over the chocolate chips.
1. Sprinkle the remaining graham cracker mixture over the marshmallows, pressing down lightly.
1. Bake for 25–30 minutes or until the top is lightly golden and marshmallows are melty.
1. Allow the bars to cool completely in the pan before slicing into 16 squares.

---

## Chocolate Fondue
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 200g chocolate (chopped)
- 1 tbsp butter
- 1/2 cup heavy cream
- 1 cup dippers: fruit, marshmallows, cake

### Instructions
1. In a small saucepan over low heat, combine the chopped chocolate, butter, and heavy cream.
1. Stir constantly until the chocolate is completely melted and the mixture is smooth and glossy.
1. Be careful not to let the mixture boil to avoid seizing the chocolate.
1. Remove from heat and stir in any optional flavorings like vanilla extract.
1. Transfer to a fondue pot or a warm bowl.
1. Serve immediately with your choice of dippers such as fruit, marshmallows, and cake cubes.

---

## Nutella Crepes
- **Sub-Category:** Stovetop
- **Original Servings:** 4-5 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 tbsp butter (melted)
- 2 eggs
- 1 tbsp sugar
- 1 1/2 cups milk
- 1/2 cup Nutella for filling

### Instructions
1. In a blender, combine flour, melted butter, eggs, sugar, and milk. Blend until smooth.
1. Let the batter rest in the refrigerator for at least 30 minutes.
1. Heat a non-stick skillet over medium-low heat and lightly grease with butter.
1. Pour about 1/4 cup of batter into the pan, tilting it to spread the batter into a thin circle.
1. Cook for 1-2 minutes until the edges brown, then flip and cook for another 30 seconds.
1. Remove the crepe and spread a tablespoon of Nutella over half of it while still warm.
1. Fold the crepe into quarters or roll it up and serve immediately.

---

## Caramel Flan
- **Sub-Category:** Custard
- **Original Servings:** 8 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup sugar (for caramel)
- 1 can evaporated milk
- 3 eggs
- 1 tsp vanilla extract
- 1 can sweetened condensed milk

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
1. In a saucepan over medium heat, melt the 1 cup of sugar until it turns into a golden-brown caramel. Pour immediately into an 8-inch round baking dish, coating the bottom.
1. In a blender, combine evaporated milk, condensed milk, eggs, and vanilla. Blend until smooth.
1. Pour the custard mixture over the hardened caramel in the baking dish.
1. Place the baking dish inside a larger roasting pan and fill the larger pan with hot water until it reaches halfway up the side of the flan dish.
1. Bake for 60-75 minutes until set but still slightly jiggly in the center.
1. Remove from the water bath and let cool, then refrigerate for at least 4 hours or overnight.
1. To serve, run a knife around the edge and invert onto a rimmed plate.

---

## Blueberry Muffins
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 12 muffins
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/3 cup vegetable oil
- 3/4 cup sugar
- 3/4 cup milk
- 2 tsp baking powder
- 1 egg
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1 cup fresh blueberries

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C) and grease a 12-cup muffin tin or line with paper liners.
1. In a large bowl, whisk together flour, sugar, baking powder, and salt.
1. In another bowl, whisk together the vegetable oil, egg, and milk.
1. Pour the wet ingredients into the dry ingredients and stir until just combined (batter will be thick).
1. Gently fold in the fresh blueberries.
1. Spoon the batter into the muffin cups, filling them nearly to the top.
1. Bake for 20-25 minutes or until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.
1. Cool in the tin for 5 minutes before transferring to a wire rack.

---

## No-Bake Cheesecake
- **Sub-Category:** No-Bake
- **Original Servings:** 8-10 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs
- 1/2 cup powdered sugar
- 1/4 cup butter (melted)
- 1 tsp vanilla extract
- 500g cream cheese (softened)
- 1 cup whipped cream

### Instructions
1. In a bowl, mix graham cracker crumbs, melted butter, and a bit of the powdered sugar until moistened.
1. Press the mixture firmly into the bottom of a 9-inch springform pan and refrigerate while preparing the filling.
1. In a large bowl, beat the softened cream cheese with the remaining powdered sugar and vanilla until smooth.
1. Gently fold the whipped cream into the cream cheese mixture until light and fluffy.
1. Pour the filling over the prepared crust and smooth the top with a spatula.
1. Cover and refrigerate for at least 4-6 hours (ideally overnight) until firm.
1. Serve chilled, optionally topped with fruit or chocolate sauce.

---

## Sticky Toffee Pudding
- **Sub-Category:** Baked
- **Original Servings:** 8 servings
- **Source:** 30_Simple_Desserts.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup pitted dates
- 1/2 cup butter
- 1 cup boiling water
- 3/4 cup sugar
- 1 tsp baking soda
- 2 eggs
- 3/4 cup all-purpose flour
- Toffee sauce: butter, brown sugar, heavy cream

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C) and grease a 9-inch square baking dish.
1. Place chopped dates in a bowl and pour boiling water over them. Stir in baking soda and let sit for 15-20 minutes.
1. In a large bowl, cream together butter and sugar until light and fluffy. Beat in the eggs one at a time, then add vanilla.
1. Gently fold in the flour and a pinch of salt, then stir in the date mixture (including the liquid).
1. Pour batter into the dish and bake for 30-35 minutes until a toothpick comes out clean.
1. For the sauce: combine butter, brown sugar, and heavy cream in a saucepan. Simmer for 3-5 minutes until thickened.
1. Poke holes in the warm cake and pour about 1/3 of the sauce over it. Serve remaining sauce on the side.

---

# Category: Starter

## Spring Rolls
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 300g minced chicken or pork (optional)
- 2 cups shredded cabbage
- 1 cup shredded carrots
- 1/2 cup sliced mushrooms
- 1/4 cup sliced bamboo shoots (optional)
- 2 green onions, finely chopped
- 1 tsp minced garlic
- 1 tsp minced ginger
- 1 tbsp oyster sauce
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1/2 tsp sugar
- 1/2 tsp white pepper
- 1 tsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp water (thickener)
- 12-15 large spring roll wrappers
- 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp water (sealing paste)
- 3-4 cups vegetable or canola oil

### Instructions
1. Sauté garlic, ginger, and minced meat in oil until cooked.
1. Add cabbage, carrots, mushrooms, and bamboo shoots; stir-fry for 2-3 minutes.
1. Add soy sauce, oyster sauce, sesame oil, sugar, and pepper. Stir in cornstarch slurry.
1. Let filling cool completely.
1. Place 2 tbsp filling on a diamond-shaped wrapper.
1. Fold bottom corner over filling, fold sides in, and roll upward tightly.
1. Seal with cornstarch paste.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C).
1. Fry rolls for 3-5 minutes until golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on wire rack or paper towels.

---

## Fresh Summer Rolls
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 10 round rice paper wrappers
- 2 oz dry rice vermicelli noodles
- 15-20 large cooked shrimp, halved lengthwise
- 1 large carrot, julienned
- 1 cucumber, julienned
- 1 red bell pepper, julienned
- 1 cup purple cabbage, shredded
- 5-10 large lettuce leaves
- Fresh mint, cilantro, and/or Thai basil leaves
- 1/4 cup creamy peanut butter (sauce)
- 1 tbsp hoisin sauce (sauce)
- 1 tsp sriracha (sauce)
- 1 clove garlic, minced (sauce)
- 1-2 tbsp warm water (sauce)

### Instructions
1. Cook rice noodles, drain, and rinse with cold water.
1. Prep all vegetables and herbs.
1. Dip rice paper in warm water for 10-15 seconds until pliable.
1. Place 2-3 shrimp halves in a row in the center of the wrapper.
1. Layer herbs, noodles, and vegetables on top of a lettuce leaf, then place on wrapper.
1. Fold bottom of wrapper up, fold sides in, and roll tightly.
1. Whisk peanut sauce ingredients together, adding water to desired consistency.
1. Serve immediately.

---

## Dumplings (Jiaozi)
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork (20% fat)
- 1/2 lb Napa cabbage, finely minced
- 3 scallions, finely chopped
- 1 tbsp minced ginger
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame oil
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp white pepper
- 1 package (50 count) dumpling wrappers
- Soy sauce, black vinegar, chili oil (for dipping sauce)

### Instructions
1. Salt minced cabbage, let sit for 15 mins, then squeeze out excess water.
1. Mix pork, cabbage, scallions, ginger, garlic, and seasonings in one direction until sticky.
1. Place 1 tbsp filling in center of wrapper, moisten edges with water.
1. Fold in half, pinch center, and create pleats on each side to seal.
1. To boil: Drop in boiling water, add cold water when they float (repeat twice), cook until translucent.
1. To pan-fry: Fry in oil for 2 mins, add 1/2 cup water, cover and steam for 5 mins, then crisp bottoms.
1. Serve with dipping sauce.

---

## Gyoza
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 2 cups Napa cabbage, finely shredded
- 1 cup garlic chives or green onions, finely chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame oil
- 1 tbsp sake
- Pinch of salt and black pepper
- 1 package (50 count) gyoza wrappers
- 2 tbsp soy sauce (sauce)
- 2 tbsp rice vinegar (sauce)
- 1 tsp chili oil (sauce)

### Instructions
1. Toss cabbage with salt, let sit for 10 mins, then squeeze out water.
1. Mix cabbage, meat, chives, garlic, ginger, and seasonings until tacky.
1. Place 1 tbsp filling in center of wrapper, wet edges.
1. Fold and create 3-5 pleats on one side, pressing against the flat back.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in skillet, sear gyoza for 2-3 mins until golden.
1. Add 1/4 cup water, cover, and steam for 3-4 mins.
1. Remove lid and cook for 1 min to re-crisp bottoms.
1. Serve with dipping sauce.

---

## Takoyaki
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 cups cold dashi stock
- 2 large eggs
- 1 tsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp cornstarch
- 4-5 oz boiled octopus, cubed
- 2-3 stalks green onions, chopped
- 2 tbsp pickled ginger, chopped
- 1/4 cup tenkasu (tempura bits)
- Takoyaki sauce, Japanese mayonnaise, Aonori, Katsuobushi (toppings)

### Instructions
1. Whisk eggs, soy sauce, flour, cornstarch, and dashi into a thin batter.
1. Heat and oil takoyaki pan generously.
1. Fill holes to the brim with batter.
1. Drop octopus piece into each hole; sprinkle onions, ginger, and tenkasu over pan.
1. Cut overflow batter between holes and flip balls 90 degrees.
1. Rotate balls frequently until golden brown and round.
1. Top with sauce, mayo, aonori, and bonito flakes.

---

## Edamame
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb frozen edamame in pods
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame oil
- 1 tbsp minced garlic
- 1 tsp grated fresh ginger
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tsp maple syrup or honey (optional)
- 1 tsp sriracha or chili flakes (optional)
- Sea salt and toasted sesame seeds (garnish)

### Instructions
1. Boil edamame in salted water for 3-5 minutes, then drain.
1. Heat sesame oil in a skillet, sauté garlic and ginger for 30-60 seconds.
1. Add edamame pods to skillet.
1. Toss with soy sauce, sweetener, and chili for 1-2 minutes until coated.
1. Garnish with sea salt and sesame seeds.

---

## Chicken Satay
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.2 lbs boneless skinless chicken thighs, in strips
- 1.5 tsp coriander seeds
- 0.5 tsp cumin seeds
- 0.5 tsp white peppercorns
- 1 tbsp lemongrass, chopped
- 1 tsp ground turmeric
- 0.5 tsp ground cinnamon
- 1/2 cup full-fat coconut milk (marinade)
- 1 tbsp palm sugar
- 3/4 tsp salt
- 1 tbsp tamarind paste
- 1 cup full-fat coconut milk (sauce)
- 2 tbsp Thai red curry paste
- 1/2 cup roasted peanuts, finely ground
- 1 tbsp palm sugar (sauce)
- 1 tbsp tamarind paste (sauce)
- 1 tsp fish sauce
- Bamboo skewers, soaked

### Instructions
1. Grind coriander, cumin, and peppercorns into powder.
1. Mix marinade ingredients with spices and marinate chicken for at least 2 hours.
1. For sauce: Simmer 1/4 cup coconut milk with curry paste until oil separates.
1. Add remaining coconut milk, peanuts, sugar, and tamarind; simmer for 5 mins.
1. Thread chicken onto skewers.
1. Grill for 2-3 minutes per side until cooked through.
1. Serve with peanut sauce.

---

## Chicken Karaage
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb boneless chicken thighs, in 1-inch pieces
- 1/2 cup potato starch or cornstarch
- Neutral oil for frying
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp sake
- 1 tbsp mirin
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tsp garlic, grated
- 1/2 tsp toasted sesame oil
- Salt and black pepper
- Lemon wedges, Japanese mayonnaise (serving)

### Instructions
1. Mix soy sauce, sake, mirin, ginger, garlic, sesame oil, salt, and pepper.
1. Marinate chicken pieces for at least 30 minutes.
1. Dredge chicken in potato starch, shaking off excess.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C).
1. Fry chicken for 3-4 minutes until light golden brown.
1. Rest chicken for 2 minutes.
1. Optionally flash-fry at 375°F (190°C) for 45-60 seconds for extra crunch.
1. Serve with lemon and mayonnaise.

---

## Tempura
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 150g cake flour or all-purpose flour
- 30g cornstarch
- 150ml cold water
- 100ml cold carbonated water
- 1 small egg, chilled
- Neutral oil for frying
- Shrimp, white fish, or squid
- Sweet potato, lotus root, broccoli, mushrooms, etc.
- 100ml dashi, 2 tbsp mirin, 2 tbsp soy sauce (dipping sauce)

### Instructions
1. Wash and dry all seafood and vegetables thoroughly.
1. Slice dense vegetables thinly; dust ingredients lightly with cornstarch.
1. Heat oil to 180°C (350°F).
1. Mix chilled egg, water, and soda water; sift in flour and cornstarch.
1. Mix briefly with chopsticks, leaving the batter lumpy.
1. Dip pieces into batter and fry in small batches for 2-3 minutes.
1. Drain on wire rack and serve with dipping sauce.

---

## Kimchi
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large head Napa cabbage (3-5 lbs)
- 1/4 cup non-iodized salt
- 1 cup daikon radish, julienned
- 2 carrots, matchsticks
- 4-6 green onions, 1-inch pieces
- 1/4 to 1/2 cup Gochugaru (Korean red pepper flakes)
- 1/4 cup minced garlic
- 1 tsp grated ginger
- 1 tsp sugar
- 3 tbsp water or fish sauce

### Instructions
1. Cut cabbage into 1-2 inch squares, toss with salt, and let sit for 1.5-2 hours.
1. Rinse cabbage 3 times and drain well.
1. Mix garlic, ginger, sugar, and liquid, then stir in gochugaru to make paste.
1. Combine cabbage, vegetables, and paste; mix well (use gloves).
1. Pack into clean jars, pressing down to remove air; leave headspace.
1. Ferment at room temperature for 1-5 days, burping daily.
1. Store in refrigerator once tangy.

---

## Korean Pancakes
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 tbsp potato starch or cornstarch
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 1/2 tsp onion powder
- 1 cup ice-cold water
- 1 large egg, lightly beaten
- 1 bunch green onions, cut into 2-3 inch lengths
- 4-6 tbsp vegetable oil
- Dipping Sauce: 2 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tbsp rice vinegar, 1 tbsp water, 1 tsp sugar, 1/2 tsp sesame oil, 1/2 tsp sesame seeds, optional gochugaru

### Instructions
1. Whisk all dipping sauce ingredients in a small bowl and set aside.
1. In a medium bowl, whisk together flour, starch, salt, garlic powder, and onion powder.
1. Add ice-cold water and the beaten egg; mix until just combined (a few lumps are okay).
1. Heat 2-3 tablespoons of oil in a large non-stick skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Pour half of the batter into the pan and arrange half of the scallions on top.
1. Cook for 3-4 minutes until the bottom is golden brown and crispy.
1. Carefully flip and cook for another 2-3 minutes, adding more oil if needed.
1. Slice into wedges and serve hot with the dipping sauce.

---

## Thai Fish Cakes
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb white fish fillets (Basa, Tilapia, or Cod)
- 2-3 tbsp Thai red curry paste
- 1 large egg
- 2 tbsp cornstarch or tapioca starch
- 1 tbsp fish sauce
- 1 tsp sugar
- 5-6 Makrut lime leaves, finely julienned
- 1/2 cup green beans, thinly sliced into rounds
- Vegetable oil for frying
- Dipping Sauce: Thai sweet chili sauce, chopped cucumber, crushed peanuts

### Instructions
1. Place fish chunks, red curry paste, egg, fish sauce, sugar, and starch in a food processor.
1. Pulse until the mixture becomes a smooth, sticky paste.
1. Transfer to a bowl and stir in the lime leaves and green beans by hand.
1. Wet your hands and shape the mixture into small discs (about 2 inches wide).
1. Heat oil in a skillet over medium heat.
1. Fry the cakes in batches for 2-3 minutes per side until deep golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve hot with dipping sauce.

---

## Tom Yum Soup
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 cups chicken stock
- 2 stalks lemongrass, bruised and cut into pieces
- 1-inch piece galangal, sliced
- 4-6 kaffir lime leaves, torn
- 2-4 Thai bird's eye chilies, bruised
- 1 lb large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 1 cup mushrooms (straw or oyster), sliced
- 1 medium tomato, cut into wedges
- 1 small white onion, cut into wedges
- 3-4 tbsp fish sauce
- 3-4 tbsp fresh lime juice
- 1 tsp sugar
- 1 tbsp Thai roasted chili paste (optional)
- Fresh cilantro and green onions for garnish

### Instructions
1. Bring chicken stock to a boil; add lemongrass, galangal, lime leaves, and chilies.
1. Simmer for 5 minutes until fragrant.
1. Add onions, mushrooms, and tomatoes; simmer for 2-3 minutes.
1. Add shrimp and cook for 1-2 minutes until pink and opaque.
1. Stir in fish sauce, sugar, and chili paste; then turn off the heat.
1. Stir in fresh lime juice after removing from heat to avoid bitterness.
1. Ladle into bowls and garnish with cilantro and green onions.

---

## Pad Thai Spring Rolls
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 8-10 large round rice paper sheets
- 4 oz thin rice vermicelli, cooked
- 1/2 lb firm tofu (matchsticks) or cooked shrimp
- 1 cup shredded carrots
- 1 cup shredded red cabbage
- 1 cucumber, julienned
- 2 green onions, sliced
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro
- 1/4 cup fresh mint
- 1/4 cup crushed roasted peanuts
- Pad Thai Sauce: 2 tbsp tamarind paste, 2 tbsp fish sauce, 1 tbsp lime juice, 1 tbsp sugar
- Peanut Sauce: 1/4 cup peanut butter, 1 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tbsp lime juice, 1 tsp honey, 1 tsp ginger

### Instructions
1. Whisk the Pad Thai sauce ingredients and the peanut dipping sauce ingredients in separate bowls.
1. Prepare all fillings: cook noodles, sear tofu, and julienne vegetables.
1. Dip a rice paper sheet in warm water for 5-10 seconds until soft.
1. Place noodles, protein, vegetables, and herbs in the lower third of the wrapper.
1. Drizzle 1 tsp of Pad Thai sauce over the filling and sprinkle with peanuts.
1. Fold the bottom and sides over the filling and roll up tightly.
1. Serve immediately with the peanut dipping sauce.

---

## Green Mango Salad
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 large green (unripe) mangoes, julienned
- 1 sweet red bell pepper, thinly sliced
- 1 cup red onion, thinly sliced
- 1/3 cup fresh coriander, chopped
- 1/3 cup fresh mint, chopped
- 1/2 cup toasted cashews or peanuts
- Dressing: 2 tbsp lime juice, 4 tsp fish sauce, 4 tsp sugar, 1 tbsp oil, 1/4 tsp chili sauce

### Instructions
1. Peel and julienne the green mangoes into thin matchsticks.
1. Whisk together all dressing ingredients until the sugar dissolves.
1. In a large bowl, combine mango, red pepper, onion, cilantro, and mint.
1. Pour the dressing over the salad and toss gently to coat.
1. Top with toasted nuts just before serving to maintain crunch.

---

## Samosa
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- Pastry: 2 cups all-purpose flour, 1/2 tsp carom seeds, 1/2 tsp salt, 4 tbsp ghee, 5-6 tbsp water
- Filling: 3-4 medium boiled potatoes, 1/2 cup green peas, 2 tbsp oil, 1 tsp cumin seeds, 1 tsp ginger, 1-2 green chilies
- Spices: 1 tsp coriander powder, 1/2 tsp garam masala, 1/2 tsp amchur, 1/4 tsp turmeric, salt
- Fresh cilantro, chopped
- Oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Mix flour, carom seeds, and salt; rub in ghee until crumbly, then add water to form a stiff dough. Rest for 30 minutes.
1. Heat oil, sauté cumin, ginger, and chilies. Add peas and mashed potatoes with all spices.
1. Cook for 3-4 minutes, stir in cilantro, and let the filling cool completely.
1. Divide dough into balls, roll into ovals, and cut in half to make semi-circles.
1. Form a cone with a semi-circle, fill with potato mixture, and seal the edges with water.
1. Deep fry on low-medium heat for 10-12 minutes until golden and crisp.

---

## Pakora
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup besan (chickpea flour)
- 2-3 tbsp rice flour
- 1/2 to 3/4 cup water
- 1 tsp cumin seeds
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp turmeric
- 1/2 tsp red chili powder
- 1 tsp carom seeds
- 1-2 green chilies, chopped
- 1 tbsp ginger-garlic paste
- Vegetables: 1 onion (sliced), 1 potato (thinly sliced), 1 cup spinach (chopped), 1/2 cup cauliflower florets
- Vegetable oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Whisk besan, rice flour, and spices in a large bowl.
1. Gradually add water to create a thick, smooth batter.
1. Fold in the prepared vegetables and chilies until thoroughly coated.
1. Heat 2 inches of oil in a deep pan over medium-high heat.
1. Drop small clumps of the mixture into the oil and fry for 3-5 minutes.
1. Turn occasionally until crisp and deep golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with chutney.

---

## Chicken Lollipop
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 10-12 chicken wings or drumettes (frenched)
- 1 tbsp ginger-garlic paste
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp red chili paste
- 1 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp vinegar or lemon juice
- 4 tbsp cornstarch
- 3 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1 egg
- Pinch of red food color (optional)
- Oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Marinate the frenched chicken with ginger-garlic paste, soy sauce, chili paste, pepper, salt, and vinegar for 30 minutes.
1. Add cornstarch, flour, egg, and food color to the marinade and mix well to form a thick coating.
1. Heat oil in a deep pan over medium-high heat.
1. Fry the chicken in batches for 5-7 minutes until cooked through.
1. Increase heat for the last minute for extra crispiness.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with Szechuan sauce.

---

## Dim Sum
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork (80% lean)
- 1/2 lb shrimp, peeled and chopped
- 4-5 dried shiitake mushrooms, soaked and minced
- 1/4 cup water chestnuts, chopped
- 1 package wonton wrappers (round)
- Seasonings: 1 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine, 2 tsp sesame oil, 1 tsp sugar, 1/2 tsp salt, 1/4 tsp white pepper, 1 tbsp cornstarch, 1 egg white
- Minced carrot for garnish

### Instructions
1. Combine pork, shrimp, mushrooms, and water chestnuts in a bowl.
1. Add all seasonings and stir vigorously in one direction for 3-5 minutes until sticky.
1. Place a tablespoon of filling in the center of a wrapper and form an open-top cylinder.
1. Flatten the top with a spoon and garnish with a dot of minced carrot.
1. Place in a lined steamer basket and steam over high heat for 8-10 minutes.
1. Serve hot with chili oil or soy sauce.

---

## Wonton Soup
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 8 cups chicken broth
- 24 oz frozen mini wontons
- 3 cups fresh spinach or baby bok choy
- 2 tbsp sesame oil
- 1 bunch green onions, whites and greens separated
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1.5 cups shredded carrots
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- Optional: 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine, 1/2 tsp white pepper
- Toppings: Sesame seeds, chili crisp

### Instructions
1. Sauté green onion whites, garlic, and ginger in sesame oil for 1-2 minutes.
1. Add carrots, soy sauce, and chicken broth; bring to a rolling boil.
1. Add wontons, reduce heat, and simmer for 5-6 minutes until they float.
1. Stir in spinach or bok choy during the last 2 minutes until wilted.
1. Ladle into bowls and garnish with green onion tops, sesame seeds, and chili crisp.

---

## Bruschetta
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs ripe Roma or vine tomatoes, diced
- 1 large baguette or loaf of crusty Italian bread
- 2-3 cloves garlic (1 minced, 1-2 whole for rubbing)
- 1/4 cup fresh basil leaves, thinly sliced
- 1/4 cup extra-virgin olive oil
- 1-2 tsp balsamic vinegar (optional)
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Topping: Combine diced tomatoes, minced garlic, sliced basil, olive oil, and balsamic vinegar in a medium bowl. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Marinate: Let the mixture sit at room temperature for 15–30 minutes to allow flavors to meld.
1. Toast the Bread: Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Brush bread slices with olive oil and toast for 5–8 minutes until golden and crisp.
1. Rub Garlic: While bread is warm, rub a peeled whole garlic clove across the surface of each slice.
1. Assemble: Top each slice of bread with a generous portion of the tomato mixture just before serving.
1. Serve: Drizzle with extra olive oil or balsamic glaze if desired.

---

## Caprese Salad
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 3–4 medium ripe tomatoes, sliced 1/4-inch thick
- 12–16 oz fresh mozzarella, sliced 1/4-inch thick
- 1 bunch fresh basil (about 1/3 cup whole leaves)
- 2–3 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil
- 1–2 tablespoons balsamic glaze or reduction (optional)
- Flaky sea salt and freshly cracked black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Layer: Alternate slices of tomato and mozzarella on a large platter or individual plates.
1. Add Basil: Tuck whole basil leaves between the tomato and mozzarella slices.
1. Season: Sprinkle generously with sea salt and black pepper.
1. Drizzle: Finish by drizzling extra virgin olive oil and balsamic glaze evenly over the top.
1. Serve: Serve immediately at room temperature.

---

## Antipasto Platter
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 oz Prosciutto, thinly sliced and rolled
- 6 oz Salami (Genoa or Soppressata)
- 6 oz Pepperoni or Capicola
- 8 oz Marinated Mozzarella balls (Ciliegine)
- 4 oz Sharp Provolone, cut into wedges
- 4 oz Parmigiano Reggiano, broken into chunks
- 1 cup Mixed Olives
- 1 cup Marinated Artichoke hearts
- 1/2 cup Roasted Red Peppers, sliced
- 1 cup Cherry tomatoes
- Fresh rosemary or basil for garnish
- Crusty Italian bread or breadsticks

### Instructions
1. Prepare Bowls: Place wet items (olives, artichokes, peppers) into small individual serving bowls.
1. Anchor Platter: Place bowls on a large board or platter as anchor points.
1. Arrange Meats: Fold or roll sliced meats and place in piles around the bowls.
1. Add Cheeses: Fill gaps with cheese selections.
1. Fill Gaps: Use fresh vegetables and tomatoes to fill remaining empty spaces.
1. Garnish & Serve: Tuck in fresh herbs and serve at room temperature with bread.
