## Arancini
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups Arborio rice
- 5 cups chicken or vegetable broth, warm
- 1/2 cup dry white wine
- 1 small onion, finely diced
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 2 tbsp unsalted butter
- 1/2 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 4 oz fresh mozzarella, cut into 1/2-inch cubes
- 1/2 cup frozen peas, thawed
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 3 large eggs, beaten
- 2 cups Italian or Panko breadcrumbs
- Neutral oil for deep frying
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Prepare Rice: Sauté onion in olive oil and butter. Add rice and toast for 2 minutes. Add wine and stir until absorbed.
1. Cook Risotto: Add warm broth one ladle at a time, stirring until absorbed. Once tender, stir in Parmesan, salt, and pepper.
1. Cool: Spread rice on a baking sheet and refrigerate for at least 2 hours until completely cold.
1. Form Balls: With damp hands, flatten 1/4 cup of rice, place a mozzarella cube and peas in the center, and roll into a tight ball.
1. Bread: Dredge balls in flour, dip in beaten eggs, and roll in breadcrumbs.
1. Fry: Heat oil to 350°F (175°C). Fry balls in batches for 3-5 minutes until golden brown.
1. Serve: Drain on paper towels and serve warm with marinara sauce.

---

## Croquettes
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2.2 lbs starchy potatoes (Russet or Yukon Gold)
- 2 large egg yolks
- 2/3 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- Pinch of nutmeg (optional)
- 3.5 oz mozzarella, cut into small strips (for filling)
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, beaten
- 1-2 cups fine breadcrumbs
- Vegetable oil for frying
- Salt to taste

### Instructions
1. Cook Potatoes: Boil whole, unpeeled potatoes until tender. Peel and mash while warm until smooth. Let cool completely.
1. Mix: Combine cooled mashed potatoes, egg yolks, Parmesan, salt, and nutmeg. Mix until smooth.
1. Shape: Form small portions into cylinders. If using cheese, insert a strip of mozzarella and seal.
1. Coat: Roll each croquette in flour, dip in beaten egg, and roll in breadcrumbs.
1. Chill: Refrigerate for at least 1 hour to prevent falling apart during frying.
1. Fry: Heat oil to 350°F (175°C). Fry in batches for 2-3 minutes until golden brown.
1. Serve: Drain on paper towels and serve warm.

---

## Patatas Bravas
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs starchy potatoes
- Olive oil for deep frying
- 3 tbsp extra virgin olive oil
- 1 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1 tbsp Smoked Spanish Paprika (mix of sweet and spicy)
- 1 cup chicken or vegetable broth
- Salt to taste
- Optional: 1 clove garlic, splash of sherry vinegar, and alioli for serving

### Instructions
1. Prepare Potatoes: Peel and cut potatoes into bite-sized chunks. Soak in water for 15 minutes, then pat completely dry.
1. Make Sauce: Heat 3 tbsp oil, stir in flour for 1 minute, then add paprika (do not burn). Gradually whisk in broth and simmer until thickened.
1. First Fry: Fry potatoes at 325°F (160°C) for 5-7 minutes until tender. Drain.
1. Second Fry: Increase heat to 375°F (190°C) and fry for 2-3 minutes until deep golden and crispy.
1. Assemble: Toss hot potatoes with salt, drizzle with Salsa Brava, and top with alioli if desired.

---

## Gazpacho
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs ripe tomatoes, roughly chopped
- 1 Italian green pepper, chopped
- 1 small cucumber, peeled and chopped
- 1-2 cloves garlic
- 1/4 small white onion (optional)
- 1 slice stale white bread, soaked and squeezed dry
- 1/2 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 2-3 tbsp sherry vinegar
- 1 tsp salt
- Optional garnishes: diced cucumber, pepper, onion, and croutons

### Instructions
1. Blend: Place tomatoes, pepper, cucumber, garlic, onion, and bread in a blender. Blend until liquefied.
1. Emulsify: Slowly drizzle in olive oil while blending on low. Add vinegar and salt.
1. Strain: Pour through a fine-mesh sieve for a smooth texture, discarding skins and seeds.
1. Chill: Refrigerate for at least 2 hours or overnight.
1. Serve: Serve very cold in bowls or glasses with garnishes.

---

## Tapas
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb large shrimp, peeled and deveined
- 10–12 cloves garlic, thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1 tsp smoked Spanish paprika
- 1 tsp red pepper flakes
- 2 tbsp dry sherry or white wine
- Juice of 1/2 lemon
- 1/2 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- Kosher salt to taste
- Crusty bread for serving

### Instructions
1. Prep: Pat shrimp completely dry and season with salt.
1. Infuse Oil: Heat olive oil, garlic, and red pepper flakes over medium-low heat until garlic is fragrant and pale golden.
1. Sauté Shrimp: Increase heat to medium. Add shrimp and paprika. Cook for 2-3 minutes until opaque.
1. Finish: Remove from heat. Stir in sherry, lemon juice, and parsley.
1. Serve: Serve immediately while sizzling with bread for dipping.

---

## French Onion Soup
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 5–6 large yellow onions, thinly sliced
- 4 tbsp unsalted butter
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup dry white wine or dry sherry
- 6 cups beef stock
- 2 sprigs fresh thyme
- 1 bay leaf
- 1 French baguette, sliced and toasted
- 1.5 to 2 cups shredded Gruyère cheese
- Salt, pepper, and 1 tsp balsamic vinegar to taste

### Instructions
1. Caramelize Onions: Melt butter and oil. Add onions and cook slowly for 45-60 minutes until deep mahogany brown.
1. Simmer: Add garlic, then deglaze with wine. Add stock, thyme, and bay leaf. Simmer for 20-30 minutes.
1. Finish Soup: Discard herbs. Stir in vinegar and season with salt and pepper.
1. Assemble: Ladle soup into oven-safe bowls. Top with toasted bread and a generous layer of Gruyère.
1. Broil: Broil for 2-4 minutes until cheese is melted and bubbly.

---

## Escargots
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 24 canned French snails, rinsed and drained
- 24 snail shells or an escargot dish
- 1 cup unsalted butter, softened
- 3–4 cloves garlic, minced into a paste
- 1 tbsp finely minced shallot
- 3 tbsp fresh flat-leaf parsley, chopped
- 1 tbsp dry white wine (optional)
- 1/2 tsp salt and 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1 fresh crusty baguette for serving

### Instructions
1. Prepare Garlic Butter: Blend softened butter, garlic, shallot, parsley, wine, salt, and pepper until smooth.
1. Assemble: Place a bit of butter in each shell/indentation, add a snail, and top with more butter to seal.
1. Bake: Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Place shells on a bed of sea salt to stay upright.
1. Cook: Bake for 10-12 minutes until butter is bubbling and sizzling.
1. Serve: Serve immediately with baguette slices.

---

## Quiche
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 (9-inch) deep-dish pie crust (store-bought or homemade)
- 6–8 slices of bacon, cooked and crumbled
- 1 cup (4 oz) Gruyère or Swiss cheese, shredded
- 1/4 cup shallots or yellow onion, finely minced
- 4 large eggs
- 1 ½ cups heavy cream (or half-and-half)
- ¼ tsp salt
- ⅛ tsp black pepper
- ⅛ tsp ground nutmeg

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C). Blind bake the pie crust for 8–10 minutes until set. Lower oven to 350°F (175°C).
1. Cook bacon until crisp, then crumble. Sauté shallots in a teaspoon of bacon fat until translucent.
1. Layer the crumbled bacon, sautéed shallots, and shredded cheese in the bottom of the warm crust.
1. In a bowl, whisk together eggs, heavy cream, salt, pepper, and nutmeg until smooth.
1. Pour the egg mixture over the fillings in the pie crust.
1. Bake for 40–50 minutes until the edges are set and golden brown, but the center still has a slight jiggle.
1. Let the quiche rest for 10–15 minutes before slicing.

---

## Cheese Soufflé
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 tbsp unsalted butter (plus extra for greasing)
- 3 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1 cup whole milk
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper
- 1 ½ cups shredded sharp cheese (Gruyère, Cheddar, or Comté)
- 4 large eggs, separated
- 1/4 tsp cream of tartar
- 2 tbsp grated Parmesan cheese

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C). Butter a 1.5-quart soufflé dish and coat with Parmesan cheese.
1. In a saucepan, melt 3 tbsp butter, whisk in flour and cook for 1-2 minutes.
1. Slowly whisk in milk and cook until thickened and smooth (3-4 minutes). Remove from heat.
1. Stir in salt, cayenne, and shredded cheese until melted. Whisk in egg yolks one at a time.
1. In a separate bowl, beat egg whites and cream of tartar until stiff peaks form.
1. Gently fold one-quarter of the whites into the cheese sauce, then carefully fold in the rest.
1. Pour into the prepared dish and bake for 25–30 minutes until puffed and golden brown. Serve immediately.

---

## Smoked Salmon Canapés
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 6–8 slices of pumpernickel or cocktail rye bread
- 4–6 oz smoked salmon, cut into thin strips
- 4 oz cream cheese, softened
- 1 tbsp fresh dill, finely chopped (plus sprigs for garnish)
- 1 tsp lemon juice
- ½ tsp lemon zest
- 1 tbsp capers, drained

### Instructions
1. Cut the bread into 1.5-inch rounds or squares using a cutter or knife.
1. In a small bowl, mix softened cream cheese, chopped dill, lemon juice, and lemon zest until smooth.
1. Spread a teaspoon of the cream cheese mixture onto each bread round.
1. Fold a piece of smoked salmon and place it on top of the cream cheese.
1. Garnish each canapé with a small sprig of dill and 2-3 capers.
1. Serve immediately or chill for up to 1 hour.

---

## Deviled Eggs
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 large eggs, hard-boiled and peeled
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise
- 1 tsp yellow mustard
- 1 tsp apple cider vinegar
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Paprika for garnish

### Instructions
1. Slice the hard-boiled eggs in half lengthwise and remove the yolks.
1. Mash the yolks in a bowl with a fork until fine.
1. Stir in mayonnaise, mustard, vinegar, salt, and pepper until smooth and creamy.
1. Spoon or pipe the yolk mixture back into the egg white halves.
1. Garnish with a sprinkle of paprika. Refrigerate for at least 30 minutes before serving.

---

## Stuffed Mushrooms
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 20 whole cremini or white button mushrooms
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 8 oz cream cheese, softened
- 1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 tsp onion powder
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped
- 1/2 cup Panko breadcrumbs
- 2 tbsp butter, melted

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Clean mushrooms and remove stems.
1. Finely chop the stems. Sauté stems and minced garlic in olive oil for 3-5 minutes until tender.
1. In a bowl, combine cream cheese, Parmesan, pepper, onion powder, parsley, and the sautéed stems.
1. Stuff each mushroom cap generously with the cream cheese mixture.
1. Mix Panko breadcrumbs with melted butter. Press the top of each mushroom into the breadcrumbs.
1. Bake on a baking sheet for 20 minutes until tender and golden brown.

---

## Garlic Bread
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large loaf of French or Italian bread
- 1/2 cup (1 stick) unsalted butter, softened
- 3–4 cloves garlic, finely minced
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, finely chopped
- 1/4 tsp salt

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).
1. In a small bowl, combine softened butter, minced garlic, parsley, and salt.
1. Slice the loaf in half lengthwise or into 1-inch thick accordion slices.
1. Spread the garlic butter generously over the cut sides or between slices.
1. For crispy bread, place halves face-up on a baking sheet. For soft bread, wrap the loaf in foil.
1. Bake for 10–15 minutes until the butter is melted and edges are golden. Broil for 1-2 minutes if extra crispiness is desired.

---

## Prawn Cocktail
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 400g cooked and peeled prawns
- ½ Iceberg lettuce, finely shredded
- 5 tbsp mayonnaise
- 2 tbsp tomato ketchup
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tsp lemon juice
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Paprika and lemon wedges for garnish

### Instructions
1. In a small bowl, whisk together mayonnaise, ketchup, Worcestershire sauce, and lemon juice. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Pat the prawns dry and toss them with two-thirds of the sauce until well coated.
1. Divide the shredded lettuce between four chilled glasses or bowls.
1. Spoon the coated prawns over the lettuce and drizzle with the remaining sauce.
1. Garnish with a dusting of paprika and a lemon wedge. Serve immediately.

---

## Herring Salad
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 8–12 oz jarred pickled herring fillets, drained and diced
- 2 medium waxy potatoes, boiled, peeled, and diced
- 1 cup cooked beets, diced
- 1 large tart apple, peeled and diced
- ½ cup dill pickles, diced
- ½ small red onion, finely chopped
- 2 hard-boiled eggs for garnish
- ½ cup sour cream
- 2 tbsp mayonnaise
- 1 tbsp white wine vinegar
- 1 tsp Dijon mustard
- 2 tbsp fresh dill, chopped

### Instructions
1. Dice herring, potatoes, beets, apple, pickles, and onion into uniform 1/2-inch cubes.
1. In a small bowl, whisk together sour cream, mayonnaise, vinegar, mustard, and fresh dill.
1. Gently toss the diced ingredients in a large bowl with the dressing until evenly coated.
1. Cover and refrigerate for 1–2 hours to allow flavors to meld.
1. Garnish with sliced hard-boiled eggs and extra dill before serving.

---

## Potato Rösti
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2–3 large starchy potatoes (approx. 1.5 lbs)
- 3 tbsp unsalted butter or ghee
- 1 tsp sea salt
- Black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Peel and coarsely grate the potatoes.
1. Place grated potatoes in a kitchen towel and squeeze firmly to remove as much liquid as possible.
1. Toss the dry potato shreds with salt and pepper.
1. Melt 2 tbsp butter in a non-stick skillet over medium heat.
1. Add potatoes to the pan, spread evenly and press down firmly to form a compact cake.
1. Cook for 10–12 minutes until the bottom is deeply golden. Flip the Rösti onto a plate.
1. Add remaining 1 tbsp butter to the pan, slide the Rösti back in, and cook for another 8–10 minutes.

---

## Beef Carpaccio
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 12–16 oz high-quality beef tenderloin
- 2 cups baby arugula
- 2 oz Parmigiano-Reggiano, shaved
- 3 tbsp extra virgin olive oil
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- Flaky sea salt and freshly cracked black pepper
- 1 tbsp capers (optional)

### Instructions
1. Wrap the beef tenderloin in plastic and freeze for 60–90 minutes to firm up.
1. Slice the beef across the grain into very thin rounds (1/8 inch or less).
1. Pound the slices between plastic wrap until paper-thin and translucent.
1. Arrange slices in a single layer on chilled plates.
1. Top with arugula, Parmesan shavings, and capers.
1. Whisk oil and lemon juice together, drizzle over the dish, and season with salt and pepper. Serve immediately.

---

## Buffalo Wings
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2½ to 3 lbs chicken wings (split into flats and drums)
- Vegetable oil (for deep-frying)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- ½ cup Frank’s RedHot Original Cayenne Pepper Sauce
- ½ cup (1 stick) unsalted butter
- 1 tbsp white vinegar or cider vinegar
- ¼ tsp cayenne pepper (optional, for extra heat)
- ℛ tsp garlic powder
- Celery sticks (for serving)
- Blue cheese dressing (for serving)

### Instructions
1. Pat the chicken wings completely dry with paper towels; season lightly with salt and pepper.
1. Heat 3–4 inches of vegetable oil in a heavy pot to 375°F (190°C).
1. Fry the wings in small batches for 12–15 minutes until golden brown and very crispy.
1. Drain wings on a wire rack or paper towels.
1. In a small saucepan, melt the butter over medium-low heat; whisk in the hot sauce, vinegar, garlic powder, and cayenne pepper.
1. Simmer the sauce for 1–2 minutes until well combined.
1. Place the hot wings in a large bowl, pour the sauce over them, and toss vigorously until thoroughly coated.
1. Serve immediately with cold celery sticks and blue cheese dressing.

---

## Chicken Tenders
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5–2 lbs chicken tenders (or boneless skinless chicken breasts sliced into 1-inch strips)
- 1 ½ cups all-purpose flour
- ¾ tsp salt
- ½ tsp black pepper
- 1 large egg
- 2 tbsp water
- Vegetable, canola, or peanut oil (for frying)
- Optional: Panko breadcrumbs (replace half the flour for extra crunch)

### Instructions
1. Heat about 2 inches of oil in a large skillet or Dutch oven to 365°F (185°C).
1. In one shallow bowl, mix flour, salt, and pepper. In a second bowl, whisk the egg and water together.
1. Dredge each chicken strip in the flour mixture, dip into the egg wash, and then place back into the flour (or Panko) for a final coating.
1. Let the breaded chicken sit on a plate for about 5 minutes to help the coating adhere.
1. Carefully fry the chicken in batches for 3–5 minutes per side until golden brown and internal temperature reaches 165°F.
1. Transfer tenders to a paper towel-lined plate to drain and sprinkle with a pinch of salt while hot.

---

## Nachos
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large bag (approx. 13 oz) tortilla chips (thick or restaurant-style)
- 2–3 cups shredded cheese (Cheddar and Monterey Jack mix)
- 1 lb ground beef
- 2 tbsp taco seasoning
- 1 can (15 oz) black beans (drained) or refried beans
- ½ cup salsa (pico de gallo or chunky)
- ¼ cup sour cream
- 1 ripe avocado (diced or mashed)
- ¼ cup pickled or fresh jalapeño slices
- 2 tbsp fresh cilantro (chopped)
- ¼ cup red or green onions (finely diced)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C).
1. Brown the ground beef in a skillet, drain fat, and stir in taco seasoning with a splash of water; simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Spread half of the tortilla chips in an even layer on a large rimmed baking sheet.
1. Top the chips with half of the cooked beef, half of the beans, and half of the shredded cheese.
1. Repeat with the remaining chips, beef, beans, and cheese to create a second layer.
1. Bake for 10–15 minutes until the cheese is completely melted and bubbling.
1. Remove from oven and immediately add fresh toppings: salsa, sour cream, avocado, onions, jalapeños, and cilantro.
1. Serve immediately.

---

## Quesadillas
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 large flour tortillas
- 1 cup shredded cheese (Cheddar, Monterey Jack, or Mexican blend)
- 1–2 tablespoons butter or olive oil
- Optional: Salsa, sour cream, or guacamole (for serving)

### Instructions
1. Heat a large non-stick skillet over medium heat and add half the butter or oil.
1. Place one tortilla in the pan and sprinkle the shredded cheese evenly over its surface.
1. Place the second tortilla on top of the cheese.
1. Cook for 2–3 minutes until the bottom tortilla is golden brown and crispy.
1. Carefully flip the quesadilla and cook the other side for another 2–3 minutes until golden and cheese is melted.
1. Let the quesadilla rest for one minute on a cutting board, then slice into 6–8 triangles.
1. Serve warm with optional toppings.

---

## Guacamole with Chips
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 3–4 ripe avocados (peeled and pitted)
- 1 lime (juiced, about 1-2 tablespoons)
- ½ cup red or white onion (finely diced)
- ½ cup fresh cilantro (chopped)
- 1–2 Roma tomatoes (diced, optional)
- 1 jalapeño (seeded and finely minced)
- 1–2 cloves garlic (minced)
- ½ tsp salt (to taste)
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- Pinch of cumin (optional)
- 1 bag tortilla chips

### Instructions
1. Place avocado flesh in a medium bowl and mash with a fork or potato masher to desired consistency.
1. Stir in lime juice immediately to prevent browning.
1. Add minced garlic, salt, pepper, and cumin; stir well.
1. Gently fold in the diced onion, cilantro, jalapeño, and tomatoes.
1. Taste and adjust seasonings (salt, lime, or jalapeño) as needed.
1. Transfer to a serving bowl and serve with tortilla chips.

---

## Jalapeño Poppers
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 12 medium-sized fresh jalapeño peppers
- 8 oz cream cheese (softened)
- 12 slices of thin-cut bacon
- ½ cup shredded sharp cheddar cheese (optional)
- ½ tsp garlic powder
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- Optional: Fresh chives or green onions (chopped for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C) and line a baking sheet with foil or parchment paper.
1. Slice each jalapeño in half lengthwise and scrape out the seeds and white membranes (use gloves).
1. In a medium bowl, combine softened cream cheese, shredded cheddar, garlic powder, and black pepper.
1. Spoon about 1 tablespoon of the cheese mixture into each jalapeño half.
1. Cut each bacon slice in half widthwise and wrap one piece tightly around each stuffed pepper half.
1. Place poppers on the baking sheet and bake for 15–20 minutes until bacon is crispy and peppers are tender.
1. Cool for 5 minutes before serving; garnish with chives if desired.

---

## Corn Dogs
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 8–10 standard-sized hot dogs
- 1 cup yellow cornmeal
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- ¼ cup granulated sugar
- 1 tablespoon baking powder
- ¼ teaspoon salt
- 1 large egg
- 1 cup buttermilk (or whole milk)
- 1 tablespoon honey (optional)
- 1 tablespoon vegetable oil
- 8–10 wooden skewers or sturdy popsicle sticks
- Cornstarch (for dusting)
- 1–2 quarts vegetable oil (for frying)

### Instructions
1. Heat about 3 inches of vegetable oil in a large pot to 350°F (175°C).
1. Pat hot dogs completely dry with paper towels; insert a skewer into each hot dog.
1. Optional: Lightly dust the hot dogs with cornstarch.
1. In a large bowl, whisk together cornmeal, flour, sugar, baking powder, and salt.
1. In a separate bowl, whisk egg, buttermilk, honey, and 1 tbsp oil; combine with dry ingredients into a thick batter.
1. Pour batter into a tall drinking glass for easy dipping.
1. Dip each hot dog into the batter to coat completely, then carefully lower into hot oil.
1. Fry 2–3 at a time for about 3 minutes, turning occasionally until golden brown.
1. Drain on a wire rack or paper-towel-lined plate.

---

## Sliders
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (80/20 or 85/15 ratio)
- 1 tsp salt
- ½ tsp black pepper
- ½ tsp garlic powder
- ½ tsp onion powder
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 12 slider buns (Hawaiian sweet rolls recommended)
- 6–12 slices of cheese (Cheddar, American, or Havarti)
- 2 tbsp melted butter (for brushing)
- Optional toppings: Pickles, caramelized onions, lettuce, tomato, condiments

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, gently mix ground beef with salt, pepper, garlic powder, onion powder, and Worcestershire sauce.
1. Divide beef into 12 equal portions (1.5–2 oz each) and shape into small patties slightly larger than the buns.
1. Heat a large skillet or griddle over medium-high heat and cook patties for 3–4 minutes per side.
1. Place a small piece of cheese on each patty during the last minute of cooking; cover pan to melt.
1. Place patties on the bottom buns, add optional toppings, and cover with top buns.
1. Alternatively, bake the entire seasoned beef mixture in a 9x13 pan, place on split rolls, top with cheese and bun tops, brush with butter, and bake at 350°F for 5 minutes.

---

## Mac and Cheese Bites
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (16 oz) elbow macaroni
- ¼ cup unsalted butter
- ¼ cup all-purpose flour
- 2 cups whole milk
- 4 cups shredded sharp cheddar cheese
- ½ tsp garlic powder
- ½ tsp smoked paprika
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 2 large eggs
- 2 tbsp milk (for egg wash)
- 1 ½ cups Panko breadcrumbs
- ½ cup all-purpose flour (for dredging)
- Vegetable or canola oil (for frying)

### Instructions
1. Boil macaroni until al dente; drain and set aside.
1. Melt butter in a saucepan, whisk in ¼ cup flour, then slowly whisk in milk until thickened. Stir in cheese and seasonings until smooth.
1. Fold in macaroni, then spread into a greased 9x13 dish and refrigerate for 3–4 hours until firm.
1. Scoop and roll the mixture into 1 to 1.5-inch balls.
1. Dredge balls in flour, dip in egg wash (eggs + 2 tbsp milk), and coat with Panko breadcrumbs.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C) and fry in batches for 3–4 minutes until golden brown.
1. Drain on a paper towel-lined plate and serve hot.

---

## Clam Chowder
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2–3 cans (6.5 oz each) chopped clams (reserve juice)
- 4–6 slices bacon (chopped)
- 1 large onion (finely diced)
- 2 stalks celery (diced)
- 3–4 medium Russet potatoes (peeled and cut into ½-inch cubes)
- 2 cloves garlic (minced)
- 1 bottle (8 oz) clam juice
- 1 cup chicken broth or water
- ℓ cup all-purpose flour
- 2 cups half-and-half
- 2 tbsp butter
- 1 bay leaf
- ½ tsp dried thyme
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste
- Fresh parsley and oyster crackers (for serving)

### Instructions
1. Cook bacon in a large pot until crisp; remove bacon and set aside, leaving fat in the pot.
1. Add butter to bacon fat; sauté onion and celery for 5–7 minutes. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in flour and cook for 1–2 minutes to remove raw taste.
1. Gradually whisk in reserved clam juice and chicken broth. Add potatoes, bay leaf, and thyme.
1. Simmer for 15–20 minutes until potatoes are tender.
1. Stir in half-and-half and chopped clams; heat through for 3–5 minutes (do not boil).
1. Remove bay leaf, season with salt and pepper, and serve with bacon bits, parsley, and crackers.

---

## Shrimp Cocktail
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 to 2 lbs large or jumbo shrimp (16/20 or 21/25 count), peeled and deveined (tails left on)
- 8 cups water
- 1 large lemon, halved
- 1 small onion, quartered
- 2 cloves garlic, smashed
- 1 stalk celery, cut into chunks
- 2 tsp salt
- 1 tsp whole peppercorns
- 2 bay leaves
- 1 tbsp Old Bay seasoning (optional)
- 1 cup ketchup
- 2–3 tbsp prepared horseradish
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1/2 tsp hot sauce (e.g., Tabasco)
- Freshly ground black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Prepare the cocktail sauce by whisking together ketchup, horseradish, lemon juice, Worcestershire sauce, hot sauce, and black pepper. Refrigerate for at least 30 minutes.
1. In a large pot, combine water, lemon halves (squeeze juice in first), onion, garlic, celery, salt, peppercorns, bay leaves, and Old Bay. Bring to a boil, then simmer for 10 minutes.
1. Add the shrimp to the pot. Cook for 2–3 minutes until pink and opaque.
1. Immediately drain the shrimp and plunge them into an ice water bath for 5 minutes until completely cold.
1. Drain the shrimp well and pat dry with paper towels.
1. Arrange the chilled shrimp on a platter or glasses and serve with the chilled cocktail sauce, garnished with lemon wedges and parsley.

---

## Onion Rings
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 large sweet onion (like Vidalia), sliced into 1/2-inch thick rings
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 tbsp cornstarch
- 1 cup buttermilk
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1 to 2 cups Panko breadcrumbs
- Vegetable oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Slice the onion into 1/2-inch thick rings and separate them.
1. Set up three shallow bowls: Bowl 1 with flour, cornstarch, salt, pepper, garlic powder, and paprika; Bowl 2 with buttermilk; Bowl 3 with Panko breadcrumbs.
1. Coat each onion ring first in the flour mixture (shake off excess), then dip in buttermilk, and finally press into the Panko breadcrumbs.
1. Heat 2 inches of oil in a heavy pot to 375°F (190°C).
1. Fry the rings in small batches for 2–3 minutes, flipping halfway, until deep golden brown.
1. Transfer to a wire rack to drain. Sprinkle with extra salt and serve hot.

---

## Mozzarella Sticks
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 12 string cheese sticks, cut in half crosswise
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs
- 1/4 cup milk
- 1 1/2 cups Panko or Italian-style breadcrumbs
- 1 tsp Italian seasoning
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Vegetable oil for frying
- Marinara sauce for dipping

### Instructions
1. Prepare three bowls: flour with garlic powder, salt, and pepper; whisked eggs and milk; breadcrumbs with Italian seasoning.
1. Coat each cheese stick in flour, then dip in the egg mixture, then roll in breadcrumbs. For a thicker crust, dip back into the egg and then the breadcrumbs again.
1. Place the breaded sticks on a parchment-lined baking sheet and freeze for at least 45–60 minutes to prevent leaking.
1. Heat 2 inches of oil in a skillet to 350°F (175°C).
1. Fry in small batches for 1–2 minutes until golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve immediately with warm marinara sauce.

---

## Chili Con Carne
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) ground beef
- 1 large yellow onion, finely diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 red bell pepper, diced
- 1 jalapeño, seeded and minced
- 2 tbsp chili powder
- 1 tbsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1 tsp dried oregano
- 1/2 tsp cayenne pepper
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1 can (28 oz) crushed or diced tomatoes
- 1 cup beef broth
- 1 can (15 oz) red kidney beans, drained and rinsed
- 1 tsp sugar or a small square of dark chocolate (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Toppings: shredded cheddar, sour cream, green onions, cilantro

### Instructions
1. In a large pot, brown the ground beef over medium-high heat. Drain excess fat.
1. Add onion, bell pepper, and jalapeño. Sauté for 5–7 minutes until soft. Stir in garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in tomato paste and all spices (chili powder, cumin, paprika, oregano, cayenne). Toast for 2 minutes.
1. Pour in crushed tomatoes and beef broth. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer covered for at least 30–60 minutes.
1. Stir in the kidney beans and optional sugar or chocolate. Simmer uncovered for 10–15 minutes until thickened.
1. Season with salt and pepper. Serve hot with desired toppings.

---

## Mini Tacos
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 1 packet (1 oz) taco seasoning
- 1/4 cup water
- 24 mini corn tortillas (4-inch street taco size)
- 1 to 2 cups shredded cheese (Monterey Jack or Mexican blend)
- 2–3 tbsp vegetable oil or cooking spray
- Sea salt to taste
- Optional toppings: sour cream, diced onions, cilantro, salsa, guacamole

### Instructions
1. Brown the ground beef in a skillet over medium-high heat. Drain grease.
1. Stir in taco seasoning and water. Simmer for 3–5 minutes until liquid is absorbed.
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Line a baking sheet with oil and lay out the tortillas.
1. Place a small amount of cheese and a tablespoon of meat on each tortilla.
1. Bake for 2–3 minutes until cheese melts and tortillas are pliable.
1. Remove and fold each tortilla in half. Return to the oven for 5–8 minutes until crispy.
1. Serve immediately with fresh toppings.

---

## Empanadas
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1 cup unsalted butter, cold and cubed
- 1 large egg
- 1/2 cup ice water
- 1 tbsp white vinegar
- 1 lb ground beef
- 1 yellow onion, finely chopped
- 1 bell pepper, finely chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp smoked paprika, 1/2 tsp dried oregano
- 2 cups shredded cheese (Monterey Jack or Mozzarella)
- Egg wash (1 egg beaten with 1 tbsp water)

### Instructions
1. Prepare dough by mixing flour and salt, cutting in butter, then adding whisked egg, water, and vinegar. Knead briefly and refrigerate for 30–60 minutes.
1. Make filling by sautéing onion, pepper, and garlic, then browning the beef. Drain fat and stir in spices. Let cool and stir in cheese.
1. Roll dough to 1/8-inch thickness and cut into 5-6 inch circles.
1. Place 2 tablespoons of filling in the center of each circle, fold into a half-moon, and seal edges with a fork.
1. To Bake: Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Brush with egg wash and bake for 20–25 minutes until golden.
1. To Fry: Heat oil to 350°F (175°C) and fry for 2–3 minutes per side.

---

## Ceviche
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb fresh, sushi-grade white fish (Snapper or Sea Bass), cut into 1/2-inch cubes
- 1 cup fresh lime juice
- 1/2 cup red onion, very thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup tomatoes, diced
- 1 jalapeño or serrano pepper, seeded and minced
- 1 medium avocado, diced
- 1/4 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
- 1/2 tsp sea salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper

### Instructions
1. Place uniform cubes of fish in a non-reactive bowl.
1. Pour lime juice over the fish until submerged. Add sliced red onions and salt.
1. Cover and refrigerate for 30 to 60 minutes until the fish turns opaque.
1. Add diced tomatoes, minced jalapeño, and cilantro. Gently toss.
1. Just before serving, fold in the diced avocado.
1. Serve immediately while very cold with tortilla chips or crackers.

---

## Arepas
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups Masarepa (pre-cooked cornmeal)
- 2 to 2.5 cups warm water
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil or butter

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, combine warm water and salt. Gradually stir in the Masarepa.
1. Let the dough rest for 5 minutes, then knead for a minute until smooth.
1. Divide into 8–10 portions and shape into disks about 1/2 to 3/4 inch thick.
1. Heat a lightly oiled skillet over medium heat and cook arepas for 5–7 minutes per side until golden spots appear.
1. Optional: Finish in a 350°F (175°C) oven for 10 minutes until they sound hollow when tapped.
1. Slice open and fill with cheese, chicken, or beans.

---

## Fried Pickles
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups dill pickle chips, patted dry
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup yellow cornmeal
- 1 tsp garlic powder, 1 tsp smoked paprika, 1/2 tsp onion powder
- 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper, 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 cup buttermilk
- Vegetable oil for frying
- Ranch dressing for dipping

### Instructions
1. Drain pickles and pat them thoroughly dry with paper towels.
1. Mix flour, cornmeal, and spices in one bowl; put buttermilk in a second bowl.
1. Heat oil in a skillet to 375°F (190°C).
1. Dredge pickles in the flour mixture, dip in buttermilk, then coat again in the flour mixture.
1. Fry in batches for 1.5 to 2 minutes per side until golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve hot with ranch.

---

## BBQ Chicken Skewers
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs boneless, skinless chicken breasts or thighs, 1-inch cubes
- 2 large bell peppers, 1-inch chunks
- 1 large red onion, 1-inch chunks
- 1 cup BBQ sauce
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 10–12 wooden or metal skewers

### Instructions
1. If using wooden skewers, soak in water for at least 30 minutes.
1. Marinate chicken cubes in 1/2 cup BBQ sauce, olive oil, garlic, paprika, salt, and pepper for 15–30 minutes.
1. Thread chicken and vegetables onto skewers, alternating pieces.
1. Heat grill to medium-high (400°F / 200°C).
1. Grill skewers for 10–15 minutes, turning every few minutes.
1. Baste with the remaining BBQ sauce during the last 5 minutes of cooking.
1. Cook until chicken internal temperature reaches 165°F (74°C). Let rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Hummus
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 (15 oz) can chickpeas, drained and rinsed
- 1/4 cup tahini
- 1/4 cup fresh lemon juice
- 1 small garlic clove, minced
- 2 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 1/2 tsp ground cumin
- 1/2 to 1 tsp salt (to taste)
- 2-3 tbsp cold water
- Garnish: Paprika, sumac, fresh parsley, and a few whole chickpeas

### Instructions
1. Process tahini and lemon juice in a food processor for 1 minute, scrape sides, and process for 30 seconds more.
1. Add olive oil, minced garlic, cumin, and salt. Process for 30 seconds.
1. Add half the chickpeas and process for 1 minute. Add remaining chickpeas and process until thick and smooth.
1. If too thick, drizzle in cold water while the processor is running until reaching desired consistency.
1. Transfer to a bowl, drizzle with olive oil, and garnish with paprika, parsley, and reserved chickpeas.

---

## Baba Ganoush
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 medium eggplants (about 2 lbs)
- 1/4 cup tahini
- 3 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 2 garlic cloves, minced
- 2 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 1/2 tsp sea salt
- Optional: 1/2 tsp ground cumin, smoked paprika, fresh parsley

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Prick eggplants with a fork.
1. Roast eggplants for 45-60 minutes until skin is charred and flesh has collapsed.
1. Let cool, then scoop out flesh and discard skin.
1. Drain flesh in a strainer for 10-20 minutes to remove excess liquid.
1. Mash eggplant with a fork (rustic) or pulse in a food processor (smooth) with tahini, lemon juice, garlic, olive oil, and salt.
1. Garnish with olive oil, parsley, and paprika before serving.

---

## Falafel
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup dried chickpeas (soaked 12-24 hours, do NOT use canned)
- 1 cup fresh parsley, roughly chopped
- 1 cup fresh cilantro, roughly chopped
- 1 small onion, chopped
- 3-4 cloves garlic
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- 1.5 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1/2 tsp baking powder
- Neutral oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Drain soaked chickpeas and pat very dry.
1. Pulse chickpeas, herbs, onion, garlic, and spices in a food processor until it reaches a coarse sand consistency.
1. Stir in flour and baking powder. Refrigerate for 30-60 minutes.
1. Form into balls or small patties using about 2 tablespoons of mixture each.
1. Fry in 350°F (175°C) oil for 3-4 minutes until deep golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve warm.

---

## Tabbouleh
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2-3 large bunches fresh parsley (about 3 cups minced)
- 1/4 cup fine bulgur (#1 grade)
- 3 medium firm tomatoes, finely diced
- 3-4 green onions, finely chopped
- 1/4 cup fresh mint leaves, finely chopped
- 1/2 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1/4 to 1/3 cup fresh lemon juice
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- Optional: Pinch of allspice or Lebanese 7-Spice

### Instructions
1. Soak bulgur in lemon juice for 15-20 minutes until softened.
1. Finely mince parsley by hand with a sharp knife (avoid food processor).
1. Combine minced parsley, mint, green onions, and diced tomatoes in a large bowl.
1. Add soaked bulgur (with any remaining lemon juice), olive oil, salt, and pepper.
1. Toss gently and refrigerate for at least 30 minutes before serving to let flavors meld.

---

## Fattoush Salad
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1-2 large pita pockets, torn into 1-inch pieces
- 1 head Romaine lettuce, chopped
- 3 Persian cucumbers, sliced
- 1 cup cherry tomatoes, halved
- 4-5 radishes, thinly sliced
- 1/2 red onion, thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- 1/4 cup fresh mint, chopped
- Dressing: 1/3 cup olive oil, 3 tbsp lemon juice, 1-2 tsp pomegranate molasses, 1-2 cloves garlic (minced), 1 tbsp sumac, salt and pepper

### Instructions
1. Toast pita pieces at 375°F (190°C) with olive oil and salt for 5-10 minutes until crispy.
1. Whisk dressing ingredients (olive oil, lemon juice, molasses, garlic, sumac, salt, pepper) in a small bowl.
1. Combine lettuce, cucumbers, tomatoes, radishes, onion, and herbs in a large bowl.
1. Add half the pita chips and the dressing just before serving. Toss gently.
1. Top with remaining pita chips and an extra sprinkle of sumac.

---

## Kibbeh
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- Shell: 2 cups fine bulgur, 1 lb very lean ground beef/lamb, 1 grated onion, 1.5 tsp 7-spice, 1 tsp salt
- Filling: 1 lb ground beef/lamb, 1 diced onion, 1/4 cup toasted pine nuts, 1 tsp 7-spice, salt and pepper, 2 tbsp olive oil
- Neutral oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Soak bulgur for 20 minutes, then squeeze out all water.
1. Make filling: Sauté onions, brown meat, stir in spices and pine nuts. Let cool.
1. Make shell: Process onion into paste, add meat and spices, pulse until smooth. Knead in bulgur.
1. Form: Take egg-sized dough ball, hollow it out with finger, stuff with filling, and seal into football shape.
1. Fry in 350°F (175°C) oil for 3-5 minutes until deep golden brown.
1. Serve warm with yogurt or tahini sauce.

---

## Shawarma Bites
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb chicken breast or thighs, 1/2-inch cubes
- Marinade: 2 tbsp olive oil, 1 tbsp lemon juice, 3 cloves garlic, 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp paprika, 1/2 tsp turmeric/cinnamon/salt
- Wraps: 3-4 large tortillas or lavash bread
- Sauce: 1/2 cup Greek yogurt, 1 tbsp tahini, 1 tsp lemon juice, 1 clove garlic
- Vegetables: Chopped cucumber, tomato, red onion, parsley, pickles

### Instructions
1. Marinate chicken cubes for at least 30 minutes.
1. Cook chicken in a skillet over medium-high heat for 8-10 minutes until browned and cooked through.
1. Spread sauce on tortilla, add chicken and chopped vegetables.
1. Roll up tightly and toast in a dry pan for 1-2 minutes per side until crispy.
1. Slice rolls into 1.5-inch 'sushi-style' bites and serve with extra sauce.

## Stuffed Grape Leaves
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 jar (16 oz) grape leaves, rinsed
- Filling: 1 lb ground beef/lamb, 1 cup uncooked short-grain rice, 1 minced onion, 1/2 cup parsley, 2 tbsp mint, 1 tsp salt, spices (allspice, cinnamon, pepper)
- Cooking: 2 cups broth, 1/2 cup lemon juice, 1/4 cup olive oil
- Base: Sliced potatoes or tomatoes

### Instructions
1. Mix filling ingredients (meat, rice, onion, herbs, spices, olive oil) in a bowl.
1. Place leaf flat (vein-side up), add 1 tbsp filling, and roll tightly like a small burrito.
1. Line pot bottom with potato/tomato slices and pack rolls tightly, seam-side down.
1. Add broth, lemon juice, and olive oil. Place a heavy plate on top to keep rolls submerged.
1. Simmer on low for 45-60 minutes until rice is tender. Rest for 20 minutes before serving.

## Labneh Dip
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup labneh (strained yogurt)
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 1 tbsp fresh dill or mint, chopped
- 1/2 tsp salt, 1/4 tsp pepper
- Toppings: Extra virgin olive oil, za'atar, red pepper flakes

### Instructions
1. Whisk together labneh, garlic, lemon juice, and fresh herbs in a bowl.
1. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
1. Spread into a shallow bowl, creating swirls with a spoon.
1. Drizzle generously with olive oil and sprinkle with za'atar and red pepper flakes.
1. Serve with warm pita or fresh vegetables.

## Pita with Dips
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- Pita Chips: 4 large pitas, 3 tbsp olive oil, 1 tsp garlic powder, 1/2 tsp salt
- Hummus: 1 can chickpeas, 1/4 cup tahini, 2 tbsp lemon juice, 1 clove garlic, 2 tbsp olive oil, 1/2 tsp cumin
- Tzatziki: 1 cup Greek yogurt, 1/2 grated cucumber (squeezed dry), 1 tbsp lemon juice, 1 clove garlic, 1 tbsp dill

### Instructions
1. Chips: Cut pitas into wedges, toss with oil/spices, and bake at 375°F for 8-12 minutes.
1. Hummus: Blend all ingredients in a food processor until smooth, adding water or chickpea liquid for consistency.
1. Tzatziki: Squeeze liquid from grated cucumber. Mix with yogurt, lemon, garlic, oil, and dill. Chill before serving.
1. Arrange chips on a platter with bowls of hummus and tzatziki.
