## Harira Soup
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1 large yellow onion, finely diced
- 2 stalks celery (with leaves), chopped small
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 lb lamb or beef, cut into 1/2-inch cubes (optional)
- 1 1/2 tsp ground ginger
- 1 tsp ground turmeric
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp paprika (sweet or smoked)
- 1/2 tsp ground cinnamon (or 1 cinnamon stick)
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)
- A pinch of saffron threads (optional)
- 1-2 tsp sea salt (to taste)
- 6 cups vegetable or chicken broth
- 1 (28 oz) can crushed tomatoes (or 2 lbs fresh, pureed)
- 1/2 cup dried red lentils, rinsed
- 1/2 cup dried green or brown lentils, rinsed
- 1 (15 oz) can chickpeas, drained and rinsed
- 1/2 cup dried vermicelli noodles (broken) or orzo
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
- 1/2 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- 1 lemon, juiced (plus wedges for serving)
- 1-2 tsp honey (optional)

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a large pot. Brown the meat if using, then set aside. Sauté onion and celery for 5-7 minutes until softened. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in ginger, turmeric, cumin, paprika, cinnamon, pepper, and cayenne. Cook for 1 minute until fragrant.
1. Add broth, tomatoes, lentils, and the browned meat. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low. Cover and simmer for 30-40 minutes until lentils are tender.
1. Stir in chickpeas and vermicelli (or orzo). Cook for 10 more minutes until pasta is al dente.
1. Stir in lemon juice, honey (if using), and half of the fresh cilantro and parsley. Adjust salt to taste.
1. Serve hot in bowls, garnished with remaining fresh herbs and lemon wedges. Traditionally served with dates.

---

## Samosa (African)
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) ground beef or lamb
- 2 medium red onions, finely diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- 1 tsp garam masala
- 1/2 tsp turmeric
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- Salt to taste
- 1-2 green chilies, finely minced
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro, finely chopped
- 1/2 cup frozen peas (optional)
- 2 cups all-purpose flour (for pastry)
- 1/2 tsp salt (for pastry)
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil (for pastry)
- 3/4 cup warm water (for pastry)
- Vegetable oil for deep frying
- 2 tbsp flour mixed with water (sealing paste)

### Instructions
1. Brown the ground meat in a skillet, breaking it into fine crumbles. Drain excess fat.
1. Add onions, garlic, ginger, and chilies. Sauté for 3-5 minutes until onions are translucent.
1. Stir in cumin, coriander, garam masala, turmeric, salt, and pepper. Cook for 2 minutes until fragrant.
1. Remove from heat, stir in cilantro and peas. Let the filling cool completely.
1. For the pastry: Mix flour, salt, oil, and water into a smooth dough. Rest for 20 minutes. Roll thin, lightly toast on a dry pan, and cut into strips.
1. Fold a strip into a cone, fill with 1-2 tbsp of mixture, and seal with the flour-water paste.
1. Deep fry in oil at 350°F (180°C) for 3-5 minutes until golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve hot with fresh lime wedges.

---

## Suya
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) Beef (Sirloin, Flank, or Topside)
- 1 cup Roasted Peanuts, finely ground
- 1 tbsp Ginger powder
- 1 tbsp Garlic powder
- 1 tbsp Onion powder
- 2-3 tbsp Cayenne pepper
- 1 tbsp Smoked paprika
- 2 Bouillon cubes (crushed)
- 1 tsp Salt
- Vegetable oil for brushing
- Bamboo or metal skewers

### Instructions
1. Slice the beef against the grain into very thin, wide fillets (about 1/8 inch thick).
1. Mix ground peanuts, ginger, garlic, onion powder, cayenne, paprika, bouillon, and salt to make the Yaji (Suya spice).
1. Thread the beef strips onto soaked skewers in a zigzag fashion.
1. Brush meat with oil, then coat heavily with the Yaji spice mix, pressing it into the meat.
1. Marinate for at least 30 minutes.
1. Grill over medium-high heat for 15-20 minutes, turning frequently, or bake at 400°F (200°C) for 15-20 minutes.
1. Brush with oil and sprinkle extra spice 5 minutes before finishing.
1. Serve with sliced red onions, tomatoes, and extra Yaji spice.

---

## Mandazi
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 4 cups All-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup Sugar
- 2 tbsp Baking powder
- 1/2 tsp Salt
- 1 tsp Ground cardamom
- 1 Egg, lightly beaten
- 1 tbsp Butter or margarine, melted
- 1 to 1 1/2 cups Warm milk or coconut milk
- Vegetable oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Whisk together flour, sugar, baking powder, salt, and cardamom in a large bowl.
1. Mix the egg, melted butter, and 1 cup of warm milk in a separate bowl.
1. Combine wet and dry ingredients. Gradually add more milk if needed to form a soft, smooth, non-sticky dough.
1. Knead the dough for 5-10 minutes until smooth and elastic.
1. Cover and let the dough rest for 30-60 minutes.
1. Divide dough into portions, roll to 1/2 inch thick, and cut into triangles or squares.
1. Deep fry in oil at 350°F (180°C) for 2-3 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve warm with tea or coffee.

---

## Kofta Balls
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) Ground beef or lamb
- 1 small onion, grated or finely minced
- 2-3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup fresh parsley, finely chopped
- 3 tbsp breadcrumbs
- 1 large egg
- 1 tbsp Baharat (or 1 tsp cumin, 1/2 tsp coriander, 1/2 tsp cinnamon, 1/2 tsp allspice)
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 425°F (220°C) and grease a baking sheet.
1. In a bowl, combine meat, onion, garlic, parsley, breadcrumbs, egg, and all spices. Mix until just combined.
1. Shape into balls about the size of a golf ball (should make 16-20).
1. Place on baking sheet and bake for 12-15 minutes until browned and cooked through (160°F internal).
1. Let rest for 5 minutes before serving.
1. Serve with pita bread, hummus, or a fresh salad.

---

## Lentil Soup
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 1 1/2 cups Red split lentils, rinsed
- 1 large onion, diced
- 1-2 carrots, diced
- 1 medium potato, diced (optional)
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1 1/2 tsp ground cumin
- 1/2 tsp ground turmeric
- 6-8 cups vegetable or chicken broth
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Juice of 1 lemon
- Fresh parsley, chopped for garnish

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a large pot. Sauté onion, carrots, and potato for 5-7 minutes until softened.
1. Stir in garlic, cumin, and turmeric. Cook for 1 minute until fragrant.
1. Add rinsed lentils and broth. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low.
1. Cover and simmer for 20-30 minutes until lentils and vegetables are tender.
1. Optional: Use an immersion blender to puree the soup until smooth.
1. Stir in lemon juice, salt, and pepper. Adjust consistency with water if too thick.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve with warm pita or lemon wedges.

---

## Sambousek
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 3 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 cup vegetable or olive oil
- 3/4 to 1 cup warm water
- 1 lb (500g) ground beef or lamb
- 1 large onion, finely chopped
- 1/4 cup pine nuts, toasted
- 1 tsp Lebanese Seven Spices (or allspice/cinnamon mix)
- 1 tbsp pomegranate molasses (optional)
- Vegetable oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Prepare dough: Mix flour and salt, rub in oil, then gradually add water while kneading until smooth. Rest for 30 minutes.
1. Prepare filling: Sauté pine nuts until golden, set aside. Cook onion until translucent, then add meat and cook until browned.
1. Stir in spices, salt, and pomegranate molasses. Let filling cool completely before adding pine nuts.
1. Roll out dough very thin (1/8 inch) and cut into 3-4 inch circles.
1. Place 1 tbsp of filling in center, fold into a half-moon, and seal edges by pinching or using a fork.
1. Deep fry in oil at 350°F (175°C) for 2-4 minutes until golden and bubbly.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve warm.

---

## Mutabbaq
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 1 1/2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup whole wheat flour (optional)
- 1 tsp salt
- 4 tbsp cooking oil
- 1/2 cup lukewarm water
- 500g minced beef, chicken, or lamb
- 5 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 medium onion, finely diced
- 1 medium tomato, diced
- 1 cup spring onions or leeks, finely chopped
- 2-3 large eggs
- 1 tsp cumin, 1/2 tsp turmeric, 1 tbsp coriander powder
- 1/2 tsp black pepper, 1/2 tsp red chili powder, salt to taste

### Instructions
1. Dough: Mix flours and salt, rub in oil, and gradually add water while kneading for 10 minutes. Divide into 6 balls, coat with oil, and rest for 30-60 minutes.
1. Filling: Sauté garlic and onions, add meat and spices. Cook until browned and dry. Add tomatoes, cook 2 minutes, then let cool completely.
1. Assembly: Whisk eggs, mix with cooled meat and spring onions. Roll dough ball until translucent thin. Place filling in center.
1. Fold dough edges over the filling to form a square pocket.
1. Fry on a lightly oiled griddle over medium-low heat for 3-4 minutes per side until golden and the egg inside is cooked.
1. Serve hot, cut into squares, with lemon wedges and green chilies.

---

## Spicy Chickpeas
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 2 cans (15 oz each) chickpeas, drained and rinsed
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 1 medium yellow onion, diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 can (15 oz) fire-roasted diced tomatoes
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/2 cup vegetable broth or water
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp chili powder (or 1/2 tsp cayenne)
- 1/2 tsp ground turmeric
- 1/2 tsp ground coriander
- 1 tbsp lemon juice
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Fresh cilantro or parsley for garnish

### Instructions
1. Sauté onion in olive oil until softened (5 minutes). Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in tomato paste and all spices (paprika, cumin, chili, turmeric, coriander). Cook for 1-2 minutes.
1. Add chickpeas, diced tomatoes, and broth. Bring to a simmer.
1. Reduce heat and cook for 10-15 minutes until sauce thickens.
1. Stir in lemon juice and season with salt and pepper.
1. Serve hot, garnished with fresh herbs, as a side or over couscous.

---

## Zaalouk
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx (Enriched via Web Search)

### Ingredients
- 1 large globe eggplant (approx 1 lb), cubed
- 3-4 large ripe tomatoes, grated or diced
- 3-4 cloves garlic, minced
- 3 tbsp extra virgin olive oil
- 2 tsp paprika
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1/2 tsp salt, 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, finely chopped
- 1/4 cup fresh cilantro, finely chopped
- Juice of 1/2 lemon or 1 tsp white vinegar

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a skillet. Add cubed eggplant and 1/4 cup water. Cover and cook for 10-15 minutes until soft.
1. Add tomatoes, garlic, paprika, cumin, salt, and pepper.
1. Simmer uncovered for 10-15 minutes, mashing the eggplant and tomatoes with a spoon into a jam-like consistency.
1. Once thickened and liquid has evaporated, stir in fresh herbs and lemon juice.
1. Cook for 1-2 more minutes, then transfer to a bowl.
1. Serve warm or at room temperature, drizzled with olive oil, with crusty bread.

---

## Mini Meat Pies
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g (1.1 lb) Lean ground beef (mince)
- 1 Small brown onion, finely diced
- 1 tbsp Vegetable oil
- ¾ cup Beef stock
- ¼ cup Tomato sauce (ketchup)
- 2 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tbsp Cornflour (cornstarch) mixed with 2 tbsp water
- Salt and pepper to taste
- 2 sheets Frozen shortcrust pastry, thawed (for the bases)
- 2 sheets Frozen puff pastry, thawed (for the lids)
- 1 Egg, lightly beaten (for egg wash)

### Instructions
1. Sauté: Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Add the onion and cook until softened (about 3 minutes).
1. Brown the Meat: Add the ground beef and cook, breaking it up with a wooden spoon, until browned. Drain any excess fat.
1. Simmer: Stir in the beef stock, tomato sauce, and Worcestershire sauce. Season with salt and pepper. Bring to a simmer for 5–10 minutes.
1. Thicken: Stir in the cornflour slurry. Continue to simmer for 1–2 minutes until the sauce is thick and glossy.
1. Cool: Remove from heat and let the filling cool completely.
1. Preheat: Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F). Grease a 12-hole muffin tin or mini pie moulds.
1. Cut the Bases: Use a round cutter to cut 12 circles from shortcrust pastry and press them into the tin.
1. Fill: Spoon the cooled meat mixture into each pastry case until nearly full.
1. Cut the Lids: Use a slightly smaller round cutter to cut 12 circles from puff pastry.
1. Seal: Place puff pastry lids over the filling and press the edges together to seal.
1. Bake: Brush with egg wash, poke a vent hole, and bake for 15–20 minutes until golden brown.

---

## Prawn Skewers
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 ½ pounds extra-large prawns, peeled and deveined
- ¼ cup olive oil
- 1 lemon, zested and juiced
- 3 garlic cloves, minced
- 1 tsp kosher salt
- ¼ tsp ground black pepper
- ¼ tsp crushed red pepper flakes (optional)
- Fresh parsley (chopped), for garnish
- Extra lemon wedges, for serving

### Instructions
1. Prepare Skewers: If using wooden skewers, soak them in water for at least 15–30 minutes.
1. Make Marinade: In a large bowl, whisk together olive oil, lemon zest, juice, garlic, salt, pepper, and red pepper flakes.
1. Marinate: Add prawns to the marinade and toss well. Refrigerate for 15 minutes.
1. Thread: Remove prawns from marinade and thread 4 to 5 onto each skewer.
1. Grill: Preheat grill or grill pan to medium-high. Cook for 2–3 minutes per side until bright pink and opaque.
1. Serve: Garnish with fresh parsley and a squeeze of lemon. Serve immediately.

---

## Fish Cakes
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) white fish fillets (cod, haddock, or pollock), cooked and flaked
- 2 large potatoes (about 2 cups), boiled and mashed
- 1 large egg, lightly beaten
- 2 green onions, finely sliced
- 3 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped
- 1 tsp sea salt
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- ½ tsp dry mustard or Old Bay seasoning (optional)
- 1 cup Panko breadcrumbs
- 2–3 tbsp vegetable or olive oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Combine: In a large bowl, mix mashed potatoes, flaked fish, egg, green onions, parsley, and seasonings.
1. Shape: Divide the mixture into 8 equal portions. Shape each into a patty about 1 inch thick.
1. Coat: Press each patty into Panko breadcrumbs, coating both sides evenly.
1. Chill: Refrigerate the patties for 30 minutes to help them firm up before frying.
1. Fry: Heat oil in a large non-stick skillet over medium heat. Fry for 3–4 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Serve: Serve hot with tartar sauce and lemon wedges.

---

## Sweet Potato Fries
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs sweet potatoes (3–4 medium)
- 2 tablespoons olive, avocado, or canola oil
- 1 tablespoon cornstarch (optional, for extra crispiness)
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1/2 teaspoon garlic powder
- 1/2 teaspoon smoked paprika
- 1/4 teaspoon black pepper

### Instructions
1. Prep: Preheat oven to 425°F (220°C). Peel and cut sweet potatoes into 1/4 to 1/2 inch matchsticks.
1. Soak: Soak cut fries in cold water for 30 minutes, then drain and pat completely dry.
1. Coat: Toss dried fries with cornstarch, then add oil and spices and toss again to coat.
1. Arrange: Spread fries in a single layer on a parchment-lined baking sheet, ensuring they do not touch.
1. Bake: Bake for 25–30 minutes, flipping halfway through, until edges are browned and centers are tender.
1. Rest: Let fries rest for 5 minutes before serving to help them firm up.

---

## Avocado Toast Bites
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 whole grain baguette, sliced into rounds
- 4 large ripe avocados
- 1 tablespoon lime or lemon juice
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Optional Toppings: Everything bagel seasoning, red pepper flakes, crumbled feta, chopped walnuts, or cherry tomatoes

### Instructions
1. Toast: Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Bake baguette slices for 7–10 minutes until golden and crisp.
1. Prepare Avocado: Mash avocado with lime juice, salt, and pepper until creamy but slightly chunky.
1. Assemble: Spread a generous spoonful of avocado onto each toasted baguette slice.
1. Garnish: Top with your chosen ingredients (e.g., feta, walnuts, or seasoning).
1. Serve: Arrange on a platter and serve immediately.

---

## Sushi Rolls
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 cups Japanese short-grain sushi rice
- 2 cups water
- 4 tbsp rice vinegar
- 2 tbsp sugar
- 1 tsp salt
- 4–6 sheets nori (toasted seaweed)
- Fillings: 1 cucumber (julienned), 1 avocado (sliced), 1/2 lb imitation crab or fish
- For serving: Soy sauce, wasabi, pickled ginger

### Instructions
1. Rice: Rinse rice until water runs clear. Cook with 2 cups water, then let sit for 10 minutes.
1. Season: Fold in a mixture of rice vinegar, sugar, and salt into the warm rice. Let cool to room temperature.
1. Prepare Fillings: Slice vegetables and proteins into long, thin strips.
1. Assemble: Place nori on a bamboo mat. Spread rice evenly, leaving a 1-inch border at the top.
1. Roll: Arrange fillings in the center and roll firmly using the mat. Seal the edge with a little water.
1. Slice: Use a sharp, damp knife to slice the roll into 6–8 pieces.

---

## Poke Bowl
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb sushi-grade ahi tuna, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1 tsp grated fresh ginger
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- ¼ cup green onions, sliced
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame seeds
- 2–4 cups cooked sushi rice
- Toppings: Avocado, cucumber, edamame, spicy mayo (mayo, sriracha, lime)

### Instructions
1. Marinate: Whisk soy sauce, vinegar, sesame oil, ginger, and garlic. Toss with tuna and green onions. Refrigerate 15–30 minutes.
1. Sauce: Mix mayonnaise, sriracha, and lime juice for spicy mayo.
1. Assemble: Divide rice into bowls. Top with marinated tuna.
1. Add Toppings: Arrange avocado, cucumber, and edamame around the fish.
1. Serve: Drizzle with spicy mayo and garnish with extra sesame seeds.

---

## Teriyaki Chicken Skewers
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs boneless, skinless chicken thighs, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 bunch scallions (cut into 1-inch pieces) or bell peppers
- 1/2 cup soy sauce
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 1/4 cup water
- 1 tbsp honey
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1 tsp rice vinegar
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, minced
- 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp water

### Instructions
1. Sauce: Simmer soy sauce, sugar, water, honey, sesame oil, vinegar, garlic, and ginger until sugar dissolves.
1. Thicken: Whisk in cornstarch slurry and simmer until thickened. Reserve some sauce for basting.
1. Marinate: Pour cooled sauce over chicken and marinate for 30 minutes.
1. Assemble: Thread chicken and scallions/peppers onto soaked skewers.
1. Cook: Grill for 10–12 minutes, turning occasionally. Baste with reserved sauce in the last 2 minutes.
1. Finish: Cook until chicken reaches 165°F and garnish with sesame seeds.

---

## Fusion Tacos
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs flank steak, thinly sliced
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- 2 tbsp toasted sesame oil
- 2 tbsp brown sugar
- 1 tbsp garlic, minced
- 1 tsp ginger, grated
- 1/2 cup sour cream
- 1–2 tbsp Gochujang (Korean chili paste)
- 12 small tortillas
- Shredded cabbage or kimchi, cilantro, and lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Marinate: Whisk soy sauce, sesame oil, sugar, garlic, and ginger. Marinate beef for 30 minutes.
1. Sauce: Mix sour cream, gochujang, and lime juice.
1. Cook: Sear beef in a hot skillet for 1–2 minutes per side until caramelized.
1. Warm: Briefly heat tortillas in a dry pan.
1. Assemble: Place beef on tortillas, top with cabbage/kimchi and cilantro. Drizzle with sauce.
1. Serve: Serve immediately with lime wedges.

---

## Crispy Calamari
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb cleaned calamari tubes (cut into rings) and tentacles
- ½ cup milk
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 ½ cups all-purpose flour
- 1/3 cup cornstarch
- 1 tsp dried oregano
- ½ tsp black pepper
- ½ tsp cayenne pepper
- Neutral oil for frying
- Lemon wedges and marinara sauce for serving

### Instructions
1. Tenderize: Soak calamari in milk and salt for 30 minutes in the refrigerator.
1. Coating: Whisk together flour, cornstarch, oregano, pepper, and cayenne.
1. Heat Oil: Heat 2–3 inches of oil in a pot to 350°F–375°F.
1. Dredge: Drain calamari and toss in the flour mixture to coat. Shake off excess.
1. Fry: Fry in batches for 2–3 minutes until light golden and crispy.
1. Drain: Transfer to a wire rack and season with salt immediately. Serve with lemon and sauce.

---

## Stuffed Bell Peppers
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 large bell peppers (any color), tops removed and seeds/ribs cleaned out
- 1 lb lean ground beef (or ground turkey/sausage)
- 1 ½ cups cooked white or brown rice
- 1 small yellow onion, diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 can (15 oz) tomato sauce or fire-roasted diced tomatoes
- 1 cup shredded mozzarella or sharp cheddar cheese
- 1 tsp Italian seasoning
- ½ tsp garlic powder
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Fresh parsley for garnish (optional)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
1. Optional: Par-cook peppers by placing them in a baking dish with ¼ cup water, cover with foil, and bake for 10–15 minutes (or boil for 3 minutes).
1. In a large skillet over medium-high heat, brown the ground meat and diced onion until no longer pink. Drain excess grease.
1. Stir in minced garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Add cooked rice, half of the tomato sauce, Italian seasoning, garlic powder, salt, and pepper. Stir until well combined.
1. Stand peppers upright in a baking dish and spoon the filling generously into each.
1. Top each pepper with the remaining tomato sauce.
1. Cover with foil and bake for 25–30 minutes.
1. Remove foil, sprinkle with shredded cheese, and bake for another 5–10 minutes until cheese is melted.
1. Garnish with fresh parsley and serve warm.

---

## Mini Pizza Bites
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 can (16 oz) refrigerated "Grands" size biscuits
- 1 ½ cups shredded mozzarella cheese
- ½ cup diced pepperoni (or sausage, olives, onions)
- 2–3 tbsp olive oil
- ½ tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp Italian seasoning
- Marinara sauce or Ranch dressing for dipping

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease a 12-cup muffin tray.
1. Cut each biscuit into 6 small pieces.
1. In a large bowl, toss biscuit pieces with olive oil, cheese, pepperoni, and seasonings until coated.
1. Divide the mixture equally into the muffin cups.
1. Bake for 15–20 minutes until golden brown and puffy.
1. Let cool for 2 minutes, then remove from pan. Serve warm with dipping sauce.

---

## Spinach Cheese Puffs
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 package (17.3 oz) frozen puff pastry sheets, thawed (2 sheets)
- 1 package (10 oz) frozen chopped spinach, thawed and squeezed very dry
- 4 oz cream cheese, softened
- ½ cup crumbled feta cheese (or shredded mozzarella)
- ¼ cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 1 large egg (for filling)
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- ½ tsp dried dill or oregano (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Egg wash: 1 egg beaten with 1 tbsp water

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Lightly grease a mini muffin tin.
1. Combine squeezed-dry spinach, cream cheese, feta, Parmesan, one egg, minced garlic, and seasonings in a bowl. Mix until creamy.
1. Unfold puff pastry sheets on a floured surface and cut each into 12 equal squares (3x4 grid).
1. Press each pastry square into a cavity of the muffin tin.
1. Spoon about 1 tablespoon of the spinach mixture into the center of each square.
1. Bring the four corners of the pastry together over the filling and pinch firmly to seal.
1. Brush the tops with egg wash.
1. Bake for 18–20 minutes until deep golden brown.
1. Cool in pan for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Baked Brie
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 wheel of Brie (8 oz to 16 oz)
- 2 tbsp honey, maple syrup, or fruit jam (fig, apricot, or raspberry)
- 1 sprig of fresh thyme or rosemary (optional)
- Sliced baguette, sturdy crackers, apple slices, or grapes for serving

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
1. Remove Brie from packaging. Optionally, lightly score the top in a crosshatch pattern.
1. Place Brie in a small, shallow ovenproof dish or on a parchment-lined baking sheet.
1. Bake for 12–15 minutes until the center feels very soft and starts to ooze slightly.
1. Immediately drizzle with honey or jam and sprinkle with fresh herbs.
1. Serve warm with accompaniments.

---

## Crab Cakes
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lump crabmeat, drained and picked for shells
- 1 large egg, lightly beaten
- ¼ cup mayonnaise
- 1 tsp Dijon mustard
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tsp Old Bay seasoning
- ½ cup panko breadcrumbs (or crushed saltine crackers)
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, finely chopped
- 1 tbsp fresh lemon juice
- 2 tbsp butter or neutral oil for frying
- Lemon wedges and tartar sauce for serving

### Instructions
1. Whisk egg, mayonnaise, Dijon mustard, Worcestershire sauce, Old Bay, parsley, and lemon juice in a large bowl.
1. Gently fold in crabmeat and panko breadcrumbs, being careful not to break up large lumps.
1. Shape mixture into 6 to 8 patties (about ½ cup each).
1. Chill patties in the refrigerator for at least 30 minutes to help them stay together.
1. Heat butter or oil in a large non-stick skillet over medium heat.
1. Cook crab cakes for 4–5 minutes per side until golden brown and heated through.
1. Serve immediately with lemon wedges and tartar sauce.

---

## Chicken Satay (Fusion)
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs boneless, skinless chicken thighs or breasts, cut into 1-inch strips
- ¼ cup full-fat coconut milk (for marinade)
- 2 stalks lemongrass, white parts only, minced
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 2 tsp curry powder
- 1 tsp turmeric powder
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- ½ tsp cumin
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp fish sauce
- 1 tbsp brown sugar
- 12–16 wooden skewers, soaked in water for 30 minutes
- Peanut Sauce: ½ cup creamy peanut butter, ½ cup coconut milk, 1 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tbsp lime juice, 1 tsp red curry paste (optional), 1 tbsp honey or brown sugar

### Instructions
1. Whisk together coconut milk, garlic, ginger, lemongrass, spices, soy sauce, fish sauce, and sugar in a large bowl.
1. Add chicken, toss to coat, and marinate for at least 1 hour (ideally 4–6 hours).
1. Thread marinated chicken onto pre-soaked skewers in a zigzag pattern.
1. Preheat grill or grill pan to medium-high and lightly oil the grates.
1. Grill skewers for 3–5 minutes per side until charred and cooked through (165°F/74°C).
1. To make sauce: Combine all peanut sauce ingredients in a small saucepan over low heat. Whisk until smooth and thickened.
1. Serve skewers warm with peanut sauce.

---

## Zucchini Fritters
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (about 2 medium) zucchini, grated
- 1 tsp salt (divided)
- ½ cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- ½ cup grated Parmesan or shredded Cheddar
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley or chives, finely chopped
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- 2–3 tbsp olive oil or vegetable oil for frying
- Sour cream or Greek yogurt for serving

### Instructions
1. Toss grated zucchini with ½ tsp salt in a colander; let sit for 10–15 minutes.
1. Squeeze zucchini in a clean towel or cheesecloth until very dry.
1. In a large bowl, combine eggs, flour, cheese, garlic, herbs, pepper, and remaining ½ tsp salt.
1. Stir in dried zucchini until well combined.
1. Heat oil in a large non-stick skillet over medium heat.
1. Drop 2 tablespoons of batter per fritter and flatten slightly.
1. Fry for 3–4 minutes per side until golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve warm with dipping sauce.

---

## Eggplant Parmesan Bites
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 medium eggplants, peeled and cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 3 large eggs, beaten with 2 tbsp water
- 2 cups Italian-style breadcrumbs
- ¾ cup grated Parmesan cheese
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Vegetable or canola oil for frying
- 1 cup marinara sauce, warmed, for dipping
- Fresh parsley, chopped, for garnish

### Instructions
1. Toss eggplant cubes with 1½ tsp salt in a colander; let sit for 30 minutes. Pat thoroughly dry.
1. Set up three bowls: 1) Flour with salt and pepper, 2) Beaten eggs, 3) Breadcrumbs mixed with Parmesan.
1. Coat each eggplant cube in flour, dip in egg wash, then roll in breadcrumb mixture.
1. Heat 3 inches of oil to 350°F (175°C) in a heavy pot.
1. Fry breaded cubes in batches for 5–8 minutes until golden and crispy.
1. Transfer to a paper towel-lined plate and sprinkle with salt.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve with warm marinara sauce.

---

## Tuna Tartare
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb sushi-grade tuna fillet, cut into ¼-inch cubes
- 1 ripe avocado, diced (optional)
- 1 ½ tbsp soy sauce
- 1 ½ tbsp Asian sesame oil
- 2 ¼ tsp fresh lime juice
- ¾ tsp fresh ginger, minced
- 1 jalapeño, finely minced
- 1 tsp Sriracha (optional)
- 2 tsp toasted sesame seeds
- 8 fresh chives, finely chopped
- Wonton chips or crackers for serving

### Instructions
1. Cut the tuna into uniform ¼-inch cubes (freezing for 15 minutes first helps).
1. In a medium bowl, whisk together soy sauce, sesame oil, lime juice, ginger, and jalapeño.
1. Gently fold diced tuna into the dressing until coated.
1. If using avocado, fold it in gently just before serving.
1. Serve immediately or refrigerate for up to 1 hour.
1. Garnish with toasted sesame seeds and chives. Serve chilled with chips.

---

## Stuffed Jalapeños
- **Source:** 100_starter_dishes_final.docx

### Ingredients
- 12 large jalapeño peppers, halved lengthwise, seeds and membranes removed
- 8 oz cream cheese, softened
- 1 cup sharp cheddar cheese, shredded
- ½ tsp garlic powder
- ¼ tsp smoked paprika (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 12 slices of bacon, cut in half crosswise
- Toothpicks (optional)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Line a baking sheet with parchment paper.
1. Slice jalapeños in half lengthwise and remove seeds/membranes (wear gloves!).
1. Mix cream cheese, cheddar, garlic powder, paprika, salt, and pepper in a bowl until smooth.
1. Fill each jalapeño half with about 1–2 tablespoons of the cheese mixture.
1. Wrap one half-slice of bacon around each pepper and secure with a toothpick if needed.
1. Place on baking sheet cheese-side up.
1. Bake for 18–22 minutes until bacon is crispy and cheese is bubbly.
1. Let cool for 5 minutes before serving.

---

# Category: Pork Dishes

## Crispy Pork Belly
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 6-8 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lb (1 kg) slab of skin-on pork belly
- 1 tbsp white vinegar (for the skin)
- 1/2 lb (200g) rock salt (for the salt crust)
- 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine (Chinese cooking wine)
- 1 tsp Chinese five-spice powder
- 1 tsp sea salt
- 1/2 tsp ground white pepper

### Instructions
1. Prick hundreds of tiny holes all over the pork skin using a sharp skewer or meat tenderizer, being careful not to pierce the fat or meat.
1. Flip the pork and rub the meat side with Shaoxing wine, five-spice powder, sea salt, and white pepper.
1. Place the pork on a plate, skin-side up, and refrigerate uncovered for at least 12 hours to air-dry the skin.
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (180°C). Create a foil 'box' around the pork, leaving only the skin exposed.
1. Brush the skin with white vinegar and cover with a 1/4-inch layer of rock salt.
1. Roast for 60 minutes. Remove from oven and discard the hardened salt crust.
1. Increase oven temperature to 450°F (230°C) or turn on the broiler.
1. Place pork on a wire rack and roast/broil for 15-25 minutes until the skin is bubbled and crispy.
1. Rest for 15 minutes before slicing skin-side down.

---

## Tonkatsu
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 boneless pork chops (loin or rib-end), 3/4 to 1 inch thick
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1 cup Panko (Japanese breadcrumbs)
- Neutral oil for deep-frying
- For sauce: 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce, 1/2 tbsp ketchup, 1/2 tbsp soy sauce, pinch of sugar

### Instructions
1. Pound pork chops to an even 1/2-inch thickness. Score the connective tissue between meat and fat to prevent curling.
1. Season both sides with salt and pepper.
1. Dredge the pork in flour, shaking off excess.
1. Dip into the beaten egg, then press firmly into the Panko to coat evenly.
1. Heat oil to 340°F-350°F (170°C-180°C).
1. Fry for 3-4 minutes per side until deep golden brown.
1. Drain on a wire rack for 1-2 minutes, then slice into strips.
1. Whisk sauce ingredients together and serve with shredded cabbage and lemon.

---

## Pork Schnitzel
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 boneless pork loin chops or steaks (6 oz each)
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1 cup breadcrumbs (plain or Panko)
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp freshly ground black pepper
- 1/2 cup neutral oil for frying
- Lemon wedges and fresh parsley for serving

### Instructions
1. Place each pork chop between plastic wrap and pound to 1/4 inch thickness.
1. Season both sides with salt and pepper.
1. Prepare three bowls: flour with salt, beaten eggs, and breadcrumbs.
1. Dredge each cutlet in flour, then egg, then breadcrumbs.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Fry cutlets in batches for 2-3 minutes per side until golden brown and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve immediately with fresh lemon juice.

---

## Pork Nuggets
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 6 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 to 2 lbs pork loin or tenderloin, cut into bite-sized pieces
- 1.5 cups crushed cheese crackers (e.g., Cheez-Its) or corn flakes
- 4 eggs whisked with 1/4 cup water or buttermilk
- Salt, pepper, garlic powder, and smoked paprika to taste
- Vegetable or canola oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Prepare crumbs by pulsing crackers or corn flakes in a food processor until fine.
1. Season pork pieces with salt, pepper, and desired spices.
1. Dip each piece into the egg mixture, then roll in the crumbs until fully coated.
1. To fry: Heat 1.5 inches of oil to 350°F and fry for about 3 minutes until internal temperature is 145°F.
1. To air fry: Cook at 375°F for 6-8 minutes.
1. To bake: Cook at 400°F on a parchment-lined sheet for 10-12 minutes.
1. Serve warm with dipping sauces like BBQ or honey mustard.

---

## Breaded Pork Chops
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 boneless or bone-in pork loin chops, 1-inch thick
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, beaten with 1 tbsp water
- 1 1/2 cups seasoned breadcrumbs
- 1 tsp garlic powder, 1/2 tsp onion powder, 1/2 tsp paprika
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 3-4 tbsp vegetable or canola oil

### Instructions
1. Pat pork chops dry and season with salt and pepper.
1. Mix flour with garlic powder, onion powder, and paprika in a shallow bowl.
1. Set up breading station: flour mixture, egg wash, and breadcrumbs.
1. Dredge each chop in flour, dip in egg wash, and coat thoroughly with breadcrumbs.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Fry for 4-6 minutes per side until golden brown and internal temperature is 145°F (63°C).
1. Rest for 3-5 minutes before serving.

---

## Chicharrón
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 6-8 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 to 4 lbs skin-on pork belly, cut into 1-inch strips or 1.5-inch cubes
- 4-6 cups water
- 1 tbsp kosher salt
- 3 cloves garlic (smashed) and 2 bay leaves
- 1 tsp baking soda (optional for extra blistered skin)
- 2 cups pork lard or neutral oil for frying
- Lime wedges and hot sauce for serving

### Instructions
1. Score the skin side of the pork belly in a crosshatch pattern without cutting through to the meat.
1. In a large pot, combine pork, water, salt, garlic, and bay leaves. Bring to a boil, then simmer for 40-50 minutes until water evaporates.
1. Remove pork and pat extremely dry with paper towels.
1. Heat lard or oil in the pot to 375°F (190°C).
1. Carefully fry pork in batches for 10-12 minutes, using a splatter screen, until skin is golden and blistered.
1. Drain on a wire rack and sprinkle with salt immediately.
1. Serve with fresh lime wedges.

---

## Lechon Kawali
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 4-6 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1 kg) pork belly slab (liempo)
- 1 head garlic, crushed
- 1 medium onion, quartered
- 3-5 dried bay leaves
- 1 tbsp whole black peppercorns
- 2 tbsp salt
- 3-4 cups neutral cooking oil
- Extra salt for rubbing

### Instructions
1. Boil pork belly in a pot with enough water to submerge, plus garlic, onion, bay leaves, peppercorns, and salt.
1. Simmer for 45-60 minutes until fork-tender. Drain and pat dry.
1. Rub the skin with extra salt and air-dry (refrigerate uncovered for 3+ hours or use a fan).
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C).
1. Carefully deep-fry the pork (skin side down first) for 7-10 minutes per side until skin is blistered.
1. Rest for 5-10 minutes before slicing. Serve with Lechon sauce or spicy vinegar.

---

## Pork Karaage
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 2 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 200g (7 oz) pork loin or shoulder, bite-sized pieces
- Marinade: 1/2 clove grated garlic, 1/2 knob grated ginger, 1/2 tbsp sake, 1 tsp soy sauce, pinch white pepper
- Coating: 1 beaten egg, 2 tbsp all-purpose flour, 1 tbsp potato starch or cornstarch
- Neutral oil for deep-frying
- Lemon wedges and Japanese mayonnaise for serving

### Instructions
1. Combine pork with marinade ingredients and let sit for 15-30 minutes.
1. Mix flour and starch in a shallow dish.
1. Knead the beaten egg into the marinated pork.
1. Dredge each piece of pork in the flour-starch mixture, shaking off excess.
1. Heat oil to 325°F-350°F (160°C-180°C).
1. Fry in batches for 4-5 minutes until golden brown.
1. Drain on a wire rack and serve hot with lemon.

---

## Pork Milanese
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 boneless pork loin chops (5 oz each)
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, beaten
- 1 1/2 cups Panko or Italian-style breadcrumbs
- 1/2 cup freshly grated Parmesan cheese (optional)
- 1/2 cup olive or vegetable oil
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Arugula salad and lemon wedges for serving

### Instructions
1. Pound pork chops between plastic wrap to 1/4-inch thickness. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Set up breading station: flour, egg wash, and breadcrumbs (mixed with Parmesan if using).
1. Dredge chops in flour, dip in egg, and coat with breadcrumbs.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Fry cutlets for 2-3 minutes per side until deep golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and sprinkle with salt.
1. Serve topped with a light arugula salad and lemon wedges.
