## Crispy Pork Strips
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Pork
- **Original Servings:** 4 servings
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb boneless pork chops or pork tenderloin, cut into 1/2-inch strips
- 1 cup buttermilk
- 2 cups seasoned Italian-style Panko breadcrumbs
- Vegetable or canola oil for frying
- Dipping sauce (e.g., Tonkatsu sauce, ranch, or honey mustard)

### Instructions
1. Soak pork strips in buttermilk for at least 30 minutes in the refrigerator.
1. Take each strip from the buttermilk and coat thoroughly in Panko, pressing to adhere.
1. Heat 1/2 inch of oil in a large frying pan over medium-high heat.
1. Fry in small batches for about 2 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Drain on a wire rack or paper towels.
1. Serve immediately with your favorite dipping sauce.

---

## Pork Sinigang
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 4–6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1kg) Pork (belly, spare ribs, or shoulder), cut into 2-inch cubes
- 8–10 cups Water
- 1 medium Onion, quartered
- 3 medium Tomatoes, quartered
- 2–3 tbsp Fish Sauce (Patis)
- 1 packet (approx. 40g) Tamarind Soup Base Mix or 4–5 tbsp tamarind paste
- 2–3 pieces Taro (Gabi), peeled and quartered
- 1 medium White Radish (Labanos), sliced diagonally
- 1 bunch String Beans (Sitaw), cut into 2-inch lengths
- 1 medium Eggplant, sliced
- 6–8 pieces Okra, ends trimmed
- 2–3 Finger Chilies (Siling Haba), whole
- 1 bunch Kangkong (Water Spinach) or baby spinach/bok choy

### Instructions
1. In a large pot, combine the pork and water. Bring to a boil and skim off any foam.
1. Add the onions, tomatoes, and fish sauce. Lower the heat, cover, and simmer for 30–45 minutes until the pork is tender.
1. Add the taro (gabi) and simmer for about 8–10 minutes until it starts to soften.
1. Stir in the tamarind soup mix or paste. Taste and adjust seasoning.
1. Add the radish and finger chilies; simmer for 2 minutes.
1. Add the string beans, okra, and eggplant; simmer for another 3–5 minutes.
1. Add the kangkong (or spinach), turn off the heat, and cover the pot for 1 minute to let the greens wilt.
1. Serve hot with steamed white rice.

---

## Pork Nilaga
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 4–6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) pork belly, ribs, or shoulder, cut into chunks
- 6–8 cups Water
- 1 medium Onion, quartered
- 1 tbsp whole black peppercorns
- 2 tbsp fish sauce (patis) or salt to taste
- 1 pork bouillon cube (optional)
- 2 medium potatoes, peeled and quartered
- 2 ears of sweet corn, cut into pieces (optional)
- 3–4 saba bananas, halved (optional)
- 1 small head of cabbage, cut into wedges
- 1 bunch of pechay (bok choy), ends trimmed
- 10–12 pieces green beans (optional)

### Instructions
1. In a large pot, combine pork and water. Bring to a boil and skim off the scum.
1. Add onion, peppercorns, and fish sauce. Simmer for 45–60 minutes until pork is tender.
1. Add corn, potatoes, and saba bananas. Cook for 10–12 minutes until potatoes are soft.
1. Add green beans, cabbage, and pechay. Simmer for 2–3 minutes.
1. Season with more fish sauce or salt if needed.
1. Serve hot with steamed rice and a side of fish sauce with calamansi and chili.

---

## Pork Tinola
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 4–6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g to 1kg pork ribs or pork belly, cut into bite-sized pieces
- 2 tbsp ginger, sliced into thin strips
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 3–5 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 large sayote (chayote) or green papaya, cut into wedges
- 1 cup chili leaves (sili leaves) or malunggay (moringa) leaves
- 1 liter water or rice washing
- 2–3 tbsp fish sauce (patis)
- 1 pork or beef broth cube (optional)
- 2 tbsp cooking oil
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a large pot. Sauté ginger, garlic, and onion until fragrant.
1. Add the pork pieces and sauté until lightly browned.
1. Pour in the fish sauce and add black pepper. Stir for 1–2 minutes.
1. Pour in water (or rice washing) and add the broth cube. Bring to a boil, then simmer for 30–40 minutes until pork is tender.
1. Add sayote or green papaya wedges and simmer for 5–8 minutes.
1. Stir in the chili or malunggay leaves, let wilt for 1 minute with heat off.
1. Serve hot with steamed white rice.

---

## Pork Menudo
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 6–8
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork shoulder, cut into small cubes
- 1/4 to 1/2 lb pork liver, cubed (optional)
- 3–4 pieces red hotdogs, sliced (optional)
- 1 large potato, cubed
- 1 medium carrot, cubed
- 1/2 cup raisins
- 1 red bell pepper, diced
- 1 cup chickpeas (garbanzo beans), drained
- 1 cup frozen green peas (optional)
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 3–4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 cup tomato sauce or 2 chopped tomatoes
- 1 cup water or broth
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 2 tbsp lemon or calamansi juice
- 2 dried bay leaves
- 3 tbsp cooking oil
- Salt, pepper, and sugar to taste

### Instructions
1. Marinate pork in soy sauce and lemon juice for 30 minutes.
1. Sauté garlic, onion, and tomatoes in oil until softened.
1. Add marinated pork and brown slightly.
1. Pour in tomato sauce and water. Add bay leaves. Simmer for 40–60 minutes until pork is tender.
1. Add liver and hotdogs. Cook for 5 minutes.
1. Add potatoes, carrots, and raisins. Simmer for 10–15 minutes until tender.
1. Add bell peppers, chickpeas, and green peas. Cook for 3–5 minutes.
1. Season with salt, pepper, and sugar. Serve hot with rice.

---

## Pork Caldereta
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 6–10
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) Pork (ribs, shoulder, or belly), cut into pieces
- 1/3 cup Pineapple juice (optional)
- 2–3 tbsp Soy sauce
- 1 tsp Black pepper
- 1 small can (approx. 85g) Liver spread
- 1 cup Tomato sauce
- 2–3 cups Water or beef broth
- 1 medium Onion, chopped
- 4 cloves Garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp Peanut butter (optional)
- 1 tbsp Fish sauce (patis) or salt to taste
- 2 medium Potatoes, quartered
- 1 medium Carrot, sliced
- 1 Red bell pepper, sliced
- 1 Green bell pepper, sliced
- 2–3 pieces Thai chili (optional)
- 1/2 cup Grated cheese (optional)

### Instructions
1. Marinate pork in pineapple juice, soy sauce, and pepper for 30–60 minutes.
1. Fry potatoes and carrots until edges are brown; set aside.
1. In the same pot, sear the pork until browned; remove and set aside.
1. Sauté garlic and onion. Add liver spread and tomato sauce.
1. Return pork to the pot and add water/marinade. Simmer for 40–50 minutes until tender.
1. Stir in peanut butter and chili peppers. Season with fish sauce.
1. Add fried potatoes, carrots, and bell peppers. Simmer for 5–8 minutes.
1. Top with grated cheese and serve hot with white rice.

---

## Pork Stew
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 ½ lbs Pork Shoulder, cut into 1-inch cubes
- ½ cup All-purpose flour
- 1 tsp Salt & ½ tsp Black pepper
- 2 tbsp Vegetable oil
- 1 large Yellow onion, diced
- 4 cloves Garlic, minced
- 4 cups Chicken or Beef broth
- ½ cup Dry white wine (optional)
- 2 tbsp Tomato paste
- 1 lb Yukon Gold potatoes, cubed
- 4 medium Carrots, sliced
- 2 stalks Celery, sliced
- 1 tsp Dried rosemary
- 1 tsp Dried thyme
- 2 Bay leaves
- 1 cup Frozen peas

### Instructions
1. Dredge pork in flour, salt, and pepper. Brown in oil in a large pot; set aside.
1. Sauté onion and celery for 5 minutes. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Deglaze with wine or broth. Stir in tomato paste, herbs, and bay leaves.
1. Return pork to pot and add broth. Simmer for 60 minutes.
1. Add potatoes and carrots. Simmer for 30–45 minutes until tender.
1. Stir in frozen peas and cook for 5 minutes.
1. Remove bay leaves and adjust seasoning before serving.

---

## Pork Pozole
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 8–10
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 lbs pork shoulder, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 12–14 cups Water
- 1 large white onion, halved
- 6 cloves garlic, peeled
- 2 bay leaves
- 1 tbsp salt
- 4 dried ancho chiles, stems and seeds removed
- 4 dried guajillo chiles, stems and seeds removed
- ½ tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp dried Mexican oregano
- 2 cans (25 oz each) white hominy, drained and rinsed
- Garnishes: Shredded cabbage, sliced radishes, diced onion, cilantro, lime wedges, avocado

### Instructions
1. Simmer pork, water, halved onion, garlic, bay leaves, and salt in a large pot for 1.5 to 2 hours.
1. Toast dried chiles, soak in hot water for 15 minutes, then blend with 1 cup broth, garlic, cumin, and oregano until smooth. Strain the sauce.
1. Remove onion halves and bay leaves from the pot. Add the chile sauce and hominy.
1. Simmer for another 30–45 minutes.
1. Serve in deep bowls and provide garnishes on the side for customization.

---

## Pork Gumbo
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 4–6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 to 1.25 lbs Pork shoulder or tenderloin, cut into cubes
- 1 lb Andouille sausage, sliced
- 1 cup All-purpose flour
- ¾ cup Vegetable oil
- 1.5 cups Yellow onion, chopped
- 1.5 cups Green bell pepper, chopped
- 1.5 cups Celery, chopped
- 3–4 cloves Garlic, minced
- 6 cups Chicken or pork stock
- 1 can (14.5 oz) Diced tomatoes (optional)
- 1 bag (12 oz) Frozen okra, sliced
- 1–2 tbsp Cajun seasoning
- 1 tsp Dried thyme
- 2 Bay leaves

### Instructions
1. Brown pork and sausage in a large pot; set aside.
1. Make a dark roux by whisking flour and oil over medium-low heat for 30–45 minutes until chocolate-colored.
1. Add onion, bell pepper, and celery to the roux. Sauté for 5–8 minutes, then add garlic.
1. Slowly whisk in stock. Add browned meats, tomatoes, seasoning, thyme, and bay leaves.
1. Simmer for 45–60 minutes until pork is tender.
1. Stir in okra and simmer for 15–20 minutes.
1. Remove bay leaves and serve over hot white rice.

---

## Pork Ramen
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork tenderloin, sliced thinly
- 1/2 cup soy sauce
- 1/4 cup water
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp grated ginger
- 1/4 cup creamy peanut butter
- 3 tbsp hoisin sauce
- 2 tbsp honey
- 3 tbsp rice wine vinegar
- 2 tbsp chili paste
- 1 tbsp sesame oil
- 2 tbsp canola oil
- 4 packages (3 oz each) ramen noodles
- Garnishes: Green onions, cilantro, peanuts, lime wedges, soft-boiled eggs

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, water, sesame oil, canola oil, honey, hoisin, peanut butter, vinegar, garlic, ginger, and chili paste.
1. Sear sliced pork in a large skillet until browned and cooked through.
1. Pour the sauce over the pork and stir to coat.
1. Cook ramen noodles in boiling water for 3 minutes; drain.
1. Toss noodles with the pork and sauce in the skillet.
1. Divide into bowls and add desired garnishes.

---

## Pork Pho
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork tenderloin (half sliced thinly, half coarsely chopped)
- 1 lb pork or beef bones (optional)
- 3 garlic cloves, smashed
- 2 medium carrots, chopped
- 2 celery stalks, chopped
- 1 medium yellow onion, chopped
- 1 (2-inch) piece ginger, sliced
- 1 bunch fresh cilantro (stems and leaves separated)
- 1 ½ tsp salt
- 1 dried bay leaf
- ¼ tsp coriander seeds
- 1 star anise
- 10 cups water
- 8 oz dried rice vermicelli noodles
- Garnishes: Lime wedges, bean sprouts, sliced red chiles, hoisin, sriracha

### Instructions
1. Brown bones (if using) in a pot. Sauté garlic, carrots, celery, onion, and ginger.
1. Add chopped pork, cilantro stems, salt, bay leaf, coriander seeds, star anise, and water. Simmer for 1 hour.
1. Strain the broth and discard solids. Bring clear broth back to a boil.
1. Add thinly sliced pork and rice vermicelli; cook for 8–10 minutes until tender.
1. Ladle into bowls and serve with fresh garnishes.

---

## Pork Adobo
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1kg) pork belly or pork shoulder, cut into 1.5-inch cubes
- 1/2 cup soy sauce
- 1/3 cup vinegar (cane or apple cider)
- 6-8 cloves garlic, crushed or minced
- 1 teaspoon whole black peppercorns
- 3-5 dried bay leaves
- 1 to 1 1/2 cups water or beef broth
- 2 tablespoons cooking oil
- 1 teaspoon brown sugar (optional)
- Salt to taste

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a large pot over medium-high heat. Brown the pork cubes on all sides.
1. Add crushed garlic and sauté for 1-2 minutes until fragrant.
1. Pour in soy sauce, water (or broth), peppercorns, and bay leaves. Bring to a boil.
1. Lower heat, cover, and simmer for 40-50 minutes until pork is fork-tender.
1. Add vinegar and let boil for 2-3 minutes without stirring to cook off the raw acidity.
1. Add sugar (if using), stir, and simmer uncovered for 5-10 minutes until sauce reduces to desired thickness.
1. Remove bay leaves and serve hot over steamed white rice.

---

## Sweet and Sour Pork
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) pork loin or tenderloin, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 tbsp soy sauce (for marinade)
- 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine (optional, for marinade)
- 1/2 tsp salt (for marinade)
- 1 egg, beaten
- 1/2 cup cornstarch (for coating)
- Oil for deep frying
- 1 red bell pepper, chunks
- 1 green bell pepper, chunks
- 1 small onion, wedges
- 1 cup pineapple chunks
- 1/2 cup water or pineapple juice
- 1/4 cup white vinegar
- 1/4 cup ketchup
- 1/4 cup sugar
- 1 tbsp soy sauce (for sauce)
- 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 2 tbsp water (slurry)

### Instructions
1. Marinate pork with 1 tbsp soy sauce, wine, and salt for 15-20 minutes.
1. Dip pork in beaten egg, then coat with cornstarch. Deep fry at 350°F (175°C) until golden brown (5-8 mins). Drain and set aside.
1. Whisk water/juice, vinegar, ketchup, sugar, and 1 tbsp soy sauce in a bowl.
1. Stir-fry onion and bell peppers for 2-3 minutes. Add pineapple and toss.
1. Pour sauce mixture into the wok. Stir in cornstarch slurry and simmer until thickened and glossy.
1. Add fried pork back to the wok. Toss quickly to coat and serve immediately.

---

## Pork Teriyaki
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) pork tenderloin or loin, cut into 3/4-inch pieces
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- 2 cups mixed vegetables (bell peppers, snow peas, broccoli, carrots)
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- 2 tbsp brown sugar
- 1 tbsp honey
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar or mirin
- 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp cold water (slurry)
- Sesame seeds and green onions for garnish

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, brown sugar, honey, garlic, ginger, and rice vinegar in a bowl.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a skillet over medium-high heat. Brown pork for 5-7 minutes until it reaches 145°F (63°C). Remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil and stir-fry vegetables for 3-5 minutes until tender-crisp.
1. Return pork to skillet. Pour sauce over the mixture.
1. Stir in cornstarch slurry. Cook for 1-2 minutes until sauce thickens into a glossy glaze.
1. Garnish with sesame seeds and green onions. Serve with rice.

---

## Char Siu
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1 kg) pork shoulder or pork butt, cut into long strips 2 inches thick
- 2 tbsp hoisin sauce
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 2 tbsp honey (plus 1-2 tbsp extra for glaze)
- 2 cubes red fermented bean curd + 1 tbsp liquid (or red food coloring)
- 2 tbsp Shaoxing wine
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 1 tsp Chinese five-spice powder
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1/2 tsp white pepper

### Instructions
1. Whisk marinade ingredients. Marinate pork for 12-48 hours in the refrigerator.
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Line a tray with foil, place a rack on top, and add water to the bottom of the pan.
1. Roast pork on the rack for 20 minutes.
1. Simmer reserved marinade for 3 minutes, then stir in extra honey. Baste pork, flip, and roast for another 15-20 minutes.
1. Broil for 2-4 minutes until edges are charred and sticky (internal temp 145°F).
1. Rest for 10 minutes, then slice against the grain.

---

## Honey Garlic Pork
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 boneless pork chops (1-inch thick)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tbsp butter
- 3-4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup honey
- 1/4 cup apple cider vinegar
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1/4 tsp red pepper flakes (optional)
- Green onions for garnish

### Instructions
1. Season pork chops with salt and pepper.
1. Heat oil and butter in a skillet. Sear pork chops for 4-5 minutes per side until golden and 145°F (63°C). Remove and keep warm.
1. Reduce heat to medium. Sauté garlic in the pan for 30-60 seconds.
1. Whisk in honey, vinegar, soy sauce, and red pepper flakes. Simmer for 3-5 minutes until thickened.
1. Return pork to the pan and spoon glaze over the meat.
1. Garnish with green onions and serve.

---

## Orange Pork
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork shoulder, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 cup cornstarch
- 1 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1 cup brown sugar
- 3/4 cup water
- 1/4 cup cane or apple cider vinegar
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1/4 tsp garlic powder
- 2 cups cooking oil for frying
- Green onions and sesame seeds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Toss pork with salt and pepper. Let rest for 20 minutes.
1. Combine water, vinegar, and soy sauce in a saucepan and boil. Add garlic powder and brown sugar. Simmer until reduced by half.
1. Heat oil. Dredge pork in cornstarch and deep fry for 5-8 minutes until golden and crisp. Drain.
1. Toss fried pork in the glaze until evenly coated.
1. Garnish with green onions and sesame seeds. Serve over rice.

---

## Pork Marsala
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork tenderloin (cut into 1-inch medallions) or 4 boneless chops
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- Salt and black pepper
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 3 tbsp unsalted butter
- 8 oz mushrooms, sliced
- 1 shallot or 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 3/4 cup dry Marsala wine
- 1/2 cup chicken broth
- 1/2 cup heavy cream (optional)
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped

### Instructions
1. Season and dredge pork in flour. Sear in olive oil and 1 tbsp butter for 3-4 minutes per side. Remove and keep warm.
1. Sauté mushrooms in remaining 2 tbsp butter for 5-6 minutes. Add shallot/garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Pour in Marsala and broth, scraping the bottom. Simmer for 3-5 minutes until reduced by half.
1. Stir in heavy cream if using. Simmer for 1 minute.
1. Return pork to skillet and simmer for 1-2 minutes until heated through.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve.

---

## Pork in Black Bean Sauce
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) lean pork, cut into thin strips
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 bell pepper, sliced
- 4-6 green onions, 1-inch pieces
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- 2 tbsp Chinese black bean paste
- 1 tbsp oyster sauce
- 1.5 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tsp sugar
- 1/2 cup chicken stock
- 2 tsp cornstarch

### Instructions
1. Whisk black bean paste, oyster sauce, soy sauce, sugar, stock, and cornstarch.
1. Stir-fry pork in 1 tbsp oil for 3-4 minutes until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Heat remaining oil. Stir-fry garlic, ginger, peppers, and green onions for 2 minutes.
1. Return pork to pan. Pour sauce mixture over ingredients.
1. Cook, stirring constantly, for 1-2 minutes until sauce thickens.
1. Serve immediately over rice or noodles.

---

## Braised Pork Belly
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 - 2 lbs pork belly, 1-inch cubes
- 5-6 slices ginger
- 3 stalks scallions, 2-inch pieces
- 2-3 whole star anise
- 1 small cinnamon stick
- 2 tbsp rock sugar (or brown sugar)
- 3 tbsp light soy sauce
- 1.5 tbsp dark soy sauce
- 2 tbsp Shaoxing wine
- 2-3 cups water
- 1 tbsp oil

### Instructions
1. Blanch pork in boiling water for 3-5 minutes. Drain, rinse, and pat dry.
1. Caramelize sugar in oil over low heat until amber syrup forms.
1. Add pork and stir-fry for 2-3 minutes to coat in caramel.
1. Add ginger, scallions, star anise, cinnamon, wine, and soy sauces.
1. Add water to cover meat. Simmer on low, covered, for 1.5 - 2 hours until tender.
1. Uncover and reduce sauce on medium-high until thick and syrupy.

---

## Pork Kare-Kare
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2.5 lbs (1 kg) pork hock (pata), sliced
- 1/2 cup creamy peanut butter
- 1.5 tbsp annatto seeds (soaked) or powder
- 5 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 1.5 tbsp cornstarch dissolved in 3 tbsp water (slurry)
- 2 eggplants, sliced
- 10-12 string beans, 2-inch pieces
- 1 bunch baby bok choy
- Salt and pepper to taste
- Sautéed shrimp paste (bagoong) for serving

### Instructions
1. Boil pork hock in water with salt for 60-90 minutes until very tender. Reserve 4 cups broth.
1. Sauté garlic and onion in oil. Add tenderized pork and sauté for 2 minutes.
1. Pour in reserved broth and annatto water. Bring to a boil.
1. Stir in peanut butter until dissolved. Simmer for 5-8 minutes.
1. Slowly stir in cornstarch slurry until thickened. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Add eggplant and string beans, cook for 5 minutes. Add bok choy and cook for 2 minutes.
1. Serve hot with steamed rice and shrimp paste on the side.

---

## Pork Fried Rice
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/2 lb pork tenderloin or boneless pork chops, diced into 1/2-inch cubes
- 3 cups cooked long-grain white rice (ideally day-old and cold)
- 2-3 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 2-3 tbsp vegetable, peanut, or grapeseed oil
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated or minced
- 3 green onions (scallions), white and green parts separated and sliced
- 1 cup frozen peas and carrots, thawed
- 3 tbsp soy sauce (low-sodium preferred)
- 1 tbsp oyster sauce (optional)
- 1 tsp toasted sesame oil
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a large skillet or wok over medium-high heat. Season pork with salt and pepper, then stir-fry until browned and cooked through (3-4 mins). Remove and set aside.
1. Add a splash of oil to the pan. Pour in beaten eggs and scramble until just set. Remove and set aside with the pork.
1. Add remaining oil to the pan. Sauté the white parts of the green onions, garlic, and ginger for 30 seconds until fragrant.
1. Add peas and carrots, stirring for 1-2 minutes. Add cold rice and break up any clumps with a spatula. Stir-fry for 2-3 minutes until heated through.
1. Pour soy sauce, oyster sauce (if using), and sesame oil over the rice. Stir well to coat.
1. Add the cooked pork and scrambled eggs back to the pan. Toss everything together for 1 minute.
1. Taste and adjust seasoning. Stir in the green parts of the scallions and serve immediately.

---

## Pork Biryani
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork shoulder or loin, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 cup plain yogurt
- 2 tbsp ginger-garlic paste
- 1 tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chili powder, 2 tsp garam masala
- 1/4 cup chopped mint leaves, 1/4 cup chopped coriander (cilantro)
- 2 1/2 cups Basmati rice, rinsed and soaked for 30 minutes
- Whole spices: 2 bay leaves, 4 green cardamoms, 4 cloves, 1 cinnamon stick, 1 star anise
- 3 large onions, thinly sliced
- 2 medium tomatoes, chopped
- 4 tbsp oil or ghee
- 1 tsp cumin seeds
- Optional: pinch of saffron soaked in 2 tbsp warm milk
- Salt to taste

### Instructions
1. Marinate: Mix pork with yogurt, ginger-garlic paste, spices (turmeric, chili, garam masala, salt), mint, and coriander. Marinate for at least 30 minutes.
1. Rice: Boil a large pot of water with whole spices and salt. Add soaked rice and cook until 70-80% done (still has a slight bite). Drain and set aside.
1. Pork Base: Heat oil/ghee in a heavy-bottomed pot. Sauté cumin seeds and onions until golden brown. Add tomatoes and cook until soft.
1. Add marinated pork and cook for 5-8 minutes until browned. Add 1/2 cup water, cover, and simmer until pork is tender (30-40 mins).
1. Layering (Dum): Spread partially cooked rice evenly over the pork layer. Drizzle saffron milk and reserved fried onions on top.
1. Seal the pot with a tight lid and cook on very low heat for 15-20 minutes.
1. Rest for 10 minutes, then gently fluff and mix before serving with raita.

---

## Pork Paella
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb boneless pork loin, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 cup uncooked short-grain white rice (like Arborio or Bomba)
- 1 small white onion, diced
- 1 large red bell pepper, sliced into strips
- 1 cup frozen peas, thawed
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 3 cups chicken broth (divided)
- 1 (15 oz) can crushed tomatoes
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tbsp smoked paprika
- 1 tbsp dried oregano
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, minced (for garnish)
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a paella pan or large skillet over medium-high heat. Add pork, paprika, and oregano. Brown pork on all sides (3-5 mins), then remove and set aside.
1. Reduce heat to medium. Sauté onion and bell pepper for 2-3 minutes. Add garlic and crushed tomatoes, simmering for 4-5 minutes until thickened slightly.
1. Stir in the uncooked rice to coat. Pour in 1.5 cups of chicken broth. Cover and cook for 12-15 minutes, stirring occasionally.
1. Add the browned pork back to the skillet with the remaining 1.5 cups of broth. Cover and simmer for 15 minutes until rice is tender and liquid is absorbed.
1. Stir in the peas and cook for 2 more minutes.
1. Garnish with fresh parsley and serve warm.

---

## Pork Jambalaya
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork tenderloin or shoulder, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1/2 lb to 3/4 lb smoked sausage (Andouille or Kielbasa), sliced
- 1 large onion, diced
- 1 green bell pepper, diced
- 1 cup celery, diced
- 2-3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 1/2 cups long-grain white rice (uncooked)
- 2 1/2 cups chicken broth
- 1 tbsp Cajun or Creole seasoning
- 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil
- 2 green onions, sliced (for garnish)
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Toss pork with salt and pepper. Heat oil in a Dutch oven over medium-high heat. Brown pork and sausage (8-10 mins), then remove to a plate.
1. In the same pot, sauté onion, bell pepper, and celery for 5-7 minutes until softened. Stir in garlic and Cajun seasoning for 30 seconds.
1. Stir in the rice until coated. Pour in the broth and return the meat and juices to the pot.
1. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low and cover tightly. Simmer for 20-25 minutes without lifting the lid.
1. Remove from heat and let sit, covered, for 5 minutes.
1. Fluff with a fork, garnish with green onions, and serve.

---

## Pork Risotto
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork loin filet or tenderloin, cut into bite-sized pieces
- 1 cup uncooked Arborio rice
- 4 cups beef or chicken broth (warmed)
- 1/4 cup milk
- 1/2 large yellow onion, diced
- 1 1/2 cups sliced mushrooms (baby bella or button)
- 2 tbsp salted butter (divided)
- 1/2 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Melt 1 tbsp butter in a large pot over medium-high heat. Add onion, mushrooms, and pork. Cook for 10 mins until pork is mostly cooked. Remove and set aside.
1. Melt remaining 1 tbsp butter in the same pan. Add Arborio rice and stir for 1 minute until edges are translucent.
1. Add warm broth 1 cup at a time, stirring frequently. Wait for each cup to be absorbed before adding the next. This takes 20-25 minutes total.
1. When the last addition of broth is nearly absorbed, stir the cooked pork, mushrooms, and milk back into the pot.
1. Stir in Parmesan cheese until melted. Season with salt and pepper and serve immediately.

---

## Pork Carbonara
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Spaghetti or Rigatoni
- 6-8 oz Guanciale, Pancetta, or thick-cut Bacon, diced
- 4 large egg yolks + 1 whole large egg
- 1 cup freshly grated Pecorino Romano or Parmesan
- 1 tsp freshly cracked black pepper
- Salt for pasta water

### Instructions
1. Boil pasta in salted water until al dente. Reserve 1 cup of starchy pasta water before draining.
1. While pasta cooks, sauté diced pork in a large skillet over medium heat until crispy (8-10 mins). Turn off heat but keep pork and fat in the pan.
1. Whisk egg yolks, whole egg, cheese, and pepper in a bowl until a paste forms.
1. Add drained pasta to the skillet with the pork and toss to coat in fat.
1. With the skillet off the heat, pour in the egg mixture and 1/4 cup of reserved pasta water.
1. Toss vigorously to create a creamy emulsion, adding more pasta water as needed for consistency.
1. Serve immediately with extra cheese and pepper.

---

## Pork Pesto Pasta
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 lean pork loin steaks or shoulder steaks, cut into 1cm strips
- 250g dried pasta (penne, fusilli, or twists)
- 1 jar (approx. 190g) prepared green or red pesto
- 150g broccoli florets (fresh or frozen)
- 600ml hot water
- 25g grated hard cheese (Cheddar or Parmesan)
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Season pork strips with salt and pepper. Sear in a large lidded pan until browned.
1. Add broccoli, half the pesto, dried pasta, and hot water. Stir to combine.
1. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low. Cover and simmer for 15-20 minutes until pasta is tender and liquid is absorbed.
1. Stir in the remaining pesto to freshen the flavor.
1. Sprinkle with grated cheese and cover for a minute to melt (or grill for 2-3 mins until golden).
1. Let stand for 2 minutes before serving.

---

## Pork Mac and Cheese
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3-4 cups cooked pulled pork
- 1-1.5 cups BBQ sauce
- 1 lb elbow macaroni or cavatappi
- 4 tbsp salted butter
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- 3 cups whole milk
- 3 cups shredded sharp cheddar (divided)
- 8 oz Velveeta or cream cheese
- 1 tsp salt, 1/2 tsp black pepper, 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- Optional: 1/2 cup panko breadcrumbs

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C) and grease a 9x13 inch dish.
1. Cook pasta until al dente, drain, and set aside. Toss pulled pork with BBQ sauce.
1. Melt butter in a saucepan, whisk in flour for 1-2 mins. Slowly whisk in milk until thickened (5-7 mins).
1. Remove from heat and stir in Velveeta and 2 cups of cheddar until smooth. Add seasonings.
1. Fold pasta into cheese sauce. Pour half into the dish. Layer BBQ pork on top, then the rest of the pasta.
1. Top with remaining cheddar and breadcrumbs. Bake for 20-25 minutes until bubbly.
1. Rest for 5-10 minutes before serving.

---

## Pork Pilaf
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs pork (shoulder or loin), cut into 1-inch cubes
- 2 cups Basmati or long-grain white rice, rinsed
- 2 large onions, chopped
- 3 large carrots, julienned
- 1 whole head of garlic (unpeeled, outer skin removed)
- 3-4 cups hot water or chicken stock
- 1/2 cup vegetable oil
- 1 tbsp cumin seeds
- 1 tsp paprika, 1/2 tsp turmeric (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Optional: 1 dried chili pepper

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a Dutch oven. Sear pork until browned (8-10 mins).
1. Add onions and sauté until golden. Stir in carrots and cook for 5 minutes.
1. Add cumin, paprika, turmeric, salt, and pepper. Pour in 1-2 cups hot water to cover and simmer for 20 minutes.
1. Spread rinsed rice in an even layer over the meat. Do not stir.
1. Carefully pour remaining hot water over a spoon to 1 inch above the rice. Push the whole garlic head into the center.
1. Cook uncovered over medium-high until surface water is absorbed. Poke holes in rice for steam.
1. Cover tightly, reduce heat to lowest, and steam for 20-25 minutes.
1. Rest for 10 minutes, remove garlic, then mix and serve.

---

## Pork Garlic Rice
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tbsp minced garlic + 1 tsp minced garlic (separated)
- 1 tbsp minced ginger
- 1/4 cup rice wine vinegar
- 1/4 cup soy sauce (or tamari) + 1 tbsp soy sauce (separated)
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 2 cups cooked rice (cold/day-old)
- 1/2 cup frozen peas, 1/2 cup frozen corn
- 1 spring onion, sliced
- 1 tbsp sesame oil
- Optional: fried eggs, sliced cucumber

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a pan. Sauté 1 tbsp garlic and ginger for 30 seconds. Add ground pork and brown.
1. Add rice wine vinegar, 1/4 cup soy sauce, and brown sugar. Cook for 5 mins until caramelized and sauce thickens. Remove and set aside.
1. In the same pan, heat a little oil and sauté 1 tsp garlic. Add peas and corn for 1-2 mins.
1. Add cold rice and stir-fry for 1 minute until heated through.
1. Remove from heat and stir in spring onion, 1 tbsp soy sauce, and sesame oil.
1. Serve caramelized pork over the garlic rice, topped with a fried egg if desired.

---

## Pork Shawarma
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) pork tenderloin or pork shoulder, sliced into thin strips
- 4 tbsp olive oil
- Juice of 1 lemon (or 2 tbsp white wine vinegar)
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1/2 tsp ground turmeric
- 1/2 tsp ground cloves or allspice
- 1/2 tsp ground nutmeg (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 4–6 large pita breads or flatbreads
- Shredded lettuce, sliced red onions, diced tomatoes, and sliced cucumbers for serving
- Tzatziki or garlic yogurt sauce (1 cup Greek yogurt, 1 minced garlic clove, 1 tbsp lemon juice, and chopped parsley)

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, whisk together the olive oil, lemon juice, minced garlic, and all the spices. Add the pork strips and toss until thoroughly coated. Cover and refrigerate for at least 2 hours (overnight is best).
1. Cook the pork using your preferred method: Stovetop: Sear in a large skillet over medium-high heat for 3–5 minutes until browned and cooked through. Oven: Roast on a baking sheet at 400°F (200°C) for 15–20 minutes. Grill: Cook on medium-high heat for 4–6 minutes per side.
1. While the pork is cooking, chop the vegetables and prepare the yogurt sauce.
1. Warm the pita bread slightly. Spread a generous spoonful of sauce in the center, add a portion of the cooked pork, and top with the fresh vegetables.
1. Fold or roll the pita tightly and serve immediately.

---

## Pork Burrito
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 cups pulled pork (leftover or freshly made)
- 1 1/2 cups cooked rice (white, brown, or Mexican-style)
- 1 1/2 cups black beans or pinto beans, drained and rinsed
- 1 cup shredded cheese (Cheddar, Monterey Jack, or Mexican blend)
- 1 red bell pepper, diced
- 1/2 red onion, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp olive oil or vegetable oil
- 6 large flour tortillas (burrito size)
- Optional toppings: Shredded lettuce, sour cream, salsa or pico de gallo, guacamole, fresh cilantro, and lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Heat the oil in a large skillet over medium heat. Sauté the onion and garlic for 2–3 minutes until fragrant, then add the bell peppers and cook for another 5 minutes until softened.
1. Add the pulled pork and beans to the skillet. Stir well and cook for 3–5 minutes until the mixture is heated through. Add a splash of water or broth if the pork is too dry.
1. Warm the tortillas in the microwave for 15–20 seconds or in a dry skillet over medium heat to make them pliable.
1. Assemble the burritos: Lay a warm tortilla flat, place about 1/4 cup of rice in the center, top with 1/2 cup of the pork and bean mixture, add cheese and desired cold toppings.
1. Fold the left and right sides of the tortilla inward, then roll tightly from the bottom toward the top.
1. Optional: Place the rolled burritos seam-side down in a hot, lightly oiled skillet for 1–2 minutes per side until golden brown and crispy.

---

## Pork Taco
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3–4 lbs pork shoulder (pork butt), cut into 2-inch chunks
- 1 orange, juiced (keep the rinds)
- 1 lime, juiced
- 1 medium white onion, quartered
- 4–6 cloves garlic, smashed
- 1/2 cup water or chicken broth
- 1 tbsp dried oregano
- 2 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tbsp kosher salt
- 1 tsp black pepper
- 16 small corn tortillas
- Toppings: 1/2 cup finely diced white onion, 1/2 cup chopped fresh cilantro, salsa verde or pico de gallo, lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Place the pork chunks, onion, garlic, orange juice and rinds, lime juice, water, and all spices into a slow cooker. Cover and cook on Low for 8–10 hours or High for 5–6 hours until fork-tender.
1. Remove the pork from the liquid and discard the onion, garlic, and orange rinds. Shred the meat using two forks.
1. Heat a large skillet over medium-high heat with a little oil. Add the shredded pork in a single layer and pour about 1/2 cup of the cooking liquid over it.
1. Cook undisturbed for 3–5 minutes until the bottom is golden and crispy, then toss and cook for another 2 minutes.
1. Warm the tortillas in a dry skillet or over an open gas flame for 30 seconds per side until soft.
1. Assemble by placing a generous spoonful of crispy carnitas onto each tortilla, topped with diced onions, cilantro, and salsa. Serve with lime wedges.

---

## Pork Quesadilla
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) ground pork
- 1/4 cup diced onion
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp canola or vegetable oil
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/4 cup water
- 1 tsp onion powder, 1 tsp dried oregano, 1 tsp paprika, 1/2 tsp cumin, 1/2 tsp salt, 1/4 tsp chili powder, 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 8 (8-inch) flour tortillas
- 2 cups shredded Mexican cheese blend (or cheddar/jack)
- Optional toppings: Sour cream, salsa, guacamole, or fresh cilantro

### Instructions
1. Heat the oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Sauté the onion and garlic for about 2 minutes until softened.
1. Add the ground pork and cook for 6–8 minutes, stirring to break the meat into small crumbles, until fully browned. Drain any excess fat.
1. Reduce heat to medium and stir in the tomato paste, water, and the entire spice blend. Simmer for 2–3 minutes until the sauce thickens and coats the meat evenly. Remove from heat.
1. Assemble the quesadillas: Place one tortilla on a flat surface, sprinkle 1/4 cup of cheese, top with 1/2 cup of pork filling, another 1/4 cup of cheese, and a second tortilla.
1. Cook in a clean non-stick skillet over medium-low heat for 2–3 minutes per side. Press down lightly with a spatula to help the cheese melt and the tortilla become golden and crisp.
1. Transfer to a cutting board, let rest for a minute, and cut into wedges. Serve with toppings.

---

## Pork Sandwich
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork loin
- 1 tbsp cooking oil
- Salt and fresh ground pepper to taste
- 1 medium onion, thinly sliced
- 1/2 lb provolone cheese, sliced
- 1 large loaf crusty French bread (or 8 individual rolls)
- Honey Mustard Sauce: 1/4 cup mayonnaise, 2 tbsp stone ground mustard, 1 tbsp honey, 1/8 tsp fresh ground pepper

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Rub the pork loin with oil and season generously with salt and pepper.
1. Roast the pork in a roasting pan for approximately 1 hour or until internal temperature reaches 145°F (63°C). Let the meat rest for 10 minutes before slicing thinly.
1. While the pork is roasting, sauté the sliced onions in a pan with a little oil over medium-low heat until soft and caramelized (15–20 minutes).
1. Whisk together the mayonnaise, stone ground mustard, honey, and pepper in a small bowl.
1. Slice the bread open and lightly toast the interior under a broiler until golden.
1. Layer the sliced pork and provolone onto the bread. Broil for 1–2 minutes until the cheese is melted and bubbly.
1. Top with caramelized onions and honey mustard sauce. Close the sandwich, slice, and serve immediately.

---

## Pulled Pork Burger
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 lbs boneless pork shoulder (pork butt)
- 3 tbsp brown sugar
- 1 tbsp smoked paprika
- 1 tbsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp onion powder
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp salt and 1 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)
- 1/2 cup apple cider vinegar
- 1/2 cup chicken broth or water
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 to 1.5 cups BBQ sauce
- 8–10 Brioche or sesame seed buns, lightly toasted
- Toppings: Coleslaw, sliced pickles, red onion, or jalapeños

### Instructions
1. Mix the brown sugar, paprika, garlic powder, onion powder, cumin, salt, pepper, and cayenne in a small bowl. Rub the mixture all over the pork shoulder.
1. Place the seasoned pork in a slow cooker and pour the vinegar, chicken broth, and Worcestershire sauce around it.
1. Cover and cook on Low for 8–10 hours or High for 5–6 hours until 'fall-apart' tender.
1. Remove the pork and shred it using two forks, discarding excess fat.
1. Drain most of the liquid from the slow cooker (leave about 1/2 cup), return the shredded pork to the pot, and stir in the BBQ sauce. Let it sit on Warm for 15–20 minutes.
1. Assemble the burgers by piling a generous amount of pulled pork onto toasted buns, topped with coleslaw and pickles.

---

## Pork Sliders
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 12-pack slider buns (e.g., Hawaiian rolls)
- 3 cups pulled pork (homemade or store-bought)
- 1/2 cup BBQ sauce
- 9–12 slices of cheese (Cheddar, Pepper Jack, or Monterey Jack)
- Pickles (optional)
- Butter Glaze: 1/4 cup melted butter, 2 tsp Worcestershire sauce, 1/2 tsp garlic salt, 1/2 tsp poppy seeds or sesame seeds
- Optional Coleslaw: 9 oz coleslaw mix, 1/2 cup mayo, 1 tbsp Dijon mustard, 1 tbsp apple cider vinegar, 1 tsp onion powder

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Slice the entire 12-pack of buns in half horizontally and place the bottom half in a 9x13-inch baking dish.
1. Spread the pulled pork evenly over the bottom buns, drizzle with BBQ sauce, and layer the cheese slices on top.
1. Place the top half of the buns over the cheese.
1. Whisk together the melted butter, Worcestershire sauce, garlic salt, and poppy seeds. Brush this glaze evenly over the tops of the buns.
1. Cover the dish with foil and bake for 20 minutes. Remove foil and bake for another 5 minutes until the cheese is bubbly and tops are golden.
1. Slice into individual sliders and serve immediately with pickles or coleslaw.

---

## Pork Empanada
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- Filling: 1 kg ground pork, 4 cloves garlic (minced), 2 white onions (minced), 2 medium potatoes (cubed small), 1 carrot (cubed small), 1 red bell pepper (finely chopped), 1 cup green peas, 1/2 cup water, 3 tsp sugar, salt and black pepper, 4 tbsp oil
- Pastry: 6 cups all-purpose flour, 1/2 cup white sugar, 1 tsp baking powder, 1 tsp salt, 2 cups cold butter (cubed), 3/4 cup cold water
- Cooking oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Prepare the filling: Sauté onions and garlic in oil, add ground pork and brown it. Add potatoes, carrots, and water; simmer until vegetables are tender. Stir in peas, bell peppers, and sugar, and cook until liquid evaporates. Cool completely.
1. Make the pastry: Whisk together dry ingredients, cut in the cold butter until it resembles coarse crumbs, then gradually add cold water and knead until a smooth dough forms.
1. Divide the dough into balls and refrigerate for 20 minutes.
1. Flatten a dough ball into a circle, place 2–3 tablespoons of filling in the center, fold over to a half-moon shape, and seal the edges by crimping with a fork or braiding.
1. Deep-fry the empanadas over medium-low heat until golden brown, then drain on paper towels.

---

## Siopao Asado
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- Filling: 1 lb (500g) pork shoulder or loin (diced small), 3 cloves garlic (minced), 1 small onion (chopped), 2 tbsp soy sauce, 2 tbsp oyster sauce, 1 tbsp hoisin sauce, 3 tbsp brown sugar, 2 star anise, 2 tbsp cornstarch in 1/4 cup water (slurry), 1 cup water, 1 tbsp oil
- Dough: 1 cup warm water, 2 1/4 tsp active dry yeast, 1/2 cup white sugar, 3 1/2 cups all-purpose flour, 3 tbsp shortening or oil, 1 tbsp baking powder, 1/2 tsp salt
- 1 tbsp vinegar for steaming water

### Instructions
1. Prepare the filling: Sauté garlic and onions, add pork and brown. Add water, sauces, sugar, and star anise; simmer for 20–30 minutes until tender. Remove star anise, stir in cornstarch slurry to thicken, and cool completely.
1. Make the dough: Activate yeast in warm water with 1 tbsp sugar. Mix with remaining dough ingredients, knead for 8–10 minutes until smooth, and let rise for 1 to 1.5 hours until doubled.
1. Divide dough into 10–12 pieces, roll into balls, then flatten into disks with thinner edges.
1. Place 1–2 tablespoons of filling in the center, pinch the edges to seal, and place on a square of parchment paper. Let rest for 15–20 minutes.
1. Steam on medium heat for 15–20 minutes (add vinegar to water). Wait 2–3 minutes before opening the lid to prevent collapsing.

---

## Pork Lumpia
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 1/2 lbs ground pork
- 1 medium carrot, finely minced
- 1 small onion, finely minced
- 2-3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1-2 eggs
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tsp salt and 1/2 tsp ground black pepper
- 30-50 thin lumpia or spring roll wrappers
- 1 beaten egg (for sealing)
- 2-3 cups cooking oil for frying
- Sweet chili sauce for dipping

### Instructions
1. Prepare the filling: Combine ground pork, minced carrots, onion, garlic, eggs, soy sauce, salt, and pepper in a bowl. Mix thoroughly.
1. Separate the lumpia wrappers and keep them covered with a damp towel.
1. Wrap the lumpia: Place about 1 to 1 1/2 tablespoons of filling on a wrapper, shape into a thin log, fold the bottom and sides, and roll tightly toward the top. Seal with the beaten egg.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C) and fry the lumpia in batches for 4–6 minutes until golden brown and cooked through.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve hot with sweet chili sauce.

---

## Lechon
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 whole pig (approx. 20kg), cleaned
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Lemongrass (tanglad) bundles
- Scallions
- Garlic, crushed
- Red onions, quartered
- Bay leaves
- Star anise
- Evaporated milk or lemon-lime soda (for glazing/basting)

### Instructions
1. Clean the pig thoroughly and pat dry with paper towels.
1. Rub the inside and outside of the pig generously with salt and pepper.
1. Fill the belly cavity with lemongrass, scallions, garlic, onions, bay leaves, and star anise.
1. Sew the belly shut with kitchen twine to keep the aromatics inside.
1. Insert a long bamboo or metal pole through the length of the pig.
1. Slow-roast over hot charcoal for 4 to 6 hours, rotating constantly to ensure even cooking.
1. During the last hour of roasting, baste the skin with evaporated milk or soda to achieve a crispy, reddish-brown finish.
1. Rest for 20-30 minutes before carving and serving.

---

## Pork BBQ Skewers
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 lbs pork shoulder, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 cup soy sauce
- 1 cup lemon-lime soda (7-Up or Sprite)
- 1 cup brown sugar
- 1 cup minced garlic
- 1/2 cup banana ketchup
- 1/2 cup cane vinegar
- 1/4 cup oyster sauce
- 2 tsp ground black pepper
- Bamboo skewers, soaked in water for 30 minutes

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, whisk together soy sauce, soda, sugar, garlic, ketchup, vinegar, oyster sauce, and pepper.
1. Add the pork pieces and toss to coat. Marinate in the refrigerator for at least 4-6 hours, or overnight.
1. Thread 4-5 pieces of pork onto each soaked bamboo skewer, alternating between lean and fatty pieces.
1. Preheat the grill to medium-high heat and lightly oil the grates.
1. Grill the skewers for 3-5 minutes per side, for a total of 10-12 minutes.
1. Baste with extra sauce (reserved marinade or a mix of ketchup and oil) during the last few minutes of grilling until glazed and slightly charred.
1. Serve hot with steamed rice and spiced vinegar.

---

## Grilled Pork Chops
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 bone-in pork loin chops (1 to 1.5 inches thick)
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 2 tbsp brown sugar
- 1 tbsp kosher salt
- 2 tsp smoked paprika
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp onion powder
- 1 tsp cracked black pepper

### Instructions
1. Pat the pork chops dry with paper towels.
1. In a small bowl, mix the brown sugar, salt, paprika, garlic powder, onion powder, and pepper.
1. Rub the olive oil over both sides of the chops, then apply the dry rub generously.
1. Preheat the grill to medium-high (400°F).
1. Sear the chops for 2 minutes per side without moving them.
1. Reduce heat to medium and continue cooking for 4-7 minutes per side until the internal temperature reaches 145°F.
1. Transfer to a plate and let rest for 5-10 minutes before serving.

---

## Inihaw na Baboy
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork belly (liempo), sliced into 1/2 inch thick pieces
- 3 tbsp soy sauce
- 5 tbsp banana ketchup
- 4 tbsp liquid seasoning (like Knorr)
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 3 tbsp calamansi or lemon juice
- 1/2 tsp ground black pepper
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil (for basting)

### Instructions
1. Combine soy sauce, ketchup, liquid seasoning, garlic powder, calamansi juice, and pepper in a bowl.
1. Add the pork belly and marinate for at least 3 hours or overnight in the refrigerator.
1. Prepare the grill for medium heat.
1. Grill each side of the pork for 5-8 minutes.
1. Baste with a mixture of soy sauce, ketchup, and oil every few minutes until charred and cooked through.
1. Rest for 5 minutes, then slice into bite-sized pieces and serve with spicy vinegar dipping sauce.

---

## Pork Satay
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs pork tenderloin, cut into 1-inch strips
- 1/2 cup coconut milk
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp brown sugar
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp ground turmeric
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- For Peanut Sauce: 1/2 cup peanut butter, 1/2 cup coconut milk, 1 tbsp soy sauce, 1 tbsp lime juice, 1/2 tsp chili sauce

### Instructions
1. Whisk together coconut milk, soy sauce, sugar, garlic, and spices in a bowl.
1. Add pork, toss to coat, and marinate for 2-8 hours.
1. Thread the pork onto soaked bamboo skewers.
1. For the sauce: Combine peanut butter, coconut milk, soy sauce, lime juice, and chili sauce in a saucepan over low heat; whisk until smooth.
1. Grill skewers over medium-high heat for 3-4 minutes per side until charred and cooked through.
1. Serve the warm skewers with the peanut dipping sauce.

## Roast Pork Belly
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2.5 lbs skin-on pork belly slab
- 1 tbsp Shaoxing wine
- 1 tsp Chinese five-spice powder
- 1.5 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp white pepper
- 1 tsp white vinegar (for the skin)
- 1/2 cup coarse sea salt (for the salt crust)

### Instructions
1. Poke hundreds of tiny holes in the skin with a skewer without piercing the meat.
1. Rub the Shaoxing wine and the spice mix (five-spice, salt, pepper) on the meat side only.
1. Place skin-side up on a plate and refrigerate uncovered for at least 6-24 hours to dry the skin.
1. Preheat oven to 350°F. Wrap the sides and bottom of the pork in foil to create a boat.
1. Brush skin with vinegar and cover with a thick layer of coarse salt. Roast for 60 minutes.
1. Remove salt crust, increase oven temp to 425°F (or broil), and roast for 20-30 minutes until skin is puffed and crispy.
1. Rest for 15 minutes, then slice skin-side down into pieces.

---

## Peri-Peri Pork
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 pork shoulder or loin steaks
- 1 roasted red bell pepper
- 1/2 lemon, juiced
- 1 tbsp apple cider vinegar
- 5 cloves garlic
- 1 tsp chili flakes
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tbsp dried oregano
- 1 tbsp olive oil

### Instructions
1. In a blender, pulse the roasted pepper, lemon juice, vinegar, garlic, and spices into a smooth paste.
1. Coat the pork steaks with the marinade and refrigerate for at least 1 hour.
1. Heat a grill or skillet over medium-high heat with a little oil.
1. Grill the steaks for 4-5 minutes per side until the internal temperature reaches 145°F.
1. Rest for 5 minutes before serving with rice or salad.

---

## Garlic Herb Pork Roast
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3-4 lb boneless pork loin roast
- 6-8 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp each fresh rosemary, thyme, and parsley, chopped
- 3 tbsp olive oil
- 1.5 tsp salt
- 1 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp onion powder
- 1 cup chicken broth

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F. Pat the roast dry.
1. In a small bowl, mix garlic, herbs, oil, salt, pepper, and onion powder into a paste.
1. Rub the herb paste all over the pork roast.
1. Place the roast fat-side up in a roasting pan. Pour chicken broth into the bottom of the pan.
1. Roast uncovered for 50-70 minutes until the internal temperature reaches 145°F.
1. Transfer to a board, tent with foil, and let rest for 10-15 minutes before slicing.

---

## Honey BBQ Pork
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs pork ribs or tenderloin
- 1/2 cup BBQ sauce
- 1/2 cup honey
- 1 tbsp apple cider vinegar
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp onion powder
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 300°F (for ribs) or 350°F (for tenderloin).
1. Whisk together BBQ sauce, honey, vinegar, garlic powder, onion powder, salt, and pepper.
1. Rub the glaze generously over the pork.
1. If roasting ribs, wrap in foil and bake for 2 hours; then unwrap, baste, and broil for 10 minutes.
1. If roasting tenderloin, sear in a pan first, then roast in the oven for 25-35 minutes, basting every 5 minutes.
1. Rest for 10 minutes before slicing and serving.

---

## Smoked Pork Ribs
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 racks of pork ribs (Baby Back or St. Louis style)
- 1/4 cup yellow mustard (as a binder)
- 1/2 cup BBQ dry rub
- 4 tbsp unsalted butter
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 1/4 cup honey
- 1/4 cup apple juice
- 1 cup BBQ sauce

### Instructions
1. Remove the membrane from the back of the ribs.
1. Coat ribs with mustard and apply the dry rub. Let sit for 30 minutes.
1. Smoke the ribs at 225°F for 3 hours, bone-side down.
1. Remove from smoker and wrap tightly in foil with butter, brown sugar, honey, and apple juice. Smoke for another 2 hours meat-side down.
1. Unwrap the ribs, place back on the grill meat-side up, and brush with BBQ sauce. Smoke for 1 final hour until the sauce is tacky.
1. Rest for 15 minutes before slicing between the bones.

---

## Pork Salad
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 pork tenderloin (approx. 3/4 lb)
- 1/4 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon black pepper
- 2/3 cup plain yogurt (fat-free or Greek)
- 1/4 cup fresh cilantro, finely chopped
- 2 tablespoons lime juice
- 1 tablespoon canola oil
- 1/2 teaspoon sugar
- 8 cups mixed salad greens
- 1 medium yellow bell pepper, sliced
- 1 package (8 oz) sliced fresh mushrooms
- 1 can (15 oz) black-eyed peas, rinsed and drained

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Season pork with salt and pepper.
1. Bake pork for 30-40 minutes until internal temperature reaches 160°F (71°C).
1. Let pork rest for 10 minutes, then cut into thin slices.
1. In a small bowl, whisk together yogurt, cilantro, lime juice, oil, sugar, and additional salt to make the dressing.
1. Arrange salad greens, bell peppers, mushrooms, and black-eyed peas on a platter or in bowls.
1. Top with pork slices and drizzle with the cilantro-lime dressing.

---

## Pork Lettuce Wraps
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 1 head of Butter, Bibb, or Iceberg lettuce
- 1 can (8 oz) water chestnuts, drained and diced
- 1 cup shredded carrots
- 1/2 medium onion, finely diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil
- 1/4 cup Hoisin sauce
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- Sliced green onions and fresh cilantro for garnish

### Instructions
1. Rinse and dry lettuce leaves, keeping them whole for wrapping.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Brown ground pork until crumbled and cooked through. Drain excess fat.
1. Add onion to the skillet and sauté for 2-3 minutes. Stir in garlic and ginger, cooking for 1 more minute.
1. Stir in water chestnuts and shredded carrots. Cook for 2 minutes.
1. In a small bowl, whisk hoisin, soy sauce, rice vinegar, and sesame oil. Pour over the pork mixture and stir to coat.
1. Spoon the mixture into lettuce leaves and garnish with green onions and cilantro.

---

## Pork Stir-Fry
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork tenderloin, cut into thin strips
- 2 cups broccoli florets
- 1 red bell pepper, sliced
- 1 medium carrot, thinly sliced
- 1/2 red onion, sliced
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- 2 tbsp honey
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp cornstarch
- 1/4 cup chicken broth

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, honey, vinegar, ginger, garlic, cornstarch, and broth to make the sauce.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a wok or large skillet. Sear pork strips for 3-5 minutes until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil and stir-fry broccoli, carrots, bell pepper, and onion for 5-7 minutes.
1. Return pork to the pan. Re-whisk the sauce and pour it over the mixture.
1. Cook for 1-2 minutes until the sauce thickens and coats everything evenly.
1. Serve immediately, optionally over brown rice or cauliflower rice.

---

## Pork Veggie Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 2 cups cooked brown rice or cauliflower rice
- 1 small yellow onion, diced
- 1 cup carrots, shredded
- 1 cup mushrooms, sliced
- 2 cups shredded cabbage or spinach
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, minced
- 1/4 cup low-sodium soy sauce
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 1 tbsp honey
- Sliced green onions and sesame seeds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Brown the ground pork in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Drain fat and set aside.
1. Sauté onions, carrots, and mushrooms in the same pan for 3-4 minutes until softened.
1. Add garlic and ginger, cooking for 1 minute until fragrant.
1. Return pork to the pan. Add cabbage (or spinach), soy sauce, vinegar, and honey.
1. Stir for 2-3 minutes until the greens are wilted and everything is well-combined.
1. Divide rice into bowls and top with the pork and vegetable mixture. Garnish with green onions and sesame seeds.

---

## Pork Quinoa Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork tenderloin, sliced into thin strips
- 1 cup quinoa, rinsed
- 2 cups chicken broth
- 2 cups broccoli florets or snap peas
- 1 red bell pepper, sliced
- 1 carrot, julienned
- 2 cups fresh baby spinach
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp honey
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp olive oil

### Instructions
1. Combine quinoa and broth in a pot. Bring to a boil, then simmer covered for 15 minutes until liquid is absorbed. Fluff with a fork.
1. Whisk soy sauce, honey, and garlic. Marinate pork strips in half of the mixture for 10 minutes.
1. Sauté pork in olive oil over medium-high heat for 4-5 minutes until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
1. In the same skillet, sauté broccoli, pepper, and carrots for 3-4 minutes. Add spinach and remaining sauce, cooking until wilted.
1. Divide quinoa into bowls, top with vegetables and pork, and serve.

---

## Pork Zoodle Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 2 large zucchinis, spiralized into zoodles
- 1 quart chicken or beef stock
- 4 baby bok choy, chopped
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 2-inch piece fresh ginger, grated
- 2 green onions, sliced
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 2 tsp fish sauce
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil
- Red pepper flakes and cilantro for garnish

### Instructions
1. Brown ground pork with garlic, ginger, and red pepper flakes in a large pot with oil for about 5 minutes.
1. Pour in the stock and bring to a simmer. Let cook for 10-15 minutes.
1. Add bok choy, green onion whites, soy sauce, and fish sauce. Simmer for 5 more minutes.
1. Place raw zoodles in serving bowls.
1. Ladle the hot pork and broth over the zoodles; the heat will soften them slightly.
1. Garnish with green onion tops and cilantro.

---

## Steamed Pork
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 100g (3.5 oz) lean ground pork or thinly sliced tenderloin
- 1 inch fresh ginger, julienned
- 2 tablespoons light soy sauce
- 1 tablespoon cornstarch
- 1-2 stalks scallions, thinly sliced
- Optional: pinch of white pepper and a few drops of sesame oil

### Instructions
1. Mix pork with soy sauce, cornstarch, and white pepper. Massage well to ensure tenderness.
1. Spread the pork thinly onto a shallow heat-proof dish (less than 1 inch thick).
1. Top the pork evenly with julienned ginger.
1. Steam on medium-high heat for 20-30 minutes until the pork is thoroughly cooked.
1. Garnish with fresh scallions and a drop of sesame oil before serving.

---

## Poached Pork
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pork tenderloin, trimmed of fat
- 1.5 cups low-fat milk or unsweetened almond milk
- 6 garlic cloves, minced
- 1/2 tsp kosher salt
- Freshly ground black pepper
- 1 tsp olive oil
- Optional: 1 tbsp cornstarch mixed with 1 tbsp water for sauce

### Instructions
1. Season pork with salt and pepper. Optionally sear in a skillet with olive oil for 2-3 minutes per side.
1. Add milk and minced garlic to a pot. Bring to a very gentle simmer (do not boil).
1. Add pork, cover, and simmer gently for 20-25 minutes until internal temperature reaches 145°F (63°C).
1. Remove pork and let it rest for 10 minutes.
1. Optional: Thicken the poaching liquid with cornstarch slurry to make a garlic sauce.
1. Slice into medallions and serve with the sauce.

---

## Pork Cabbage Salad
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1/2 lb pork shoulder or tenderloin, poached and sliced
- 1/2 head green cabbage, thinly shredded
- 1 large carrot, julienned
- 1/2 red onion, thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup fresh mint or cilantro, chopped
- 3 tbsp fish sauce
- 3 tbsp sugar
- 2 tbsp fresh lime juice
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 1-2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/4 cup roasted peanuts, crushed

### Instructions
1. Poach pork in water with salt and ginger for 15-20 minutes. Cool and slice into thin strips.
1. Combine cabbage, carrots, and onions in a large bowl. Soak onions in ice water first to mellow them.
1. Whisk fish sauce, sugar, lime juice, vinegar, and garlic to make the dressing.
1. Toss the vegetables and pork with the dressing and half the herbs. Let sit for 5-10 minutes.
1. Garnish with remaining herbs and crushed peanuts before serving.

---

## Pork Avocado Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 2 ripe avocados, sliced
- 3 cups cooked brown rice
- 3 tbsp gochujang (Korean chili paste)
- 2 tbsp mirin
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp sesame oil
- Sliced green onions and sesame seeds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Cook ground pork in a large skillet over high heat until browned.
1. Stir in gochujang, mirin, garlic, ginger, soy sauce, and sesame oil.
1. Cook for 5-10 minutes, stirring frequently, until the pork is slightly crispy and caramelized.
1. Divide rice into four bowls.
1. Top each bowl with the caramelized pork and half an avocado (sliced).
1. Garnish with green onions and sesame seeds.

---

## Pork Pot Pie
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 ½ cups cooked pork, cubed
- 2 ½ cups frozen mixed vegetables (peas, carrots, corn)
- ¼ cup butter
- ½ cup all-purpose flour
- 1 can (14.5 oz) chicken or vegetable broth
- ¾ cup whole milk
- 1 ½ cups shredded cheddar cheese
- ½ tsp seasoned salt
- Dash of black pepper
- 1 sheet frozen puff pastry, thawed
- 1 egg, beaten (for egg wash)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 425°F (220°C). Lightly grease an 11x7-inch baking dish.
1. In a large saucepan over medium heat, melt the butter. Stir in the flour until smooth and cook for 1 minute.
1. Gradually whisk in the broth and milk. Bring to a boil, stirring constantly, and cook for 1–2 minutes until thickened.
1. Stir in the cubed pork, frozen vegetables, shredded cheese, salt, and pepper. Cook until cheese is melted.
1. Pour the mixture into the prepared baking dish.
1. Roll out the puff pastry to fit the top of the dish. Place over the filling and press edges to seal.
1. Cut a few small slits in the top of the pastry and brush with the beaten egg.
1. Bake for 18–22 minutes until the pastry is puffed and golden brown.
1. Let stand for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Baked Pork Chops
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 bone-in or boneless pork chops (1 to 1.5 inches thick)
- 2 tablespoons olive oil
- 1 tablespoon brown sugar
- 1 teaspoon smoked paprika
- 1 teaspoon garlic powder
- 1 teaspoon onion powder
- 1 teaspoon kosher salt
- ½ teaspoon black pepper
- 2 tablespoons butter (for topping)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Line a baking sheet with parchment paper or foil.
1. Pat the pork chops dry with paper towels.
1. In a small bowl, mix the brown sugar, paprika, garlic powder, onion powder, salt, and pepper.
1. Brush both sides of the pork chops with olive oil, then rub the spice mixture generously over both sides.
1. Place the chops on the baking sheet and bake for 15 to 25 minutes depending on thickness.
1. Pork is done when it reaches an internal temperature of 145°F (63°C).
1. Remove from oven, top each chop with a small pat of butter, and let rest for 5 to 10 minutes.

---

## Pork Casserole
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4-6 pork chops (bone-in or boneless)
- 4-6 medium potatoes, peeled and sliced into 1/4-inch rounds
- 2 medium carrots, sliced
- 1 medium onion, thinly sliced
- 1 can (10.5 oz) cream of mushroom soup
- 1 cup chicken or beef broth
- 2 tbsp butter or oil
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 1 cup shredded cheddar cheese (optional topping)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C). Grease a 9x13-inch baking dish.
1. Season pork chops with salt, pepper, and half the garlic powder and paprika.
1. Brown pork chops in a skillet with butter or oil for 2-3 minutes per side. Set aside.
1. In the same skillet, whisk together the cream soup, broth, and remaining seasonings.
1. Layer the sliced potatoes, carrots, and onions in the baking dish. Pour half the gravy over them.
1. Place the pork chops on top and pour the remaining gravy over the meat.
1. Cover tightly with foil and bake for 45-50 minutes.
1. Remove foil, sprinkle with cheese if using, and bake for another 10-15 minutes until vegetables are tender.
1. Let rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Pork Lasagna
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 1 medium onion, finely chopped
- 3-4 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1 jar (24-28 oz) marinara sauce
- 1 tsp dried oregano
- 1 tsp dried basil
- 15 oz ricotta cheese
- 1 large egg
- ½ cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped
- 9-12 lasagna noodles (oven-ready or boiled)
- 3 cups shredded mozzarella cheese

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).
1. Brown ground pork with onion in a skillet. Drain excess fat. Add garlic and tomato paste; cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in marinara sauce, oregano, and basil. Simmer on low for 15-20 minutes.
1. In a bowl, combine ricotta, egg, Parmesan, and parsley.
1. Spread 1 cup of meat sauce in a 9x13 inch dish. Top with 3-4 noodles.
1. Layer with 1/3 of the ricotta mixture, 1 cup of mozzarella, and 1 cup of meat sauce. Repeat layers.
1. Finish with noodles, remaining sauce, and a generous topping of mozzarella.
1. Cover with foil and bake for 25 minutes. Remove foil and bake for 15-20 minutes until bubbly.
1. Let stand for 15 minutes before slicing.

---

## Pork Enchiladas
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3-4 cups cooked shredded pork (pulled pork or carnitas)
- 10-12 corn or flour tortillas
- 2 cups red enchilada sauce
- 2 cups shredded Mexican blend cheese
- 1 small onion, diced
- 1 can (4 oz) diced green chiles
- 1 tsp ground cumin

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Spread 1/2 cup of enchilada sauce in a 9x13 inch dish.
1. In a bowl, mix shredded pork, diced onions, green chiles, cumin, and 1/2 cup of the sauce.
1. Warm tortillas until pliable. Place 1/3 cup of filling in each, roll tightly, and place seam-side down in the dish.
1. Pour remaining enchilada sauce over the rolls and sprinkle with the remaining cheese.
1. Cover with foil and bake for 20 minutes.
1. Remove foil and bake for another 10-15 minutes until cheese is melted and bubbly.
1. Rest for 5 minutes and garnish with cilantro or sour cream.

---

## Stuffed Pork Peppers
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4-6 large bell peppers, tops removed and de-seeded
- 1 lb ground pork
- 1 ½ to 2 cups cooked rice
- 1 small onion, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 can (15 oz) tomato sauce
- 1 tbsp Italian seasoning
- 1 cup shredded mozzarella or cheddar cheese
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C). Grease a 9x13 inch baking dish.
1. In a large skillet, brown the ground pork with the diced onion. Drain excess fat.
1. Add minced garlic and cook for 1 minute. Stir in cooked rice, tomato sauce, seasonings, and 1/4 cup of the cheese.
1. Stand the peppers upright in the baking dish and spoon the mixture into each pepper.
1. Cover tightly with foil and bake for 25-30 minutes.
1. Remove foil, sprinkle with remaining cheese, and bake for 5-10 minutes until cheese is melted.
1. Serve garnished with fresh herbs.

---

## Pork Pie
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 800g pork shoulder, finely chopped
- 400g pork belly, finely chopped
- 250g smoked bacon, cubed small
- 1 tbsp fresh sage, chopped
- ½ tsp ground mace
- ¼ tsp ground nutmeg
- 1 tsp white pepper
- 575g plain flour
- 200g lard
- 220ml water
- 1 tsp salt
- 300ml pork stock
- 3-4 gelatine sheets

### Instructions
1. Mix chopped pork shoulder, belly, bacon, and seasonings. Chill for a few hours.
1. Make pastry: Heat water and lard until boiled. Pour into flour and salt mixture. Stir until dough forms.
1. While dough is warm, mold into a cylinder shape (hand-raised) or press into a springform tin.
1. Pack meat filling tightly into the pastry. Roll out lid, place on top, and crimp edges to seal.
1. Cut a small hole in the center of the lid and brush with egg wash.
1. Bake at 180°C (350°F) for 30 mins, then reduce to 160°C (320°F) and bake for 60-90 mins.
1. Dissolve gelatine in warm stock. Once pie is cool but still warm, pour liquid stock through the hole.
1. Chill in the refrigerator overnight before serving cold.

---

## Pork Bake
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4-6 pork chops (about 1-inch thick)
- 1 ½ cups long-grain white rice, uncooked
- 1 can (10.5 oz) cream of mushroom soup
- 1 ½ cups chicken broth
- 1 packet onion soup mix
- Garlic powder, salt, and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C) and grease a 9x13 inch baking dish.
1. In the dish, stir together uncooked rice, soup, broth, and half the onion soup mix.
1. Season pork chops with garlic powder, salt, and pepper. Place on top of the rice.
1. Sprinkle the remaining onion soup mix over the chops.
1. Cover tightly with foil and bake for 30 minutes.
1. Remove foil and bake for another 30 minutes until rice is tender and pork is cooked through.
1. Let rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Pork Shepherd’s Pie
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 2 lbs potatoes, peeled and cubed
- 4 tbsp butter
- ½ cup milk
- 1 cup shredded Cheddar cheese
- 1 medium onion, diced
- 1 large carrot, diced
- ¾ cup frozen peas
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- ¾ cup chicken stock
- 1 tsp dried thyme

### Instructions
1. Boil potatoes until tender. Mash with butter, milk, and half the cheese. Set aside.
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).
1. Sauté onion and carrot in a skillet. Add ground pork and cook until browned.
1. Stir in tomato paste, Worcestershire sauce, thyme, and stock. Simmer until thickened.
1. Stir in frozen peas. Transfer mixture to a baking dish.
1. Spread mashed potatoes over the top and sprinkle with remaining cheese.
1. Bake for 25-30 minutes until golden brown and bubbling.
1. Let rest for 10 minutes before serving.
