## Cheesy Baked Pork
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4-6 pork chops
- 4-5 medium potatoes, thinly sliced
- 2 cups shredded Cheddar cheese
- 1 can (10.5 oz) cream of mushroom soup
- ½ cup milk
- ½ cup sour cream
- 1 onion, thinly sliced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- Salt, pepper, garlic powder, and paprika to taste

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C). Grease a 9x13-inch baking dish.
1. Season and sear pork chops in a skillet until golden. Set aside.
1. Mix soup, milk, sour cream, garlic, and half the cheese.
1. Layer half of the potatoes and onions in the dish, pour half the sauce over. Repeat layers.
1. Cover with foil and bake for 30 minutes.
1. Remove foil, arrange pork chops on top, and sprinkle with remaining cheese.
1. Bake uncovered for 25-30 minutes until potatoes are tender and pork is done.
1. Let rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Pork Bulgogi
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (680g) Pork belly, shoulder, or butt (thinly sliced)
- 1 medium Onion (thinly sliced)
- 3–4 Green Onions (cut into 2-inch pieces)
- 1 tbsp Cooking Oil (vegetable or canola)
- 3 tbsp Gochujang (Korean red chili paste)
- 2 tbsp Gochugaru (Korean red chili flakes)
- 3 tbsp Soy Sauce
- 2 tbsp Sugar (or honey/brown sugar)
- 2 tbsp Mirin (rice wine)
- 1 tbsp Minced Garlic
- 1 tsp Minced Ginger
- 1 tbsp Sesame Oil
- 1/4 tsp Black Pepper
- 2 tbsp Grated Apple or Pear (optional)
- Toasted sesame seeds (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Marinade: In a large mixing bowl, combine gochujang, gochugaru, soy sauce, sugar, mirin, garlic, ginger, sesame oil, pepper, and optional grated fruit. Whisk until smooth.
1. Marinate: Add the thinly sliced pork and the sliced onions to the bowl. Massage the marinade into the meat until every slice is well-coated. Let it sit for at least 30 minutes.
1. Cook: Heat a large skillet or wok over medium-high heat with 1 tablespoon of oil. Once hot, add the pork in a single layer (work in batches if necessary).
1. Sear: Let the pork sear for 2–3 minutes without moving it to get a nice char, then stir-fry for another 4–5 minutes until fully cooked and caramelized.
1. Finish: Toss in the green onions during the last minute of cooking.
1. Serve: Transfer to a plate and garnish with toasted sesame seeds. Serve over steamed white rice.

---

## Tonkotsu Ramen
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 lbs (1.5kg) Pork bones (femurs, trotters, or neck bones)
- 1 large Onion (halved)
- 1 head of Garlic (halved)
- 2-inch piece of Ginger (sliced)
- 1 bunch of Green Onions
- 2 lbs Pork belly (rolled and tied for chashu)
- 1/2 cup Soy sauce
- 1/2 cup Mirin
- 1/2 cup Sake
- 1/4 cup Sugar
- 2 cloves Garlic (for chashu)
- 1-inch Ginger (for chashu)
- 4–6 large Eggs
- 1/4 cup Soy sauce (for tare)
- 2 tbsp Mirin (for tare)
- 1 tsp Salt
- 4–6 portions Fresh or dried ramen noodles
- Garnish: Sliced green onions, wood ear mushrooms, nori (seaweed) sheets, black garlic oil

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Broth: Blanch pork bones in boiling water for 15 minutes. Drain and scrub the bones under cold water to remove scum. Return cleaned bones to the pot with aromatics and fresh water.
1. Simmer: Bring to a rolling boil, then reduce to a steady simmer for 12 hours. Keep bones submerged; add water as needed. Strain the liquid through a fine-mesh sieve once creamy and opaque.
1. Prepare Chashu & Eggs: Sear pork belly, then simmer in a pot with soy sauce, mirin, sake, sugar, garlic, and ginger for 2–3 hours. Boil eggs for 6.5 minutes, peel, and marinate in the chashu liquid for at least 4 hours.
1. Prepare Tare: Combine soy sauce, mirin, and salt in a small saucepan. Simmer for 5 minutes and set aside.
1. Assembly: Add 2–3 tablespoons of Tare to the bottom of each bowl. Pour about 1.5 cups of boiling hot Tonkotsu Broth into the bowl and stir.
1. Noodles & Toppings: Add cooked ramen noodles to the broth. Arrange slices of chashu, a halved marinated egg, green onions, and nori on top. Serve immediately.

---

## Pork Yakitori
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 750g (1.6 lbs) Pork belly (skin removed, cut into 1-inch cubes)
- 2 bunches of Green Onions (negi), cut into 1.5-inch lengths
- 100ml Soy sauce
- 100ml Mirin
- 2.5 tbsp Brown sugar
- 1 clove Garlic (crushed, optional)
- 1 tsp Grated ginger (optional)
- Bamboo skewers (soaked in water for 30 minutes)

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Sauce: Combine soy sauce, mirin, and sugar in a small saucepan. Simmer over medium heat for 10 minutes until it reduces to a glossy glaze.
1. Assemble Skewers: Thread the pork cubes onto the soaked skewers, alternating with pieces of green onion.
1. Grill: Preheat grill to medium-high. Place skewers on the grill and cook for 8–10 minutes total, turning every 2–3 minutes.
1. Basting: During the last 3 minutes of cooking, brush the skewers generously with the thickened sauce (tare) several times to create a caramelized crust.
1. Serve: Drizzle any remaining sauce over the skewers and serve hot. Optionally sprinkle with sesame seeds or shichimi togarashi.

---

## Pork Katsu Curry
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 boneless Pork loin chops (1/2 inch thick)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 1/2 cup All-purpose flour
- 2 large Eggs (beaten)
- 1.5 cups Panko breadcrumbs
- Vegetable oil (for frying)
- 1 large Onion (sliced)
- 2 medium Carrots (chopped)
- 2 medium Potatoes (cubed)
- 3.5 cups Water or chicken broth
- 100g Japanese curry roux (e.g., S&B Golden Curry)
- 4 cups cooked Japanese short-grain rice

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Curry Sauce: Sauté onions in a large pot until translucent. Add carrots and potatoes, sauté for 2 minutes. Pour in water/broth and simmer for 15 minutes until vegetables are tender.
1. Thicken Curry: Turn off heat, break the curry roux into the pot, and stir until dissolved. Simmer on low for another 5 minutes until thickened.
1. Prepare Pork Katsu: Tenderize pork chops and season with salt and pepper. Dredge in flour, dip in egg, and coat firmly with Panko.
1. Fry Katsu: Heat 1/2 inch of oil in a skillet to 340°F (170°C). Fry pork for 3–4 minutes per side until golden brown. Drain on a wire rack and slice into strips.
1. Assembly: Place rice on one half of a plate. Lay the sliced pork katsu next to the rice. Ladle the hot curry sauce over the other half of the plate.

---

## Hainanese Pork Rice
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g Pork loin or shoulder (sliced into 1cm chops)
- 1 tbsp Light soy sauce
- 1 tsp Five-spice powder
- 1 tsp Sesame oil
- 1/2 tsp Sugar
- 1 Egg (for marinade)
- Pinch of White pepper
- 1/2 cup All-purpose flour
- 1-2 Eggs (for coating)
- 15-20 Cream crackers (crushed into fine crumbs)
- 1 Onion (sliced)
- 1 Tomato (wedged)
- 1/2 cup Frozen peas
- 1 cup Chicken stock
- 3 tbsp Tomato ketchup
- 2 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tbsp Sugar (for sauce)
- 1 tbsp Cornstarch (mixed with 2 tbsp water)

### Instructions
1. Marinate Pork: Pound pork slices to tenderize. Mix with soy sauce, five-spice, sesame oil, sugar, egg, and white pepper. Marinate for at least 30 minutes.
1. Bread Pork: Coat each piece of pork in flour, then dip into the egg wash, and finally press firmly into the cracker crumbs.
1. Fry: Heat oil to medium-high and fry the pork chops until golden and crispy (3–4 minutes per side). Slice into strips.
1. Make Gravy: Sauté onions until translucent. Add tomatoes and peas. Pour in chicken stock, ketchup, Worcestershire sauce, and sugar. Bring to a boil and thicken with cornstarch slurry.
1. Serve: Place sliced crispy pork over steamed rice and pour the hot gravy over the top.

---

## Pork Korma
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (900g) boneless lean Pork (1-inch cubes)
- 50g Butter or ghee
- 2 large Onions (finely chopped)
- 1.5 tsp Ground ginger
- 1 tsp Minced garlic
- 2 tbsp Ground coriander
- 1/2 tsp Mild chili powder
- 1/4 tsp Ground cinnamon
- 1/4 tsp Ground mace
- 450ml Natural plain yogurt
- 50g Ground almonds
- 150ml Double cream (heavy cream)
- 1 tsp Salt
- Fresh cilantro (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Sauté Base: Melt butter/ghee in a large pot. Fry onions until golden brown. Stir in ginger, garlic, chili powder, and ground coriander for 1 minute.
1. Brown Pork: Add pork cubes and cook until browned on all sides.
1. Add Yogurt: Stir in salt and 4 tablespoons of yogurt. Cook until liquid evaporates. Repeat this process, adding 4 tbsp at a time, until all yogurt is incorporated.
1. Finish Sauce: Mix ground almonds and cream together, then stir into the pork. Add cinnamon and mace.
1. Simmer: Bring to a gentle boil, then simmer covered on low for 25–30 minutes until pork is tender. Add a splash of water if the sauce is too thick.
1. Serve: Garnish with fresh cilantro and serve with basmati rice or naan.

---

## Pork Manchurian
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) Pork (bite-sized cubes)
- 1 tsp Ginger (finely chopped)
- 1 tsp Garlic (finely chopped)
- 1 tsp Turmeric powder
- 1.5 tbsp Chili powder
- 1 tsp Vinegar
- 1 tbsp Oil (for marinade)
- Salt to taste
- 3 tbsp Oil (for sautéing)
- 2 medium Onions (diced)
- 1 tsp Ginger paste
- 1 tsp Garlic paste
- 2–3 Green chilies (sliced)
- 1/2 cup Capsicum (cubed, optional)
- 2 tbsp Soy sauce
- 2 tbsp Tomato sauce/ketchup
- 2 tbsp Cornstarch (mixed with water slurry)
- Fresh coriander or spring onions (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Marination: Mix pork with ginger, garlic, turmeric, chili powder, vinegar, oil, and salt. Marinate for at least 2 hours.
1. Pre-Cook: Cook marinated pork in a pot until tender. Reserve any liquid released during cooking.
1. Sauté: Heat oil in a wok. Sauté onions until translucent. Add ginger paste, garlic paste, and green chilies. Sauté for 2 minutes.
1. Build Sauce: Add capsicum (if using). Stir in cornstarch slurry and reserved pork liquid. Simmer until thickened, then add soy sauce and tomato sauce.
1. Combine: Toss the cooked pork into the sauce until well-coated. Cook for 5–10 minutes on low heat.
1. Serve: Garnish with coriander or spring onions and serve hot with fried rice or noodles.

---

## Pork Laksa
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 300g diced Pork (loin or fillet)
- 225g Fresh hokkien noodles
- 1/4 cup Store-bought Laksa paste
- 400ml can light Coconut milk
- 2 cups Boiling water
- 1 bunch Baby bok choy (stems sliced, leaves shredded)
- 100g Bean sprouts
- 2 tbsp Lemon or lime juice
- 3 tsp Fish sauce
- Fresh coriander and 1 sliced red chilli (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Simmer Base: In a large saucepan, combine coconut milk and laksa paste. Cover and simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Build Broth: Add boiling water, citrus juice, and fish sauce. Cover and simmer for 3 minutes.
1. Prepare Noodles: Soak hokkien noodles in boiling water for 3 minutes. Drain and divide among four serving bowls.
1. Cook Pork & Greens: Add bok choy stems and diced pork to the laksa broth. Cook covered for 3 minutes. Stir in shredded leaves and cook for 2 minutes.
1. Assemble: Place half of the bean sprouts in the bowls. Ladle hot soup and pork over the noodles.
1. Serve: Top with remaining bean sprouts, coriander, and sliced chilli.

---

## Pork Pad Thai
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs boneless Pork loin (thinly sliced)
- 1 lb uncooked medium Rice stick noodles
- 2 Eggs (beaten)
- 8 oz Fresh bean sprouts
- 3/4 cup Cubed tofu
- 1/3 cup Peanut or vegetable oil
- 1/4 cup Minced garlic
- 1/3 cup Sugar
- 1/4 cup Thai fish sauce
- 1/4 cup Fresh lime juice and zest
- 1/2 cup Bias-cut Green onions
- 1/4 cup Ground roasted peanuts
- Fresh cilantro and lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Prepare Noodles: Soak rice noodles in hot water for about 30 minutes until softened but still firm. Drain.
1. Stir-Fry: Heat oil in a wok over high heat. Add pork and garlic, stir-fry for 3 minutes until cooked through.
1. Season: Stir in sugar, fish sauce, lime juice, and zest. Mix well.
1. Scramble Eggs: Push pork to the sides, pour eggs into the center, and cook for 2–3 minutes until set. Toss with pork.
1. Combine: Add drained noodles, bean sprouts, and tofu. Toss over medium-high heat until noodles are tender and dish is heated through.
1. Serve: Top with green onions and peanuts. Serve with lime wedges and cilantro.

---

## Pork Sate Lilit
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) Minced pork
- 2 tbsp Light palm sugar
- 2 tbsp Tamarind paste
- 1 tbsp Coconut milk
- 2 Kaffir lime leaves (thinly sliced)
- 36 Skewers (Lemongrass stalks or bamboo sticks)
- Spice Paste: 2 onions, 4 garlic cloves, 4 bird's-eye chillies, 20g ginger, 20g galangal, 10g turmeric, 1 tsp peppercorns, 2 cloves, 1 nutmeg, 5g coriander seeds, 2 candlenuts
- Fried onion flakes (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Prepare Spice Paste: Grind all spice paste ingredients into a smooth, fragrant paste using a food processor or mortar and pestle.
1. Combine: Mix minced pork with the spice paste, palm sugar, tamarind, coconut milk, lime leaves, and salt until sticky and well-combined.
1. Shape Satay: Take about 30g of the mixture and wrap it around the end of a skewer (lemongrass or bamboo), covering about 3 inches.
1. Grill: Heat a grill to medium-high. Grill skewers for 4–5 minutes per side until golden brown and cooked through.
1. Serve: Garnish with fried onion flakes and serve with Sambal Matah or jasmine rice.

---

## Pork Omelette
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 large eggs
- 1/2 lb (225g) ground pork
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 small shallot, minced
- 5-6 stalks of scallions, chopped
- 2 tbsp fish sauce
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 2 tbsp neutral cooking oil (canola, vegetable, or avocado oil)

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, combine the ground pork with the minced garlic, shallots, fish sauce, salt, and pepper. Mix well.
1. Crack the 6 eggs into the bowl with the pork. Beat the eggs and pork together until the meat is broken up and evenly distributed. Stir in the chopped scallions.
1. Place a large (10-12 inch) non-stick skillet over medium-high heat and add the cooking oil.
1. Once the oil is hot, pour in the entire egg and pork mixture. Use a spatula to gently push the egg around the center for the first minute to help it cook faster.
1. Let the omelette sit undisturbed for 4-5 minutes until the bottom is golden brown and the top is mostly set.
1. If the omelette is too large to flip in one piece, cut it into quarters with your spatula and flip each section individually. Cook the second side for another 3-4 minutes until golden brown and the pork is fully cooked through.

---

## Pork Scramble
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork sausage
- 10 oz package frozen home fries or diced potatoes
- 1/3 cup green bell pepper, chopped
- 1/3 cup red bell pepper, chopped
- 8 large eggs
- 1/2 cup milk
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. In a large skillet over medium heat, add the sausage, potatoes, and chopped peppers. Crumble the sausage as it cooks.
1. Continue cooking until the sausage is fully browned and the potatoes are tender and slightly crispy.
1. While the sausage mixture is cooking, whisk together the eggs and milk in a small bowl until well combined.
1. Pour the egg mixture directly over the sausage and potatoes in the skillet.
1. Stir gently and constantly until the eggs are cooked through and set.
1. Serve warm.

---

## Pork Sandwich Melt
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pulled pork (store-bought or leftover)
- 1 cup barbecue sauce
- 8 slices of Texas-style toast or sourdough
- 16 slices of Colby Jack or Cheddar cheese (4 per sandwich)
- 2 cups prepared coleslaw (optional)
- 4 tbsp softened butter

### Instructions
1. In a saucepan over low heat, combine the pulled pork and BBQ sauce. Stir often for about 15 minutes until heated through.
1. Butter one side of each bread slice.
1. Place 4 slices of bread butter-side down on a griddle or large skillet. Top each with 2 slices of cheese, 1/2 cup of the warm BBQ pork, 1/2 cup of coleslaw (if using), and 2 more slices of cheese.
1. Top with the remaining bread slices, butter-side up.
1. Cook over medium-low heat for 4-5 minutes per side until the bread is golden brown and the cheese is fully melted.

---

## Pork Panini
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 slices (1/3" thick) cooked boneless pork roast (approx. 8 oz)
- 8 slices sourdough bread
- 1 cup shredded mozzarella cheese
- 2 tomatoes, sliced
- 1/3 cup mayonnaise
- 1/3 cup chopped fresh basil
- 1 egg, beaten
- 1/3 cup plain dry breadcrumbs
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- Cooking spray

### Instructions
1. In a small bowl, stir together the mayonnaise and chopped fresh basil. Set aside.
1. Dip each slice of cooked pork into the beaten egg, then press into the breadcrumbs until evenly coated.
1. Heat olive oil in a large nonstick skillet over medium heat. Cook breaded pork for about 2 minutes per side until golden brown and crispy. Transfer to a plate.
1. Spread the basil mayo on one side of all 8 bread slices. On 4 of the slices, layer sliced tomatoes, the crispy pork, and mozzarella cheese. Top with remaining bread slices.
1. Lightly coat the skillet with cooking spray and heat over medium-low heat. Grill sandwiches for about 3 minutes per side, pressing down slightly, until toasted and cheese is melted.

---

## Pork Flatbread
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4-6 large flatbreads or Naan
- 1.5 lbs leftover pulled pork
- 1 cup BBQ sauce (plus extra for drizzling)
- 2 cups shredded Cheddar or Monterey Jack cheese
- 1 small red onion, thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup pickled jalapeños
- Chopped green onions or fresh cilantro for garnish

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven or grill to 425°F (220°C).
1. In a bowl, toss the pulled pork with about 1/2 cup of BBQ sauce until evenly coated.
1. Lay flatbreads on a baking sheet. Spread a thin layer of BBQ sauce on each, then top with the sauced pork, shredded cheese, and red onions.
1. Bake for 10-12 minutes, or until the cheese is bubbly and the edges of the flatbread are crisp.
1. Remove from oven. Top with jalapeños, a drizzle of extra sauce, and a sprinkle of green onions or cilantro.

---

## Pork Pizza
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pizza dough
- 1/2 cup barbecue sauce (plus 1-2 tbsp for tossing)
- 1 to 1.5 cups cooked pulled pork, shredded
- 1.5 to 2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese
- 1/2 small red onion, thinly sliced
- 1 jalapeno, thinly sliced (optional)
- 2 green onions, sliced for garnish
- Fresh cilantro for garnish

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 475°F (245°C).
1. Toss the shredded pulled pork with 1-2 tablespoons of BBQ sauce.
1. On a lightly floured surface, roll or stretch the dough into a 12-inch circle. Transfer to a pizza pan or parchment paper.
1. Spread 1/2 cup BBQ sauce evenly over the dough. Sprinkle about 1 cup of cheese over the sauce.
1. Distribute the pulled pork, red onions, and jalapenos over the cheese. Top with the remaining cheese.
1. Bake for 12-15 minutes until the crust is golden brown and the cheese is bubbly.
1. Garnish with green onions and cilantro. Let sit for 2-3 minutes before slicing.

---

## Pork Toast
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 150g (1/3 lb) ground pork
- 7 slices white sandwich bread, crusts removed and cut into 4 squares each
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 6 cilantro stems, finely chopped
- 1/2 tsp ground white pepper
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1/2 tsp sugar
- 1/2 large egg, beaten
- 2 tbsp toasted sesame seeds (optional)
- Neutral oil for frying

### Instructions
1. In a mortar and pestle or small food processor, pound garlic, cilantro, and white pepper into a fine paste.
1. In a mixing bowl, combine ground pork, the garlic paste, soy sauce, sugar, and the half-beaten egg. Mix until slightly sticky.
1. Spread about 1 teaspoon of the pork mixture onto each square of bread. Press down firmly. Sprinkle with sesame seeds if using.
1. Heat oil in a skillet to 350°F (175°C). Place bread meat-side down first. Fry for 1-2 minutes until pork is cooked.
1. Flip and fry the bread side for 30 seconds until golden. Drain on paper towels.
1. Serve immediately with sweet chili sauce or cucumber relish.

---

## Pork Wrap Melt
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb leftover pulled pork
- 1/2 cup BBQ sauce
- 4 large flour tortillas
- 1 cup sharp cheddar cheese, shredded
- 1 cup prepared coleslaw
- 1 large onion, thinly sliced
- 1 tbsp unsalted butter
- Salt to taste
- Cooking spray

### Instructions
1. Heat a skillet over medium-low heat and add butter. Add sliced onions and a pinch of salt. Cook, stirring occasionally, for 30-40 minutes until caramelized.
1. Mix the pulled pork with BBQ sauce until well coated.
1. Lay a tortilla flat. Spread 1/4 cup coleslaw in the center. Top with 1/4 of the pork mixture, 1/4 of the caramelized onions, and 1/4 cup cheese.
1. Fold the sides toward the center and roll tightly into a burrito shape. Place seam-side down.
1. Heat a skillet over medium heat with cooking spray. Grill wraps seam-side down first for 2-3 minutes per side until golden and cheese is melted.

---

## Pork Rice Bowl
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 6
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork
- 1/4 cup low-sodium soy sauce
- 1 tbsp corn starch
- 1/2 tsp ginger powder
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp sugar
- 3 cups cooked rice (brown or jasmine)
- 1 cup cucumber, sliced
- 1 cup carrot, shredded
- 1/2 cup cilantro, chopped
- 1/2 cup low-fat sour cream mixed with 1-2 tsp Sriracha

### Instructions
1. In a large skillet over medium-high heat, brown the ground pork until cooked through. Drain any excess fat.
1. In a small bowl, whisk together soy sauce, corn starch, ginger powder, garlic powder, and sugar.
1. Pour the sauce mixture into the skillet with the pork. Cook for 1 minute until thickened and coating the meat.
1. Divide cooked rice into 6 bowls.
1. Top each bowl with glazed pork, cucumber slices, shredded carrots, and cilantro.
1. Drizzle with the spicy sriracha-sour cream mixture and serve.

---

## Pork Stir-Fry Noodles
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Original Servings:** 4
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground pork or thinly sliced pork tenderloin
- 8 oz dried egg noodles or rice noodles
- 2 tbsp sesame oil
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1-inch piece ginger, minced
- 2-3 cups mixed stir-fry vegetables (broccoli, peppers, carrots)
- 4 tbsp soy sauce
- 3-4 tbsp sweet chili sauce
- 1 tbsp brown sugar
- 2-3 green onions, chopped

### Instructions
1. Cook noodles according to package instructions. Drain and set aside.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a large wok over high heat. Brown the pork until crispy (5-8 minutes).
1. Add remaining oil, garlic, ginger, and the white parts of green onions. Cook for 1 minute.
1. Add mixed vegetables and stir-fry for 3-4 minutes until crisp-tender.
1. Whisk together soy sauce, sweet chili sauce, and brown sugar. Pour over the pork and vegetables.
1. Add cooked noodles to the pan and toss for 1-2 minutes until well-coated.
1. Garnish with green onion tops and serve.

# Category: Beef Dishes

## Chicken Fried Steak
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4–6 cube steaks (about 1.5 lbs total)
- 2 cups all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs
- 1/2 cup whole milk or buttermilk
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 1/2 tsp paprika
- Pinch of cayenne pepper
- Vegetable oil for frying
- For the White Gravy:
- 4 tbsp pan drippings
- 4 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 2 cups whole milk
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Pound the cube steaks with a meat mallet until they are about 1/4-inch thick.
1. In one shallow bowl, whisk together the flour, salt, pepper, garlic powder, paprika, and cayenne.
1. In a second bowl, beat the eggs and milk together.
1. Dredge each steak in the flour mixture, dip into the egg mixture, and then back into the flour mixture, pressing firmly.
1. Heat 1/2 inch of oil in a large skillet to 350°F. Fry steaks in batches for 3–4 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. To make gravy: Pour off all but 4 tbsp of oil. Whisk in 4 tbsp of flour and cook for 1-2 minutes.
1. Slowly whisk in the milk and simmer until thickened. Season with salt and plenty of black pepper.
1. Serve the steaks smothered in the hot gravy.

---

## Beef Schnitzel
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4 thin-cut beef steaks (top round or sirloin)
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1 1/2 cups breadcrumbs (Panko or traditional)
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 1/2 tsp smoked paprika
- 1/2 cup vegetable oil for frying
- Lemon wedges and fresh parsley for garnish

### Instructions
1. Place beef steaks between plastic wrap and pound with a mallet to 1/4 inch thickness.
1. Set up a dredging station with three bowls: flour mixed with seasonings, beaten eggs, and breadcrumbs.
1. Coat each steak in flour (shake off excess), dip in egg wash, and press firmly into breadcrumbs.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Fry steaks in batches for 2–3 minutes per side until golden and crispy.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve immediately with fresh lemon wedges and parsley.

---

## Crispy Beef Strips
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb beef (sirloin, flank, or ribeye), sliced into thin strips
- 1/2 cup cornstarch
- 1 egg white
- Vegetable oil for frying
- For the Sauce:
- 3 tbsp soy sauce
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 2 tbsp hoisin sauce
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp sweet chili sauce
- 1/4 cup water
- 1 tsp cornstarch (mixed into sauce)
- Sesame seeds and green onions for garnish

### Instructions
1. Slice beef against the grain into very thin strips.
1. Toss beef with egg white, then dredge in cornstarch until well-coated.
1. Heat 1/2 inch of oil in a wok or skillet to 375°F. Fry beef in small batches for 2–3 minutes until very crispy.
1. Drain beef on paper towels.
1. In a separate skillet, whisk sauce ingredients together and bring to a simmer until thickened.
1. Quickly toss the crispy beef in the sauce until evenly coated.
1. Garnish with sesame seeds and green onions. Serve immediately.

---

## Beef Milanese
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb top round or sirloin steaks, sliced very thin
- 1/2 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, whisked
- 1 cup breadcrumbs
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 2 tbsp grated Parmesan cheese
- 1/2 cup vegetable oil

### Instructions
1. Pound the steaks to about 1/8-inch thickness using a meat mallet.
1. Prepare breading station: flour mixed with salt/pepper, whisked eggs, and breadcrumbs mixed with garlic powder and Parmesan.
1. Dredge each steak in flour, dip in egg, and press firmly into the breadcrumb mixture.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Fry steaks for 2–3 minutes per side until golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with lemon wedges or a side of pasta.

---

## Breaded Beef Cutlets
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 1/2 lbs thin-sliced beef (top round or cube steak)
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 large eggs, beaten
- 1 cup breadcrumbs or crushed saltine crackers
- 1/2 cup vegetable oil

### Instructions
1. Pound the beef cutlets until thin and even. Season with salt, pepper, and garlic powder.
1. Set up three bowls for breading: flour, beaten eggs, and breadcrumbs/crackers.
1. Coat each cutlet in flour, then egg, and finally the breadcrumbs, pressing to adhere.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Fry cutlets for 3–4 minutes per side until the coating is golden and the meat is cooked through.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve warm.

---

## Beef Tempura
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.3 lbs beef fillet or sirloin, cut into 1x3cm strips
- 2 tsp grated ginger
- 1 tsp sesame oil
- 1/4 cup plain flour (for dusting)
- For the Batter:
- 1/2 cup plain flour
- 1/2 cup cornstarch
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 large egg
- 2/3 cup ice-cold water
- Oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Marinate beef strips with ginger and sesame oil for 20 minutes.
1. Heat oil in a deep pot to 350°F.
1. Whisk egg and ice-cold water together, then stir in the flour, cornstarch, and salt until just combined (lumps are okay).
1. Dust marinated beef strips in the extra flour, then dip into the tempura batter.
1. Carefully drop beef into hot oil and fry in batches for 3–4 minutes until light golden and crispy.
1. Drain on a wire rack to maintain crispness.

---

## Crispy Chili Beef
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb sirloin or flank steak, sliced into thin strips
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1/2 cup cornflour (cornstarch)
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp Chinese five spice
- Vegetable oil for frying
- For the Sauce:
- 3–4 tbsp sweet chili sauce
- 2 tbsp ketchup
- 2 tbsp rice wine vinegar
- 2 tbsp light soy sauce
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1-2 red chilies, sliced

### Instructions
1. Toss beef strips with egg, salt, pepper, and five spice. Coat thoroughly with cornflour.
1. Heat oil in a wok and fry beef in batches until very crispy and dark brown (3-5 mins). Drain.
1. Remove most oil, leaving 1 tbsp. Sauté garlic, ginger, and chilies.
1. Add sauce ingredients and simmer until thickened and glossy.
1. Quickly toss the crispy beef in the sauce and serve immediately over rice.

---

## Beef Croquettes
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb minced beef
- 1 medium onion, finely chopped
- 2 tbsp butter or oil
- 3 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup beef stock
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, chopped
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- For the Coating:
- 1/2 cup flour
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1 cup breadcrumbs
- Vegetable oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Brown the minced beef in a skillet, then remove with a slotted spoon.
1. Sauté onion in the remaining fat until soft.
1. Stir in 3 tbsp flour, then gradually whisk in beef stock until it forms a thick sauce.
1. Mix in the beef, Worcestershire sauce, parsley, salt, and pepper. Chill the mixture for 1–2 hours.
1. Shape the chilled mixture into cylinders.
1. Dredge each cylinder in flour, dip in egg, and coat with breadcrumbs.
1. Fry in 350°F oil for 3–4 minutes until golden brown.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with mustard or gravy.

---

## Beef Nuggets
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.1 lbs (1/2 kg) ground beef
- 2 tsp onion powder
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp salt
- 1 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp paprika
- 1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- For Breading:
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 egg, beaten
- 1 cup breadcrumbs
- Oil for deep frying

### Instructions
1. Mix ground beef with seasonings and Parmesan cheese.
1. Shape the mixture into small nugget sizes.
1. Bread each nugget by dredging in flour, dipping in egg, and coating in breadcrumbs.
1. Chill breaded nuggets for 30 minutes in the refrigerator.
1. Deep fry in 350°F oil for 3–5 minutes until golden brown and cooked through.
1. Drain on paper towels and serve with dipping sauce.

---

## Beef Katsu
- **Style:** Fried & Crispy Beef
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 large sirloin steaks (about 1/2 lb each)
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1 cup Panko breadcrumbs
- Vegetable oil for frying
- For Katsu Sauce: 1/4 cup ketchup, 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce, 1 tbsp soy sauce, 1/2 tsp sugar

### Instructions
1. Pound steaks to 1/2-inch thickness and season with salt and pepper.
1. Set up breading station with flour, beaten egg, and Panko.
1. Dredge steak in flour, dip in egg, and press firmly into Panko.
1. Heat 1-2 inches of oil to 350°F. Fry steaks for 2–3 minutes per side until golden.
1. Let rest for 1-2 minutes, then slice into 1/2-inch strips.
1. Serve with katsu sauce and shredded cabbage.

---

## Beef Bourguignon
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3 lbs (1.4 kg) beef chuck or brisket, cut into 2-inch chunks
- 6 oz (170g) thick-cut bacon or lardons, chopped
- 1 large white onion, diced
- 2 large carrots, sliced into 1/2-inch rounds
- 4–6 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh thyme (or 3–4 sprigs)
- 2 bay leaves
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 3 cups dry red wine (Pinot Noir, Merlot, or Burgundy)
- 2–3 cups beef stock
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 2 tbsp butter
- 1 lb (450g) fresh mushrooms (cremini or button), halved or quartered
- 12–15 small pearl onions (fresh or frozen)
- Chopped fresh parsley for garnish
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Pat the beef chunks dry with paper towels. Season with salt and pepper.
1. In a large Dutch oven, heat olive oil over medium heat. Crisp the bacon, then remove and set aside.
1. Increase heat to medium-high and sear the beef chunks in batches until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté the diced onion and sliced carrots for 5–8 minutes in the same fat. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in tomato paste and flour. Cook for 2 minutes, stirring constantly.
1. Slowly pour in the red wine while scraping the bottom of the pot. Return beef and bacon to the pot.
1. Add enough beef stock to just cover the meat. Add thyme and bay leaves.
1. Cover and cook in a preheated oven at 325°F (160°C) for 2.5 to 3 hours, or simmer on very low heat on the stovetop.
1. While the stew simmers, sauté mushrooms and pearl onions in butter in a separate skillet until golden brown.
1. Stir the mushrooms and pearl onions into the stew 20 minutes before it is finished.
1. Remove bay leaves and thyme sprigs. Garnish with fresh parsley and serve over mashed potatoes or egg noodles.

---

## Beef Stroganoff
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) Sirloin steak, sliced into thin strips against the grain
- 8 oz (225g) Cremini or white button mushrooms, sliced
- 1 medium yellow onion, thinly sliced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp butter
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1.5 cups beef broth
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tsp Dijon mustard
- 1/2 cup full-fat sour cream (at room temperature)
- 12 oz (340g) wide egg noodles, cooked
- Fresh parsley, chopped for garnish
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Season beef strips with salt and pepper. Heat olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat.
1. Sear the beef quickly in batches until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Melt butter in the same skillet. Sauté onions and mushrooms for 5–7 minutes until golden brown.
1. Add minced garlic and cook for 30 seconds. Sprinkle flour over the mixture and stir for 1–2 minutes.
1. Slowly pour in beef broth, Worcestershire sauce, and Dijon mustard. Simmer for 3–5 minutes until thickened.
1. Reduce heat to low. Stir the browned beef and its juices back into the skillet for 1 minute.
1. Remove from heat and stir in the sour cream until smooth. Do not boil once sour cream is added.
1. Serve over hot egg noodles and garnish with fresh parsley.

---

## Bulalo
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1 kg) beef shank (bulalo cut) with bone marrow
- 2 ears of sweet corn, cut into pieces
- 1 small head of cabbage, quartered
- 1 cup Baguio beans (green beans), trimmed
- 1 medium yellow onion, quartered
- 2 medium potatoes, halved (optional)
- 2 stalks of onion leeks, sliced (optional)
- 8–10 cups of water
- 1 tbsp whole black peppercorns
- 3–4 tbsp fish sauce (patis), adjusted to taste
- Salt to taste

### Instructions
1. Parboil beef shanks for 5–10 minutes. Drain and rinse the meat to remove impurities.
1. Return cleaned beef to the pot with fresh water, onions, and peppercorns. Bring to a boil.
1. Lower heat and simmer for 1.5 to 2.5 hours until meat is fork-tender (or 30-45 mins in a pressure cooker).
1. Periodically skim off any foam or excess fat from the surface.
1. Add corn and potatoes. Simmer for 10–15 minutes until cooked through.
1. Season with fish sauce and salt to taste.
1. Add Baguio beans and cabbage. Cook for another 2–3 minutes until vegetables are tender-crisp.
1. Serve hot with steamed white rice and a side of fish sauce with calamansi and chili.

---

## Sinigang na Baka
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) beef brisket, ribs, or shank, cubed
- 2–3 medium tomatoes, quartered
- 1 large onion, quartered
- 2–3 pieces taro (gabi), peeled and halved
- 1 medium radish (labanos), sliced
- 10–12 pieces okra
- 1 bundle string beans (sitaw), cut into 2-inch lengths
- 1–2 pieces long green chili (siling haba)
- 1 bundle water spinach (kangkong) or bok choy
- 8–10 cups water or rice washing
- 1 packet (40g) tamarind soup base mix (Sinigang mix)
- Fish sauce (patis) and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Combine beef and water in a large pot. Bring to a boil and skim off the scum.
1. Add onions and tomatoes. Cover and simmer for 1.5 to 2 hours until beef is very tender.
1. Add taro and radish. Cook for 8–10 minutes until taro is soft.
1. Stir in the tamarind soup mix, fish sauce, and black pepper. Adjust seasonings to taste.
1. Add string beans, okra, and green chilies. Simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Add water spinach or bok choy. Turn off heat immediately and cover to wilt the greens.
1. Serve hot with steamed white rice and fish sauce with chili.

---

## Nilagang Baka
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1 kg) beef shank, brisket, or ribs
- 2–3 medium potatoes, quartered
- 1 small cabbage, quartered
- 1 bunch pechay (bok choy)
- 10–12 pieces green beans (Baguio beans)
- 1 large white onion, quartered
- 2 pieces corn on the cob, cut into parts (optional)
- 8–10 cups water
- 2 tbsp fish sauce (patis)
- 1 tsp whole black peppercorns
- Salt to taste

### Instructions
1. In a large pot, combine beef, water, onion, and peppercorns. Bring to a boil.
1. Skim off the gray foam from the surface for a clear broth.
1. Lower heat, cover, and simmer for 1.5 to 2 hours until beef is fork-tender.
1. Add corn and potatoes. Cook for about 10 minutes until potatoes are nearly soft.
1. Pour in fish sauce and add salt to taste.
1. Add green beans, cabbage, and pechay. Cover and cook for 2–3 minutes.
1. Serve hot with steamed white rice and fish sauce with calamansi.

---

## Beef Pho
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 4–5 lbs beef bones and 1 lb beef brisket or chuck
- 2 medium yellow onions, halved and charred
- 4-inch piece of ginger, sliced and charred
- 5 star anise, 1 cinnamon stick, 4 cloves, 1 tbsp coriander seeds
- 1/4 cup fish sauce
- 1 oz rock sugar or 2 tbsp brown sugar
- 1.5–2 lbs flat rice noodles (banh pho)
- 1 lb sirloin or flank steak, sliced paper-thin
- 1/2 yellow onion, sliced paper-thin
- 3 scallions, thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup cilantro, chopped
- Bean sprouts, Thai basil, lime wedges, jalapeños for garnish
- Hoisin and Sriracha for serving
- 6 quarts water

### Instructions
1. Parboil bones for 10 minutes, then drain and rinse thoroughly.
1. Char onions and ginger. Toast star anise, cinnamon, cloves, and coriander seeds.
1. Return bones to pot with 6 quarts of water, charred aromatics, toasted spices, brisket, sugar, and salt.
1. Simmer for 3–6 hours, skimming fat periodically. Remove brisket after 1.5 hours, chill and slice.
1. Cook rice noodles according to package instructions and divide into bowls.
1. Top noodles with brisket slices, raw thin beef slices, onions, scallions, and cilantro.
1. Bring broth to a rolling boil and ladle over the beef to cook it instantly.
1. Serve immediately with a side platter of fresh herbs, sprouts, lime, and sauces.

---

## Beef Ramen
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) sirloin or flank steak, thinly sliced
- 4 cups (1 liter) beef broth
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, grated
- 3 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp fish sauce (optional)
- 1 tsp sugar
- 2–3 packs ramen noodles
- 2–4 large eggs, soft-boiled
- 1 cup sliced mushrooms
- 2 cups baby spinach or bok choy
- 1 tbsp vegetable or sesame oil
- Sliced green onions and sesame seeds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Boil eggs for 6-7 minutes for a soft yolk, then peel and slice in half.
1. Heat oil in a pot and sear steak slices for 1-2 minutes. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté garlic, ginger, and mushrooms for 2-3 minutes.
1. Add beef broth, soy sauce, fish sauce, and sugar. Simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Add ramen noodles to the broth and cook for 2-3 minutes. Stir in spinach at the last minute.
1. Divide noodles and broth into bowls. Top with seared beef, egg, green onions, and sesame seeds.

---

## Goulash
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs beef chuck or shanks, 1-inch cubes
- 3 large onions, diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 carrots, diced
- 2 medium potatoes, cubed
- 1 red bell pepper, diced
- 2 tomatoes, diced
- 1/4 cup sweet Hungarian paprika
- 1 tsp caraway seeds
- 2 bay leaves
- 4–5 cups beef broth
- 2 tbsp lard, butter, or oil
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Sour cream for serving (optional)

### Instructions
1. Brown beef cubes in fat in a large Dutch oven. Set aside.
1. Sauté onions until starting to brown. Add garlic and bell peppers; cook for 2 minutes.
1. Remove from heat briefly and stir in the paprika.
1. Return beef to pot. Add tomatoes, broth, caraway seeds, and bay leaves. Bring to a boil.
1. Lower heat, cover, and simmer for 1.5 to 2 hours until beef is tender.
1. Stir in potatoes and carrots. Simmer for another 20–30 minutes until soft.
1. Remove bay leaves and serve with a dollop of sour cream and crusty bread.

---

## Beef Caldereta
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1kg) beef chuck, brisket, or short ribs, cubed
- 4–5 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 1 cup tomato sauce
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 2–3 cups beef broth or water
- 1 can (3–4 oz) liver spread
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1–2 tbsp fish sauce (patis)
- 2–3 pieces bay leaves
- 2 medium potatoes, cubed
- 2 medium carrots, sliced
- 1 red and 1 green bell pepper, cut into squares
- ½ cup green peas
- ½ cup grated cheese (cheddar or quick-melt)
- 3 tbsp cooking oil
- Salt, pepper, and chili peppers (optional) to taste

### Instructions
1. Brown the beef chunks in oil in a large pot. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté garlic and onions until translucent.
1. Return beef to pot. Add tomato sauce, paste, soy sauce, fish sauce, bay leaves, and broth.
1. Simmer for 1 to 1.5 hours until beef is fork-tender.
1. Add potatoes and carrots. Simmer for 10–15 minutes until soft.
1. Stir in liver spread and grated cheese until sauce is creamy and thick.
1. Add bell peppers, peas, and olives. Cook for 3–5 minutes.
1. Adjust seasonings and serve hot over steamed white rice.

---

## Beef Kare-Kare
- **Style:** Soups & Stews
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (900g) beef chuck, short ribs, or shank, cubed
- 6 cups water or beef broth
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- ¾ cup creamy peanut butter
- 2 tbsp annatto powder dissolved in water
- 3 tbsp toasted rice flour slurry
- 2 medium eggplants, sliced
- 1 bunch string beans (sitao), cut into pieces
- 2 bunches bok choy (pechay)
- 2 tbsp cooking oil
- Shrimp paste (bagoong guisado) for serving
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Boil beef in water until fork-tender (1.5 to 2 hours). Reserve the broth.
1. Sauté garlic and onions in a separate pan. Add beef and sauté for 2 minutes.
1. Pour in 4 cups of the reserved broth and bring to a simmer.
1. Stir in peanut butter and annatto water until fully incorporated.
1. Slowly pour in the rice flour slurry and simmer for 5–10 minutes until thickened.
1. Add string beans and eggplant. Simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Add bok choy and cook for 2–3 minutes until tender but vibrant.
1. Serve hot with a side of sautéed shrimp paste and steamed rice.

---

## Beef Adobo
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs beef chuck, brisket, or short ribs, cut into 1.5-inch cubes
- 1 whole head of garlic, crushed and peeled
- 3–4 dried bay leaves
- ½ cup soy sauce
- ⅓ cup white vinegar (cane or coconut vinegar)
- 1 cup water or beef broth
- 1 tbsp whole black peppercorns
- 1 tbsp brown sugar
- 2 tbsp cooking oil
- Optional: 1 small onion, sliced
- Optional: coconut milk for Adobo sa Gata

### Instructions
1. Marinate the beef in soy sauce, crushed garlic, peppercorns, and bay leaves for at least 30 minutes.
1. Heat oil in a large pot over medium-high heat. Remove beef from marinade (reserve liquid) and sear in batches until browned.
1. Pour reserved marinade and water into the pot. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low. Cover and simmer for 1 to 1.5 hours until beef is fork-tender.
1. Pour in the vinegar and simmer undisturbed for 2–3 minutes to allow the harsh acidity to cook off.
1. Stir in the brown sugar and simmer uncovered for 10–15 minutes until the sauce thickens and becomes glossy.
1. Adjust taste with more sugar or salt if needed. Serve hot over steamed white rice.

---

## Beef Rendang
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1 kg) beef chuck or short ribs, cut into 1.5 to 2-inch cubes
- Spice Paste: 10–12 dried red chilies (soaked), 6–8 shallots, 5 cloves garlic, 2-inch galangal, 2-inch ginger, 1-inch turmeric, 2 stalks lemongrass (white parts only)
- 2 cups (500ml) thick coconut milk
- 2 stalks lemongrass, bruised (green tops)
- 4–6 kaffir lime leaves, torn
- 1 cinnamon stick
- 3 star anise
- 1 tbsp tamarind paste mixed with water
- 2 tbsp palm sugar (Gula Melaka) or brown sugar
- 1 tsp salt
- Kerisik: ½ cup toasted grated coconut pounded into an oily paste

### Instructions
1. Blend all Spice Paste ingredients into a smooth paste.
1. Heat oil in a heavy-bottomed pot. Sauté the spice paste, cinnamon, star anise, and bruised lemongrass until oil separates and it smells fragrant.
1. Add beef cubes and cook for 5 minutes until no longer raw on the outside.
1. Pour in coconut milk, tamarind water, kaffir lime leaves, and turmeric leaf. Bring to a gentle boil, then reduce heat to low.
1. Cover loosely and simmer for 2 to 2.5 hours, stirring every 20 minutes.
1. Stir in kerisik, palm sugar, and salt once the sauce has thickened and beef is tender.
1. Remove lid and continue cooking on low, stirring frequently, until liquid evaporates and oil separates. The beef should 'fry' in the spices until dark brown (30–45 mins).
1. Discard whole spices and serve with coconut rice or jasmine rice.

---

## Beef Teriyaki
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs flap meat, skirt steak, or sirloin, sliced across the grain into 1-inch strips
- ⅓ cup soy sauce
- ¼ cup water
- 2 tbsp mirin
- 1 tbsp rice wine vinegar
- ¼ cup granulated sugar + 3 tbsp brown sugar
- ½ tsp garlic powder or 2 cloves minced garlic
- ½ tsp ground ginger or 1 tsp fresh grated ginger
- 1½ tsp cornstarch whisked with 1 tbsp cold water (slurry)
- 1–2 tbsp vegetable oil
- Garnish: Sesame seeds and sliced green onions

### Instructions
1. In a small saucepan, combine soy sauce, water, mirin, vinegar, sugars, garlic, and ginger. Bring to a simmer.
1. Whisk in the cornstarch slurry and simmer for 5–10 minutes until thickened. Let it cool slightly.
1. Stir-fry method: Heat oil in a large skillet or wok over high heat.
1. Add beef strips in batches and sear for 1–2 minutes per side until browned.
1. Pour the teriyaki sauce over the beef and toss for 1 minute until glazed and bubbly.
1. Alternatively, broil the beef for 5–7 minutes on a foil-lined tray.
1. Serve immediately over rice, garnished with sesame seeds and green onions.

---

## Mongolian Beef
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) flank steak, sliced thinly against the grain
- ¼ cup cornstarch
- 2–3 tbsp vegetable oil
- ½ cup soy sauce (low-sodium recommended)
- ½ cup brown sugar, packed
- ½ cup water
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, minced or grated
- 2–3 cloves garlic, minced
- ¼ tsp red pepper flakes (optional)
- Garnish: 2–3 green onions (1-inch pieces), sesame seeds

### Instructions
1. Toss sliced beef with cornstarch until evenly coated. Let sit for 5–10 minutes.
1. Whisk together soy sauce, brown sugar, water, ginger, garlic, and red pepper flakes.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet or wok over medium-high heat. Sear beef in batches for 1–2 minutes per side until crispy. Remove and set aside.
1. Pour sauce mixture into the skillet and bring to a boil. Simmer for 2–3 minutes until it thickens into a glaze.
1. Add seared beef back to the skillet and toss to coat.
1. Stir in green onions and cook for 1 minute until softened.
1. Serve immediately over steamed white rice.

---

## Beef Bulgogi
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) ribeye or top sirloin, thinly sliced against the grain
- 1 small onion, thinly sliced
- 2-3 scallions, cut into 2-inch pieces
- ¼ cup soy sauce
- 2 tbsp brown sugar (or 1 tbsp sugar + 1 tbsp honey)
- 2 tbsp sesame oil
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp ginger, grated
- ½ Asian pear, grated or blended (or red apple/mirin)
- 1 tbsp Gochujang (optional)
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- Garnish: Toasted sesame seeds, extra green onions

### Instructions
1. In a large bowl, whisk together soy sauce, brown sugar, sesame oil, garlic, ginger, pear, gochujang, and pepper.
1. Add beef, onions, and scallions to the marinade. Massage and refrigerate for at least 2 hours (preferably overnight).
1. Heat a cast-iron skillet or wok over high heat with a small amount of oil.
1. Cook beef in single-layer batches for 2–3 minutes per side until slightly charred and cooked through.
1. Garnish with sesame seeds and green onions.
1. Serve with steamed rice and lettuce wraps (ssam).

---

## Beef Tapa
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) beef sirloin, flank steak, or tenderloin, thinly sliced
- ¼ cup soy sauce
- 3 tbsp calamansi juice (or lemon/lime juice)
- 1 head of garlic, finely minced
- 2 tbsp sugar (brown or white)
- ½ tsp salt
- ½ tsp ground black pepper
- ¼ tsp baking soda (optional tenderizer)
- 2–3 tbsp cooking oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, calamansi juice, minced garlic, sugar, salt, and pepper.
1. Add beef slices and massage the marinade into the meat. Refrigerate for 6–24 hours.
1. Heat a large skillet over medium heat with 1 tbsp oil.
1. Add beef and marinade. Simmer until liquid has almost completely evaporated.
1. Add another tbsp of oil, increase heat, and fry for 3–5 minutes until browned and caramelized.
1. Serve as part of Tapsilog with garlic fried rice and a fried egg.

---

## Beef Mechado
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs (1kg) beef chuck roast, cut into 2-inch cubes
- ¼ cup soy sauce
- 3 tbsp calamansi juice (or lemon juice)
- ½ tsp black pepper
- 2 tbsp cooking oil
- 1 medium yellow onion, sliced
- 4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 cup tomato sauce
- 1 cup beef broth or water
- 2 dried bay leaves
- 2 medium potatoes, cubed
- 2 medium carrots, sliced
- 1 red bell pepper, sliced into strips
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Marinate beef in soy sauce, calamansi juice, and pepper for at least 30 minutes.
1. Heat oil in a large pot. Sear beef cubes in batches until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onions and garlic in the same pot until translucent.
1. Return beef to the pot. Add reserved marinade, tomato sauce, broth, and bay leaves.
1. Bring to a boil, then simmer covered for 1 to 1.5 hours until beef is tender.
1. Add potatoes and carrots; simmer for 15–20 minutes.
1. Add bell peppers and cook for another 3–5 minutes. Adjust seasoning and serve hot with rice.

---

## Bistek Tagalog
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) beef sirloin or flank, sliced very thinly
- ¼ cup calamansi juice (or lemon juice)
- ½ cup soy sauce
- 5–6 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 large white or yellow onions, sliced into rings
- ½ tsp ground black pepper
- 1 cup water or beef stock
- 3–4 tbsp cooking oil
- Optional: 1 tsp sugar, 1 large fried potato

### Instructions
1. Marinate beef in soy sauce, calamansi juice, garlic, and pepper for at least 30 minutes.
1. Sauté onion rings in oil until slightly softened but crunchy. Remove and set aside.
1. Drain beef (reserve marinade) and pan-fry slices in batches until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Pour reserved marinade and water into the skillet. Bring to a boil and simmer for 5 minutes.
1. Return beef to the pan and simmer for 2–3 minutes until tender and sauce is absorbed.
1. Transfer to a platter and top with the sautéed onion rings. Serve with steamed rice.

---

## Beef Curry
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 600g (1.3 lbs) diced beef (stewing steak)
- 1 onion, sliced
- 1 red bell pepper and 1 green bell pepper, chopped
- 3 cloves garlic, crushed
- 2 cm fresh ginger, grated
- 1 tsp dried chili flakes
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- 3 tsp smoked paprika
- 3 tsp garam masala
- 400ml passata or tinned tomatoes
- 200ml coconut milk
- 1 tbsp olive oil, salt, pepper
- 2 tbsp fresh coriander (cilantro)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 160°C / 325°F.
1. Soften onions in an ovenproof pan for 5 minutes.
1. Add garlic, ginger, and all spices. Fry for 1 minute.
1. Add passata, coconut milk, beef, and peppers. Bring to a boil.
1. Cover and cook in the oven for 2.5 hours until beef is tender.
1. Stir in fresh coriander before serving with rice and naan.

---

## Massaman Beef Curry
- **Style:** Saucy & Main Dishes
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) beef chuck or stew meat, diced
- 12 oz (340g) potatoes, diced
- 1 medium onion, cut into wedges
- ¼ cup roasted peanuts
- 3 tbsp Massaman curry paste
- 14 oz (400ml) full-fat coconut milk
- 1 cup beef broth or water
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- 1 tbsp tamarind puree
- 1 tbsp palm sugar or brown sugar
- 1 tbsp fish sauce
- Optional whole spices: 1 cinnamon stick, 3-5 cardamom pods, 3 cloves

### Instructions
1. Sear beef chunks in oil until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Fry curry paste (and whole spices) in oil for 1–2 minutes until fragrant.
1. Return beef to pot. Add coconut milk and broth. Simmer covered for 1.5 to 2 hours until beef is tender.
1. Add potatoes, onions, and half the peanuts. Simmer for 20–25 minutes until potatoes are soft.
1. Season with tamarind, sugar, and fish sauce. Adjust to balance sweet, salty, and sour.
1. Garnish with remaining peanuts and serve over jasmine rice.

---

## Spaghetti Bolognese
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) Ground beef (85% or 90% lean)
- 1 medium Onion, finely diced
- 2-3 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 medium Carrot, finely diced
- 1 stalk Celery, finely diced (optional)
- 2 tbsp Olive oil
- 1 can (28 oz / 800g) Crushed tomatoes or tomato passata
- 2 tbsp Tomato paste
- 1/2 cup Dry red wine (e.g., Cabernet or Merlot)
- 1/2 cup Whole milk (optional)
- 1 tsp Dried oregano or Italian seasoning
- 1-2 Dried bay leaves
- 1 tsp Sugar (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 12-16 oz (340-450g) Spaghetti
- Freshly grated Parmesan cheese (for garnish)
- Chopped fresh parsley (for garnish)

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a large skillet or Dutch oven over medium heat. Add onion, carrot, and celery. Cook for 5-7 minutes until soft. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Increase heat to medium-high. Add ground beef and cook until browned, breaking it into crumbles. Drain excess fat.
1. Pour in red wine and simmer for 2-3 minutes, scraping the bottom of the pan.
1. Stir in tomato paste, crushed tomatoes, oregano, bay leaves, sugar, and milk (if using). Reduce heat to low and simmer for at least 20-30 minutes (ideally 1.5-2 hours).
1. While sauce simmers, cook spaghetti in salted boiling water until al dente. Reserve 1/2 cup of pasta water before draining.
1. Remove bay leaves from the sauce. Toss cooked spaghetti into the sauce, adding reserved pasta water if needed to coat perfectly.
1. Serve topped with Parmesan cheese and fresh parsley.

---

## Beef Lasagna
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (80/20 or lean)
- 1 medium onion, finely chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 (15 oz.) can tomato sauce
- 1 (15 oz.) can crushed tomatoes
- 2 (6 oz.) cans tomato paste
- 1/2 cup water
- 2 tbsp sugar
- 2 tsp Italian seasoning
- 1 tsp dried basil
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 15 oz. Ricotta cheese
- 1 large egg
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, minced
- 1/2 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 3 cups shredded Mozzarella cheese (divided)
- 1 tsp Italian seasoning (for cheese mixture)
- 12 lasagna noodles (regular or oven-ready)

### Instructions
1. Prepare Meat Sauce: Brown ground beef and onion in a large skillet. Drain fat. Add garlic, tomato sauce, crushed tomatoes, tomato paste, water, sugar, Italian seasoning, basil, salt, and pepper. Simmer for 30 minutes.
1. Prepare Cheese Mixture: Combine ricotta, egg, parsley, Parmesan, 1 cup of mozzarella, and 1 tsp Italian seasoning in a bowl.
1. Cook Noodles: Boil regular noodles until al dente and drain. (Skip for oven-ready noodles).
1. Assemble: Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C). Spread 1/2 cup sauce in a 9x13 dish. Layer: noodles, 1/3 ricotta mixture, 1/3 meat sauce. Repeat twice. Top with final noodles, remaining sauce, and 2 cups mozzarella.
1. Bake: Cover with foil and bake for 25 minutes. Remove foil and bake for 20-25 minutes until bubbly. Rest for 15-20 minutes before serving.

---

## Beef Biryani
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) stewing beef or chuck, 1-inch cubes
- 2 large onions, thinly sliced
- 2 tbsp ginger-garlic paste
- 3 medium tomatoes, chopped
- 1/2 cup plain Greek yogurt
- 1 tbsp coriander powder
- 1.5 tsp red chili powder
- 1/2 tsp turmeric
- 1 tsp garam masala
- Salt to taste
- Whole spices: 2 bay leaves, 1 cinnamon stick, 4 green cardamoms, 4 cloves, 1 star anise
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
- 1/2 cup fresh mint, chopped
- 1/2 cup oil or ghee
- 3 cups Basmati rice, soaked for 30 minutes
- A pinch of saffron or yellow food coloring mixed with 2 tbsp milk
- 1 tbsp lemon juice

### Instructions
1. Prepare Beef Masala: Fry onions in oil until golden brown. Reserve half. Add whole spices, beef, and ginger-garlic paste to remaining onions; sauté 5 mins. Add tomatoes and ground spices. Simmer covered until beef is tender (45-60 mins). Stir in yogurt, garam masala, and half the herbs.
1. Prepare Rice: Boil water with whole spices and salt. Add rice and parboil until 70-80% done. Drain.
1. Layering: In a heavy pot, layer half the rice, then all the beef masala, fried onions, and herbs. Top with remaining rice. Drizzle saffron milk and lemon juice.
1. Steam (Dum): Cover tightly and cook on lowest heat for 15-20 minutes. Fluff gently before serving.

---

## Beef Fried Rice
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef or thinly sliced flank steak
- 3 cups cold, cooked white rice (jasmine or long-grain)
- 1 cup frozen peas and carrots, thawed
- 1 small white onion, diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, minced
- 2-3 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 3-4 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp sesame oil
- 1 tbsp oyster sauce (optional)
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- 2 green onions, sliced
- Sesame seeds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Brown the beef in 1 tbsp oil until cooked through. Remove and set aside.
1. Scramble eggs in the same skillet until set. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onion, garlic, ginger, and peas/carrots in remaining oil until tender.
1. Add cold rice to the skillet. Stir-fry for 3-5 minutes, breaking up clumps.
1. Add beef and eggs back to the pan. Pour in soy sauce, sesame oil, and oyster sauce. Toss thoroughly for 1-2 minutes.
1. Garnish with green onions and sesame seeds. Serve warm.

---

## Beef Paella
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) Beef (sirloin or ribeye), cut into 1-inch chunks
- 2 cups Bomba or Calasparra rice
- 4 cups Beef broth
- 1 tsp Saffron threads, soaked in 2 tbsp warm broth
- 1 tsp Smoked Paprika
- 3 tbsp Extra virgin olive oil
- 1 large Onion, finely chopped
- 4 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 Red bell pepper, diced
- 2 medium Tomatoes, grated or diced
- 1 cup Frozen peas
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Fresh parsley, chopped
- Lemon wedges

### Instructions
1. Sear beef in olive oil in a wide pan until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onion and bell pepper until softened. Add garlic for 1 minute.
1. Stir in tomatoes and paprika; cook for 3-4 minutes until thickened.
1. Add rice and stir to coat. Pour in beef broth and saffron liquid. Do not stir again.
1. Simmer uncovered on low-medium heat for 15-18 minutes.
1. Nestle beef and peas into the rice when liquid is almost gone.
1. Once liquid is absorbed and a crust (socarrat) forms on the bottom, turn off heat.
1. Cover with a towel and rest for 5-10 minutes.
1. Garnish with parsley and serve with lemon wedges.

---

## Beef Risotto
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g (1.1 lbs) ribeye or sirloin steak
- 1 cup Arborio rice
- 2 cups hot beef stock
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 125g button mushrooms, quartered
- 1 red bell pepper, chopped
- 1 Tbsp olive oil
- 60g butter
- 2 Tbsp tomato paste
- 1/2 cup grated Parmesan cheese
- 1 Tbsp fresh basil, chopped
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Fry the steak in olive oil to desired doneness. Remove and rest.
1. In the same pan, melt butter and sauté onion and garlic until soft.
1. Add mushrooms and red pepper; fry for 2 minutes.
1. Stir in Arborio rice and tomato paste. Season with salt and pepper. Toast for 1-2 minutes.
1. Add hot beef stock one ladle at a time, stirring frequently until liquid is absorbed before adding more.
1. Continue for about 30 minutes until rice is tender and creamy.
1. Stir in Parmesan and basil.
1. Slice rested steak and serve over the risotto.

---

## Beef Jambalaya
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Beef Chuck Roast, 1-inch pieces
- 12 oz Smoked Beef Sausage, sliced
- 1 tbsp Cajun seasoning
- 2 tbsp Vegetable oil (divided)
- 1 cup Onion, diced
- 1/2 cup Green bell pepper, diced
- 1/2 cup Celery, diced
- 1 tbsp Garlic, minced
- 14 oz can Diced tomatoes
- 1 cup Beef broth
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1/2 tsp Salt
- 1/2 tsp Dried thyme or file powder
- 1/4 tsp Red pepper flakes (optional)
- 1 Bay leaf
- 3 cups Cooked white rice
- Hot sauce to taste
- Sliced green onions and parsley for garnish

### Instructions
1. Toss beef and sausage with Cajun seasoning. Brown in 1 tbsp oil; remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onion, bell pepper, celery, and garlic in remaining oil for 7-10 minutes.
1. Stir in tomatoes, broth, Worcestershire, salt, thyme, red pepper, and bay leaf. Add meat back in.
1. Bring to boil, then simmer covered for 20-25 minutes.
1. Discard bay leaf. Stir in cooked rice and simmer 3-5 minutes until liquid is absorbed.
1. Stir in hot sauce and garnish with green onions and parsley.

---

## Beef Pilaf
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) beef chuck or sirloin, 1-inch cubes
- 2.5 to 3 cups long-grain rice (Basmati or Jasmine)
- 2 medium onions, sliced
- 3-5 medium carrots, julienned
- 1 whole head of garlic, top sliced off
- 1/3 to 1/2 cup cooking oil
- 4-5 cups hot water or beef broth
- 2 tsp salt
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp paprika
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp ground coriander (optional)
- 2-3 bay leaves

### Instructions
1. Brown beef in oil in a Dutch oven for 7-10 minutes.
1. Add onions and sauté until golden. Add carrots and cook 5 minutes.
1. Add spices and 2 cups hot water. Simmer covered for 40-45 minutes until meat is tender.
1. Spread rinsed rice evenly over meat and veggies. Do not stir.
1. Pour remaining hot water over rice (1 inch above rice). Add remaining salt and bay leaves.
1. Push garlic head into the center of the rice.
1. Boil, then reduce to low. Cover tightly and cook 15-20 minutes.
1. Rest covered for 10 minutes. Remove garlic and bay leaves, then toss and serve.

---

## Beef Yakisoba
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb fresh Yakisoba noodles
- 10 oz (300g) flank steak or sirloin, thinly sliced
- 2 cups shredded green cabbage
- 1 medium carrot, julienned
- 1/2 onion, thinly sliced
- 4 green onions, 2-inch pieces
- 1 cup sliced shiitake mushrooms (optional)
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil
- 4 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 2 tbsp Soy sauce
- 2 tbsp Oyster sauce
- 1 tbsp Ketchup
- 2 tsp Brown sugar
- Garnish: pickled red ginger, sesame seeds

### Instructions
1. Whisk together Worcestershire sauce, soy sauce, oyster sauce, ketchup, and sugar.
1. Loosen fresh noodles with warm water or cook dried noodles.
1. Sear beef in 1 tbsp oil over high heat until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onions and carrots for 2 minutes. Add cabbage and mushrooms; cook 2-3 minutes.
1. Add noodles and beef back to the pan. Toss together.
1. Pour sauce over the mixture. Toss for 2-3 minutes until coated and sauce thickens. Stir in green onions.
1. Serve garnished with pickled ginger and sesame seeds.

---

## Beef Nasi Goreng
- **Style:** Pasta & Rice
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 350g (12 oz) beef steak, thinly sliced
- 3 tbsp kecap manis (divided)
- 1.5 tbsp vegetable oil (divided)
- 4 cups cooked, chilled Jasmine rice
- 2 tbsp fish sauce or soy sauce
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 red chili, chopped
- 1 onion, chopped
- 1/4 tsp ground ginger
- 1/4 tsp ground turmeric
- 1 cup mung bean sprouts
- 2 carrots, grated
- 4 eggs (for frying)
- Spring onions, coriander, lime wedges for garnish

### Instructions
1. Marinate beef in 1 tbsp kecap manis for 10 minutes.
1. Sear beef in 1/2 tbsp oil over high heat until browned. Remove and set aside.
1. Sauté onion, garlic, chili, ginger, and turmeric in 1 tbsp oil until fragrant.
1. Add chilled rice, 2 tbsp kecap manis, fish sauce, carrots, and bean sprouts. Stir-fry 2-3 minutes on high heat.
1. Return beef to the wok and stir for 1 minute.
1. Serve topped with a fried egg and garnished with spring onions, coriander, and lime.

---

## Beef Shawarma
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs flank steak, flap steak, or top sirloin (sliced very thinly against the grain)
- 1/4 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1/4 cup white wine vinegar (or apple cider vinegar)
- Juice and zest of 1 lemon
- 4 garlic cloves, minced
- 1 medium yellow onion, thinly sliced
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp ground coriander
- 1 tsp sweet paprika
- 1 tsp ground turmeric
- 1/2 tsp ground cinnamon
- 1/2 tsp ground cloves
- 1/2 tsp cayenne pepper (optional)
- 1 tsp kosher salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 4–6 large pita breads or wraps
- Tahini sauce (tahini paste, lemon juice, garlic, and water)
- Diced tomatoes, cucumbers, and fresh parsley for serving
- Optional: Pickled cucumbers, pickled red onions, or hummus

### Instructions
1. Slice the beef into thin, bite-sized strips (about 1/4-inch thick) against the grain.
1. In a large bowl, whisk together olive oil, vinegar, lemon juice, zest, and all spices. Add beef, sliced onions, and minced garlic. Toss to coat and marinate for at least 1 hour.
1. Heat a large cast-iron skillet or grill pan over high heat. Cook beef strips in batches for 8–12 minutes until browned and slightly charred.
1. Warm the pita bread. Spread tahini sauce or hummus inside, add cooked beef, followed by tomato-cucumber salad and pickles.
1. Drizzle with extra tahini sauce and a squeeze of fresh lemon. Serve immediately.

---

## Beef Burrito
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) ground beef (lean 85/15 or 90/10 preferred)
- 1 medium onion, finely chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp smoked paprika
- 1/2 tsp chili powder
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/4 cup beef stock or water
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 5–6 large (10-inch) flour tortillas
- 2 cups shredded Mexican cheese blend
- Optional: Cooked rice, black beans, shredded lettuce, diced tomatoes, sour cream, salsa, or guacamole

### Instructions
1. Heat a large skillet over medium-high heat. Brown ground beef, breaking it into small crumbles. Drain excess fat.
1. Add chopped onion and sauté for 3–5 minutes until softened. Stir in minced garlic and cook for 30–60 seconds.
1. Stir in cumin, paprika, chili powder, salt, pepper, tomato paste, and beef stock. Simmer for 5–10 minutes until thickened.
1. Briefly warm tortillas in a dry skillet or microwave to make them pliable.
1. Place about 1/2 cup of beef mixture in the center of a tortilla. Add cheese and optional toppings.
1. Fold the sides over the filling, then fold the bottom edge tightly and roll away from you to seal.
1. Optional: Toast rolled burritos seam-side down in a hot skillet for 1–2 minutes per side until golden.

---

## Beef Taco
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (85/15 lean-to-fat ratio)
- 1 small yellow onion, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/2 cup water or beef broth
- 1 tbsp olive or vegetable oil
- 1 tsp chili powder
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1/2 tsp paprika
- 1/4 tsp garlic powder
- 1/4 tsp onion powder
- 1/4 tsp dried oregano
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 8–10 hard taco shells or small tortillas
- Toppings: Shredded lettuce, diced tomatoes, shredded cheddar cheese, sour cream, lime wedges

### Instructions
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Brown ground beef for 3–5 minutes. Drain excess fat.
1. Add diced onion and cook for 2–3 minutes. Stir in garlic and cook for 30 seconds.
1. Add chili powder, cumin, paprika, garlic powder, onion powder, oregano, salt, pepper, and tomato paste. Stir to coat.
1. Pour in water or broth. Reduce heat and simmer for 3–5 minutes until thickened.
1. Warm taco shells or tortillas according to package instructions.
1. Fill each shell with beef mixture and add desired toppings. Serve with lime wedges.

---

## Beef Quesadilla
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (90/10 lean preferred)
- 1/2 medium onion, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp taco seasoning
- 1 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/4 cup water
- 4–6 large flour tortillas
- 2 cups shredded cheese (Monterey Jack, Cheddar, or Mexican blend)
- 1–2 tbsp butter or oil for the pan
- Optional: 1/2 bell pepper (diced), 1/2 cup corn kernels

### Instructions
1. In a large skillet, brown ground beef with onions (and peppers if using). Drain excess fat.
1. Add garlic, taco seasoning, tomato paste, and water. Simmer for 2–3 minutes until liquid has mostly evaporated.
1. Wipe the skillet clean and return to medium heat with a small pat of butter.
1. Place a tortilla in the pan. Sprinkle cheese over the surface, then spread 1/2 cup beef mixture over one half.
1. Once cheese begins to melt, fold the empty half over the beef and press down.
1. Cook for 2–3 minutes per side until golden brown and crispy. Repeat for remaining tortillas.

---

## Beef Burger
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g (1.1 lbs) ground beef (80/20 lean-to-fat ratio)
- 1 small onion, very finely chopped
- 1 large egg, lightly beaten
- 1 tsp mixed dried herbs (optional)
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 1 tbsp olive or vegetable oil
- 4 hamburger buns (brioche or white), toasted
- 4 slices of cheese (Cheddar, American, or Swiss)
- Toppings: Lettuce, sliced tomato, red onion rings, pickles
- Condiments: Ketchup, mustard, mayonnaise

### Instructions
1. Sauté chopped onions for 3–5 minutes until soft. Let cool.
1. In a bowl, combine beef, cooled onions, egg, herbs, salt, and pepper. Mix until just combined; do not overwork.
1. Divide into 4 equal portions and shape into patties about 3/4-inch thick.
1. Make a shallow indentation in the center of each patty with your thumb.
1. Optional: Refrigerate patties for 30 minutes to help them stay together.
1. Heat oil in a skillet or preheat grill to medium-high. Cook patties for 5–6 minutes per side.
1. Place a slice of cheese on each patty during the last minute of cooking to melt.
1. Assemble burgers by placing lettuce on the bottom bun, followed by the patty, tomato, onion, and condiments.

---

## Beef Sliders
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (80/20 or 85/15 ratio)
- 12-count package Hawaiian rolls or mini slider buns
- 6–8 slices of Cheddar, American, or Havarti cheese
- 1/2 small yellow onion, finely diced
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce (optional)
- 2 tbsp butter, melted
- 1 tsp sesame seeds or Everything Bagel seasoning
- Optional: Pickle chips, shredded lettuce, sliced tomatoes

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Mix beef with diced onions, salt, pepper, garlic powder, and Worcestershire sauce.
1. Press the beef mixture into a 9x13 inch baking pan in an even layer. Bake for 15–20 minutes. Drain excess grease.
1. Slice the entire pack of rolls in half horizontally. Place the bottom half on a baking sheet.
1. Slide the cooked beef patty onto the buns, layer with cheese, and place the top half of the rolls on top.
1. Brush tops with melted butter and seeds. Bake for 5 minutes until cheese is melted and buns are toasted. Cut into individual sliders.

---

## Beef Empanada
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (90% lean)
- 1 large onion, finely chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tbsp sweet paprika
- 2 tsp dried oregano
- 1/2 cup sliced green olives (optional)
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 10–12 store-bought empanada discs
- 1 egg, beaten with 1 tbsp water (egg wash)

### Instructions
1. Heat olive oil in a skillet. Sauté onion for 5 minutes, then add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Add ground beef and cook until fully browned. Drain excess fat.
1. Stir in cumin, paprika, oregano, salt, and pepper. Simmer for 2–3 minutes.
1. Remove from heat and stir in olives and parsley. Let filling cool for 10 minutes.
1. Place a spoonful of filling in the center of an empanada disc.
1. Fold dough over filling to form a half-moon. Crimp edges shut with a fork.
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Place empanadas on a lined baking sheet and brush with egg wash.
1. Bake for 20–25 minutes until golden brown and crispy.

---

## Beef Siopao
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 500g beef chuck or brisket, finely cubed or ground
- 1 medium onion, minced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- 2 tbsp oyster sauce
- 1/3 cup brown sugar
- 1 cup water or beef broth
- 2 tbsp cornstarch dissolved in 1/4 cup water (slurry)
- 4 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 tbsp active dry yeast
- 1/2 cup white sugar
- 1.5 cups warm water
- 1/4 cup vegetable oil or shortening
- 2 tsp baking powder
- 1/2 tsp salt
- Optional: Hard-boiled egg wedges, star anise, bay leaf

### Instructions
1. Sauté garlic and onion, add beef and brown. Simmer with soy sauce, oyster sauce, sugar, and water until meat is tender. Thicken with slurry and cool completely.
1. Activate yeast in warm water and sugar. Mix with flour, remaining sugar, salt, oil, and baking powder. Knead until smooth and let rise for 1 hour.
1. Divide dough into 12–15 balls. Flatten each, add a spoonful of beef filling (and egg wedge), and pinch to seal.
1. Place buns on parchment paper squares and let rest for 15–20 minutes.
1. Steam on medium heat for 15 minutes. Let rest for 2 minutes before opening the lid to prevent collapsing.

---

## Beef Lumpia
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) ground beef (90/10 lean)
- 1 medium carrot, finely minced
- 1 small onion, finely minced
- 3–4 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 large egg
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1–2 tbsp oyster sauce
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 30–40 lumpia wrappers
- 1 egg, beaten for sealing
- 2–3 cups cooking oil for frying

### Instructions
1. In a bowl, combine beef, carrot, onion, garlic, egg, soy sauce, and oyster sauce. Season with salt and pepper and mix well.
1. Place 1 tablespoon of mixture on a lumpia wrapper. Fold in sides and roll tightly. Seal the edge with egg wash.
1. Heat oil to 350°F (175°C). Fry rolls in batches for 4–6 minutes until golden brown and meat is cooked through.
1. Drain on paper towels. Serve with sweet chili sauce or spicy vinegar.

---

## Philly Cheesesteak
- **Style:** Street Food & Snacks
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Ribeye steak, thinly sliced
- 4–8 slices of White American or Provolone cheese
- 1 large yellow onion, thinly sliced
- 2–4 soft hoagie rolls
- 2 tbsp vegetable oil or butter
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Optional: Garlic powder, green bell peppers, mushrooms

### Instructions
1. Freeze steak for 30–60 minutes, then slice against the grain as thinly as possible.
1. Sauté onions (and peppers if using) in a skillet until softened and lightly caramelized. Remove from pan.
