1. Add more oil and cook steak on high heat until browned. Season with salt, pepper, and garlic powder.
1. Mix onions back with the meat. Divide into portions and top with cheese to melt.
1. Scoop cheesy meat into sliced hoagie rolls and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Steak
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 thick-cut steaks (Ribeye or Strip)
- Kosher salt
- Freshly ground black pepper
- 2 tbsp high-smoke point oil (e.g., canola or grapeseed)
- 3 tbsp unsalted butter
- 3 cloves garlic, smashed
- 2 sprigs fresh rosemary or thyme

### Instructions
1. Remove steaks from the refrigerator 30-45 minutes before cooking to reach room temperature. Pat dry thoroughly with paper towels.
1. Season both sides generously with salt and pepper.
1. Heat oil in a heavy cast-iron skillet over high heat until it just begins to smoke.
1. Carefully place steaks in the pan. Sear for 3-4 minutes per side without moving them to develop a deep brown crust.
1. Reduce heat to medium-high. Add butter, garlic, and herbs to the skillet.
1. Once butter is melted and foaming, tilt the pan and use a large spoon to continuously baste the steaks with the flavored butter for another 2-3 minutes.
1. Check for desired doneness (135°F for medium-rare).
1. Transfer steaks to a cutting board and let rest for 5-10 minutes before slicing to retain juices.

---

## Prime Rib
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 Standing Rib Roast (5–10 lbs, bone-in or boneless)
- 2-3 tbsp olive oil
- 2 tbsp Kosher salt
- 1 tbsp freshly cracked black pepper
- 4-6 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh rosemary, chopped
- 1 tbsp fresh thyme, chopped

### Instructions
1. Temper the meat by removing it from the fridge 2 hours before cooking.
1. Preheat oven to 500°F (260°C).
1. In a small bowl, mix olive oil, garlic, salt, pepper, and herbs to create a rub.
1. Pat the roast dry and rub the herb paste over the entire surface.
1. Place roast in a heavy roasting pan, fat side up. Bake at 500°F for 15 minutes to create a crust.
1. Reduce oven temperature to 325°F (165°C) without opening the door.
1. Roast until internal temperature reaches 125°F for medium-rare (approx. 12-15 minutes per pound).
1. Remove from oven and tent loosely with foil. Let rest for 20-30 minutes before carving.

---

## Roast Beef
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3–4 lb beef roast (Top Round, Eye of Round, or Sirloin Tip)
- 2 tbsp extra-virgin olive oil
- 4 tsp Kosher salt
- 1 tbsp freshly ground black pepper
- 3 cloves garlic, finely chopped
- 1 tbsp fresh rosemary, finely chopped
- 1 tbsp fresh thyme, finely chopped

### Instructions
1. Bring the beef to room temperature for 60 minutes and pat dry.
1. Mix oil, garlic, salt, pepper, and herbs into a paste; rub all over the roast.
1. Preheat oven to 450°F (230°C).
1. Place roast on a rack in a roasting pan and sear in the oven for 15 minutes.
1. Lower heat to 325°F (165°C) and continue roasting until internal temp hits 135°F (medium-rare) or 145°F (medium).
1. Remove from oven, tent with foil, and rest for 15-20 minutes.
1. Slice thinly against the grain for serving.

---

## Beef BBQ
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 3–4 lbs boneless beef chuck roast
- 1.5 to 2 cups BBQ sauce (divided)
- 1/2 cup beef stock
- 1 tbsp apple cider vinegar
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 2 tbsp brown sugar
- 1 tsp each: garlic powder, onion powder
- 1/2 tsp each: salt, black pepper

### Instructions
1. Mix brown sugar, garlic powder, onion powder, salt, and pepper; rub over the roast.
1. Optional: Sear the roast in a hot skillet for 2 minutes per side for extra flavor.
1. Place roast in a slow cooker. Add beef stock, vinegar, and Worcestershire sauce around the meat.
1. Pour 1 cup of BBQ sauce over the top.
1. Cook on Low for 8-10 hours (or High for 5-6 hours) until fork-tender.
1. Transfer meat to a bowl and shred with two forks, removing excess fat.
1. Return shredded beef to slow cooker, add remaining BBQ sauce, and warm for 15 minutes before serving.

---

## Beef Satay
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs flank steak or sirloin, sliced into thin 1-inch wide strips
- 1/4 cup full-fat coconut milk
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp each: brown sugar, lime juice, fish sauce (optional)
- 1 tbsp minced garlic
- 1 tsp each: minced ginger, turmeric powder, ground coriander
- 1/2 tsp ground cumin
- Peanut Sauce: 1/2 cup peanut butter, 1/2 cup coconut milk, 1 tbsp red curry paste, 1 tbsp lime juice

### Instructions
1. Whisk marinade ingredients and toss with beef. Refrigerate for at least 1 hour (up to overnight).
1. Soak bamboo skewers in water for 30 minutes.
1. Thread beef onto skewers in an accordion fashion.
1. Make peanut sauce: Combine sauce ingredients in a pan over medium-low heat; stir until smooth and thickened.
1. Preheat grill or grill pan to medium-high. Oil the grates.
1. Grill skewers for 2-3 minutes per side until charred and cooked through.
1. Serve hot with warm peanut sauce.

---

## Carne Asada
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs skirt steak or flank steak
- 1/3 cup olive oil
- 1/4 cup soy sauce
- 1/3 cup fresh lime juice
- 1/4 cup fresh orange juice
- 4-6 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
- 1 jalapeño, minced
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- 1 tsp dried Mexican oregano

### Instructions
1. Whisk oil, soy sauce, citrus juices, garlic, cilantro, and spices in a bag or bowl.
1. Add steak and marinate in the fridge for 2-4 hours (no more than 8).
1. Preheat grill to high heat (450°F).
1. Remove steak from marinade (discard marinade) and grill for 3-5 minutes per side for skirt steak (5-7 for flank).
1. Aim for internal temp of 130°F-135°F.
1. Let rest for 10 minutes under foil.
1. Slice thinly against the grain and serve in tortillas.

---

## Beef Kebabs
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 to 2 lbs top sirloin, cut into 1-inch cubes
- 1 large red onion, 1-inch chunks
- 2 bell peppers, 1-inch chunks
- 8-12 whole mushrooms
- 1/4 cup olive oil
- 2 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp dried oregano
- 1/2 tsp black pepper

### Instructions
1. Soak wooden skewers for 30 minutes.
1. Whisk oil, soy sauce, Worcestershire, garlic, and seasonings. Marinate beef for at least 30 minutes.
1. Thread beef and vegetables onto skewers, alternating pieces.
1. Preheat grill to medium-high (400°F).
1. Grill for 8-10 minutes, turning every few minutes, until beef is cooked to preference.
1. Rest for 3-5 minutes before serving.

---

## Churrasco
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2.5 to 3 lbs Picanha (Top Sirloin Cap with fat cap)
- 2-3 tbsp coarse sea salt (Sal Grosso)
- Optional: 2 cloves garlic and 1 tbsp olive oil for rub
- Chimichurri (optional): Parsley, garlic, red wine vinegar, olive oil, red pepper flakes

### Instructions
1. Slice Picanha into 2-inch thick steaks, cutting with the grain.
1. Fold steaks into a 'C' shape (fat cap out) and thread onto a long metal skewer.
1. Rub generously with coarse salt; let sit for 10 minutes then shake off excess.
1. Grill over high heat (charcoal preferred), searing fat side first then rotating.
1. Once browned, shave thin slices directly off the skewer for serving.
1. Return skewer to grill to continue cooking internal layers.

---

## Beef Yakitori
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb beef sirloin or flap meat, 1-inch cubes
- 2 green onions, 1-inch pieces
- 1/2 cup soy sauce
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 2 tbsp mirin
- 2 tbsp sake or water
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1/2 tsp grated ginger
- Sesame seeds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Simmer soy sauce, sugar, mirin, sake, garlic, and ginger for 5-8 minutes until slightly thickened into a glaze (Tare).
1. Thread beef and green onions onto soaked bamboo skewers.
1. Preheat grill or broiler to medium-high.
1. Grill for 2-3 minutes per side.
1. In the last 2 minutes of cooking, baste generously with the Tare sauce.
1. Remove and garnish with sesame seeds. Serve with extra sauce.

---

## Smoked Brisket
- **Style:** Grilled & Roasted
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 whole packer beef brisket (12–14 lbs)
- 1/4 cup coarse Kosher salt
- 1/4 cup coarse ground black pepper
- 2 tbsp yellow mustard (as binder)
- Spritz: 1 cup apple cider vinegar mixed with 1 cup water

### Instructions
1. Trim brisket, leaving 1/4 inch of the fat cap. Apply mustard then generous salt and pepper rub.
1. Preheat smoker to 225°F (107°C) using oak or hickory.
1. Place brisket in smoker (fat side down) and smoke until internal temp reaches 160°F-165°F (approx. 6-8 hours).
1. Spritz with vinegar mixture every hour after the first 3 hours.
1. Wrap tightly in peach butcher paper or foil once 'bark' is set (around 165°F).
1. Continue smoking until internal temp reaches 203°F and is probe-tender.
1. Rest in a cooler for at least 2 hours before slicing against the grain.

---

## Beef Salad
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb flank steak or sirloin
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp oil
- Salt and pepper to taste
- 3 tbsp lime juice (about 2 limes)
- 2 tbsp fish sauce
- 1 tbsp brown sugar or palm sugar
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1/2 tsp red chili flakes or 1 fresh Thai bird's eye chili, finely minced
- 1 head Romaine lettuce or 4 cups mixed greens
- 1 cucumber, sliced
- 1 cup cherry tomatoes, halved
- 1/2 red onion, thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro
- 1/4 cup fresh mint leaves
- 1/4 cup crushed roasted peanuts (optional garnish)

### Instructions
1. Rub the steak with soy sauce, oil, salt, and pepper. Grill or pan-sear over high heat for 3–4 minutes per side (for medium-rare).
1. Let the meat rest for 5–10 minutes before slicing thinly against the grain.
1. In a small bowl, whisk together lime juice, fish sauce, sugar, garlic, and chili until sugar dissolves.
1. In a large bowl, combine lettuce, cucumber, tomatoes, red onion, cilantro, and mint.
1. Add the sliced beef to the bowl, drizzle with dressing, and toss gently.
1. Sprinkle with crushed peanuts before serving.

---

## Thai Beef Salad
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb sirloin, flank, or ribeye steak
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper
- 1 tbsp fish sauce (for marinade)
- 1 tbsp lime juice (for marinade)
- 2-3 tbsp fish sauce (for dressing)
- 3 tbsp fresh lime juice (for dressing)
- 2 tsp palm sugar or brown sugar
- 1-2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1-2 Thai bird's eye chilies, finely sliced
- 4 cups mixed salad greens or chopped romaine lettuce
- 1 English cucumber, halved and thinly sliced
- 1 cup cherry tomatoes, halved
- 1/2 small red onion, very thinly sliced
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro, roughly torn
- 1/2 cup fresh mint leaves, roughly torn
- Crushed roasted salted peanuts or toasted rice powder (optional)

### Instructions
1. Season the steak with salt, pepper, fish sauce, and lime juice. Grill or pan-sear over medium-high heat until medium-rare (3–4 minutes per side).
1. Transfer steak to a plate and let it rest for 10 minutes.
1. Whisk together the dressing ingredients: fish sauce, lime juice, sugar, garlic, and chilies until sugar dissolves.
1. In a large mixing bowl, combine greens, cucumber, tomatoes, red onion, cilantro, and mint.
1. Slice the rested steak thinly across the grain.
1. Add beef and any juices to the salad bowl, pour dressing over, toss gently, and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Lettuce Wraps
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 1 tbsp olive oil or sesame oil
- 1 red bell pepper, finely diced
- 1 can (8 oz) water chestnuts, drained and finely chopped
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1/4 cup green onions, thinly sliced
- 1 head Butter, Bibb, or Romaine lettuce
- 3 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tbsp rice vinegar
- 1 tbsp brown sugar or honey
- 1 tsp toasted sesame oil
- 1/2 tsp red pepper flakes (optional)
- 1 tsp cornstarch (optional)

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, rice vinegar, brown sugar, sesame oil, red pepper flakes, and cornstarch. Set aside.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Brown the ground beef, breaking it into crumbles, until cooked through (5-7 minutes). Drain excess grease.
1. Add red bell pepper, water chestnuts, garlic, and ginger to the skillet. Sauté for 3–4 minutes.
1. Pour the sauce over the beef mixture and stir for 1–2 minutes until thickened and evenly coated.
1. Remove from heat and stir in green onions.
1. Spoon the beef mixture into lettuce leaves and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Stir-Fry
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb sirloin or flank steak, thinly sliced against the grain
- 2 tbsp vegetable or avocado oil, divided
- 4 cups mixed vegetables (broccoli, carrots, bell pepper, snap peas)
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp fresh ginger, minced
- 1/2 cup low-sodium beef broth
- 1/3 cup low-sodium soy sauce
- 2 tbsp honey or brown sugar
- 1 tbsp cornstarch
- 1 tsp sesame oil (optional)

### Instructions
1. Whisk together broth, soy sauce, honey, cornstarch, and sesame oil in a small bowl.
1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a large skillet or wok over high heat. Sear beef strips for 2–3 minutes until browned, then remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil and stir-fry mixed vegetables for 4–5 minutes until crisp-tender.
1. Add garlic and ginger, cook for 30 seconds, then return beef to the pan.
1. Whisk the sauce again and pour over the beef and veggies. Stir for 1–2 minutes until sauce thickens.
1. Serve immediately over rice or noodles.

---

## Beef Veggie Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 2 cups sliced zucchini
- 1 cup matchstick carrots
- 1 red bell pepper, diced
- 1 bunch green onions, sliced
- 1/3 cup brown sugar
- 1/3 cup low-sodium soy sauce
- 1 1/2 tbsp sesame oil
- 2-3 tbsp Gochujang (optional)
- 3/4 tsp ground ginger
- 3/4 tsp garlic powder
- 2 cups cooked white or brown rice

### Instructions
1. Brown and crumble ground beef in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Drain excess grease.
1. Add zucchini, carrots, bell pepper, and most of the green onions. Sauté for 7–10 minutes until tender-crisp.
1. Stir in brown sugar, soy sauce, sesame oil, Gochujang, ginger, and garlic powder.
1. Simmer for 5 minutes to let flavors meld and sauce thicken.
1. Divide rice into bowls, top with beef mixture, and garnish with remaining green onions.

---

## Beef Quinoa Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 cup dry quinoa, rinsed
- 2 cups water or chicken broth
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/4 tsp fresh ginger, minced
- 1/3 cup brown sugar
- 1/4 cup low-sodium soy sauce
- 1 tbsp sesame oil
- 1/2 tsp crushed red pepper flakes
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 2 green onions, sliced
- Sesame seeds (optional garnish)

### Instructions
1. Combine quinoa and water/broth in a pot. Bring to a boil, cover, and simmer for 15 minutes. Fluff with a fork.
1. Heat oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Brown the beef and drain excess fat.
1. Stir in garlic and ginger, cooking for 1 minute.
1. Whisk together brown sugar, soy sauce, sesame oil, and red pepper flakes. Pour over beef.
1. Simmer for 3–5 minutes until sauce thickens. Season with salt and pepper.
1. Divide quinoa into bowls, top with beef, and garnish with green onions and sesame seeds.

---

## Beef Zoodle Bowl
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb extra lean ground beef or thinly sliced steak
- 1.5 lbs zucchini noodles (zoodles)
- 3 green onions, sliced
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame seeds
- 2 tbsp low-sodium tamari or soy sauce
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame oil
- 1 tbsp honey or brown sugar
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- 1/4 tsp red pepper flakes (optional)

### Instructions
1. Whisk together tamari, sesame oil, honey, garlic, ginger, and red pepper flakes.
1. Brown the beef in a large skillet over medium-high heat (about 5 minutes). Drain excess fat.
1. Pour the sauce over the beef and add zoodles to the skillet.
1. Flash sauté for 2–3 minutes until zoodles are heated through but still firm.
1. Remove from heat, stir in green onions, and sprinkle with sesame seeds.

---

## Steamed Beef
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb flank steak, thinly sliced against the grain
- 1 tbsp soy sauce
- 1 tsp ginger, minced
- 1 tsp cornstarch
- 1 tsp oil
- 1/4 tsp sugar
- 2 green onions, thinly sliced
- 1 tsp hot peanut oil (optional)

### Instructions
1. Toss the sliced beef with soy sauce, minced ginger, cornstarch, oil, and sugar. Let marinate for 15 minutes.
1. Spread the beef thinly and evenly on a heatproof plate.
1. Place the plate in a steamer over boiling water.
1. Steam on high heat for 8–10 minutes until just tender.
1. Garnish with fresh scallions and a drizzle of hot peanut oil if desired.

---

## Poached Beef
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 600g–800g beef eye fillet, trimmed of fat
- 1 liter low-sodium beef or chicken stock
- 1 small onion, halved
- 2 carrots, peeled and halved
- 2 bay leaves
- 1 sprig rosemary
- 3-4 sprigs fresh thyme
- 1 tsp whole black peppercorns
- 175ml dry white wine (optional)
- Salt and black pepper for seasoning

### Instructions
1. Combine stock, onion, carrots, bay leaves, rosemary, thyme, peppercorns, and wine in a large pot. Simmer for 10-15 minutes.
1. Season the beef fillet with salt and pepper.
1. Gently lower the beef into the shimmering liquid, ensuring it is submerged.
1. Poach for 18–20 minutes for medium-rare (adjust time for desired doneness).
1. Remove beef and let it rest for 10 minutes before slicing into medallions.
1. Serve with the poached carrots and a light herb vinaigrette.

---

## Beef Avocado Salad
- **Style:** Healthy & Light
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs sirloin steak
- 1 tsp garlic powder
- 1 tsp chili powder
- Salt and pepper to taste
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- 8 cups chopped Romaine lettuce
- 2 large avocados, sliced or cubed
- 1 large cucumber, sliced
- 4 green onions, thinly sliced
- 1/4 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 1 large lemon, juiced
- 2 tbsp fresh parsley, finely chopped

### Instructions
1. Season the steak with salt, pepper, garlic powder, and chili powder.
1. Cook in a skillet over medium-high heat for 5-6 minutes per side (medium-rare).
1. Let steak rest for 5 minutes, then slice thinly against the grain.
1. Whisk together olive oil, lemon juice, parsley, salt, and pepper for the dressing.
1. In a large bowl, toss lettuce, cucumber, and green onions.
1. Top with avocado and steak strips, drizzle with dressing, and serve.

---

## Beef Pot Pie
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 ½ lbs sirloin or chuck roast, cut into ½-inch cubes
- 1 medium yellow onion, diced
- 2 carrots, peeled and sliced into rounds
- 2 celery ribs, sliced
- 1 cup frozen peas
- 1 cup potatoes, peeled and diced (optional)
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp salt (plus more for seasoning beef)
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1/2 tsp dried thyme or rosemary
- 3 tbsp butter or olive oil
- 1/3 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 cups beef broth
- 1/2 cup whole milk or heavy cream
- 2 store-bought or homemade pie crusts
- 1 egg, beaten (for egg wash)

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).
1. In a large skillet, brown the beef in batches with oil/salt/pepper; remove and set aside.
1. In the same pan, melt butter and sauté onion, carrots, and celery for 5 minutes. Add garlic and cook for 30 seconds.
1. Sprinkle flour over vegetables and stir for 1 minute. Slowly whisk in beef broth and milk; simmer until thickened (3-5 minutes).
1. Stir in the beef, potatoes (par-boiled if preferred), peas, Worcestershire sauce, and herbs. Adjust seasoning and remove from heat.
1. Place one pie crust into a 9-inch pie plate. Pour in the filling and top with the second crust.
1. Trim and crimp the edges to seal. Cut 3-4 slits in the top crust.
1. Brush with egg wash and bake for 35-45 minutes until the crust is golden and filling is bubbling.
1. Let rest for 10 minutes before slicing.

---

## Meatloaf
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs ground beef (80-85% lean)
- 3/4 cup breadcrumbs (Panko or Italian)
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1/3 cup milk
- 1 small onion, finely diced
- 2-3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup ketchup (plus extra for glaze)
- 1-2 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1 tsp Italian seasoning
- Glaze: 1/4 cup ketchup, 1 tbsp brown sugar, 1 tsp mustard

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease a loaf pan or line a baking sheet.
1. In a large bowl, combine beef, breadcrumbs, eggs, milk, onion, garlic, 1/2 cup ketchup, Worcestershire, and seasonings.
1. Mix until just combined (do not overmix).
1. Shape into a loaf in the pan or on the baking sheet. Bake for 40 minutes.
1. Whisk glaze ingredients together. Spread over the meatloaf after the initial 40-minute bake.
1. Bake for another 15-20 minutes until internal temperature reaches 160°F (71°C).
1. Rest for 10 minutes before slicing.

---

## Beef Casserole
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 800g (1.75 lbs) beef chuck or stewing steak, 3cm cubes
- 2 tbsp plain flour
- 2 large onions, diced
- 3-4 large carrots, sliced
- 2-3 large potatoes, cubed
- 2 stalks celery, sliced
- 2 tbsp olive oil
- 1 tbsp tomato paste
- 500ml (2 cups) beef stock
- 250ml (1 cup) dry red wine (optional)
- 1 tsp Worcestershire sauce
- 2 bay leaves
- 1 tsp dried thyme
- Salt and black pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Toss beef chunks in flour, salt, and pepper until coated.
1. In a Dutch oven, brown the beef in oil over medium-high heat; set aside.
1. Sauté onions, carrots, and celery for 5 minutes. Stir in tomato paste and cook for 1 minute.
1. Deglaze the pan with wine or stock, scraping up the browned bits.
1. Return beef to the pot. Add potatoes, stock, Worcestershire, and herbs. Ensure liquid covers ingredients.
1. Cover and bake at 160°C (325°F) for 2.5-3 hours, or simmer on low on the stovetop for 2-2.5 hours.
1. Remove bay leaves and adjust seasoning before serving.

---

## Moussaka
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 large eggplants, sliced into 1/2-inch rounds
- 2-3 medium potatoes, sliced (optional)
- 1.5 lbs ground beef
- 1 large onion, diced
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1/2 cup dry red wine
- 1 cup tomato passata or crushed tomatoes
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1/2 cup beef stock
- 1 tsp dried oregano
- 1/2 tsp ground cinnamon
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley, chopped
- Béchamel: 4 tbsp butter, 5 tbsp flour, 2.5 cups milk, 1/2 cup grated cheese, 1/4 tsp nutmeg, 1-2 egg yolks

### Instructions
1. Salt eggplant slices and let sit for 30 minutes. Rinse and pat dry.
1. Roast or fry eggplant and potato slices until softened; set aside.
1. In a pan, brown beef with onion and garlic. Drain excess fat.
1. Stir in tomato paste, wine, passata, stock, and spices. Simmer for 30-40 minutes until thick. Stir in parsley.
1. For béchamel: Melt butter, whisk in flour. Gradually add milk until thick. Remove from heat and stir in cheese, nutmeg, and egg yolks.
1. Layer potatoes (if using), then eggplant, then the meat sauce in a 9x13 dish.
1. Pour béchamel over the top and sprinkle with extra cheese.
1. Bake at 350°F (180°C) for 45-50 minutes until golden brown.
1. Rest for 20-30 minutes before serving.

---

## Beef Enchiladas
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 1 small onion, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 oz taco seasoning packet
- 1/4 cup water or beef broth
- 8-10 medium tortillas
- 2 cups red enchilada sauce
- 2 cups shredded cheese (Cheddar or Monterey Jack)
- Optional: 4 oz diced green chiles, black beans, sour cream, cilantro

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease a 9x13 baking dish.
1. Brown beef and onion; drain fat. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in taco seasoning and water; simmer for 3-5 minutes until evaporated.
1. Spread 1/2 cup of sauce in the bottom of the dish.
1. Fill tortillas with beef mixture and cheese; roll tightly and place seam-side down in dish.
1. Top with remaining sauce and cheese. Cover with foil.
1. Bake for 20 minutes covered, then 5-10 minutes uncovered until bubbly.
1. Rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Stuffed Bell Peppers
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 6 large bell peppers (any color)
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 2 cups cooked rice
- 1 medium onion, diced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 15 oz tomato sauce
- 1 cup shredded mozzarella or cheddar cheese
- 1 tsp Italian seasoning
- 1 tsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper
- 1/2 cup water

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C). Cut tops off peppers and remove seeds.
1. Brown beef and onion in a skillet; drain grease. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
1. Stir in rice, half of the tomato sauce, and seasonings. Mix well.
1. Stand peppers in a baking dish. Spoon filling into each pepper.
1. Pour remaining tomato sauce over peppers and add 1/2 cup water to the bottom of the dish.
1. Cover with foil and bake for 35 minutes.
1. Remove foil, add cheese to the tops, and bake uncovered for 10 minutes until cheese is melted and peppers are tender.

---

## Shepherd’s Pie
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs ground beef
- 1 medium onion, diced
- 2 large carrots, diced
- 1 cup frozen peas
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1.5 cups beef broth
- 1 tbsp Worcestershire sauce
- 2.5 lbs potatoes, peeled and cubed
- 4 tbsp butter
- 1/2 cup milk or cream
- 1 tsp dried thyme
- 1 tsp dried rosemary
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Boil potatoes until tender (15-20 mins). Drain and mash with butter and milk. Season with salt/pepper.
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C).
1. Brown beef in a large skillet; drain fat. Add onion and carrots, sauté for 5-7 mins.
1. Stir in garlic, thyme, and rosemary (1 min). Stir in tomato paste and flour (2 mins).
1. Gradually add beef broth and Worcestershire; simmer until thickened. Stir in peas.
1. Transfer filling to a baking dish and spread mashed potatoes over the top. Create ridges with a fork.
1. Bake for 25-30 minutes until golden brown and bubbly.

---

## Beef Bake
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 lbs round steak or stew meat, 1-inch cubes
- 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 envelope onion soup mix
- 1 1/3 cups sliced carrots
- 4 oz sliced mushrooms, drained
- 14.5 oz diced tomatoes, undrained
- 1/2 cup water
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C).
1. In a casserole dish, toss beef cubes with flour until coated.
1. Bake uncovered for 20 minutes.
1. Remove from oven and stir in onion soup mix, carrots, mushrooms, tomatoes, and water.
1. Cover tightly and bake at 350°F or 400°F for 1.5 hours until beef is fork-tender.
1. Serve over hot cooked noodles or rice.

---

## Pastitsio
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Bucatini or Ziti pasta
- 2 lbs ground beef
- 1 large onion, chopped
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 28 oz crushed tomatoes
- 2 tbsp tomato paste
- 1 cinnamon stick
- 1/4 tsp ground cloves
- Pasta binder: 2 egg whites, 1 cup feta or parmesan cheese
- Béchamel: 1/2 cup butter, 3/4 cup flour, 4 cups warm milk, 2 egg yolks, 1/2 cup grated cheese, 1/4 tsp nutmeg
- Salt and pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Cook pasta until just under al dente. Drain and toss with egg whites and cheese.
1. Brown beef with onion and garlic. Add tomatoes, paste, cinnamon, cloves, salt, and pepper. Simmer for 30-40 mins until thick.
1. For béchamel: Melt butter, whisk in flour. Gradually whisk in warm milk until thick. Add yolks, cheese, and nutmeg.
1. Layer pasta in a greased 9x13 dish. Spread meat sauce (cinnamon stick removed) over pasta.
1. Top with béchamel and extra cheese.
1. Bake at 350°F (175°C) for 45-55 minutes until golden brown.
1. Rest for 30-45 minutes before slicing to ensure clean squares.

---

## Beef Tamale Pie
- **Style:** Baked & Comfort Food
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef
- 1 small onion, diced
- 1 bell pepper, diced
- 15 oz diced tomatoes
- 1 cup corn kernels
- 1 packet taco seasoning
- 8.5 oz corn muffin mix (e.g., Jiffy)
- 1 large egg
- 1/3 cup milk
- 1 cup shredded cheddar cheese
- Optional: black beans, sour cream, jalapeños

### Instructions
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C). Grease a 9x9 baking dish.
1. Brown beef, onion, and bell pepper; drain grease.
1. Stir in taco seasoning, tomatoes, and corn. Simmer for 5 minutes.
1. In a bowl, mix corn muffin mix, egg, and milk until just combined.
1. Pour beef mixture into the dish. Spread cornbread batter evenly over the top.
1. Bake for 15-20 minutes until the cornbread is golden brown.
1. Sprinkle cheese on top and bake for 2-3 minutes until melted.
1. Rest for 5 minutes before serving.

---

## Beef Bulgogi
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs (700g) Ribeye or Top Sirloin, thinly sliced
- 1/2 Asian Pear, grated
- 1/4 cup Soy Sauce
- 2 tbsp Brown Sugar or honey
- 2 tbsp Toasted Sesame Oil
- 3 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 tsp Fresh Ginger, grated
- 1 tbsp Mirin (optional)
- 1/2 tsp Black Pepper
- 1 tbsp Gochujang (optional)
- 1 small Onion, thinly sliced
- 2-3 Green Onions, cut into 2-inch pieces
- 1 tbsp Toasted Sesame Seeds
- Vegetable Oil for frying

### Instructions
1. Whisk together the grated pear, soy sauce, brown sugar, sesame oil, garlic, ginger, mirin, and black pepper in a large bowl.
1. Add the thinly sliced beef and sliced onions to the bowl. Massage the marinade into the meat. Cover and refrigerate for at least 2 hours (overnight preferred).
1. Heat a cast-iron skillet or grill pan over high heat with vegetable oil until smoking hot.
1. Cook the beef in batches in a single layer for 2-3 minutes until browned and slightly caramelized. Flip and cook for another minute.
1. Toss in the green onions during the last minute of cooking the final batch.
1. Transfer to a platter and garnish with toasted sesame seeds and extra green onions.

---

## Beef Sukiyaki
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) high-quality beef (ribeye or sirloin), paper-thin slices
- 1/2 cup Soy Sauce
- 1/2 cup Mirin
- 1/4 cup Sake (optional)
- 3-4 tbsp Sugar
- 1/2 cup Water or Dashi
- 1 block Grilled Tofu, cubed
- 8.5 oz Shirataki noodles, rinsed and drained
- 1 bunch Enoki mushrooms
- 4-6 Shiitake mushrooms
- 2 stalks Negi or green onions, sliced diagonally
- 2 cups Napa cabbage, chopped
- 1 bundle Shungiku or spinach
- 4 large eggs (for dipping)
- 1 tbsp vegetable oil or beef tallow

### Instructions
1. Whisk together soy sauce, mirin, sake, sugar, and water to make the broth (warishita).
1. Parboil shirataki noodles for 1 minute, then drain.
1. Heat a shallow skillet or sukiyaki pot over medium-high heat with oil or tallow.
1. Sear a few slices of beef quickly, sprinkling with a pinch of sugar.
1. Pour half the broth over the beef and push beef to one side.
1. Arrange tofu, mushrooms, noodles, and vegetables in separate sections of the pot and add remaining broth.
1. Cover and simmer for 5-10 minutes until vegetables are tender.
1. Serve with individual bowls of whisked raw egg for dipping.

---

## Beef Hot Pot
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs thinly sliced beef (ribeye or sirloin)
- 2.25 cups Water
- 1/2 cup Soy Sauce
- 1/2 cup Sake
- 1/2 cup Mirin
- 1/4 cup Sugar
- 1/4 cup Hot Chili Oil (optional)
- 1 bunch Green Onions, 2-inch pieces
- 8 oz Napa Cabbage, 2-inch strips
- 5 oz Enoki Mushrooms
- 14 oz Extra Firm Tofu, 1-inch cubes
- 12 oz Fresh Ramen Noodles
- 5 oz Dandelion Greens or Spinach
- Fresh egg yolks for dipping (optional)

### Instructions
1. Combine water, soy sauce, sake, mirin, sugar, and chili oil in a bowl.
1. Heat 3 tbsp oil in a large pot over medium-high heat. Sauté green onions and tofu until browned.
1. Add cabbage, mushrooms, and noodles. Pour the broth over ingredients.
1. Bring to a simmer, cover, and cook for 10 minutes.
1. Stir in greens until wilted. Add thinly sliced beef and cook for 2-3 minutes until done.
1. Serve immediately, traditionally with raw egg yolk for dipping.

---

## Mapo Tofu with Beef
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1.5 lbs soft or medium-firm Tofu, 1-inch cubes
- 1/4 lb Ground Beef
- 2 tsp minced Ginger
- 1.5 tbsp minced Garlic
- 2 Scallions, whites and greens separated
- 2-3 tbsp Doubanjiang (Chili Bean Paste)
- 1.5 tbsp Fermented Black Beans (Douchi), rinsed and chopped
- 1 tsp Sichuan Peppercorns, toasted and ground
- 1 cup Chicken Stock or water
- 1 tbsp Light Soy Sauce
- 1 tsp Dark Soy Sauce
- 1 tbsp Shaoxing Wine
- 1 tsp Sugar
- 1 tbsp Cornstarch mixed with 2 tbsp cold water
- 2 tbsp neutral Oil

### Instructions
1. Simmer tofu cubes in salted water for 1-2 minutes, then drain.
1. Toast Sichuan peppercorns in a dry wok, then grind into powder.
1. Heat oil in a wok over high heat and brown the ground beef until crispy.
1. Reduce heat to medium, add ginger, garlic, and scallion whites. Sauté until fragrant.
1. Add doubanjiang and fermented black beans. Stir-fry until the oil turns red.
1. Add Shaoxing wine, soy sauces, sugar, and chicken stock. Bring to a boil.
1. Carefully add tofu and simmer for 3-5 minutes.
1. Stir in cornstarch slurry in stages until the sauce thickens.
1. Off heat, stir in half the ground peppercorns and scallion greens.
1. Serve topped with remaining peppercorn powder.

---

## Beef Korma
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg Beef chuck or gravy beef, 3cm cubes
- 2 tbsp Ghee or vegetable oil
- 1 large Onion, chopped
- 2 cloves Garlic, crushed
- 1/4 cup Korma Curry Paste
- 1 cup Water or beef stock
- 1 cup plain Greek Yogurt
- 2 tbsp Brown Sugar (optional)
- Salt to taste
- Fresh Coriander for garnish
- Fried Cashews or toasted Almonds for garnish

### Instructions
1. Heat ghee in a large pan and brown beef in batches. Set aside.
1. Reduce heat, sauté onions until softened, then add garlic for 1 minute.
1. Add korma paste and sauté for 1 minute until fragrant.
1. Return beef to pan. Stir in water/stock, yogurt, and brown sugar. Season with salt.
1. Simmer covered on low heat for 1 to 1.5 hours until beef is tender.
1. Stir through coriander and serve over basmati rice.

---

## Beef Vindaloo
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 kg (2.2 lbs) boneless Beef (chuck or stewing), 1-inch cubes
- 3 medium Onions, finely sliced
- 2-3 tbsp Vegetable Oil
- 8-10 whole Kashmiri red chillies
- 1/2 cup White Vinegar
- 4 cloves Garlic
- 1-inch piece fresh Ginger, peeled
- 1 tsp Cumin Seeds
- 1 tsp Mustard Seeds
- 1/2 tsp Black Peppercorns
- 4-5 whole Cloves
- 1-inch Cinnamon stick
- 1 Bay Leaf
- 1 tsp Sugar (optional)
- Salt to taste

### Instructions
1. Toast cumin, mustard seeds, peppercorns, cloves, cinnamon, and bay leaf until fragrant, then grind into powder.
1. Blend ground spices with chillies, vinegar, garlic, and ginger into a smooth paste. Marinate beef in this paste for at least 2 hours.
1. Fry onions in oil until deep golden brown. Add beef and sear.
1. Stir in vindaloo paste and fry for 3-5 minutes until oil separates.
1. Add 1 cup water, bring to boil, then simmer covered for 45-60 minutes until beef is tender.
1. Season with salt and sugar. Simmer uncovered to thicken if needed.

---

## Beef Laksa
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 850g Gravy Beef or chuck steak, 3cm pieces
- 230g Laksa Paste
- 1.5 tbsp Lemongrass Paste
- 2 Shallots or 1 red onion, chopped
- 2 Garlic cloves, crushed
- 1 Red Chilli, chopped (optional)
- 4 cups Beef Stock
- 400ml Coconut Milk
- 1/4 cup Lime Juice
- 1 tbsp Fish Sauce (optional)
- 250g Rice Stick Noodles
- 1 cup Bean Sprouts
- Spring onions, Coriander, Mint, Lime wedges for garnish

### Instructions
1. Brown beef in oil in batches. Return all beef to the pan.
1. Add laksa paste, lemongrass, onion, garlic, and chilli. Cook for 2 minutes.
1. Add beef stock and coconut milk. Simmer covered on low for 2 to 2.5 hours until beef is tender.
1. Stir in lime juice and fish sauce.
1. Cook rice noodles according to packet instructions and divide into bowls.
1. Ladle soup and beef over noodles. Garnish with bean sprouts, herbs, and lime.

---

## Beef Pad Thai
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Sirloin, flank steak, or ribeye, thinly sliced
- 8 oz Rice Noodles (dried wide or medium)
- 3 tbsp Tamarind Paste
- 3 tbsp Fish Sauce
- 3 tbsp Brown Sugar or coconut sugar
- 1 tbsp Oyster Sauce
- 1 tsp Sriracha or chili flakes (optional)
- 2 Eggs, lightly beaten
- 3 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh Ginger, grated
- 2 cups fresh Bean Sprouts
- 4 Scallions, 1-inch pieces
- 2 tbsp neutral Oil
- Crushed peanuts, Lime wedges, fresh Cilantro for garnish

### Instructions
1. Soak rice noodles in hot water for 20-30 minutes until al dente. Drain.
1. Whisk tamarind, fish sauce, sugar, oyster sauce, and sriracha to make the sauce.
1. Sear beef in 1 tbsp oil over high heat for 1-2 minutes per side. Remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil, sauté garlic and ginger for 30 seconds.
1. Push aromatics aside, scramble eggs until just cooked.
1. Add noodles and sauce. Toss for 2-3 minutes, adding water if too dry.
1. Return beef to pan, add bean sprouts and scallions. Toss for 1 minute.
1. Garnish with peanuts, cilantro, and lime.

---

## Beef Sate Lilit
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (500g) Ground Beef
- 1/4 cup grated Coconut, toasted
- 2-3 tbsp thick Coconut Milk
- 12-15 Lemongrass stalks (for skewers)
- 4-5 Shallots, minced
- 3 cloves Garlic, minced
- 2-3 Red Chilies, minced
- 1 tsp Ginger, grated
- 1 tsp Galangal, grated
- 1/2 tsp Turmeric powder
- 1 tsp ground Coriander
- 1 tbsp Palm Sugar
- 1 tsp Tamarind Paste
- 2 Kaffir Lime Leaves, finely shredded
- Salt and Pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Blend shallots, garlic, chilies, ginger, galangal, turmeric, coriander, sugar, and tamarind into a paste. Sauté for 2-3 minutes, then cool.
1. Combine ground beef, coconut, coconut milk, lime leaves, and spice paste in a bowl. Mix until tacky.
1. Trim and lightly crush the bulbous end of lemongrass stalks.
1. Wrap a portion of meat mixture around the bulbous end of each lemongrass stalk, pressing firmly.
1. Grill skewers over medium heat for 3-5 minutes per side until cooked and charred.
1. Serve with sambal matah or sweet soy sauce.

---

## Beef Teppanyaki
- **Style:** Asian & Specialty
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb (450g) Sirloin, Ribeye, or NY Strip, thinly sliced
- 3 tbsp Soy Sauce
- 2 tbsp Mirin
- 1 tsp Garlic powder or 2 cloves minced garlic
- 1 tsp black Pepper
- 1/2 tsp ground Ginger
- 3 tbsp Vegetable or canola oil
- 1 large Onion, sliced into rings (optional)
- 1 cup sliced Mushrooms (optional)
- 1 bunch Asparagus or sliced bell peppers (optional)
- 1 tbsp Soy Sauce for seasoning vegetables

### Instructions
1. Whisk soy sauce, mirin, garlic, pepper, and ginger. Marinate beef for at least 1 hour.
1. Heat a large flat griddle or heavy skillet over medium-high heat until very hot.
1. Drizzle 2 tbsp oil. Sear beef in a single layer for 1-2 minutes per side. Remove and set aside.
1. Add remaining oil and stir-fry optional vegetables for 3-5 minutes. Season with soy sauce.
1. Return beef to pan for 30 seconds to combine and toss with juices.
1. Serve hot with steamed rice or dipping sauce like ponzu.

---

## Beef Omelette
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2–3 large eggs
- 2 oz (approx. 1/4 cup) ground beef (80/20 or lean)
- 2 tbsp finely chopped onion
- 2 tbsp chopped bell peppers (optional)
- ½ tsp salt
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- ½ tsp chili powder (optional)
- ½ tbsp butter or cooking oil
- Optional: Shredded cheddar cheese, chopped cilantro, or sliced avocado

### Instructions
1. Cook the Beef Filling: Place a small skillet over medium-high heat. Add the ground beef and chopped onions. Cook until the beef is thoroughly browned and the onions are translucent (about 3–5 minutes).
1. Season with a pinch of salt, pepper, and chili powder. Drain any excess grease and set the filling aside in a small bowl.
1. Prepare the Eggs: In a separate bowl, crack the eggs and whisk them vigorously with a pinch of salt and pepper until the yolks and whites are fully combined and slightly frothy.
1. Cook the Omelette: Wipe the skillet clean and return it to medium heat. Add the butter or oil. Once the butter is melted and bubbling slightly, pour in the egg mixture. Tilt the pan to ensure the eggs cover the entire bottom.
1. Use a spatula to gently lift the edges, allowing the raw egg to flow underneath.
1. Assemble: When the eggs are mostly set but the top still looks slightly moist, spoon the warm beef filling onto one-half of the omelette. If using cheese, sprinkle it over the beef now.
1. Fold and Serve: Carefully fold the empty half of the omelette over the beef filling using a spatula.
1. Let it sit for another 30–60 seconds to ensure the center is warm and any cheese is melted.
1. Slide the omelette onto a plate and garnish with cilantro or avocado if desired.

---

## Beef Scramble
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 1 yellow onion, diced
- 3 cups frozen hash browns (shredded or cubed)
- 4 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1 can (14.5 oz) diced tomatoes, undrained
- 4 slices sharp cheddar cheese (or 1 cup shredded)
- 1/4 cup water
- 1/2 tsp paprika
- Salt and pepper to taste
- Optional: Chopped cilantro or green onions for garnish

### Instructions
1. Brown the Beef: In a large skillet over medium heat, cook the ground beef and diced onion until the meat is no longer pink. Drain any excess fat.
1. Season: Stir in the paprika, salt, and pepper.
1. Add Potatoes: Add the frozen hash browns to the skillet. Cook, stirring occasionally, until the potatoes are thawed and starting to soften.
1. Simmer: Pour in the water and the undrained diced tomatoes. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce the heat to low. Cover and simmer for about 5–10 minutes until the potatoes are tender.
1. Scramble the Eggs: Increase the heat to medium-low. Pour the beaten eggs over the beef and potato mixture. Stir gently and cook until the eggs are fully set to your preference.
1. Melt the Cheese: Lay the cheese slices (or sprinkle shredded cheese) over the top. Cover the skillet for 1–2 minutes until the cheese is melted and gooey.
1. Serve: Garnish with fresh cilantro or green onions if desired. Serve hot.

---

## Beef Sandwich Melt
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb sliced or shredded roast beef (deli-style or leftover)
- 8 slices of bread (Sourdough, Rye, or thick-cut White)
- 8–16 slices of cheese (Sharp Cheddar, Swiss, or Provolone)
- 2–3 tbsp butter, softened
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- Optional: Caramelized onions, horseradish mayo, or Dijon mustard

### Instructions
1. Warm the Beef: Heat a large skillet over medium heat. Add the roast beef and season with salt and pepper. Toss for 2–3 minutes until heated through. Remove the beef and set it aside.
1. Prepare the Bread: Wipe the skillet clean. Butter one side of each slice of bread.
1. Assemble: Place 4 slices of bread in the skillet, buttered-side down. Top each with a slice of cheese, a generous portion of the warm roast beef, and another slice of cheese. Top with the remaining bread slices, buttered-side up.
1. Grill: Cook for 3–4 minutes per side over medium heat until the bread is golden brown and the cheese is completely melted.
1. Serve: Remove from the pan, slice diagonally, and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Panini
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 2 slices of hearty artisan bread (Sourdough, Ciabatta, or Focaccia)
- ¼ lb thinly sliced deli roast beef
- 2 slices of Provolone, Swiss, or Sharp Cheddar
- Small handful of baby spinach or arugula
- 2 thin slices of tomato
- 1 tbsp mayonnaise (or garlic aioli)
- 1 tsp horseradish (optional)
- ½ tbsp olive oil or softened butter

### Instructions
1. Preheat: Turn on your panini press or heat a grill pan over medium-high heat.
1. Prep the Bread: Lightly brush the outside of each bread slice with olive oil or butter.
1. Layer the Inside: Place one slice of bread oiled-side down. Spread the mayonnaise (and horseradish, if using) on the top side. Layer on one slice of cheese, followed by the roast beef, tomatoes, and spinach. Top with the second slice of cheese and the final slice of bread, oiled-side up.
1. Grill: Place the sandwich in the panini press. Close the lid and cook for 3 to 5 minutes, or until the bread is golden brown and the cheese has completely melted.
1. Serve: Carefully remove the panini, let it rest for one minute, cut it diagonally, and enjoy!

---

## Beef Flatbread
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb ground beef (lean 90/10 recommended)
- 4 large flatbreads (or store-bought pizza dough/naan)
- 1 cup shredded mozzarella or crumbled feta
- 1 small red onion, thinly sliced
- 2 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp ground cumin
- ½ tsp ground coriander
- ½ tsp dried oregano
- Salt & Pepper to taste
- 1 tbsp olive oil
- Optional: Fresh parsley, cherry tomatoes, tzatziki sauce

### Instructions
1. Preheat: Preheat your oven to 400°F (200°C). Line a large baking sheet with parchment paper.
1. Cook the Beef: In a large skillet, heat 1 tbsp olive oil over medium-high heat. Add the ground beef and cook until browned (about 5–7 minutes). Drain any excess fat.
1. Sauté Aromatics: Add the sliced red onion to the skillet with the beef. Cook for 3–4 minutes until the onion is softened. Stir in the minced garlic, cumin, coriander, oregano, salt, and pepper. Cook for 1 more minute until fragrant, then remove from heat.
1. Assemble the Flatbreads: Place the flatbreads on the prepared baking sheet. Evenly distribute the beef and onion mixture across the four flatbreads.
1. Add Cheese: Sprinkle the mozzarella or feta cheese over the beef mixture.
1. Bake: Bake for 8–10 minutes, or until the cheese is melted and bubbly and the edges of the flatbread are golden brown.
1. Garnish and Serve: Remove from the oven and top with fresh parsley, cherry tomatoes, and a drizzle of tzatziki if desired. Slice and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Pizza
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb pizza dough
- 1/2 lb to 1 lb lean ground beef
- 1 small onion, chopped
- 3 garlic cloves, minced
- 1/2 tsp dried oregano
- 1/4 tsp salt
- 1/4 tsp black pepper
- 1/4 to 1/2 cup pizza sauce
- 3/4 cup shredded mozzarella
- 3/4 cup shredded cheddar
- Optional: Sliced bell peppers, black olives, or fresh basil

### Instructions
1. Preheat Oven: Preheat oven to 500°F (260°C).
1. Cook the Beef: In a skillet over medium-high heat, cook ground beef with chopped onion and garlic. Season with oregano, salt, and pepper. Cook for 3–5 minutes until browned. Drain excess fat and set aside.
1. Prepare the Dough: Roll or stretch the dough into a 12-inch circle. Transfer it to a greased pizza pan.
1. Assemble: Spread pizza sauce evenly over the dough. Distribute the cooked beef mixture over the sauce. Sprinkle mozzarella and cheddar cheeses over the top.
1. Bake: Bake for 10–12 minutes, or until the crust is golden brown and the cheese is bubbling.
1. Serve: Let the pizza rest for 2–3 minutes before slicing.

---

## Beef Toast
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 jar (2.25 oz) or 1 pouch (3 oz) dried chipped beef, chopped
- 2 tbsp butter
- 2 tbsp all-purpose flour
- 1 ½ to 2 cups whole milk
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- 4–6 slices of sturdy white bread, sourdough, or Texas toast
- Optional: pinch of cayenne or garlic powder

### Instructions
1. Rinse the Beef (Optional): Rinse the chopped beef under cold water and pat dry before cooking to reduce saltiness.
1. Make the Roux: In a medium skillet over medium heat, melt the butter. Whisk in the flour and cook for 1–2 minutes until slightly nutty.
1. Build the Sauce: Slowly whisk in the milk, a little at a time. Continue whisking until the sauce thickens and begins to simmer.
1. Combine: Stir in the chopped beef and black pepper. Let it simmer for 2–3 minutes until the beef is heated through and the sauce is creamy.
1. Serve: Toast your bread until golden brown. Spoon the warm beef and gravy generously over the toast and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Wrap Melt
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Ground Beef
- 1 large Bell Pepper, thinly sliced
- 4 large Flour Tortillas
- 1 cup Shredded Cheddar or Monterey Jack
- 4 tbsp Sour Cream
- 2 tbsp Cream Cheese
- Hot sauce to taste
- 1 tbsp Butter
- Salt and Black Pepper to taste

### Instructions
1. Prepare Sauce: Stir together the sour cream, cream cheese, and hot sauce. Microwave for 20–30 seconds to soften, then stir until smooth.
1. Cook Filling: Heat a large pan over medium-high heat. Add the ground beef and sliced peppers. Season with salt and pepper. Cook until browned (about 5–7 minutes). Drain any excess grease.
1. Assemble: Spread the creamy sauce over one half of each tortilla. Top with the beef and pepper mixture, then sprinkle generously with cheese. Fold the tortillas in half.
1. The Melt: Melt 1 tbsp of butter in the pan over medium heat. Place the folded wraps in the pan and cook for 3–4 minutes per side until the tortilla is golden brown and the cheese is fully melted.
1. Serve: Cut into wedges and serve immediately.

---

## Beef Rice Bowl
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb lean ground beef
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 1 tsp fresh ginger, grated
- ¼ cup soy sauce
- ¼ cup brown sugar
- 2 tsp toasted sesame oil
- ¼ tsp crushed red pepper flakes (optional)
- ¼ tsp black pepper
- 2–3 cups hot cooked rice (Jasmine or Calrose)
- 2 green onions, thinly sliced
- 1 tbsp toasted sesame seeds

### Instructions
1. Brown the Beef: In a large skillet over medium-high heat, cook the ground beef and minced garlic until browned and no longer pink (about 5–7 minutes).
1. Drain: Carefully drain any excess grease from the skillet.
1. Prepare the Sauce: Whisk together the soy sauce, brown sugar, sesame oil, ginger, red pepper flakes, and black pepper.
1. Simmer: Pour the sauce over the cooked beef. Let the mixture simmer over medium-low heat for 2–3 minutes until the sauce thickens slightly.
1. Assemble: Divide the hot rice into four bowls. Top each with a generous portion of the beef mixture.
1. Garnish: Sprinkle with sliced green onions and sesame seeds before serving.

## Beef Stir-Fry Noodles
- **Style:** Quick Meals
- **Source:** 200_pork_beef_dishes.docx

### Ingredients
- 1 lb Top Sirloin or Flank Steak, sliced thinly against the grain
- 8 oz Noodles (rice noodles, udon, or ramen)
- 2 tbsp Cooking Oil
- 1 Red Bell Pepper, thinly sliced
- 1 Large Onion, thinly sliced
- 2 Carrots, julienned
- 8 oz Broccoli florets
- 1/2 cup Soy Sauce
- 4–6 cloves Garlic, minced
- 1 tbsp Fresh Ginger, grated
- 2 tbsp Brown Sugar
- 1 tbsp Oyster Sauce (optional)
- 1 tbsp Sesame Oil
- 1 tbsp Cornstarch
- 1 tsp Chili Garlic Sauce (optional)

### Instructions
1. Prepare the Sauce: Whisk together the soy sauce, minced garlic, grated ginger, brown sugar, sesame oil, cornstarch, and optional oyster/chili sauce.
1. Cook the Noodles: Prepare your noodles according to the package instructions. Drain and set aside.
1. Sear the Beef: Heat 1 tbsp oil in a large wok or skillet. Add the beef slices and cook for 2–3 minutes until browned. Remove the beef and set aside.
1. Stir-Fry Vegetables: Add the remaining tablespoon of oil. Add the onions and cook for 2 minutes. Add the bell peppers, carrots, and broccoli. Stir-fry for 3–5 minutes until crisp-tender.
1. Combine: Return the cooked beef and noodles to the pan with the vegetables.
1. Thicken: Pour the sauce over the mixture. Toss for 1–2 minutes until the sauce has thickened and evenly coats the noodles and beef.
1. Serve: Garnish with sesame seeds or sliced green onions and serve immediately.

---
